Vālmīki Rāmāyaṇa
 Yuddhakāṇḍa
a śrutvā hanumato vākyaṃ yathāvad abhibhāṣitam
c rāmaḥ prītisamāyukto vākyam uttaram abravīt
a kṛtaṃ hanumatā kāryaṃ sumahad bhuvi duṣkaram
c manasāpi yad anyena na śakyaṃ dharaṇītale
a na hi taṃ paripaśyāmi yas tareta mahārṇavam
c anyatra garuṇād vāyor anyatra ca hanūmataḥ
a devadānavayakṣāṇāṃ gandharvoragarakṣasām
c apradhṛṣyāṃ purīṃ laṅkāṃ rāvaṇena surakṣitām
a praviṣṭaḥ sattvam āśritya jīvan ko nāma niṣkramet
c ko viśet sudurādharṣāṃ rākṣasaiś ca surakṣitām
e yo vīryabalasaṃpanno na samaḥ syād dhanūmataḥ
a bhṛtyakāryaṃ hanumatā sugrīvasya kṛtaṃ mahat
c evaṃ vidhāya svabalaṃ sadṛśaṃ vikramasya ca
a yo hi bhṛtyo niyuktaḥ san bhartrā karmaṇi duṣkare
c kuryāt tadanurāgeṇa tam āhuḥ puruṣottamam
a niyukto nṛpateḥ kāryaṃ na kuryād yaḥ samāhitaḥ
c bhṛtyo yuktaḥ samarthaś ca tam āhuḥ puruṣādhamam
a tanniyoge niyuktena kṛtaṃ kṛtyaṃ hanūmatā
c na cātmā laghutāṃ nītaḥ sugrīvaś cāpi toṣitaḥ
a ahaṃ ca raghuvaṃśaś ca lakṣmaṇaś ca mahābalaḥ
c vaidehyā darśanenādya dharmataḥ parirakṣitāḥ
a idaṃ tu mama dīnasyā mano bhūyaḥ prakarṣati
c yad ihāsya priyākhyātur na kurmi sadṛśaṃ priyam
a eṣa sarvasvabhūtas tu pariṣvaṅgo hanūmataḥ
c mayā kālam imaṃ prāpya dattas tasya mahātmanaḥ
a sarvathā sukṛtaṃ tāvat sītāyāḥ parimārgaṇam
c sāgaraṃ tu samāsādya punar naṣṭaṃ mano mama
a kathaṃ nāma samudrasya duṣpārasya mahāmbhasaḥ
c harayo dakṣiṇaṃ pāraṃ gamiṣyanti samāhitāḥ
a yady apy eṣa tu vṛttānto vaidehyā gadito mama
c samudrapāragamane harīṇāṃ kim ivottaram
a ity uktvā śokasaṃbhrānto rāmaḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥ
c hanūmantaṃ mahābāhus tato dhyānam upāgamat
a taṃ tu śokaparidyūnaṃ rāmaṃ daśarathātmajam
c uvāca vacanaṃ śrīmān sugrīvaḥ śokanāśanam
a kiṃ tvaṃ saṃtapyase vīra yathānyaḥ prākṛtas tathā
c maivaṃ bhūs tyaja saṃtāpaṃ kṛtaghna iva sauhṛdam
a saṃtāpasya ca te sthānaṃ na hi paśyāmi rāghava
c pravṛttāv upalabdhāyāṃ jñāte ca nilaye ripoḥ
a dhṛtimāñ śāstravit prājñaḥ paṇḍitaś cāsi rāghava
c tyajemāṃ pāpikāṃ buddhiṃ kṛtvātmevārthadūṣaṇīm
a samudraṃ laṅghayitvā tu mahānakrasamākulam
c laṅkām ārohayiṣyāmo haniṣyāmaś ca te ripum
a nirutsāhasya dīnasya śokaparyākulātmanaḥ
c sarvārthā vyavasīdanti vyasanaṃ cādhigacchati
a ime śūrāḥ samarthāś ca sarve no hariyūthapāḥ
c tvatpriyārthaṃ kṛtotsāhāḥ praveṣṭum api pāvakam
a eṣāṃ harṣeṇa jānāmi tarkaś cāsmin dṛḍho mama
c vikrameṇa samāneṣye sītāṃ hatvā yathā ripum
a setur atra yathā vadhyed yathā paśyema tāṃ purīm
c tasya rākṣasarājasya tathā tvaṃ kuru rāghava
a dṛṣṭvā tāṃ hi purīṃ laṅkāṃ trikūṭaśikhare sthitām
c hataṃ ca rāvaṇaṃ yuddhe darśanād upadhāraya
a setubaddhaḥ samudre ca yāval laṅkā samīpataḥ
c sarvaṃ tīrṇaṃ ca vai sainyaṃ jitam ity upadhāryatām
a ime hi samare śūrā harayaḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
c tad alaṃ viklavā buddhī rājan sarvārthanāśanī
a puruṣasya hi loke 'smiñ śokaḥ śauryāpakarṣaṇaḥ
c yat tu kāryaṃ manuṣyeṇa śauṇḍīryam avalambatā
e śūrāṇāṃ hi manuṣyāṇāṃ tvadvidhānāṃ mahātmanām
a vinaṣṭe vā pranaṣṭe vā śokaḥ sarvārthanāśanaḥ
c tvaṃ tu buddhimatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvaśāstrārthakovidaḥ
a madvidhaiḥ sacivaiḥ sārtham ariṃ jetum ihārhasi
c na hi paśyāmy ahaṃ kaṃ cit triṣu lokeṣu rāghava
a gṛhītadhanuṣo yas te tiṣṭhed abhimukho raṇe
c vānareṣu samāsaktaṃ na te kāryaṃ vipatsyate
a acirād drakṣyase sītāṃ tīrtvā sāgaram akṣayam
c tad alaṃ śokam ālambya krodham ālamba bhūpate
a niśceṣṭāḥ kṣatriyā mandāḥ sarve caṇḍasya bibhyati
c laṅganārthaṃ ca ghorasya samudrasya nadīpateḥ
a sahāsmābhir ihopetaḥ sūkṣmabuddhir vicāraya
c ime hi samare śūrā harayaḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
a tān arīn vidhamiṣyanti śilāpādapavṛṣṭibhiḥ
c kathaṃ cit paripaśyāmas te vayaṃ varuṇālayam
a kim uktvā bahudhā cāpi sarvathā vijayī bhavān
a sugrīvasya vacaḥ śrutvā hetumat paramārthavit
c pratijagrāha kākutstho hanūmantam athābravīt
a tarasā setubandhena sāgarocchoṣaṇena vā
c sarvathā susamartho 'smi sāgarasyāsya laṅghane
a kati durgāṇi durgāyā laṅkāyās tad bravīhi me
c jñātum icchāmi tat sarvaṃ darśanād iva vānara
a balasya parimāṇaṃ ca dvāradurgakriyām api
c gupti karma ca laṅkāyā rakṣasāṃ sadanāni ca
a yathāsukhaṃ yathāvac ca laṅkāyām asi dṛṣṭavān
c saram ācakṣva tattvena sarvathā kuśalo hy asi
a śrutvā rāmasya vacanaṃ hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
c vākyaṃ vākyavidāṃ śreṣṭho rāmaṃ punar athābravīt
a śrūyatāṃ sarvam ākhyāsye durgakarmavidhānataḥ
c guptā purī yathā laṅkā rakṣitā ca yathā balaiḥ
a parāṃ samṛddhiṃ laṅkāyāḥ sāgarasya ca bhīmatām
c vibhāgaṃ ca balaughasya nirdeśaṃ vāhanasya ca
a prahṛṣṭā muditā laṅkā mattadvipasamākulā
c mahatī rathasaṃpūrṇā rakṣogaṇasamākulā
a dṛḍhabaddhakavāṭāni mahāparighavanti ca
c dvārāṇi vipulāny asyāś catvāri sumahānti ca
a vapreṣūpalayantrāṇi balavanti mahānti ca
c āgataṃ parasainyaṃ tais tatra pratinivāryate
a dvāreṣu saṃskṛtā bhīmāḥ kālāyasamayāḥ śitāḥ
c śataśo rocitā vīraiḥ śataghnyo rakṣasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
a sauvarṇaś ca mahāṃs tasyāḥ prākāro duṣpradharṣaṇaḥ
c maṇividrumavaidūryamuktāvicaritāntaraḥ
a sarvataś ca mahābhīmāḥ śītatoyā mahāśubhāḥ
c agādhā grāhavatyaś ca parikhā mīnasevitāḥ
a dvāreṣu tāsāṃ catvāraḥ saṃkramāḥ paramāyatāḥ
c yantrair upetā bahubhir mahadbhir dṛḍhasaṃdhibhiḥ
a trāyante saṃkramās tatra parasainyāgame sati
c yantrais tair avakīryante parikhāsu samantataḥ
a ekas tv akampyo balavān saṃkramaḥ sumahādṛḍhaḥ
c kāñcanair bahubhiḥ stambhair vedikābhiś ca śobhitaḥ
a svayaṃ prakṛtisaṃpanno yuyutsū rāma rāvaṇaḥ
c utthitaś cāpramattaś ca balānām anudarśane
a laṅkā purī nirālambā devadurgā bhayāvahā
c nādeyaṃ pārvataṃ vanyaṃ kṛtrimaṃ ca caturvidham
a sthitā pāre samudrasya dūrapārasya rāghava
c naupathaś cāpi nāsty atra nirādeśaś ca sarvataḥ
a śailāgre racitā durgā sā pūr devapuropamā
c vājivāraṇasaṃpūrṇā laṅkā paramadurjayā
a parighāś ca śataghnyaś ca yantrāṇi vividhāni ca
c śobhayanti purīṃ laṅkāṃ rāvaṇasya durātmanaḥ
a ayutaṃ rakṣasām atra paścimadvāram āśritam
c śūlahastā durādharṣāḥ sarve khaḍgāgrayodhinaḥ
a niyutaṃ rakṣasām atra dakṣiṇadvāram āśritam
c caturaṅgeṇa sainyena yodhās tatrāpy anuttamāḥ
a prayutaṃ rakṣasām atra pūrvadvāraṃ samāśritam
c carmakhaḍgadharāḥ sarve tathā sarvāstrakovidāḥ
a arbudaṃ rakṣasām atra uttaradvāram āśritam
c rathinaś cāśvavāhāś ca kulaputrāḥ supūjitāḥ
a śataṃ śatasahasrāṇāṃ madhyamaṃ gulmam āśritam
c yātudhānā durādharṣāḥ sāgrakoṭiś ca rakṣasām
a te mayā saṃkramā bhagnāḥ parikhāś cāvapūritāḥ
c dagdhā ca nagarī laṅkā prākārāś cāvasāditāḥ
a yena kena tu mārgeṇa tarāma varuṇālayam
c hateti nagarī laṅkāṃ vānarair avadhāryatām
a aṅgado dvivido maindo jāmbavān panaso nalaḥ
c nīlaḥ senāpatiś caiva balaśeṣeṇa kiṃ tava
a plavamānā hi gatvā tāṃ rāvaṇasya mahāpurīm
c saprakārāṃ sabhavanām ānayiṣyanti maithilīm
a evam ājñāpaya kṣipraṃ balānāṃ sarvasaṃgraham
c muhūrtena tu yuktena prasthānam abhirocaya
a śrutvā hanūmato vākyaṃ yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ
c tato 'bravīn mahātejā rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
a yāṃ nivedayase laṅkāṃ purīṃ bhīmasya rakṣasaḥ
c kṣipram enāṃ vadhiṣyāmi satyam etad bravīmi te
a asmin muhūrte sugrīva prayāṇam abhirocaye
c yukto muhūrto vijayaḥ prāpto madhyaṃ divākaraḥ
a uttarā phalgunī hy adya śvas tu hastena yokṣyate
c abhiprayāma sugrīva sarvānīkasamāvṛtāḥ
a nimittāni ca dhanyāni yāni prādurbhavanti me
c nihatya rāvaṇaṃ sītām ānayiṣyāmi jānakīm
a upariṣṭād dhi nayanaṃ sphuramāṇam idaṃ mama
c vijayaṃ samanuprāptaṃ śaṃsatīva manoratham
a agre yātu balasyāsya nīlo mārgam avekṣitum
c vṛtaḥ śatasahasreṇa vānarāṇāṃ tarasvinām
a phalamūlavatā nīla śītakānanavāriṇā
c pathā madhumatā cāśu senāṃ senāpate naya
a dūṣayeyur durātmānaḥ pathi mūlaphalodakam
c rākṣasāḥ parirakṣethās tebhyas tvaṃ nityam udyataḥ
a nimneṣu vanadurgeṣu vaneṣu ca vanaukasaḥ
c abhiplutyābhipaśyeyuḥ pareṣāṃ nihataṃ balam
a sāgaraughanibhaṃ bhīmam agrānīkaṃ mahābalāḥ
c kapisiṃhā prakarṣantu śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a gajaś ca girisaṃkāśo gavayaś ca mahābalaḥ
c gavākṣaś cāgrato yāntu gavāṃ dṛptā ivarṣabhāḥ
a yātu vānaravāhinyā vānaraḥ plavatāṃ patiḥ
c pālayan dakṣiṇaṃ pārśvam ṛṣabho vānararṣabhaḥ
a gandhahastīva durdharṣas tarasvī gandhamādanaḥ
c yātu vānaravāhinyāḥ savyaṃ pārśvam adhiṣṭhitaḥ
a yāsyāmi balamadhye 'haṃ balaugham abhiharṣayan
c adhiruhya hanūmantam airāvatam iveśvaraḥ
a aṅgadenaiṣa saṃyātu lakṣmaṇaś cāntakopamaḥ
c sārvabhaumeṇa bhūteśo draviṇādhipatir yathā
a jāmbavāṃś ca suṣeṇaś ca vegadarśī ca vānaraḥ
c ṛkṣarājo mahāsattvaḥ kukṣiṃ rakṣantu te trayaḥ
a rāghavasya vacaḥ śrutvā sugrīvo vāhinīpatiḥ
c vyādideśa mahāvīryān vānarān vānararṣabhaḥ
a te vānaragaṇāḥ sarve samutpatya yuyutsavaḥ
c guhābhyaḥ śikharebhyaś ca āśu pupluvire tadā
a tato vānararājena lakṣmaṇena ca pūjitaḥ
c jagāma rāmo dharmātmā sasainyo dakṣiṇāṃ diśam
a śataiḥ śatasahasraiś ca koṭībhir ayutair api
c vāraṇābhiś ca haribhir yayau parivṛtas tadā
a taṃ yāntam anuyāti sma mahatī harivāhinī
a hṛṣṭāḥ pramuditāḥ sarve sugrīveṇābhipālitāḥ
c āplavantaḥ plavantaś ca garjantaś ca plavaṃgamāḥ
e kṣvelanto ninadantaś ca jagmur vai dakṣiṇāṃ diśam
a bhakṣayantaḥ sugandhīni madhūni ca phalāni ca
c udvahanto mahāvṛkṣān mañjarīpuñjadhāriṇaḥ
a anyonyaṃ sahasā dṛṣṭā nirvahanti kṣipanti ca
c patantaś cotpatanty anye pātayanty apare parān
a rāvaṇo no nihantavyaḥ sarve ca rajanīcarāḥ
c iti garjanti harayo rāghavasya samīpataḥ
a purastād ṛṣabho vīro nīlaḥ kumuda eva ca
c pathānaṃ śodhayanti sma vānarair bahubhiḥ saha
a madhye tu rājā sugrīvo rāmo lakṣmaṇa eva ca
c bahubhir balibhir bhīmair vṛtāḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥ
a hariḥ śatabalir vīraḥ koṭībhir daśabhir vṛtaḥ
c sarvām eko hy avaṣṭabhya rarakṣa harivāhinīm
a koṭīśataparīvāraḥ kesarī panaso gajaḥ
c arkaś cātibalaḥ pārśvam ekaṃ tasyābhirakṣati
a suṣeṇo jāmbavāṃś caiva ṛkṣair bahubhir āvṛtaḥ
c sugrīvaṃ purataḥ kṛtvā jaghanaṃ saṃrarakṣatuḥ
a teṣāṃ senāpatir vīro nīlo vānarapuṃgavaḥ
c saṃpatan patatāṃ śreṣṭhas tad balaṃ paryapālayat
a darīmikhaḥ prajaṅghaś ca jambho 'tha rabhasaḥ kapiḥ
c sarvataś ca yayur vīrās tvarayantaḥ plavaṃgamān
a evaṃ te hariśārdūlā gacchanto baladarpitāḥ
c apaśyaṃs te giriśreṣṭhaṃ sahyaṃ drumalatāyutam
a sāgaraughanibhaṃ bhīmaṃ tad vānarabalaṃ mahat
c niḥsasarpa mahāghoṣaṃ bhīmavega ivārṇavaḥ
a tasya dāśaratheḥ pārśve śūrās te kapikuñjarāḥ
c tūrṇam āpupluvuḥ sarve sadaśvā iva coditāḥ
a kapibhyām uhyamānau tau śuśubhate nararṣabhau
c mahadbhyām iva saṃspṛṣṭau grāhābhyāṃ candrabhāskarau
a tam aṅgadagato rāmaṃ lakṣmaṇaḥ śubhayā girā
c uvāca pratipūrṇārthaḥ smṛtimān pratibhānavān
a hṛtām avāpya vaidehīṃ kṣipraṃ hatvā ca rāvaṇam
c samṛddhārthaḥ samṛddhārthām ayodhyāṃ pratiyāsyasi
a mahānti ca nimittāni divi bhūmau ca rāghava
c śubhānti tava paśyāmi sarvāṇy evārthasiddhaye
a anu vāti śubho vāyuḥ senāṃ mṛduhitaḥ sukhaḥ
c pūrṇavalgusvarāś ceme pravadanti mṛgadvijāḥ
a prasannāś ca diśaḥ sarvā vimalaś ca divākaraḥ
c uśanā ca prasannārcir anu tvāṃ bhārgavo gataḥ
a brahmarāśir viśuddhaś ca śuddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
c arciṣmantaḥ prakāśante dhruvaṃ sarve pradakṣiṇam
a triśaṅkur vimalo bhāti rājarṣiḥ sapurohitaḥ
c pitāmahavaro 'smākam iṣkvākūṇāṃ mahātmanām
a vimale ca prakāśete viśākhe nirupadrave
c nakṣatraṃ param asmākam ikṣvākūṇāṃ mahātmanām
a nairṛtaṃ nairṛtānāṃ ca nakṣatram abhipīḍyate
c mūlaṃ mūlavatā spṛṣṭaṃ dhūpyate dhūmaketunā
a saraṃ caitad vināśāya rākṣasānām upasthitam
c kāle kālagṛhītānāṃ nakatraṃ grahapīḍitam
a prasannāḥ surasāś cāpo vanāni phalavanti ca
c pravānty abhyadhikaṃ gandhā yathartukusumā drumāḥ
a vyūḍhāni kapisainyāni prakāśante 'dhikaṃ prabho
c devānām iva sainyāni saṃgrāme tārakāmaye
a evam ārya samīkṣyaitān prīto bhavitum arhasi
c iti bhrātaram āśvāsya hṛṣṭaḥ saumitrir abravīt
a athāvṛtya mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ jagāma mahatī camūḥ
c ṛkṣavānaraśārdūlair nakhadaṃṣṭrāyudhair vṛtā
a karāgraiś caraṇāgraiś ca vānarair uddhataṃ rajaḥ
c bhaumam antardadhe lokaṃ nivārya savituḥ prabhām
a sā sma yāti divārātraṃ mahatī harivāhinī
c hṛṣṭapramuditā senā sugrīveṇābhirakṣitā
a vanarās tvaritaṃ yānti sarve yuddhābhinandanaḥ
c mumokṣayiṣavaḥ sītāṃ muhūrtaṃ kvāpi nāsata
a tataḥ pādapasaṃbādhaṃ nānāmṛgasamākulam
c sahyaparvatam āsedur malayaṃ ca mahī dharam
a kānanāni vicitrāṇi nadīprasravaṇāni ca
c paśyann api yayau rāmaḥ sahyasya malayasya ca
a campakāṃs tilakāṃś cūtān aśokān sinduvārakān
c karavīrāṃś ca timiśān bhañjanti sma plavaṃgamāḥ
a phalāny amṛtagandhīni mūlāni kusumāni ca
c bubhujur vānarās tatra pādapānāṃ balotkaṭāḥ
a droṇamātrapramāṇāni lambamānāni vānarāḥ
c yayuḥ pibanto hṛṣṭās te madhūni madhupiṅgalāḥ
a pādapān avabhañjanto vikarṣantas tathā latāḥ
c vidhamanto girivarān prayayuḥ plavagarṣabhāḥ
a vṛkṣebhyo 'nye tu kapayo nardanto madhudarpitāḥ
c anye vṛkṣān prapadyante prapatanty api cāpare
a babhūva vasudhā tais tu saṃpūrṇā haripuṃgavaiḥ
c yathā kamalakedāraiḥ pakvair iva vasuṃdharā
a mahendram atha saṃprāpya rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ
c adhyārohan mahābāhuḥ śikharaṃ drumabhūṣitam
a tataḥ śikharam āruhya rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ
c kūrmamīnasamākīrṇam apaśyat salilāśayam
a te sahyaṃ samatikramya malayaṃ ca mahāgirim
c āsedur ānupūrvyeṇa samudraṃ bhīmaniḥsvanam
a avaruhya jagāmāśu velāvanam anuttamam
c rāmo ramayatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ sasugrīvaḥ salakṣmaṇaḥ
a atha dhautopalatalāṃ toyaughaiḥ sahasotthitaiḥ
c velām āsādya vipulāṃ rāmo vacanam abravīt
a ete vayam anuprāptāḥ sugrīva varuṇālayam
c ihedānīṃ vicintā sā yā na pūrvaṃ samutthitā
a ataḥ paramatīro 'yaṃ sāgaraḥ saritāṃ pati
c na cāyam anupāyena śakyas taritum arṇavaḥ
a tad ihaiva niveśo 'stu mantraḥ prastūyatām iha
c yathedaṃ vānarabalaṃ paraṃ pāram avāpnuyāt
a itīva sa mahābāhuḥ sītāharaṇakarśitaḥ
c rāmaḥ sāgaram āsādya vāsam ājñāpayat tadā
a saṃprāpto mantrakālo naḥ sāgarasyeha laṅghane
c svāṃ svāṃ senāṃ samutsṛjya mā ca kaś cit kuto vrajet
e gacchantu vānarāḥ śūrā jñeyaṃ channaṃ bhayaṃ ca naḥ
a rāmasya vacanaṃ śrutvā sugrīvaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
c senāṃ nyaveśayat tīre sāgarasya drumāyute
a virarāja samīpasthaṃ sāgarasya tu tad balam
c madhupāṇḍujalaḥ śrīmān dvitīya iva sāgaraḥ
a velāvanam upāgamya tatas te haripuṃgavāḥ
c viniviṣṭāḥ paraṃ pāraṃ kāṅkṣamāṇā mahodadheḥ
a sā mahārṇavam āsādya hṛṣṭā vānaravāhinī
c vāyuvegasamādhūtaṃ paśyamānā mahārṇavam
a dūrapāram asaṃbādhaṃ rakṣogaṇaniṣevitam
c paśyanto varuṇāvāsaṃ niṣedur hariyūthapāḥ
a caṇḍanakragrahaṃ ghoraṃ kṣapādau divasakṣaye
c candrodaye samādhūtaṃ praticandrasamākulam
a caṇḍānilamahāgrāhaiḥ kīrṇaṃ timitimiṃgilaiḥ
c dīptabhogair ivākrīrṇaṃ bhujaṃgair varuṇālayam
a avagāḍhaṃ mahāsattair nānāśailasamākulam
c durgaṃ drugam amārgaṃ tam agādham asurālayam
a makarair nāgabhogaiś ca vigāḍhā vātalohitāḥ
c utpetuś ca nipetuś ca pravṛddhā jalarāśayaḥ
a agnicūrṇam ivāviddhaṃ bhāskarāmbumanoragam
c surāriviṣayaṃ ghoraṃ pātālaviṣamaṃ sadā
a sāgaraṃ cāmbaraprakhyam ambaraṃ sāgaropamam
c sāgaraṃ cāmbaraṃ ceti nirviśeṣam adṛśyata
a saṃpṛktaṃ nabhasā hy ambhaḥ saṃpṛktaṃ ca nabho 'mbhasā
c tādṛgrūpe sma dṛśyete tārā ratnasamākule
a samutpatitameghasya vīcci mālākulasya ca
c viśeṣo na dvayor āsīt sāgarasyāmbarasya ca
a anyonyair āhatāḥ saktāḥ sasvanur bhīmaniḥsvanāḥ
c ūrmayaḥ sindhurājasya mahābherya ivāhave
a ratnaughajalasaṃnādaṃ viṣaktam iva vāyunā
c utpatantam iva kruddhaṃ yādogaṇasamākulam
a dadṛśus te mahātmāno vātāhatajalāśayam
c aniloddhūtam ākāśe pravalgatam ivormibhiḥ
e bhrāntormijalasaṃnādaṃ pralolam iva sāgaram
a sā tu nīlena vidhivat svārakṣā susamāhitā
c sāgarasyottare tīre sādhu senā niveśitā
a maindaś ca dvividhaś cobhau tatra vānarapuṃgavau
c viceratuś ca tāṃ senāṃ rakṣārthaṃ sarvato diśam
a niviṣṭāyāṃ tu senāyāṃ tīre nadanadīpateḥ
c pārśvasthaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmo vacanam abravīt
a śokaś ca kila kālena gacchatā hy apagacchati
c mama cāpaśyataḥ kāntām ahany ahani vardhate
a na me duḥkhaṃ priyā dūre na me duḥkhaṃ hṛteti ca
c etad evānuśocāmi vayo 'syā hy ativartate
a vāhi vāta yataḥ kanyā tāṃ spṛṣṭvā mām api spṛśa
c tvayi me gātrasaṃsparśaś candre dṛṣṭisamāgamaḥ
a tan me dahati gātrāṇi viṣaṃ pītam ivāśaye
c hā nātheti priyā sā māṃ hriyamāṇā yad abravīt
a tadviyogendhanavatā taccintāvipulārciṣā
c rātriṃ divaṃ śarīraṃ me dahyate madanāgninā
a avagāhyārṇavaṃ svapsye saumitre bhavatā vinā
c kathaṃ cit prajvalan kāmaḥ samāsuptaṃ jale dahet
a bahv etat kāmayānasya śakyam etena jīvitum
c yad ahaṃ sā ca vāmorur ekāṃ dharaṇim āśritau
a kedārasyeva kedāraḥ sodakasya nirūdakaḥ
c upasnehena jīvāmi jīvantīṃ yac chṛṇomi tām
a kadā tu khalu susśoṇīṃ śatapatrāyatekṣaṇām
c vijitya śatrūn drakṣyāmi sītāṃ sphītām iva śriyam
a kadā nu cārubimbauṣṭhaṃ tasyāḥ padmam ivānanam
c īṣadunnamya pāsyāmi rasāyanam ivāturaḥ
a tau tasyāḥ saṃhatau pīnau stanau tālaphalopamau
c kadā nu khalu sotkampau hasantyā māṃ bhajiṣyataḥ
a sā nūnam asitāpāṅgī rakṣomadhyagatā satī
c mannāthā nāthahīneva trātāraṃ nādhigacchati
a kadā vikṣobhya rakṣāṃsi sā vidhūyotpatiṣyati
c vidhūya jaladān nīlāñ śaśilekhā śaratsv iva
a svabhāvatanukā nūnaṃ śokenānaśanena ca
c bhūyas tanutarā sītā deśakālaviparyayāt
a kadā nu rākṣasendrasya nidhāyorasi sāyakān
c sītāṃ pratyāhariṣyāmi śokam utsṛjya mānasaṃ
a kadā nu khalu māṃ sādhvī sītāmarasutopamā
c sotkaṇṭhā kaṇṭham ālambya mokṣyaty ānandajaṃ jalam
a kadā śokam imaṃ ghoraṃ maithilī viprayogajam
c sahasā vipramokṣyāmi vāsaḥ śukletaraṃ yathā
a evaṃ vilapatas tasya tatra rāmasya dhīmataḥ
c dinakṣayān mandavapur bhāskaro 'stam upāgamat
a āśvāsito lakṣmaṇena rāmaḥ saṃdhyām upāsata
c smaran kamalapatrākṣīṃ sītāṃ śokākulīkṛtaḥ
a laṅkāyāṃ tu kṛtaṃ karma ghoraṃ dṛṣṭvā bhavāvaham
c rākṣasendro hanumatā śakreṇeva mahātmanā
e abravīd rākṣasān sarvān hriyā kiṃ cid avāṅmukhaḥ
a dharṣitā ca praviṣṭā ca laṅkā duṣprasahā purī
c tena vānaramātreṇa dṛṣṭā sītā ca jānakī
a prasādo dharṣitaś caityaḥ pravarā rākṣasā hatāḥ
c āvilā ca purī laṅkā sarvā hanumatā kṛtā
a kiṃ kariṣyāmi bhadraṃ vaḥ kiṃ vā yuktam anantaram
c ucyatāṃ naḥ samarthaṃ yat kṛtaṃ ca sukṛtaṃ bhavet
a mantramūlaṃ hi vijayaṃ prāhur āryā manasvinaḥ
c tasmād vai rocaye mantraṃ rāmaṃ prati mahābalāḥ
a trividhāḥ puruṣā loke uttamādhamamadhyamāḥ
c teṣāṃ tu samavetānāṃ guṇadoṣaṃ vadāmy aham
a mantribhir hitasaṃyuktaiḥ samarthair mantranirṇaye
c mitrair vāpi samānārthair bāndhavair api vā hitaiḥ
a sahito mantrayitvā yaḥ karmārambhān pravartayet
c daive ca kurute yatnaṃ tam āhuḥ puruṣottamam
a eko 'rthaṃ vimṛśed eko dharme prakurute manaḥ
c ekaḥ kāryāṇi kurute tam āhur madhyamaṃ naram
a guṇadoṣāv aniścitya tyaktvā daivavyapāśrayam
c kariṣyāmīti yaḥ kāryam upekṣet sa narādhamaḥ
a yatheme puruṣā nityam uttamādhamamadhyamāḥ
c evaṃ mantro 'pi vijñeya uttamādhamamadhyamaḥ
a aikamatyam upāgamya śāstradṛṣṭena cakṣuṣā
c mantriṇo yatra nirastās tam āhur mantram uttamam
a bahvyo 'pi matayo gatvā mantriṇo hy arthanirṇaye
c punar yatraikatāṃ prāptaḥ sa mantro madhyamaḥ smṛtaḥ
a anyonyamatim āsthāya yatra saṃpratibhāṣyate
c na caikamatye śreyo 'sti mantraḥ so 'dhama ucyate
a tasmāt sumantritaṃ sādhu bhavanto mantrisattamāḥ
c kāryaṃ saṃpratipadyantām etat kṛtyatamaṃ mama
a vānarāṇāṃ hi vīrāṇāṃ sahasraiḥ parivāritaḥ
c rāmo 'bhyeti purīṃ laṅkām asmākam uparodhakaḥ
a tariṣyati ca suvyaktaṃ rāghavaḥ sāgaraṃ sukham
c tarasā yuktarūpeṇa sānujaḥ sabalānugaḥ
a asminn evaṃgate kārye viruddhe vānaraiḥ saha
c hitaṃ pure ca sainye ca sarvaṃ saṃmantryatāṃ mama
a ity uktā rākṣasendreṇa rākṣasās te mahābalāḥ
c ūcuḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve rāvaṇaṃ rākṣaseśvaram
a rājan parighaśaktyṛṣṭiśūlapaṭṭasasaṃkulam
c sumahan no balaṃ kasmād viṣādaṃ bhajate bhavān
a kailāsaśikharāvāsī yakṣair bahubhir āvṛtaḥ
c sumahat kadanaṃ kṛtvā vaśyas te dhanadaḥ kṛtaḥ
a sa maheśvarasakhyena ślāghamānas tvayā vibho
c nirjitaḥ samare roṣāl lokapālo mahābalaḥ
a vinihatya ca yakṣaughān vikṣobhya ca vigṛhya ca
c tvayā kailāsaśikharād vimānam idam āhṛtam
a mayena dānavendreṇa tvadbhayāt sakhyam icchatā
c duhitā tava bhāryārthe dattā rākṣasapuṃgava
a dānavendro madhur nāma vīryotsikto durāsadaḥ
c vigṛhya vaśam ānītaḥ kumbhīnasyāḥ sukhāvahaḥ
a nirjitās te mahābāho nāgā gatvā rasātalam
c vāsukis takṣakaḥ śaṅkho jaṭī ca vaśam āhṛtāḥ
a akṣayā balavantaś ca śūrā labdhavarāḥ punaḥ
c tvayā saṃvatsaraṃ yuddhvā samare dānavā vibho
a svabalaṃ samupāśritya nītā vaśam ariṃdama
c māyāś cādhigatās tatra bahavo rākṣasādhipa
a śūrāś ca balavantaś ca varuṇasya sutā raṇe
c nirjitās te mahābāho caturvidhabalānugāḥ
a mṛtyudaṇḍamahāgrāhaṃ śālmalidvīpamaṇḍitam
c avagāhya tvayā rājan yamasya balasāgaram
a jayaś ca viplulaḥ prāpto mṛtyuś ca pratiṣedhitaḥ
c suyuddhena ca te sarve lokās tatra sutoṣitāḥ
a kṣatriyair bahubhir vīraiḥ śakratulyaparākramaiḥ
c āsīd vasumatī pūrṇā mahadbhir iva pādapaiḥ
a teṣāṃ vīryaguṇotsāhair na samo rāghavo raṇe
c prasahya te tvayā rājan hatāḥ paramadurjayāḥ
a rājan nāpad ayukteyam āgatā prākṛtāj janāt
c hṛdi naiva tvayā kāryā tvaṃ vadhiṣyasi rāghavam
a tato nīlāmbudanibhaḥ prahasto nāma rākṣasaḥ
c abravīt prāñjalir vākyaṃ śūraḥ senāpatis tadā
a devadānavagandharvāḥ piśācapatagoragāḥ
c na tvāṃ dharṣayituṃ śaktāḥ kiṃ punar vānarā raṇe
a sarve pramattā viśvastā vañcitāḥ sma hanūmatā
c na hi me jīvato gacchej jīvan sa vanagocaraḥ
a sarvāṃ sāgaraparyantāṃ saśailavanakānanām
c karomy avānarāṃ bhūmim ājñāpayatu māṃ bhavān
a rakṣāṃ caiva vidhāsyāmi vānarād rajanīcara
c nāgamiṣyati te duḥkhaṃ kiṃ cid ātmāparādhajam
a abravīc ca susaṃkruddho durmukho nāma rākṣasaḥ
c idaṃ na kṣamaṇīyaṃ hi sarveṣāṃ naḥ pradharṣaṇam
a ayaṃ paribhavo bhūyaḥ purasyāntaḥpurasya ca
c śrīmato rākṣasendrasya vānarendrapradharṣaṇam
a asmin muhūrte hatvaiko nivartiṣyāmi vānarān
c praviṣṭān sāgaraṃ bhīmam ambaraṃ vā rasātalam
a tato 'bravīt susaṃkruddho vajradaṃṣṭro mahābalaḥ
c pragṛhya parighaṃ ghoraṃ māṃsaśoṇitarūpitam
a kiṃ vo hanumatā kāryaṃ kṛpaṇena tapasvinā
c rāme tiṣṭhati durdharṣe sugrīve sahalakṣmaṇe
a adya rāmaṃ sasugrīvaṃ parigheṇa salakṣmaṇam
c āgamiṣyāmi hatvaiko vikṣobhya harivāhinīm
a kaumbhakarṇis tato vīro nikumbho nāma vīryavān
c abravīt paramakurddho rāvaṇaṃ lokarāvaṇam
a sarve bhavantas tiṣṭhantu mahārājena saṃgatāḥ
c aham eko haniṣyāmi rāghavaṃ sahalakṣmaṇam
a tato vajrahanur nāma rākṣasaḥ parvatopamaḥ
c kruddhaḥ parilihan vaktraṃ jihvayā vākyam abravīt
a svairaṃ kurvantu kāryāṇi bhavanto vigatajvarāḥ
c eko 'haṃ bhakṣayiṣyāmi tān sarvān hariyūthapān
a svasthāḥ krīḍantu niścintāḥ pibantu madhuvāruṇīm
c aham eko haniṣyāmi sugrīvaṃ sahalakṣmaṇam
e sāṅgadaṃ ca hanūmantaṃ rāmaṃ ca raṇakuñjaram
a tato nikumbho rabhasaḥ sūryaśatrur mahābalaḥ
c suptaghno yajñakopaś ca mahāpārśvo mahoaraḥ
a agniketuś ca durdharṣo raśmiketuś ca rākṣasaḥ
c indrajic ca mahātejā balavān rāvaṇātmajaḥ
a prahasto 'tha virūpākṣo vajradaṃṣṭro mahābalaḥ
c dhūmrākṣaś cātikāyaś ca durmukhaś caiva rākṣasaḥ
a parighān paṭṭasān prāsāñ śaktiśūlaparaśvadhān
c cāpāni ca sabāṇāni khaḍgāṃś ca vipulāñ śitān
a pragṛhya paramakruddhāḥ samutpatya ca rākṣasāḥ
c abruvan rāvaṇaṃ sarve pradīptā iva tejasā
a adya rāmaṃ vadhiṣyāmaḥ sugrīvaṃ ca salakṣmaṇam
c kṛpaṇaṃ ca hanūmantaṃ laṅkā yena pradharṣitā
a tān gṛhītāyudhān sarvān vārayitvā vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c abravīt prāñjalir vākyaṃ punaḥ pratyupaveśya tān
a apy upāyais tribhis tāta yo 'rthaḥ prāptuṃ na śakyate
c tasya vikramakālāṃs tān yuktān āhur manīṣiṇaḥ
a pramatteṣv abhiyukteṣu daivena prahateṣu ca
c vikramās tāta sidhyanti parīkṣya vidhinā kṛtāḥ
a apramattaṃ kathaṃ taṃ tu vijigīṣuṃ bale sthitam
c jitaroṣaṃ durādharṣaṃ pradharṣayitum icchatha
a samudraṃ laṅghayitvā tu ghoraṃ nadanadīpatim
c kṛtaṃ hanumatā karma duṣkaraṃ tarkayeta kaḥ
a balāny aparimeyāni vīryāṇi ca niśācarāḥ
c pareṣāṃ sahasāvajñā na kartavyā kathaṃ cana
a kiṃ ca rākṣasarājasya rāmeṇāpakṛtaṃ purā
c ājahāra janasthānād yasya bhāryāṃ yaśasvinaḥ
a kharo yady ativṛttas tu rāmeṇa nihato raṇe
c avaśyaṃ prāṇināṃ prāṇā rakṣitavyā yathā balam
a etannimittaṃ vaidehī bhayaṃ naḥ sumahad bhavet
c āhṛtā sā parityājyā kalahārthe kṛte na kim
a na naḥ kṣamaṃ vīryavatā tena dharmānuvartinā
c vairaṃ nirarthakaṃ kartuṃ dīyatām asya maithilī
a yāvan na sagajāṃ sāśvāṃ bahuratnasamākulām
c purīṃ dārayate bāṇair dīyatām asya maithilī
a yāvat sughorā mahatī durdharṣā harivāhinī
c nāvaskandati no laṅkāṃ tāvat sītā pradīyatām
a vinaśyed dhi purī laṅkā śūrāḥ sarve ca rākṣasāḥ
c rāmasya dayitā patnī na svayaṃ yadi dīyate
a prasādaye tvāṃ bandhutvāt kuruṣva vacanaṃ mama
c hitaṃ pathyaṃ tv ahaṃ brūmi dīyatām asya maithilī
a purā śaratsūryamarīcisaṃnibhān
navāgrapuṅkhān sudṛḍhān nṛpātmajaḥ
c sṛjaty amoghān viśikhān vadhāya te
pradīyatāṃ dāśarathāya maithilī
a tyajasva kopaṃ sukhadharmanāśanaṃ
bhajasva dharmaṃ ratikīrtivardhanam
c prasīda jīvema saputrabāndhavāḥ
pradīyatāṃ dāśarathāya maithilī
a suniviṣṭaṃ hitaṃ vākyam uktavantaṃ vibhīṣaṇam
c abravīt paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ rāvaṇaḥ kālacoditaḥ
a vaset saha sapatnena kruddhenāśīviṣeṇa vā
c na tu mitrapravādena saṃvasec chatrusevinā
a jānāmi śīlaṃ jñātīnāṃ sarvalokeṣu rākṣasa
c hṛṣyanti vyasaneṣv ete jñātīnāṃ jñātayaḥ sadā
a pradhānaṃ sādhakaṃ vaidyaṃ dharmaśīlaṃ ca rākṣasa
c jñātayo hy avamanyante śūraṃ paribhavanti ca
a nityam anyonyasaṃhṛṣṭā vyasaneṣv ātatāyinaḥ
c pracchannahṛdayā ghorā jñātayas tu bhayāvahāḥ
a śrūyante hastibhir gītāḥ ślokāḥ padmavane kva cit
c pāśahastān narān dṛṣṭvā śṛṇu tān gadato mama
a nāgnir nānyāni śastrāṇi na naḥ pāśā bhayāvahāḥ
c ghorāḥ svārthaprayuktās tu jñātayo no bhayāvahāḥ
a upāyam ete vakṣyanti grahaṇe nātra saṃśayaḥ
c kṛtsnād bhayāj jñātibhayaṃ sukaṣṭaṃ viditaṃ ca naḥ
a vidyate goṣu saṃpannaṃ vidyate brāhmaṇe damaḥ
c vidyate strīṣu cāpalyaṃ vidyate jñātito bhayam
a tato neṣṭam idaṃ saumya yad ahaṃ lokasatkṛtaḥ
c aiśvaryam abhijātaś ca ripūṇāṃ mūrdhni ca sthitaḥ
a anyas tv evaṃvidhaṃ brūyād vākyam etan niśācara
c asmin muhūrte na bhavet tvāṃ tu dhik kulapāṃsanam
a ity uktaḥ paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ nyāyavādī vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c utpapāta gadāpāṇiś caturbhiḥ saha rākṣasaiḥ
a abravīc ca tadā vākyaṃ jātakrodho vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c antarikṣagataḥ śrīmān bhrātaraṃ rākṣasādhipam
a sa tvaṃ bhrātāsi me rājan brūhi māṃ yad yad icchasi
c idaṃ tu paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ na kṣamāmy anṛtaṃ tava
a sunītaṃ hitakāmena vākyam uktaṃ daśānana
c na gṛhṇanty akṛtātmānaḥ kālasya vaśam āgatāḥ
a sulabhāḥ puruṣā rājan satataṃ priyavādinaḥ
c apriyasya tu pathyasya vaktā śrotā ca durlabhaḥ
a baddhaṃ kālasya pāśena sarvabhūtāpahāriṇā
c na naśyantam upekṣeyaṃ pradīptaṃ śaraṇaṃ yathā
a dīptapāvakasaṃkāśaiḥ śitaiḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c na tvām icchāmy ahaṃ draṣṭuṃ rāmeṇa nihataṃ śaraiḥ
a śūrāś ca balavantaś ca kṛtāstrāś ca raṇājire
c kālābhipannā sīdanti yathā vālukasetavaḥ
a ātmānaṃ sarvathā rakṣa purīṃ cemāṃ sarākṣasām
c svasti te 'stu gamiṣyāmi sukhī bhava mayā vinā
a nivāryamāṇasya mayā hitaiṣiṇā
na rocate te vacanaṃ niśācara
c parītakālā hi gatāyuṣo narā
hitaṃ na gṛhṇanti suhṛdbhir īritam
a ity uktvā paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ rāvaṇaṃ rāvaṇānujaḥ
c ājagāma muhūrtena yatra rāmaḥ salakṣmaṇaḥ
a taṃ meruśikharākāraṃ dīptām iva śatahradām
c gaganasthaṃ mahīsthās te dadṛśur vānarādhipāḥ
a tam ātmapañcamaṃ dṛṣṭvā sugrīvo vānarādhipaḥ
c vānaraiḥ saha durdharṣaś cintayām āsa buddhimān
a cintayitvā muhūrtaṃ tu vānarāṃs tān uvāca ha
c hanūmatpramukhān sarvān idaṃ vacanam uttamam
a eṣa sarvāyudhopetaś caturbhiḥ saha rākṣasaiḥ
c rākṣaso 'bhyeti paśyadhvam asmān hantuṃ na saṃśayaḥ
a sugrīvasya vacaḥ śrutvā sarve te vānarottamāḥ
c sālān udyamya śailāṃś ca idaṃ vacanam abruvan
a śīghraṃ vyādiśa no rājan vadhāyaiṣāṃ durātmanām
c nipatantu hatāś caite dharaṇyām alpajīvitāḥ
a teṣāṃ saṃbhāṣamāṇānām anyonyaṃ sa vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c uttaraṃ tīram āsādya khastha eva vyatiṣṭhata
a uvāca ca mahāprājñaḥ svareṇa mahatā mahān
c sugrīvaṃ tāṃś ca saṃprekṣya khastha eva vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a rāvaṇo nāma durvṛtto rākṣaso rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c tasyāham anujo bhrātā vibhīṣaṇa iti śrutaḥ
a tena sītā janasthānād dhṛtā hatvā jaṭāyuṣam
c ruddhvā ca vivaśā dīnā rākṣasībhiḥ surakṣitā
a tam ahaṃ hetubhir vākyair vividhaiś ca nyadarśayam
c sādhu niryātyatāṃ sītā rāmāyeti punaḥ punaḥ
a sa ca na pratijagrāha rāvaṇaḥ kālacoditaḥ
c ucyamāno hitaṃ vākyaṃ viparīta ivauṣadham
a so 'haṃ paruṣitas tena dāsavac cāvamānitaḥ
c tyaktvā putrāṃś ca dārāṃś ca rāghavaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
a sarvalokaśaraṇyāya rāghavāya mahātmane
c nivedayata māṃ kṣipraṃ vibhīṣaṇam upasthitam
a etat tu vacanaṃ śrutvā sugrīvo laghuvikramaḥ
c lakṣmaṇasyāgrato rāmaṃ saṃrabdham idam abravīt
a rāvaṇasyānujo bhrātā vibhīṣaṇa iti śrutaḥ
c caturbhiḥ saha rakṣobhir bhavantaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
a rāvaṇena praṇihitaṃ tam avehi vibhīṣaṇam
c tasyāhaṃ nigrahaṃ manye kṣamaṃ kṣamavatāṃ vara
a rākṣaso jihmayā buddhyā saṃdiṣṭo 'yam upasthitaḥ
c prahartuṃ māyayā channo viśvaste tvayi rāghava
a badhyatām eṣa tīvreṇa daṇḍena sacivaiḥ saha
c rāvaṇasya nṛśaṃsasya bhrātā hy eṣa vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a evam uktvā tu taṃ rāmaṃ saṃrabdho vāhinīpatiḥ
c vākyajño vākyakuśalaṃ tato maunam upāgamat
a sugrīvasya tu tad vākyaṃ śrutvā rāmo mahābalaḥ
c samīpasthān uvācedaṃ hanūmatpramukhān harīn
a yad uktaṃ kapirājena rāvaṇāvarajaṃ prati
c vākyaṃ hetumad atyarthaṃ bhavadbhir api tac chrutam
a suhṛdā hy arthakṛccheṣu yuktaṃ buddhimatā satā
c samarthenāpi saṃdeṣṭuṃ śāśvatīṃ bhūtim icchatā
a ity evaṃ paripṛṣṭās te svaṃ svaṃ matam atandritāḥ
c sopacāraṃ tadā rāmam ūcur hitacikīrṣavaḥ
a ajñātaṃ nāsti te kiṃ cit triṣu lokeṣu rāghava
c ātmānaṃ pūjayan rāma pṛcchasy asmān suhṛttayā
a tvaṃ hi satyavrataḥ śūro dhārmiko dṛḍhavikramaḥ
c parīkṣya kārā smṛtimān nisṛṣṭātmā suhṛtsu ca
a tasmād ekaikaśas tāvad bruvantu sacivās tava
c hetuto matisaṃpannāḥ samarthāś ca punaḥ punaḥ
a ity ukte rāghavāyātha matimān aṅgado 'grataḥ
c vibhīṣaṇaparīkṣārtham uvāca vacanaṃ hariḥ
a śatroḥ sakāśāt saṃprāptaḥ sarvathā śaṅkya eva hi
c viśvāsayogyaḥ sahasā na kartavyo vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a chādayitvātmabhāvaṃ hi caranti śaṭhabuddhayaḥ
c praharanti ca randhreṣu so 'narthaḥ sumahān bhavet
a arthānarthau viniścitya vyavasāyaṃ bhajeta ha
c guṇataḥ saṃgrahaṃ kuryād doṣatas tu visarjayet
a yadi doṣo mahāṃs tasmiṃs tyajyatām aviśaṅkitam
c guṇān vāpi bahūñ jñātvā saṃgrahaḥ kriyatāṃ nṛpa
a śarabhas tv atha niścitya sārthaṃ vacanam abravīt
c kṣipram asmin naravyāghra cāraḥ pratividhīyatām
a praṇidhāya hi cāreṇa yathāvat sūkṣmabuddhinā
c parīkṣya ca tataḥ kāryo yathānyāyaṃ parigrahaḥ
a jāmbavāṃs tv atha saṃprekṣya śāstrabuddhyā vicakṣaṇaḥ
c vākyaṃ vijñāpayām āsa guṇavad doṣavarjitam
a baddhavairāc ca pāpāc ca rākṣasendrād vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c adeśa kāle saṃprāptaḥ sarvathā śaṅkyatām ayam
a tato maindas tu saṃprekṣya nayāpanayakovidaḥ
c vākyaṃ vacanasaṃpanno babhāṣe hetumattaram
a vacanaṃ nāma tasyaiṣa rāvaṇasya vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c pṛcchyatāṃ madhureṇāyaṃ śanair naravareśvara
a bhāvam asya tu vijñāya tatas tattvaṃ kariṣyasi
c yadi dṛṣṭo na duṣṭo vā buddhipūrvaṃ nararṣabha
a atha saṃskārasaṃpanno hanūmān sacivottamaḥ
c uvāca vacanaṃ ślakṣṇam arthavan madhuraṃ laghu
a na bhavantaṃ matiśreṣṭhaṃ samarthaṃ vadatāṃ varam
c atiśāyayituṃ śakto bṛhaspatir api bruvan
a na vādān nāpi saṃgharṣān nādhikyān na ca kāmataḥ
c vakṣyāmi vacanaṃ rājan yathārthaṃ rāmagauravāt
a arthānarthanimittaṃ hi yad uktaṃ sacivais tava
c tatra doṣaṃ prapaśyāmi kriyā na hy upapadyate
a ṛte niyogāt sāmarthyam avaboddhuṃ na śakyate
c sahasā viniyogo hi doṣavān pratibhāti me
a cārapraṇihitaṃ yuktaṃ yad uktaṃ sacivais tava
c arthasyāsaṃbhavāt tatra kāraṇaṃ nopapadyate
a adeśa kāle saṃprāpta ity ayaṃ yad vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c vivakṣā cātra me 'stīyaṃ tāṃ nibodha yathā mati
a sa eṣa deśaḥ kālaś ca bhavatīha yathā tathā
c puruṣāt puruṣaṃ prāpya tathā doṣaguṇāv api
a daurātmyaṃ rāvaṇe dṛṣṭvā vikramaṃ ca tathā tvayi
c yuktam āgamanaṃ tasya sadṛśaṃ tasya buddhitaḥ
a ajñātarūpaiḥ puruṣaiḥ sa rājan pṛcchyatām iti
c yad uktam atra me prekṣā kā cid asti samīkṣitā
a pṛcchyamāno viśaṅketa sahasā buddhimān vacaḥ
c tatra mitraṃ praduṣyeta mithyapṛṣṭaṃ sukhāgatam
a aśakyaḥ sahasā rājan bhāvo vettuṃ parasya vai
c antaḥ svabhāvair gītais tair naipuṇyaṃ paśyatā bhṛśam
a na tv asya bruvato jātu lakṣyate duṣṭabhāvatā
c prasannaṃ vadanaṃ cāpi tasmān me nāsti saṃśayaḥ
a aśaṅkitamatiḥ svastho na śaṭhaḥ parisarpati
c na cāsya duṣṭā vāk cāpi tasmān nāstīha saṃśayaḥ
a ākāraś chādyamāno 'pi na śakyo vinigūhitum
c balād dhi vivṛṇoty eva bhāvam antargataṃ nṛṇām
a deśakālopapannaṃ ca kāryaṃ kāryavidāṃ vara
c saphalaṃ kurute kṣipraṃ prayogeṇābhisaṃhitam
a udyogaṃ tava saṃprekṣya mithyāvṛttaṃ ca rāvaṇam
c vālinaś ca vadhaṃ śrutvā sugrīvaṃ cābhiṣecitam
a rājyaṃ prārthayamānaś ca buddhipūrvam ihāgataḥ
c etāvat tu puraskṛtya yujyate tv asya saṃgrahaḥ
a yathāśakti mayoktaṃ tu rākṣasasyārjavaṃ prati
c tvaṃ pramāṇaṃ tu śeṣasya śrutvā buddhimatāṃ vara
a atha rāmaḥ prasannātmā śrutvā vāyusutasya ha
c pratyabhāṣata durdharṣaḥ śrutavān ātmani sthitam
a mamāpi tu vivakṣāsti kā cit prati vibhīṣaṇam
c śrutam icchāmi tat sarvaṃ bhavadbhiḥ śreyasi sthitaiḥ
a mitrabhāvena saṃprāptaṃ na tyajeyaṃ kathaṃ cana
c doṣo yady api tasya syāt satām etad agarhitam
a rāmasya vacanaṃ śrutvā sugrīvaḥ plavageśvaraḥ
c pratyabhāṣata kākutsthaṃ sauhārdenābhicoditaḥ
a kim atra citraṃ dharmajña lokanāthaśikhāmaṇe
c yat tvam āryaṃ prabhāṣethāḥ sattvavān sapathe sthitaḥ
a mama cāpy antarātmāyaṃ śuddhiṃ vetti vibhīṣaṇam
c anumanāc ca bhāvāc ca sarvataḥ suparīkṣitaḥ
a tasmāt kṣipraṃ sahāsmābhis tulyo bhavatu rāghava
c vibhīṣaṇo mahāprājñaḥ sakhitvaṃ cābhyupaitu naḥ
a sa sugrīvasya tad vākyayṃ rāmaḥ śrutvā vimṛśya ca
c tataḥ śubhataraṃ vākyam uvāca haripuṃgavam
a suduṣṭo vāpy aduṣṭo vā kim eṣa rajanīcaraḥ
c sūkṣmam apy ahitaṃ kartuṃ mamāśaktaḥ kathaṃ cana
a piśācān dānavān yakṣān pṛthivyāṃ caiva rākṣasān
c aṅgulyagreṇa tān hanyām icchan harigaṇeśvara
a śrūyate hi kapotena śatruḥ śaraṇam āgataḥ
c arcitaś ca yathānyāyaṃ svaiś ca māṃsair nimantritaḥ
a sa hi taṃ pratijagrāha bhāryā hartāram āgatam
c kapoto vānaraśreṣṭha kiṃ punar madvidho janaḥ
a ṛṣeḥ kaṇvasya putreṇa kaṇḍunā paramarṣiṇā
c śṛṇu gāthāṃ purā gītāṃ dharmiṣṭhāṃ satyavādinā
a baddhāñjalipuṭaṃ dīnaṃ yācantaṃ śaraṇāgatam
c na hanyād ānṛśaṃsyārtham api śatruṃ paraṃ pata
a ārto vā yadi vā dṛptaḥ pareṣāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
c ariḥ prāṇān parityajya rakṣitavyaḥ kṛtātmanā
a sa ced bhayād vā mohād vā kāmād vāpi na rakṣati
c svayā śaktyā yathātattvaṃ tat pāpaṃ lokagarhitam
a vinaṣṭaḥ paśyatas tasya rakṣiṇaḥ śaraṇāgataḥ
c ādāya sukṛtaṃ tasya sarvaṃ gacched arakṣitaḥ
a evaṃ doṣo mahān atra prapannānām arakṣaṇe
c asvargyaṃ cāyaśasyaṃ ca balavīryavināśanam
a kariṣyāmi yathārthaṃ tu kaṇḍor vacanam uttamam
c dharmiṣṭhaṃ ca yaśasyaṃ ca svargyaṃ syāt tu phalodaye
a sakṛd eva prapannāya tavāsmīti ca yācate
c abhayaṃ sarvabhūtebhyo dadāmy etad vrataṃ mama
a ānayainaṃ hariśreṣṭha dattam asyābhayaṃ mayā
c vibhīṣaṇo vā sugrīva yadi vā rāvaṇaḥ svayam
a tatas tu sugrīvavaco niśamya tad
dharīśvareṇābhihitaṃ nareśvaraḥ
c vibhīṣaṇenāśu jagāma saṃgamaṃ
patatrirājena yathā puraṃdaraḥ
a rāghaveṇābhaye datte saṃnato rāvaṇānujaḥ
c khāt papātāvaniṃ hṛṣṭo bhaktair anucaraiḥ saha
a sa tu rāmasya dharmātmā nipapāta vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c pādayoḥ śaraṇānveṣī caturbhiḥ saha rākṣasaiḥ
a abravīc ca tadā rāmaṃ vākyaṃ tatra vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c dharmayuktaṃ ca yuktaṃ ca sāmprataṃ saṃpraharṣaṇam
a anujo rāvaṇasyāhaṃ tena cāsmy avamānitaḥ
c bhavantaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
a parityaktā mayā laṅkā mitrāṇi ca dhanāni ca
c bhavadgataṃ me rājyaṃ ca jīvitaṃ ca sukhāni ca
a rākṣasānāṃ vadhe sāhyaṃ laṅkāyāś ca pradharṣaṇe
c kariṣyāmi yathāprāṇaṃ pravekṣyāmi ca vāhinīm
a iti bruvāṇaṃ rāmas tu pariṣvajya vibhīṣaṇam
c abravīl lakṣmaṇaṃ prītaḥ samudrāj jalam ānaya
a tena cemaṃ mahāprājñam abhiṣiñca vibhīṣaṇam
c rājānaṃ rakṣasāṃ kṣipraṃ prasanne mayi mānada
a evam uktas tu saumitrir abhyaṣiñcad vibhīṣaṇam
c madhye vānaramukhyānāṃ rājānaṃ rāmaśāsanāt
a taṃ prasādaṃ tu rāmasya dṛṣṭvā sadyaḥ plavaṃgamāḥ
c pracukruśur mahānādān sādhu sādhv iti cābruvan
a abravīc ca hanūmāṃś ca sugrīvaś ca vibhīṣaṇam
c kathaṃ sāgaram akṣobhyaṃ tarāma varuṇālayam
a upāyair abhigacchāmo yathā nadanadīpatim
c tarāma tarasā sarve sasainyā varuṇālayam
a evam uktas tu dharmajñaḥ pratyuvāca vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c samudraṃ rāghavo rājā śaraṇaṃ gantum arhati
a khānitaḥ sagareṇāyam aprameyo mahodadhiḥ
c kartum arhati rāmasya jñāteḥ kāryaṃ mahodadhiḥ
a evaṃ vibhīṣaṇenokte rākṣasena vipaścitā
c prakṛtyā dharmaśīlasya rāghavasyāpy arocata
a sa lakṣmaṇaṃ mahātejāḥ sugrīvaṃ ca harīśvaram
c satkriyārthaṃ kriyādakṣaḥ smitapūrvam uvāca ha
a vibhīṣaṇasya mantro 'yaṃ mama lakṣmaṇa rocate
c brūhi tvaṃ sahasugrīvas tavāpi yadi rocate
a sugrīvaḥ paṇḍito nityaṃ bhavān mantravicakṣaṇaḥ
c ubhābhyāṃ saṃpradhāryāryaṃ rocate yat tad ucyatām
a evam uktau tu tau vīrāv ubhau sugrīvalakṣmaṇau
c samudācāra saṃyuktam idaṃ vacanam ūcatuḥ
a kimarthaṃ no naravyāghra na rociṣyati rāghava
c vibhīṣaṇena yat tūktam asmin kāle sukhāvaham
a abaddhvā sāgare setuṃ ghore 'smin varuṇālaye
c laṅkā nāsādituṃ śakyā sendrair api surāsuraiḥ
a vibhīṣaṇasya śūrasya yathārthaṃ kriyatāṃ vacaḥ
c alaṃ kālātyayaṃ kṛtvā samudro 'yaṃ niyujyatām
a evam uktaḥ kuśāstīrṇe tīre nadanadīpateḥ
c saṃviveśa tadā rāmo vedyām iva hutāśanaḥ
a tasya rāmasya suptasya kuśāstīrṇe mahītale
c niyamād apramattasya niśās tisro 'ticakramuḥ
a na ca darśayate mandas tadā rāmasya sāgaraḥ
c prayatenāpi rāmeṇa yathārham abhipūjitaḥ
a samudrasya tataḥ kruddho rāmo raktāntalocanaḥ
c samīpastham uvācedaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ śubhalakṣmaṇam
a paśya tāvad anāryasya pūjyamānasya lakṣmaṇa
c avalepaṃ samudrasya na darśayati yat svayam
a praśamaś ca kṣamā caiva ārjavaṃ priyavāditā
c asāmarthyaṃ phalanty ete nirguṇeṣu satāṃ guṇāḥ
a ātmapraśaṃsinaṃ duṣṭaṃ dhṛṣṭaṃ viparidhāvakam
c sarvatrotsṛṣṭadaṇḍaṃ ca lokaḥ satkurute naram
a na sāmnā śakyate kīrtir na sāmnā śakyate yaśaḥ
c prāptuṃ lakṣmaṇa loke 'smiñ jayo vā raṇamūdhani
a adya madbāṇanirbhinnair makarair makarālayam
c niruddhatoyaṃ saumitre plavadbhiḥ paśya sarvataḥ
a mahābhogāni matsyānāṃ kariṇāṃ ca karān iha
c bhogāṃś ca paśya nāgānāṃ mayā bhinnāni lakṣmaṇa
a saśaṅkhaśuktikā jālaṃ samīnamakaraṃ śaraiḥ
c adya yuddhena mahatā samudraṃ pariśoṣaye
a kṣamayā hi samāyuktaṃ mām ayaṃ makarālayaḥ
c asamarthaṃ vijānāti dhik kṣamām īdṛśe jane
a cāpam ānaya saumitre śarāṃś cāśīviṣopamān
c adyākṣobhyam api kruddhaḥ kṣobhayiṣyāmi sāgaram
a velāsu kṛtamaryādaṃ sahasormisamākulam
c nirmaryādaṃ kariṣyāmi sāyakair varuṇālayam
a evam uktvā dhanuṣpāṇiḥ krodhavisphāritekṣaṇaḥ
c babhūva rāmo durdharṣo yugāntāgnir iva jvalan
a saṃpīḍya ca dhanur ghoraṃ kampayitvā śarair jagat
c mumoca viśikhān ugrān vajrāṇīva śatakratuḥ
a te jvalanto mahāvegās tejasā sāyakottamāḥ
c praviśanti samudrasya salilaṃ trastapannagam
a tato vegaḥ samudrasya sanakramakaro mahān
c saṃbabhūva mahāghoraḥ samārutaravas tadā
a mahormimālāvitataḥ śaṅkhaśuktisamākulaḥ
c sadhūmaparivṛttormiḥ sahasābhūn mahodadhiḥ
a vyathitāḥ pannagāś cāsan dīptāsyā dīptalocanāḥ
c dānavāś ca mahāvīryāḥ pātālatalavāsinaḥ
a ūrmayaḥ sindhurājasya sanakramakarās tadā
c vindhyamandarasaṃkāśāḥ samutpetuḥ sahasraśaḥ
a āghūrṇitataraṅgaughaḥ saṃbhrāntoragarākṣasaḥ
c udvartita mahāgrāhaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ salilāśayaḥ
a tato madhyāt samudrasya sāgaraḥ svayam utthitaḥ
c udayan hi mahāśailān meror iva divākaraḥ
e pannagaiḥ saha dīptāsyaiḥ samudraḥ pratyadṛśyata
a snigdhavaidūryasaṃkāśo jāmbūnadavibhūṣitaḥ
c raktamālyāmbaradharaḥ padmapatranibhekṣaṇaḥ
a sāgaraḥ samatikramya pūrvam āmantrya vīryavān
c abravīt prāñjalir vākyaṃ rāghavaṃ śarapāṇinam
a pṛthivī vāyur ākāśam āpo jyotiś ca rāghavaḥ
c svabhāve saumya tiṣṭhanti śāśvataṃ mārgam āśritāḥ
a tat svabhāvo mamāpy eṣa yad agādho 'ham aplavaḥ
c vikāras tu bhaved rādha etat te pravadāmy aham
a na kāmān na ca lobhād vā na bhayāt pārthivātmaja
c grāhanakrākulajalaṃ stambhayeyaṃ kathaṃ cana
a vidhāsye rāma yenāpi viṣahiṣye hy ahaṃ tathā
c grāhā na prahariṣyanti yāvat senā tariṣyati
a ayaṃ saumya nalo nāma tanujo viśvakarmaṇaḥ
c pitrā dattavaraḥ śrīmān pratimo viśvakarmaṇaḥ
a eṣa setuṃ mahotsāhaḥ karotu mayi vānaraḥ
c tam ahaṃ dhārayiṣyāmi tathā hy eṣa yathā pitā
a evam uktvodadhir naṣṭaḥ samutthāya nalas tataḥ
c abravīd vānaraśreṣṭho vākyaṃ rāmaṃ mahābalaḥ
a ahaṃ setuṃ kariṣyāmi vistīrṇe varuṇālaye
c pituḥ sāmarthyam āsthāya tattvam āha mahodadhiḥ
a mama mātur varo datto mandare viśvakarmaṇā
c aurasas tasya putro 'haṃ sadṛśo viśvakarmaṇā
a na cāpy aham anukto vai prabrūyām ātmano guṇān
c kāmam adyaiva badhnantu setuṃ vānarapuṃgavāḥ
a tato nisṛṣṭarāmeṇa sarvato hariyūthapāḥ
c abhipetur mahāraṇyaṃ hṛṣṭāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ
a te nagān nagasaṃkāśāḥ śākhāmṛgagaṇarṣabhāḥ
c babhañjur vānarās tatra pracakarṣuś ca sāgaram
a te sālaiś cāśvakarṇaiś ca dhavair vaṃśaiś ca vānarāḥ
c kuṭajair arjunais tālais tikalais timiśair api
a bilvakaiḥ saptaparṇaiś ca karṇikāraiś ca puṣpitaiḥ
c cūtaiś cāśokavṛkṣaiś ca sāgaraṃ samapūrayan
a samūlāṃś ca vimūlāṃś ca pādapān harisattamāḥ
c indraketūn ivodyamya prajahrur harayas tarūn
a prakṣipyamāṇair acalaiḥ sahasā jalam uddhatam
c samutpatitam ākāśam apāsarpat tatas tataḥ
a daśayojanavistīrṇaṃ śatayojanam āyatam
c nalaś cakre mahāsetuṃ madhye nadanadīpateḥ
a śilānāṃ kṣipyamāṇānāṃ śailānāṃ tatra pātyatām
c babhūva tumulaḥ śabdas tadā tasmin mahodadhau
a sa nalena kṛtaḥ setuḥ sāgare makarālaye
c śuśubhe subhagaḥ śrīmān svātīpatha ivāmbare
a tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
a āplavantaḥ plavantaś ca garjantaś ca plavaṃgamāḥ
c tam acintyam asahyaṃ ca adbhutaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
e dadṛśuḥ sarvabhūtāni sāgare setubandhanam
a tāni koṭisahasrāṇi vānarāṇāṃ mahaujasām
c badhnantaḥ sāgare setuṃ jagmuḥ pāraṃ mahodadheḥ
a viśālaḥ sukṛtaḥ śrīmān subhūmiḥ susamāhitaḥ
c aśobhata mahāsetuḥ sīmanta iva sāgare
a tataḥ pare samudrasya gadāpāṇir vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c pareṣām abhighatārtham atiṣṭhat sacivaiḥ saha
a agratas tasya sainyasya śrīmān rāmaḥ salakṣmaṇaḥ
c jagāma dhanvī dharmātmā sugrīveṇa samanvitaḥ
a anye madhyena gacchanti pārśvato 'nye plavaṃgamāḥ
c salile prapatanty anye mārgam anye na lebhire
e ke cid vaihāyasa gatāḥ suparṇā iva pupluvuḥ
a ghoṣeṇa mahatā ghoṣaṃ sāgarasya samucchritam
c bhīmam antardadhe bhīmā tarantī harivāhinī
a vānarāṇāṃ hi sā tīrṇā vāhinī nala setunā
c tīre niviviśe rājñā bahumūlaphalodake
a tad adbhutaṃ rāghava karma duṣkaraṃ
samīkṣya devāḥ saha siddhacāraṇaiḥ
c upetya rāmaṃ sahitā maharṣibhiḥ
samabhyaṣiñcan suśubhair jalaiḥ pṛthak
a jayasva śatrūn naradeva medinīṃ
sasāgarāṃ pālaya śāśvatīḥ samāḥ
c itīva rāmaṃ naradevasatkṛtaṃ
śubhair vacobhir vividhair apūjayan
a sabale sāgaraṃ tīrṇe rāme daśarathātmaje
c amātyau rāvaṇaḥ śrīmān abravīc chukasāraṇau
a samagraṃ sāgaraṃ tīrṇaṃ dustaraṃ vānaraṃ balam
c abhūtapūrvaṃ rāmeṇa sāgare setubandhanam
a sāgare setubandhaṃ tu na śraddadhyāṃ kathaṃ cana
c avaśyaṃ cāpi saṃkhyeyaṃ tan mayā vānaraṃ balam
a bhavantau vānaraṃ sainyaṃ praviśyānupalakṣitau
c parimāṇaṃ ca vīryaṃ ca ye ca mukhyāḥ plavaṃgamāḥ
a mantriṇo ye ca rāmasya sugrīvasya ca saṃmatāḥ
c ye pūrvam abhivartante ye ca śūrāḥ plavaṃgamāḥ
a sa ca setur yathā baddhaḥ sāgare salilārṇave
c niveśaś ca yathā teṣāṃ vānarāṇāṃ mahātmanām
a rāmasya vyavasāyaṃ ca vīryaṃ praharaṇāni ca
c lakṣmaṇasya ca vīrasya tattvato jñātum arhatha
a kaś ca senāpatis teṣāṃ vānarāṇāṃ mahaujasām
c etaj jñātvā yathātattvaṃ śīghram agantum arhathaḥ
a iti pratisamādiṣṭau rākṣasau śukasāraṇau
c harirūpadharau vīrau praviṣṭau vānaraṃ balam
a tatas tad vānaraṃ sainyam acintyaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c saṃkhyātuṃ nādhyagacchetāṃ tadā tau śukasāraṇau
a tat sthitaṃ parvatāgreṣu nirdareṣu guhāsu ca
c samudrasya ca tīreṣu vaneṣūpavaneṣu ca
a taramāṇaṃ ca tīrṇaṃ ca tartukāmaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
c niviṣṭaṃ niviśac caiva bhīmanādaṃ mahābalam
a tau dadarśa mahātejāḥ pracchannau ca vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c ācacakṣe 'tha rāmāya gṛhītvā śukasāraṇau
e laṅkāyāḥ samanuprāptau cārau parapuraṃjayau
a tau dṛṣṭvā vyathitau rāmaṃ nirāśau jīvite tadā
c kṛtāñjalipuṭau bhītau vacanaṃ cedam ūcatuḥ
a āvām ihāgatau saumya rāvaṇaprahitāv ubhau
c parijñātuṃ balaṃ kṛtsnaṃ tavedaṃ raghunandana
a tayos tad vacanaṃ śrutvā rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ
c abravīt prahasan vākyaṃ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ
a yadi dṛṣṭaṃ balaṃ kṛtsnaṃ vayaṃ vā susamīkṣitāḥ
c yathoktaṃ vā kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ chandataḥ pratigamyatām
a praviśya nagarīṃ laṅkāṃ bhavadbhyāṃ dhanadānujaḥ
c vaktavyo rakṣasāṃ rājā yathoktaṃ vacanaṃ mama
a yad balaṃ ca samāśritya sītāṃ me hṛtavān asi
c tad darśaya yathākāmaṃ sasainyaḥ sahabāndhavaḥ
a śvaḥkāle nagarīṃ laṅkāṃ saprākārāṃ satoraṇām
c rākṣasaṃ ca balaṃ paśya śarair vidhvaṃsitaṃ mayā
a ghoraṃ roṣam ahaṃ mokṣye balaṃ dhāraya rāvaṇa
c śvaḥkāle vajravān vajraṃ dānaveṣv iva vāsavaḥ
a iti pratisamādiṣṭau rākṣasau śukasāraṇau
c āgamya nagarīṃ laṅkām abrūtāṃ rākṣasādhipam
a vibhīṣaṇagṛhītau tu vadhārhau rākṣaseśvara
c dṛṣṭvā dharmātmanā muktau rāmeṇāmitatejasā
a ekasthānagatā yatra catvāraḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ
c lokapālopamāḥ śūrāḥ kṛtāstrā dṛḍhavikramāḥ
a rāmo dāśarathiḥ śrīmāṃl lakṣmaṇaś ca vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c sugrīvaś ca mahātejā mahendrasamavikramaḥ
a ete śaktāḥ purīṃ laṅkāṃ saprākārāṃ satoraṇām
c utpāṭya saṃkrāmayituṃ sarve tiṣṭhantu vānarāḥ
a yādṛśaṃ tasya rāmasya rūpaṃ praharaṇāni ca
c vadhiṣyati purīṃ laṅkām ekas tiṣṭhantu te trayaḥ
a rāmalakṣmaṇaguptā sā sugrīveṇa ca vāhinī
c babhūva durdharṣatarā sarvair api surāsuraiḥ
a prahṛṣṭarūpā dhvajinī vanaukasāṃ
mahātmanāṃ saṃprati yoddhum icchatām
c alaṃ virodhena śamo vidhīyatāṃ
pradīyatāṃ dāśarathāya maithilī
a tad vacaḥ pathyam aklībaṃ sāraṇenābhibhāṣitam
c niśamya rāvaṇo rājā pratyabhāṣata sāraṇam
a yadi mām abhiyuñjīran devagandharvadānavāḥ
c naiva sītāṃ pradāsyāmi sarvalokabhayād api
a tvaṃ tu saumya paritrasto haribhir nirjito bhṛśam
c pratipradānam adyaiva sītāyāḥ sādhu manyase
e ko hi nāma sapatno māṃ samare jetum arhati
a ity uktvā paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ
c āruroha tataḥ śrīmān prāsādaṃ himapāṇḍuram
e bahutālasamutsedhaṃ rāvaṇo 'tha didṛkṣayā
a tābhyāṃ carābhyāṃ sahito rāvaṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
c paśyamānaḥ samudraṃ ca parvatāṃś ca vanāni ca
e dadarśa pṛthivīdeśaṃ susaṃpūrṇaṃ plavaṃgamaiḥ
a tad apāram asaṃkhyeyaṃ vānarāṇāṃ mahad balam
c ālokya rāvaṇo rājā paripapraccha sāraṇam
a eṣāṃ vānaramukhyānāṃ ke śūrāḥ ke mahābalāḥ
c ke pūrvam abhivartante mahotsāhāḥ samantataḥ
a keṣāṃ śṛṇoti sugrīvaḥ ke vā yūthapayūthapāḥ
c sāraṇācakṣva me sarvaṃ ke pradhānāḥ plavaṃgamāḥ
a sāraṇo rākṣasendrasya vacanaṃ paripṛcchataḥ
c ācacakṣe 'tha mukhyajño mukhyāṃs tāṃs tu vanaukasaḥ
a eṣa yo 'bhimukho laṅkāṃ nardaṃs tiṣṭhati vānaraḥ
c yūthapānāṃ sahasrāṇāṃ śatena parivāritaḥ
a yasya ghoṣeṇa mahatā saprākārā satoraṇā
c laṅkā pravepate sarvā saśailavanakānanā
a sarvaśākhāmṛgendrasya sugrīvasya mahātmanaḥ
c balāgre tiṣṭhate vīro nīlo nāmaiṣa yūthapaḥ
a bāhū pragṛhya yaḥ padbhyāṃ mahīṃ gacchati vīryavān
c laṅkām abhimukhaḥ kopād abhīkṣṇaṃ ca vijṛmbhate
a giriśṛṅgapratīkāśaḥ padmakiñjalkasaṃnibhaḥ
c sphoṭayaty abhisaṃrabdho lāṅgūlaṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ
a yasya lāṅgūlaśabdena svanantīva diśo daśa
c eṣa vānararājena surgrīveṇābhiṣecitaḥ
e yauvarājye 'ṅgado nāma tvām āhvayati saṃyuge
a ye tu viṣṭabhya gātrāṇi kṣveḍayanti nadanti ca
c utthāya ca vijṛmbhante krodhena haripuṃgavāḥ
a ete duṣprasahā ghorāś caṇḍāś caṇḍaparākramāḥ
c aṣṭau śatasahasrāṇi daśakoṭiśatāni ca
a ya enam anugacchanti vīrāś candanavāsinaḥ
c eṣa āśaṃsate laṅkāṃ svenānīkena marditum
a śveto rajatasaṃkāśaḥ sabalo bhīmavikramaḥ
c buddhimān vānaraḥ śūras triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ
a tūrṇaṃ sugrīvam āgamya punar gacchati vānaraḥ
c vibhajan vānarīṃ senām anīkāni praharṣayan
a yaḥ purā gomatītīre ramyaṃ paryeti parvatam
c nāmnā saṃkocano nāma nānānagayuto giriḥ
a tatra rājyaṃ praśāsty eṣa kumudo nāma yūthapaḥ
c yo 'sau śatasahasrāṇāṃ sahasraṃ parikarṣati
a yasya vālā bahuvyāmā dīrghalāṅgūlam āśritāḥ
c tāmrāḥ pītāḥ sitāḥ śvetāḥ prakīrṇā ghorakarmaṇaḥ
a adīno roṣaṇaś caṇḍaḥ saṃgrāmam abhikāṅkṣati
c eṣaivāśaṃsate laṅkāṃ svenānīkena marditum
a yas tv eṣa siṃhasaṃkāśaḥ kapilo dīrghakesaraḥ
c nibhṛtaḥ prekṣate laṅkāṃ didhakṣann iva cakṣuṣā
a vindhyaṃ kṛṣṇagiriṃ sahyaṃ parvataṃ ca sudarśanam
c rājan satatam adhyāste rambho nāmaiṣa yūthapaḥ
a śataṃ śatasahasrāṇāṃ triṃśac ca hariyūthapāḥ
c parivāryānugacchanti laṅkāṃ marditum ojasā
a yas tu karṇau vivṛṇute jṛmbhate ca punaḥ punaḥ
c na ca saṃvijate mṛtyor na ca yūthād vidhāvati
a mahābalo vītabhayo ramyaṃ sālveya parvatam
c rājan satatam adhyāste śarabho nāma yūthapaḥ
a etasya balinaḥ sarve vihārā nāma yūthapāḥ
c rājañ śatasahasrāṇi catvāriṃśat tathaiva ca
a yas tu megha ivākāśaṃ mahān āvṛtya tiṣṭhati
c madhye vānaravīrāṇāṃ surāṇām iva vāsavaḥ
a bherīṇām iva saṃnādo yasyaiṣa śrūyate mahān
c ghoraḥ śākhāmṛgendrāṇāṃ saṃgrāmam abhikāṅkṣatām
a eṣa parvatam adhyāste pāriyātram anuttamam
c yuddhe duṣprasaho nityaṃ panaso nāma yūthapaḥ
a enaṃ śatasahasrāṇāṃ śatārdhaṃ paryupāsate
c yūthapā yūthapaśreṣṭhaṃ yeṣāṃ yūthāni bhāgaśaḥ
a yas tu bhīmāṃ pravalgantīṃ camūṃ tiṣṭhati śobhayan
c sthitāṃ tīre samudrasya dvitīya iva sāgaraḥ
a eṣa dardarasaṃkāśo vinato nāma yūthapaḥ
c pibaṃś carati parṇāśāṃ nadīnām uttamāṃ nadīm
a ṣaṣṭiḥ śatasahasrāṇi balam asya plavaṃgamāḥ
c tvām āhvayati yuddhāya krathano nāma yūthapaḥ
a yas tu gairikavarṇābhaṃ vapuḥ puṣyati vānaraḥ
c gavayo nāma tejasvī tvāṃ krodhād abhivartate
a enaṃ śatasahasrāṇi saptatiḥ paryupāsate
c eṣa āśaṃsate laṅkāṃ svenānīkena marditum
a ete duṣprasahā ghorā balinaḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
c yūthapā yūthapaśreṣṭhā yeṣāṃ saṃkhyā na vidyate
a tāṃs tu te 'haṃ pravakṣyāmi prekṣamāṇasya yūthapān
c rāghavārthe parākrāntā ye na rakṣanti jīvitam
a snigdhā yasya bahuśyāmā bālā lāṅgūlam āśritāḥ
c tāmrāḥ pītāḥ sitāḥ śvetāḥ prakīrṇā ghorakarmaṇaḥ
a pragṛhītāḥ prakāśante sūryasyeva marīcayaḥ
c pṛthivyāṃ cānukṛṣyante haro nāmaiṣa yūthapaḥ
a yaṃ pṛṣṭhato 'nugacchanti śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
c drumān udyamya sahitā laṅkārohaṇatatparāḥ
a eṣa koṭīsahasreṇa vānarāṇāṃ mahaujasām
c ākāṅkṣate tvāṃ saṃgrāme jetuṃ parapuraṃjaya
a nīlān iva mahāmeghāṃs tiṣṭhato yāṃs tu paśyasi
c asitāñ janasaṃkāśān yuddhe satyaparākramān
a nakhadaṃṣṭrāyudhān vīrāṃs tīkṣṇakopān bhayāvahān
c asaṃkhyeyān anirdeśyān paraṃ pāram ivodadheḥ
a parvateṣu ca ye ke cid viṣameṣu nadīṣu ca
c ete tvām abhivartante rājann ṛṣkāḥ sudāruṇāḥ
a eṣāṃ madhye sthito rājan bhīmākṣo bhīmadarśanaḥ
c parjanya iva jīmūtaiḥ samantāt parivāritaḥ
a ṛkṣavantaṃ giriśreṣṭham adhyāste narmadāṃ piban
c sarvarkṣāṇām adhipatir dhūmro nāmaiṣa yūthapaḥ
a yavīyān asya tu bhrātā paśyainaṃ parvatopamam
c bhrātrā samāno rūpeṇa viśiṣṭas tu parākrame
a sa eṣa jāmbavān nāma mahāyūthapayūthapaḥ
c praśānto guruvartī ca saṃprahāreṣv amarṣaṇaḥ
a etena sāhyaṃ sumahat kṛtaṃ śakrasya dhīmatā
c devāsure jāmbavatā labdhāś ca bahavo varāḥ
a āruhya parvatāgrebhyo mahābhravipulāḥ śilāḥ
c muñcanti vipulākārā na mṛtyor udvijanti ca
a rākṣasānāṃ ca sadṛśāḥ piśācānāṃ ca romaśāḥ
c etasya sainye bahavo vicaranty agnitejasaḥ
a yaṃ tv enam abhisaṃrabdhaṃ plavamānam iva sthitam
c prekṣante vānarāḥ sarve sthitaṃ yūthapayūthapam
a eṣa rājan sahasrākṣaṃ paryupāste harīśvaraḥ
c balena balasaṃpanno rambho nāmaiṣa yūthapaḥ
a yaḥ sthitaṃ yojane śailaṃ gacchan pārśvena sevate
c ūrdhvaṃ tathaiva kāyena gataḥ prāpnoti yojanam
a yasmān na paramaṃ rūpaṃ catuṣpādeṣu vidyate
c śrutaḥ saṃnādano nāma vānarāṇāṃ pitāmahaḥ
a yena yuddhaṃ tadā dattaṃ raṇe śakrasya dhīmatā
c parājayaś ca na prāptaḥ so 'yaṃ yūthapayūthapaḥ
e yasya vikramamāṇasya śakrasyeva parākramaḥ
a eṣa gandharvakanyāyām utpannaḥ kṛṣṇavartmanā
c purā devāsure yuddhe sāhyārthaṃ tridivaukasām
a yasya vaiśravaṇo rājā jambūm upaniṣevate
c yo rājā parvatendrāṇāṃ bahukiṃnarasevinām
a vihārasukhado nityaṃ bhrātus te rākṣasādhipa
c tatraiṣa vasati śrīmān balavān vānararṣabhaḥ
e yuddheṣv akatthano nityaṃ krathano nāma yūthapaḥ
a vṛtaḥ koṭisahasreṇa harīṇāṃ samupasthitaḥ
c eṣaivāśaṃsate laṅkāṃ svenānīkena marditum
a yo gaṅgām anu paryeti trāsayan hastiyūthapān
c hastināṃ vānarāṇāṃ ca pūrvavairam anusmaran
a eṣa yūthapatir netā gacchan giriguhāśayaḥ
c harīṇāṃ vāhinī mukhyo nadīṃ haimavatīm anu
a uśīra bījam āśritya parvataṃ mandaropamam
c ramate vānaraśreṣṭho divi śakra iva svayam
a enaṃ śatasahasrāṇāṃ sahasram abhivartate
c eṣa durmarṣaṇo rājan pramāthī nāma yūthapaḥ
a vātenevoddhataṃ meghaṃ yam enam anupaśyasi
c vivartamānaṃ bahuśo yatraitad bahulaṃ rajaḥ
a ete 'sitamukhā ghorā golāṅgūlā mahābalāḥ
c śataṃ śatasahasrāṇi dṛṣṭvā vai setubandhanam
a golāṅgūlaṃ mahāvegaṃ gavākṣaṃ nāma yūthapam
c parivāryābhivartante laṅkāṃ marditum ojasā
a bhramarācaritā yatra sarvakāmaphaladrumāḥ
c yaṃ sūryatulyavarṇābham anuparyeti parvatam
a yasya bhāsā sadā bhānti tadvarṇā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ
c yasya prasthaṃ mahātmāno na tyajanti maharṣayaḥ
a tatraiṣa ramate rājan ramye kāñcanaparvate
c mukhyo vānaramukhyānāṃ kesarī nāma yūthapaḥ
a ṣaṣṭir girisahasrāṇāṃ ramyāḥ kāñcanaparvatāḥ
c teṣāṃ madhye girivaras tvam ivānagha rakṣasām
a tatraite kapilāḥ śvetās tāmrāsyā madhupiṅgalāḥ
c nivasanty uttamagirau tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrānakhāyudhāḥ
a siṃha iva caturdaṃṣṭrā vyāghrā iva durāsadāḥ
c sarve vaiśvanarasamā jvalitāśīviṣopamāḥ
a sudīrghāñcitalāṅgūlā mattamātaṃgasaṃnibhāḥ
c mahāparvatasaṃkāśā mahājīmūtanisvanāḥ
a eṣa caiṣām adhipatir madhye tiṣṭhati vīryavān
c nāmnā pṛthivyāṃ vikhyāto rājañ śatabalīti yaḥ
e eṣaivāśaṃsate laṅkāṃ svenānīkena marditum
a gajo gavākṣo gavayo nalo nīlaś ca vānaraḥ
c ekaika eva yūthānāṃ koṭibhir daśabhir vṛtaḥ
a tathānye vānaraśreṣṭhā vindhyaparvatavāsinaḥ
c na śakyante bahutvāt tu saṃkhyātuṃ laghuvikramāḥ
a sarve mahārāja mahāprabhāvāḥ
sarve mahāśailanikāśakāyāḥ
c sarve samarthāḥ pṛthivīṃ kṣaṇena
kartuṃ pravidhvastavikīrṇaśailām
a sāraṇasya vacaḥ śrutvā rāvaṇaṃ rākṣasādhipam
c balam ālokayan sarvaṃ śuko vākyam athābravīt
a sthitān paśyasi yān etān mattān iva mahādvipān
c nyagrodhān iva gāṅgeyān sālān haimavatīn iva
a ete duṣprasahā rājan balinaḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
c daityadānavasaṃkāśā yuddhe devaparākramāḥ
a eṣāṃ koṭisahasrāṇi nava pañcaca sapta ca
c tathā śaṅkhasahasrāṇi tathā vṛndaśatāni ca
a ete sugrīvasacivāḥ kiṣkindhānilayāḥ sadā
c harayo devagandharvair utpannāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
a yau tau paśyasi tiṣṭhantau kumārau devarūpiṇau
c maindaś ca dvividaś cobhau tābhyāṃ nāsti samo yudhi
a brahmaṇā samanujñātāv amṛtaprāśināv ubhau
c āśaṃsete yudhā laṅkām etau marditum ojasā
a yāv etāv etayoḥ pārśve sthitau parvatasaṃnibhau
c sumukho vimukhaś caiva mṛtyuputrau pituḥ samau
a yaṃ tu paśyasi tiṣṭhantaṃ prabhinnam iva kuñjaram
c yo balāt kṣobhayet kruddhaḥ samudram api vānaraḥ
a eṣo 'bhigantā laṅkāyā vaidehyās tava ca prabho
c enaṃ paśya purā dṛṣṭaṃ vānaraṃ punar āgatam
a jyeṣṭhaḥ kesariṇaḥ putro vātātmaja iti śrutaḥ
c hanūmān iti vikhyāto laṅghito yena sāgaraḥ
a kāmarūpī hariśreṣṭho balarūpasamanvitaḥ
c anivāryagatiś caiva yathā satatagaḥ prabhuḥ
a udyantaṃ bhāskaraṃ dṛṣṭvā bālaḥ kila pipāsitaḥ
c triyojanasahasraṃ tu adhvānam avatīrya hi
a ādityam āhariṣyāmi na me kṣut pratiyāsyati
c iti saṃcintya manasā puraiṣa baladarpitaḥ
a anādhṛṣyatamaṃ devam api devarṣidānavaiḥ
c anāsādyaiva patito bhāskarodayane girau
a patitasya kaper asya hanur ekā śilātale
c kiṃ cid bhinnā dṛḍhahanor hanūmān eṣa tena vai
a satyam āgamayogena mamaiṣa vidito hariḥ
c nāsya śakyaṃ balaṃ rūpaṃ prabhāvo vānubhāṣitum
a eṣa āśaṃsate laṅkām eko marditum ojasā
c yaś caiṣo 'nantaraḥ śūraḥ śyāmaḥ padmanibhekṣaṇaḥ
a ikṣvākūṇām atiratho loke vikhyāta pauruṣaḥ
c yasmin na calate dharmo yo dharmaṃ nātivartate
a yo brāhmam astraṃ vedāṃś ca veda vedavidāṃ varaḥ
c yo bhindyād gaganaṃ bāṇaiḥ parvatāṃś cāpi dārayet
a yasya mṛtyor iva krodhaḥ śakrasyeva parākramaḥ
c sa eṣa rāmas tvāṃ yoddhuṃ rājan samabhivartate
a yaś caiṣa dakṣiṇe pārśve śuddhajāmbūnadaprabhaḥ
c viśālavakṣās tāmrākṣo nīlakuñcitamūrdhajaḥ
a eṣo 'sya lakṣmaṇo nāma bhrātā prāṇasamaḥ priyaḥ
c naye yuddhe ca kuśalaḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ
a amarṣī durjayo jetā vikrānto buddhimān balī
c rāmasya dakṣiṇo bāhur nityaṃ prāṇo bahiścaraḥ
a na hy eṣa rāghavasyārthe jīvitaṃ parirakṣati
c eṣaivāśaṃsate yuddhe nihantuṃ sarvarākṣasān
a yas tu savyam asau pakṣaṃ rāmasyāśritya tiṣṭhati
c rakṣogaṇaparikṣipto rājā hy eṣa vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a śrīmatā rājarājena laṅkāyām abhiṣecitaḥ
c tvām eva pratisaṃrabdho yuddhāyaiṣo 'bhivartate
a yaṃ tu paśyasi tiṣṭhantaṃ madhye girim ivācalam
c sarvaśākhāmṛgendrāṇāṃ bhartāram aparājitam
a tejasā yaśasā buddhyā jñānenābhijanena ca
c yaḥ kapīn ati babhrāja himavān iva parvatān
a kiṣkindhāṃ yaḥ samadhyāste guhāṃ sagahanadrumām
c durgāṃ parvatadurgasthāṃ pradhānaiḥ saha yūthapaiḥ
a yasyaiṣā kāñcanī mālā śobhate śatapuṣkarā
c kāntā devamanuṣyāṇāṃ yasyāṃ lakṣmīḥ pratiṣṭhitā
a etāṃ ca mālāṃ tārāṃ ca kapirājyaṃ ca śāśvatam
c sugrīvo vālinaṃ hatvā rāmeṇa pratipāditaḥ
a evaṃ koṭisahasreṇa śaṅkūnāṃ ca śatena ca
c sugrīvo vānarendras tvāṃ yuddhārtham abhivartate
a imāṃ mahārājasamīkṣya vāhinīm
upasthitāṃ prajvalitagrahopamām
c tataḥ prayatnaḥ paramo vidhīyatāṃ
yathā jayaḥ syān na paraiḥ parājayaḥ
a śukena tu samākhyātāṃs tān dṛṣṭvā hariyūthapān
c samīpasthaṃ ca rāmasya bhrātaraṃ svaṃ vibhīṣaṇam
a lakṣmaṇaṃ ca mahāvīryaṃ bhujaṃ rāmasya dakṣiṇam
c sarvavānararājaṃ ca sugrīvaṃ bhīmavikramam
a kiṃ cid āvignahṛdayo jātakrodhaś ca rāvaṇaḥ
c bhartsayām āsa tau vīrau kathānte śukasāraṇau
a adhomukhau tau praṇatāv abravīc chukasāraṇau
c roṣagadgadayā vācā saṃrabdhaḥ paruṣaṃ vacaḥ
a na tāvat sadṛśaṃ nāma sacivair upajīvibhiḥ
c vipriyaṃ nṛpater vaktuṃ nigrahapragrahe vibhoḥ
a ripūṇāṃ pratikūlānāṃ yuddhārtham abhivartatām
c ubhābhyāṃ sadṛśaṃ nāma vaktum aprastave stavam
a ācāryā guravo vṛddhā vṛthā vāṃ paryupāsitāḥ
c sāraṃ yad rājaśāstrāṇām anujīvyaṃ na gṛhyate
a gṛhīto vā na vijñāto bhāro jñānasya vochyate
c īdṛśaiḥ sacivair yukto mūrkhair diṣṭyā dharāmy aham
a kiṃ nu mṛtyor bhayaṃ nāsti māṃ vaktuṃ paruṣaṃ vacaḥ
c yasya me śāsato jihvā prayacchati śubhāśubham
a apy eva dahanaṃ spṛṣṭvā vane tiṣṭhanti pādapāḥ
c rājadoṣaparāmṛṣṭās tiṣṭhante nāparādhinaḥ
a hanyām aham imau pāpau śatrupakṣapraśaṃsakau
c yadi pūrvopakārair me na krodho mṛdutāṃ vrajet
a apadhvaṃsata gacchadhvaṃ saṃnikarṣād ito mama
c na hi vāṃ hantum icchāmi smarann upakṛtāni vām
e hatāv eva kṛtaghnau tau mayi snehaparāṅmukhau
a evam uktau tu savrīḍau tāv ubhau śukasāraṇau
c rāvaṇaṃ jayaśabdena pratinandyābhiniḥsṛtau
a abravīt sa daśagrīvaḥ samīpasthaṃ mahodaram
c upasthāpaya śīghraṃ me cārān nītiviśāradān
a tataś carāḥ saṃtvaritāḥ prāptāḥ pārthivaśāsanāt
c upasthitāḥ prāñjalayo vardhayitvā jayāśiṣā
a tān abravīt tato vākyaṃ rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ
c cārān pratyayikāñ śūrān bhaktān vigatasādhvasān
a ito gacchata rāmasya vyavasāyaṃ parīkṣatha
c mantreṣv abhyantarā ye 'sya prītyā tena samāgatāḥ
a kathaṃ svapiti jāgarti kim anyac ca kariṣyati
c vijñāya nipuṇaṃ sarvam āgantavyam aśeṣataḥ
a cāreṇa viditaḥ śatruḥ paṇḍitair vasudhādhipaiḥ
c yuddhe svalpena yatnena samāsādya nirasyate
a cārās tu te tathety uktvā prahṛṣṭā rākṣaseśvaram
c kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ jagmur yatra rāmaḥ salakṣmaṇaḥ
a te suvelasya śailasya samīpe rāmalakṣmaṇau
c pracchannā dadṛśur gatvā sasugrīvavibhīṣaṇau
a te tu dharmātmanā dṛṣṭā rākṣasendreṇa rākṣasāḥ
c vibhīṣaṇena tatrasthā nigṛhītā yadṛcchayā
a vānarair arditās te tu vikrāntair laghuvikramaiḥ
c punar laṅkām anuprāptāḥ śvasanto naṣṭacetasaḥ
a tato daśagrīvam upasthitās te
cārā bahirnityacarā niśācarāḥ
c gireḥ suvelasya samīpavāsinaṃ
nyavedayan bhīmabalaṃ mahābalāḥ
a tatas tam akṣobhya balaṃ laṅkādhipataye carāḥ
c suvele rāghavaṃ śaile niviṣṭaṃ pratyavedayan
a cārāṇāṃ rāvaṇaḥ śrutvā prāptaṃ rāmaṃ mahābalam
c jātodvego 'bhavat kiṃ cic chārdūlaṃ vākyam abravīt
a ayathāvac ca te varṇo dīnaś cāsi niśācara
c nāsi kaccid amitrāṇāṃ kruddhānāṃ vaśam āgataḥ
a iti tenānuśiṣṭas tu vācaṃ mandam udīrayat
c tadā rākṣasaśārdūlaṃ śārdūlo bhayavihvalaḥ
a na te cārayituṃ śakyā rājan vānarapuṃgavāḥ
c vikrāntā balavantaś ca rāghaveṇa ca rakṣitāḥ
a nāpi saṃbhāṣituṃ śakyāḥ saṃpraśno 'tra na labhyate
c sarvato rakṣyate panthā vānaraiḥ parvatopamaiḥ
a praviṣṭamātre jñāto 'haṃ bale tasminn acārite
c balād gṛhīto bahubhir bahudhāsmi vidāritaḥ
a jānubhir muṣṭibhir dantais talaiś cābhihato bhṛśam
c pariṇīto 'smi haribhir balavadbhir amarṣaṇaiḥ
a pariṇīya ca sarvatra nīto 'haṃ rāmasaṃsadam
c rudhirādigdhasarvāṅgo vihvalaś calitendriyaḥ
a haribhir vadhyamānaś ca yācamānaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
c rāghaveṇa paritrāto jīvāmi ha yadṛcchayā
a eṣa śailaiḥ śilābhiś ca pūrayitvā mahārṇavam
c dvāram āśritya laṅkāyā rāmas tiṣṭhati sāyudhaḥ
a garuḍavyūham āsthāya sarvato haribhir vṛtaḥ
c māṃ visṛjya mahātejā laṅkām evābhivartate
a purā prākāram āyāti kṣipram ekataraṃ kuru
c sītāṃ cāsmai prayacchāśu suyuddhaṃ vā pradīyatām
a manasā saṃtatāpātha tac chrutvā rākṣasādhipaḥ
c śārdūlasya mahad vākyam athovāca sa rāvaṇaḥ
a yadi māṃ pratiyudhyeran devagandharvadānavāḥ
c naiva sītāṃ pradāsyāmi sarvalokabhayād api
a evam uktvā mahātejā rāvaṇaḥ punar abravīt
c cāritā bhavatā senā ke 'tra śūrāḥ plavaṃgamāḥ
a kīdṛśāḥ kiṃprabhāvāś ca vānarā ye durāsadāḥ
c kasya putrāś ca pautrāś ca tattvam ākhyāhi rākṣasa
a tatr atra pratipatsyāmi jñātvā teṣāṃ balābalam
c avaśyaṃ balasaṃkhyānaṃ kartavyaṃ yuddham icchatā
a athaivam uktaḥ śārdūlo rāvaṇenottamaś caraḥ
c idaṃ vacanam ārebhe vaktuṃ rāvaṇasaṃnidhau
a atharkṣarajasaḥ putro yudhi rājan sudurjayaḥ
c gadgadasyātha putro 'tra jāmbavān iti viśrutaḥ
a gadgadasyaiva putro 'nyo guruputraḥ śatakratoḥ
c kadanaṃ yasya putreṇa kṛtam ekena rakṣasām
a suṣeṇaś cāpi dharmātmā putro dharmasya vīryavān
c saumyaḥ somātmajaś cātra rājan dadhimukhaḥ kapiḥ
a sumukho durmukhaś cātra vegadarśī ca vānaraḥ
c mṛtyur vānararūpeṇa nūnaṃ sṛṣṭaḥ svayambhuvā
a putro hutavahasyātha nīlaḥ senāpatiḥ svayam
c anilasya ca putro 'tra hanūmān iti viśrutaḥ
a naptā śakrasya durdharṣo balavān aṅgado yuvā
c maindaś ca dvividaś cobhau balināv aśvisaṃbhavau
a putrā vaivasvatasyātra pañcakālāntakopamāḥ
c gajo gavākṣo gavayaḥ śarabho gandhamādanaḥ
a śveto jyotirmukhaś cātra bhāskarasyātmasaṃbhavau
c varuṇasya ca putro 'tha hemakūṭaḥ plavaṃgamaḥ
a viśvakarmasuto vīro nalaḥ plavagasattamaḥ
c vikrānto vegavān atra vasuputraḥ sudurdharaḥ
a daśavānarakoṭyaś ca śūrāṇāṃ yuddhakāṅkṣiṇām
c śrīmatāṃ devaputrāṇāṃ śeṣān nākhyātum utsahe
a putro daśarathasyaiṣa siṃhasaṃhanano yuvā
c dūṣaṇo nihato yena kharaś ca triśirās tathā
a nāsti rāmasya sadṛśo vikrame bhuvi kaś cana
c virādho nihato yena kabandhaś cāntakopamaḥ
a vaktuṃ na śakto rāmasya naraḥ kaś cid guṇān kṣitau
c janasthānagatā yena tāvanto rākṣasā hatāḥ
a lakṣmaṇaś cātra dharmātmā mātaṃgānām ivarṣabhaḥ
c yasya bāṇapathaṃ prāpya na jīved api vāsavaḥ
a rākṣasānāṃ variṣṭhaś ca tava bhrātā vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c parigṛhya purīṃ laṅkāṃ rāghavasya hite rataḥ
a iti sarvaṃ samākhyātaṃ tavedaṃ vānaraṃ balam
c suvele 'dhiṣṭhitaṃ śaile śeṣakārye bhavān gatiḥ
a tatas tam akṣobhyabalaṃ laṅkāyāṃ nṛpateś caraḥ
c suvele rāghavaṃ śaile niviṣṭaṃ pratyavedayan
a cārāṇāṃ rāvaṇaḥ śrutvā prāptaṃ rāmaṃ mahābalam
c jātodvego 'bhavat kiṃ cit sacivāṃś cedam abravīt
a mantriṇaḥ śīghram āyāntu sarve vai susamāhitāḥ
c ayaṃ no mantrakālo hi saṃprāpta iva rākṣasāḥ
a tasya tac chāsanaṃ śrutvā mantriṇo 'bhyāgaman drutam
c tataḥ saṃmantrayām āsa sacivai rākṣasaiḥ saha
a mantrayitvā sa durdharṣaḥ kṣamaṃ yat samanantaram
c visarjayitvā sacivān praviveśa svam ālayam
a tato rākṣasam āhūya vidyujjihvaṃ mahābalam
c māyāvidaṃ mahāmāyaḥ prāviśad yatra maithilī
a vidyujjihvaṃ ca māyājñam abravīd rākṣasādhipaḥ
c mohayiṣyāmahe sītāṃ māyayā janakātmajām
a śiro māyāmayaṃ gṛhya rāghavasya niśācara
c māṃ tvaṃ samupatiṣṭhasva mahac ca saśaraṃ dhanuḥ
a evam uktas tathety āha vidyujjihvo niśācaraḥ
c tasya tuṣṭo 'bhavad rājā pradadau ca vibhūṣaṇam
a aśokavanikāyāṃ tu praviveśa mahābalaḥ
c tato dīnām adainyārhāṃ dadarśa dhanadānujaḥ
e adhomukhīṃ śokaparām upaviṣṭāṃ mahītale
a bhartāram eva dhyāyantīm aśokavanikāṃ gatām
c upāsyamānāṃ ghorābhī rākṣasībhir adūrataḥ
a upasṛtya tataḥ sītāṃ praharṣan nāma kīrtayan
c idaṃ ca vacanaṃ dhṛṣṭam uvāca janakātmajām
a sāntvyamānā mayā bhadre yam upāśritya valgase
c khara hantā sa te bhartā rāghavaḥ samare hataḥ
a chinnaṃ te sarvato mūlaṃ darpas te nihato mayā
c vyasanenātmanaḥ sīte mama bhāryā bhaviṣyasi
a alpapuṇye nivṛttārthe mūḍhe paṇḍitamānini
c śṛṇu bhartṛbadhaṃ sīte ghoraṃ vṛtravadhaṃ yathā
a samāyātaḥ samudrāntaṃ māṃ hantuṃ kila rāghavaḥ
c vānarendrapraṇītena balena mahatā vṛtaḥ
a saṃniviṣṭaḥ samudrasya tīram āsādya dakṣiṇam
c balena mahatā rāmo vrajaty astaṃ divākare
a athādhvani pariśrāntam ardharātre sthitaṃ balam
c sukhasuptaṃ samāsādya cāritaṃ prathamaṃ caraiḥ
a tat prahastapraṇītena balena mahatā mama
c balam asya hataṃ rātrau yatra rāmaḥ sulakṣmaṇaḥ
a paṭṭasān parighān khaḍgāṃś cakrān daṇḍān mahāyasān
c bāṇajālāni śūlāni bhāsvarān kūṭamudgarān
a yaṣṭīś ca tomarān prāsaṃś cakrāṇi musalāni ca
c udyamyodyamya rakṣobhir vānareṣu nipātitāḥ
a atha suptasya rāmasya prahastena pramāthinā
c asaktaṃ kṛtahastena śiraś chinnaṃ mahāsinā
a vibhīṣaṇaḥ samutpatya nigṛhīto yadṛcchayā
c diśaḥ pravrājitaḥ sarvair lakṣmaṇaḥ plavagaiḥ saha
a sugrīvo grīvayā śete bhagnayā plavagādhipaḥ
c nirastahanukaḥ śete hanūmān rākṣasair hataḥ
a jāmbavān atha jānubhyām utpatan nihato yudhi
c paṭṭasair bahubhiś chinno nikṛttaḥ pādapo yathā
a maindaś ca dvividaś cobhau nihatau vānararṣabhau
c niḥśvasantau rudantau ca rudhireṇa samukṣitau
a asinābhyāhataś chinno madhye ripuniṣūdanaḥ
c abhiṣṭanati medinyāṃ panasaḥ panaso yathā
a nārācair bahubhiś chinnaḥ śete daryāṃ darīmukhaḥ
c kumudas tu mahātejā niṣkūjan sāyakair hataḥ
a aṅgado bahubhiś chinnaḥ śarair āsādya rākṣasaiḥ
c pātito rudhirodgārī kṣitau nipatito 'ṅgadaḥ
a harayo mathitā nāgai rathajālais tathāpare
c śāyitā mṛditās tatra vāyuvegair ivāmbudāḥ
a pradrutāś ca pare trastā hanyamānā jaghanyataḥ
c abhidrutās tu rakṣobhiḥ siṃhair iva mahādvipāḥ
a sāgare patitāḥ ke cit ke cid gaganam āśritāḥ
c ṛkṣā vṛkṣān upārūḍhā vānarais tu vimiśritāḥ
a sāgarasya ca tīreṣu śaileṣu ca vaneṣu ca
c piṅgākṣās te virūpākṣair bahubhir bahavo hatāḥ
a evaṃ tava hato bhartā sasainyo mama senayā
c kṣatajārdraṃ rajodhvastam idaṃ cāsyāhṛtaṃ śiraḥ
a tataḥ paramadurdharṣo rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c sītāyām upaśṛṇvantyāṃ rākṣasīm idam abravīt
a rākṣasaṃ krūrakarmāṇaṃ vidyujjihvaṃ tvam ānaya
c yena tad rāghavaśiraḥ saṃgrāmāt svayam āhṛtam
a vidyujjihvas tato gṛhya śiras tat saśarāsanam
c praṇāmaṃ śirasā kṛtvā rāvaṇasyāgrataḥ sthitaḥ
a tam abravīt tato rājā rāvaṇo rākṣasaṃ sthitam
c vidyujjihvaṃ mahājihvaṃ samīpaparivartinam
a agrataḥ kuru sītāyāḥ śīghraṃ dāśaratheḥ śiraḥ
c avasthāṃ paścimāṃ bhartuḥ kṛpaṇā sādhu paśyatu
a evam uktaṃ tu tad rakṣaḥ śiras tat priyadarśanam
c upanikṣipya sītāyāḥ kṣipram antaradhīyata
a rāvaṇaś cāpi cikṣepa bhāsvaraṃ kārmukaṃ mahat
c triṣu lokeṣu vikhyātaṃ sītām idam uvāca ha
a idaṃ tat tava rāmasya kārmukaṃ jyāsamanvitam
c iha prahastenānītaṃ hatvā taṃ niśi mānuṣam
a sa vidyujjihvena sahaiva tac chiro
dhanuś ca bhūmau vinikīrya rāvaṇaḥ
c videharājasya sutāṃ yaśasvinīṃ
tato 'bravīt tāṃ bhava me vaśānugā
a sā sītā tac chiro dṛṣṭvā tac ca kārmukam uttamam
c sugrīvapratisaṃsargam ākhyātaṃ ca hanūmatā
a nayane mukhavarṇaṃ ca bhartus tat sadṛśaṃ mukham
c keśān keśāntadeśaṃ ca taṃ ca cūḍāmaṇiṃ śubham
a etaiḥ sarvair abhijñānair abhijñāya suduḥkhitā
c vijagarhe 'tha kaikeyīṃ krośantī kurarī yathā
a sakāmā bhava kaikeyi hato 'yaṃ kulanandanaḥ
c kulam utsāditaṃ sarvaṃ tvayā kalahaśīlayā
a āryeṇa kiṃ nu kaikeyyāḥ kṛtaṃ rāmeṇa vipriyam
c yad gṛhāc cīravasanas tayā prasthāpito vanam
a evam uktvā tu vaidehī vepamānā tapasvinī
c jagāma jagatīṃ bālā chinnā tu kadalī yathā
a sā muhūrtāt samāśvasya pratilabhya ca cetanām
c tac chiraḥ samupāghrāya vilalāpāyatekṣaṇā
a hā hatāsmi mahābāho vīravratam anuvratā
c imāṃ te paścimāvasthāṃ gatāsmi vidhavā kṛtā
a prathamaṃ maraṇaṃ nāryā bhartur vaiguṇyam ucyate
c suvṛttaḥ sādhuvṛttāyāḥ saṃvṛttas tvaṃ mamāgrataḥ
a duḥkhād duḥkhaṃ prapannāyā magnāyāḥ śokasāgare
c yo hi mām udyatas trātuṃ so 'pi tvaṃ vinipātitaḥ
a sā śvaśrūr mama kausalyā tvayā putreṇa rāghava
c vatseneva yathā dhenur vivatsā vatsalā kṛtā
a ādiṣṭaṃ dīrgham āyus te yair acintyaparākrama
c anṛtaṃ vacanaṃ teṣām alpāyur asi rāghava
a atha vā naśyati prajñā prājñasyāpi satas tava
c pacaty enaṃ tathā kālo bhūtānāṃ prabhavo hy ayam
a adṛṣṭaṃ mṛtyum āpannaḥ kasmāt tvaṃ nayaśāstravit
c vyasanānām upāyajñaḥ kuśalo hy asi varjane
a tathā tvaṃ saṃpariṣvajya raudrayātinṛśaṃsayā
c kālarātryā mayācchidya hṛtaḥ kamalalocanaḥ
a upaśeṣe mahābāho māṃ vihāya tapasvinīm
c priyām iva śubhāṃ nārīṃ pṛthivīṃ puruṣarṣabha
a arcitaṃ satataṃ yatnād gandhamālyair mayā tava
c idaṃ te matpriyaṃ vīra dhanuḥ kāñcanabhūṣitam
a pitrā daśarathena tvaṃ śvaśureṇa mamānagha
c pūrvaiś ca pitṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ nūnaṃ svarge samāgataḥ
a divi nakṣatrabhūtas tvaṃ mahat karma kṛtaṃ priyam
c puṇyaṃ rājarṣivaṃśaṃ tvam ātmanaḥ samupekṣase
a kiṃ mān na prekṣase rājan kiṃ māṃ na pratibhāṣase
c bālāṃ bālena saṃprāptāṃ bhāryāṃ māṃ sahacāriṇīm
a saṃśrutaṃ gṛhṇatā pāṇiṃ cariṣyāmīti yat tvayā
c smara tan mama kākutstha naya mām api duḥkhitām
a kasmān mām apahāya tvaṃ gato gatimatāṃ vara
c asmāl lokād amuṃ lokaṃ tyaktvā mām iha duḥkhitām
a kalyāṇair ucitaṃ yat tat pariṣvaktaṃ mayaiva tu
c kravyādais tac charīraṃ te nūnaṃ viparikṛṣyate
a agniṣṭomādibhir yajñair iṣṭavān āptadakṣiṇaiḥ
c agnihotreṇa saṃskāraṃ kena tvaṃ tu na lapsyase
a pravrajyām upapannānāṃ trayāṇām ekam āgatam
c pariprakṣyati kausalyā lakṣmaṇaṃ śokalālasā
a sa tasyāḥ paripṛcchantyā vadhaṃ mitrabalasya te
c tava cākhyāsyate nūnaṃ niśāyāṃ rākṣasair vadham
a sā tvāṃ suptaṃ hataṃ śrutvā māṃ ca rakṣogṛhaṃ gatām
c hṛdayena vidīrṇena na bhaviṣyati rāghava
a sādhu pātaya māṃ kṣipraṃ rāmasyopari rāvaṇaḥ
c samānaya patiṃ patnyā kuru kalyāṇam uttamam
a śirasā me śiraś cāsya kāyaṃ kāyena yojaya
c rāvaṇānugamiṣyāmi gatiṃ bhartur mahātmanaḥ
e muhūrtam api necchāmi jīvituṃ pāpajīvinā
a śrutaṃ mayā vedavidāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ pitur gṛhe
c yāsāṃ strīṇāṃ priyo bhartā tāsāṃ lokā mahodayāḥ
a kṣamā yasmin damas tyāgaḥ satyaṃ dharmaḥ kṛtajñatā
c ahiṃsā caiva bhūtānāṃ tam ṛte kā gatir mama
a iti sā duḥkhasaṃtaptā vilalāpāyatekṣaṇā
c bhartuḥ śiro dhanus tatra samīkṣya janakātmajā
a evaṃ lālapyamānāyāṃ sītāyāṃ tatra rākṣasaḥ
c abhicakrāma bhartāram anīkasthaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
a vijayasvāryaputreti so 'bhivādya prasādya ca
c nyavedayad anuprāptaṃ prahastaṃ vāhinīpatim
a amātyaiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ prahastaḥ samupasthitaḥ
c kiṃ cid ātyayikaṃ kāryaṃ teṣāṃ tvaṃ darśanaṃ kuru
a etac chrutvā daśagrīvo rākṣasaprativeditam
c aśokavanikāṃ tyaktvā mantriṇāṃ darśanaṃ yayau
a sa tu sarvaṃ samarthyaiva mantribhiḥ kṛtyam ātmanaḥ
c sabhāṃ praviśya vidadhe viditvā rāmavikramam
a antardhānaṃ tu tac chīrṣaṃ tac ca kārmukam uttamam
c jagāma rāvaṇasyaiva niryāṇasamanantaram
a rākṣasendras tu taiḥ sārdhaṃ mantribhir bhīmavikramaiḥ
c samarthayām āsa tadā rāmakāryaviniścayam
a avidūrasthitān sarvān balādhyakṣān hitaiṣiṇaḥ
c abravīt kālasadṛśo rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ
a śīghraṃ bherīninādena sphuṭakoṇāhatena me
c samānayadhvaṃ sainyāni vaktavyaṃ ca na kāraṇam
a tatas tatheti pratigṛhya tad vaco
balādhipās te mahad ātmano balam
c samānayaṃś caiva samāgataṃ ca te
nyavedayan bhartari yuddhakāṅkṣiṇi
a sītāṃ tu mohitāṃ dṛṣṭvā saramā nāma rākṣasī
c āsasādāśu vaidehīṃ priyāṃ praṇayinī sakhī
a sā hi tatra kṛtā mitraṃ sītayā rakṣyamāṇayā
c rakṣantī rāvaṇād iṣṭā sānukrośā dṛḍhavratā
a sā dadarśa sakhīṃ sītāṃ saramā naṣṭacetanām
c upāvṛtyotthitāṃ dhvastāṃ vaḍavām iva pāṃsuṣu
a tāṃ samāśvāsayām āsa sakhī snehena suvratā
c uktā yad rāvaṇena tvaṃ pratyuktaṃ ca svayaṃ tvayā
a sakhīsnehena tad bhīru mayā sarvaṃ pratiśrutam
c līnayā ganahe śūhye bhayam utsṛjya rāvaṇāt
e tava hetor viśālākṣi na hi me jīvitaṃ priyam
a sa saṃbhrāntaś ca niṣkrānto yat kṛte rākṣasādhipaḥ
c tac ca me viditaṃ sarvam abhiniṣkramya maithili
a na śakyaṃ sauptikaṃ kartuṃ rāmasya viditātmanaḥ
c vadhaś ca puruṣavyāghre tasminn evopapadyate
a na caiva vānarā hantuṃ śakyāḥ pādapayodhinaḥ
c surā devarṣabheṇeva rāmeṇa hi surakṣitāḥ
a dīrghavṛttabhujaḥ śrīmān mahoraskaḥ pratāpavān
c dhanvī saṃhananopeto dharmātmā bhuvi viśrutaḥ
a vikrānto rakṣitā nityam ātmanaś ca parasya ca
c lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā kuśalī nayaśāstravit
a hantā parabalaughānām acintyabalapauruṣaḥ
c na hato rāghavaḥ śrīmān sīte śatrunibarhaṇaḥ
a ayuktabuddhikṛtyena sarvabhūtavirodhinā
c iyaṃ prayuktā raudreṇa māyā māyāvidā tvayi
a śokas te vigataḥ sarvaḥ kalyāṇaṃ tvām upasthitam
c dhruvaṃ tvāṃ bhajate lakṣmīḥ priyaṃ prītikaraṃ śṛṇu
a uttīrya sāgaraṃ rāmaḥ saha vānarasenayā
c saṃniviṣṭaḥ samudrasya tīram āsādya dakṣiṇam
a dṛṣṭo me paripūrṇārthaḥ kākutsthaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
c sahitaiḥ sāgarāntasthair balais tiṣṭhati rakṣitaḥ
a anena preṣitā ye ca rākṣasā laghuvikramaḥ
c rāghavas tīrṇa ity evaṃ pravṛttis tair ihāhṛtā
a sa tāṃ śrutvā viśālākṣi pravṛttiṃ rākṣasādhipaḥ
c eṣa mantrayate sarvaiḥ sacivaiḥ saha rāvaṇaḥ
a iti bruvāṇā saramā rākṣasī sītayā saha
c sarvodyogena sainyānāṃ śabdaṃ śuśrāva bhairavam
a daṇḍanirghātavādinyāḥ śrutvā bheryā mahāsvanam
c uvāca saramā sītām idaṃ madhurabhāṣiṇī
a saṃnāhajananī hy eṣā bhairavā bhīru bherikā
c bherīnādaṃ ca gambhīraṃ śṛṇu toyadanisvanam
a kalpyante mattamātaṃgā yujyante rathavājinaḥ
c tatra tatra ca saṃnaddhāḥ saṃpatanti padātayaḥ
a āpūryante rājamārgāḥ sainyair adbhutadarśanaiḥ
c vegavadbhir nadadbhiś ca toyaughair iva sāgaraḥ
a śāstrāṇāṃ ca prasannānāṃ carmaṇāṃ varmaṇāṃ tathā
c rathavājigajānāṃ ca bhūṣitānāṃ ca rakṣasām
a prabhāṃ visṛjatāṃ paśya nānāvarṇāṃ samutthitām
c vanaṃ nirdahato dharme yathārūpaṃ vibhāvasoḥ
a ghaṇṭānāṃ śṛṇu nirghoṣaṃ rathānāṃ śṛṇu nisvanam
c hayānāṃ heṣamāṇānāṃ śṛṇu tūryadhvaniṃ yathā
a udyatāyudhahastānāṃ rākṣasendrānuyāyinām
c saṃbhramo rakṣasām eṣa tumulo lomaharṣaṇaḥ
a śrīs tvāṃ bhajati śokaghnī rakṣasāṃ bhayam āgatam
c rāmāt kamalapatrākṣi daityānām iva vāsavāt
a avajitya jitakrodhas tam acintyaparākramaḥ
c rāvaṇaṃ samare hatvā bhartā tvādhigamiṣyati
a vikramiṣyati rakṣaḥsu bhartā te sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
c yathā śatruṣu śatrughno viṣṇunā saha vāsavaḥ
a āgatasya hi rāmasya kṣipram aṅkagatāṃ satīm
c ahaṃ drakṣyāmi siddhārthāṃ tvāṃ śatrau vinipātite
a aśrūṇy ānandajāni tvaṃ vartayiṣyasi śobhane
c samāgamya pariṣvaktā tasyorasi mahorasaḥ
a acirān mokṣyate sīte devi te jaghanaṃ gatām
c dhṛtām etāṃ bahūn māsān veṇīṃ rāmo mahābalaḥ
a tasya dṛṣṭvā mukhaṃ devi pūrṇacandram ivoditam
c mokṣyase śokajaṃ vāri nirmokam iva pannagī
a rāvaṇaṃ samare hatvā nacirād eva maithili
c tvayā samagraṃ priyayā sukhārho lapsyate sukham
a samāgatā tvaṃ rāmeṇa modiṣyasi mahātmanā
c suvarṣeṇa samāyuktā yathā sasyena medinī
a girivaram abhito 'nuvartamāno
haya iva maṇḍalam āśu yaḥ karoti
c tam iha śaraṇam abhyupehi devi
divasakaraṃ prabhavo hy ayaṃ prajānām
a atha tāṃ jātasaṃtāpāṃ tena vākyena mohitām
c saramā hlādayām āsa pṛtivīṃ dyaur ivāmbhasā
a tatas tasyā hitaṃ sakhyāś cikīrṣantī sakhī vacaḥ
c uvāca kāle kālajñā smitapūrvābhibhāṣiṇī
a utsaheyam ahaṃ gatvā tvadvākyam asitekṣaṇe
c nivedya kuśalaṃ rāme praticchannā nivartitum
a na hi me kramamāṇāyā nirālambe vihāyasi
c samartho gatim anvetuṃ pavano garuḍo 'pi vā
a evaṃ bruvāṇāṃ tāṃ sītā saramāṃ punar abravīt
c madhuraṃ ślakṣṇayā vācā pūrvaśokābhipannayā
a samarthā gaganaṃ gantum api vā tvaṃ rasātalam
c avagacchāmy akartavyaṃ kartavyaṃ te madantare
a matpriyaṃ yadi kartavyaṃ yadi buddhiḥ sthirā tava
c jñātum icchāmi taṃ gatvā kiṃ karotīti rāvaṇaḥ
a sa hi māyābalaḥ krūro rāvaṇaḥ śatrurāvaṇaḥ
c māṃ mohayati duṣṭātmā pītamātreva vāruṇī
a tarjāpayati māṃ nityaṃ bhartsāpayati cāsakṛt
c rākṣasībhiḥ sughorābhir yā māṃ rakṣanti nityaśaḥ
a udvignā śaṅkitā cāsmi na ca svasthaṃ mano mama
c tad bhayāc cāham udvignā aśokavanikāṃ gatāḥ
a yadi nāma kathā tasya niścitaṃ vāpi yad bhavet
c nivedayethāḥ sarvaṃ tat paro me syād anugrahaḥ
a sā tv evaṃ bruvatīṃ sītāṃ saramā valgubhāṣiṇī
c uvāca vacanaṃ tasyāḥ spṛśantī bāṣpaviklavam
a eṣa te yady abhiprāyas tasmād gacchāmi jānaki
c gṛhya śatror abhiprāyam upāvṛttāṃ ca paśya mām
a evam uktvā tato gatvā samīpaṃ tasya rakṣasaḥ
c śuśrāva kathitaṃ tasya rāvaṇasya samantriṇaḥ
a sā śrutvā niścayaṃ tasya niścayajñā durātmanaḥ
c punar evāgamat kṣipram aśokavanikāṃ tadā
a sā praviṣṭā punas tatra dadarśa janakātmajām
c pratīkṣamāṇāṃ svām eva bhraṣṭapadmām iva śriyam
a tāṃ tu sītā punaḥ prāptāṃ saramāṃ valgubhāṣiṇīm
c pariṣvajya ca susnigdhaṃ dadau ca svayam āsanam
a ihāsīnā sukhaṃ sarvam ākhyāhi mama tattvataḥ
c krūrasya niścayaṃ tasya rāvaṇasya durātmanaḥ
a evam uktā tu saramā sītayā vepamānayā
c kathitaṃ sarvam ācaṣṭa rāvaṇasya samantriṇaḥ
a jananyā rākṣasendro vai tvanmokṣārthaṃ bṛhadvacaḥ
c aviddhena ca vaidehi mantrivṛddhena bodhitaḥ
a dīyatām abhisatkṛtya manujendrāya maithilī
c nidarśanaṃ te paryāptaṃ janasthāne yad adbhutam
a laṅghanaṃ ca samudrasya darśanaṃ ca hanūmataḥ
c vadhaṃ ca rakṣasāṃ yuddhe kaḥ kuryān mānuṣo bhuvi
a evaṃ sa mantrivṛddhaiś ca mātrā ca bahu bhāṣitaḥ
c na tvām utsahate moktum artahm arthaparo yathā
a notsahaty amṛto moktuṃ yuddhe tvām iti maithili
c sāmātyasya nṛśaṃsasya niścayo hy eṣa vartate
a tad eṣā susthirā buddhir mṛtyulobhād upasthitā
c bhayān na śaktas tvāṃ moktum anirastas tu saṃyuge
e rākṣasānāṃ ca sarveṣām ātmanaś ca vadhena hi
a nihatya rāvaṇaṃ saṃkhye sarvathā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c pratineṣyati rāmas tvām ayodhyām asitekṣaṇe
a etasminn antare śabdo bherīśaṅkhasamākulaḥ
c śruto vai sarvasainyānāṃ kampayan dharaṇītalam
a śrutvā tu taṃ vānarasainyaśabdaṃ
laṅkāgatā rākṣasarājabhṛtyāḥ
c naṣṭaujaso dainyaparītaceṣṭāḥ
śreyo na paśyanti nṛpasya doṣaiḥ
a tena śaṅkhavimiśreṇa bherīśabdena rāghavaḥ
c upayato mahābāhū rāmaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
a taṃ ninādaṃ niśamyātha rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c muhūrtaṃ dhyānam āsthāya sacivān abhyudaikṣata
a atha tān sacivāṃs tatra sarvān ābhāṣya rāvaṇaḥ
c sabhāṃ saṃnādayan sarvām ity uvāca mahābalaḥ
a taraṇaṃ sāgarasyāpi vikramaṃ balasaṃcayam
c yad uktavanto rāmasya bhavantas tan mayā śrutam
e bhavataś cāpy ahaṃ vedmi yuddhe satyaparākramān
a tatas tu sumahāprājño mālyavān nāma rākṣasaḥ
c rāvaṇasya vacaḥ śrutvā mātuḥ paitāmaho 'bravīt
a vidyāsv abhivinīto yo rājā rājan nayānugaḥ
c sa śāsti ciram aiśvaryam arīṃś ca kurute vaśe
a saṃdadhāno hi kālena vigṛhṇaṃś cāribhiḥ saha
c svapakṣavardhanaṃ kurvan mahad aiśvaryam aśnute
a hīyamānena kartavyo rājñā saṃdhiḥ samena ca
c na śatrum avamanyeta jyāyān kurvīta vigraham
a tan mahyaṃ rocate saṃdhiḥ saha rāmeṇa rāvaṇa
c yadartham abhiyuktāḥ sma sītā tasmai pradīyatām
a tasya devarṣayaḥ sarve gandharvāś ca jayaiṣiṇaḥ
c virodhaṃ mā gamas tena saṃdhis te tena rocatām
a asṛjad bhagavān pakṣau dvāv eva hi pitāmahaḥ
c surāṇām asurāṇāṃ ca dharmādharmau tadāśrayau
a dharmo hi śrūyate pakṣaḥ surāṇāṃ ca mahātmanām
c adharmo rakṣasaṃ pakṣo hy asurāṇāṃ ca rāvaṇa
a dharmo vai grasate 'dharmaṃ tataḥ kṛtam abhūd yugam
c adharmo grasate dharmaṃ tatas tiṣyaḥ pravartate
a tat tvayā caratā lokān dharmo vinihato mahān
c adharmaḥ pragṛhītaś ca tenāsmadbalinaḥ pare
a sa pramādād vivṛddhas te 'dharmo 'hir grasate hi naḥ
c vivardhayati pakṣaṃ ca surāṇāṃ surabhāvanaḥ
a viṣayeṣu prasaktena yatkiṃcitkāriṇā tvayā
c ṛṣīṇām agnikalpānām udvego janito mahān
e teṣāṃ prabhāvo durdharṣaḥ pradīpta iva pāvakaḥ
a tapasā bhāvitātmāno dharmasyānugrahe ratāḥ
c mukhyair yajñair yajanty ete nityaṃ tais tair dvijātayaḥ
a juhvaty agnīṃś ca vidhivad vedāṃś coccair adhīyate
c abhibhūya ca rakṣāṃsi brahmaghoṣān udairayan
e diśo vipradrutāḥ sarve stanayitnur ivoṣṇage
a ṛṣīṇām agnikalpānām agnihotrasamutthitaḥ
c ādatte rakṣasāṃ tejo dhūmo vyāpya diśo daśa
a teṣu teṣu ca deśeṣu puṇyeṣu ca dṛḍhavrataiḥ
c caryamāṇaṃ tapas tīvraṃ saṃtāpayati rākṣasān
a utpātān vividhān dṛṣṭvā ghorān bahuvidhāṃs tathā
c vināśam anupaśyāmi sarveṣāṃ rakṣasām aham
a kharābhis tanitā ghorā meghāḥ pratibhayaṃkaraḥ
c śoṇitenābhivarṣanti laṅkām uṣṇena sarvataḥ
a rudatāṃ vāhanānāṃ ca prapatanty asrabindavaḥ
c dhvajā dhvastā vivarṇāś ca na prabhānti yathāpuram
a vyālā gomāyavo gṛdhrā vāśanti ca subhairavam
c praviśya laṅkām aniśaṃ samavāyāṃś ca kurvate
a kālikāḥ pāṇḍurair dantaiḥ prahasanty agrataḥ sthitāḥ
c striyaḥ svapneṣu muṣṇantyo gṛhāṇi pratibhāṣya ca
a gṛhāṇāṃ balikarmāṇi śvānaḥ paryupabhuñjate
c kharā goṣu prajāyante mūṣikā nakulaiḥ saha
a mārjārā dvīpibhiḥ sārdhaṃ sūkarāḥ śunakaiḥ saha
c kiṃnarā rākṣasaiś cāpi sameyur mānuṣaiḥ saha
a pāṇḍurā raktapādāś ca vihagāḥ kālacoditāḥ
c rākṣasānāṃ vināśāya kapotā vicaranti ca
a cīkī kūcīti vāśantyaḥ śārikā veśmasu sthitāḥ
c patanti grathitāś cāpi nirjitāḥ kalahaiṣiṇaḥ
a karālo vikaṭo muṇḍaḥ puruṣaḥ kṛṣṇapiṅgalaḥ
c kālo gṛhāṇi sarveṣāṃ kāle kāle 'nvavekṣate
e etāny anyāni duṣṭāni nimittāny utpatanti ca
a viṣṇuṃ manyāmahe rāmaṃ mānuṣaṃ deham āsthitam
c na hi mānuṣamātro 'sau rāghavo dṛḍhavikramaḥ
a yena baddhaḥ samudrasya sa setuḥ paramādbhutaḥ
c kuruṣva nararājena saṃdhiṃ rāmeṇa rāvaṇa
a idaṃ vacas tatra nigadya mālyavan
parīkṣya rakṣo'dhipater manaḥ punaḥ
c anuttameṣūttamapauruṣo balī
babhūva tūṣṇīṃ samavekṣya rāvaṇam
a tat tu mālyavato vākyaṃ hitam uktaṃ daśānanaḥ
c na marṣayati duṣṭātmā kālasya vaśam āgataḥ
a sa baddhvā bhrukuṭiṃ vaktre krodhasya vaśam āgataḥ
c amarṣāt parivṛttākṣo mālyavantam athābravīt
a hitabuddhyā yad ahitaṃ vacaḥ paruṣam ucyate
c parapakṣaṃ praviśyaiva naitac chrotragataṃ mama
a mānuṣaṃ kṛpaṇaṃ rāmam ekaṃ śākhāmṛgāśrayam
c samarthaṃ manyase kena tyaktaṃ pitrā vanālayam
a rakṣasām īśvaraṃ māṃ ca devatānāṃ bhayaṃkaram
c hīnaṃ māṃ manyase kena ahīnaṃ sarvavikramaiḥ
a vīradveṣeṇa vā śaṅke pakṣapātena vā ripoḥ
c tvayāhaṃ paruṣāṇy uktaḥ paraprotsāhanena vā
a prabhavantaṃ padasthaṃ hi paruṣaṃ ko 'hbidhāsyati
c paṇḍitaḥ śāstratattvajño vinā protsāhanād ripoḥ
a ānīya ca vanāt sītāṃ padmahīnām iva śriyam
c kimarthaṃ pratidāsyāmi rāghavasya bhayād aham
a vṛtaṃ vānarakoṭībhiḥ sasugrīvaṃ salakṣmaṇam
c paśya kaiś cid ahobhis tvaṃ rāghavaṃ nihataṃ mayā
a dvandve yasya na tiṣṭhanti daivatāny api saṃyuge
c sa kasmād rāvaṇo yuddhe bhayam āhārayiṣyati
a dvidhā bhajyeyam apy evaṃ na nameyaṃ tu kasya cit
c eṣa me sahajo doṣaḥ svabhāvo duratikramaḥ
a yadi tāvat samudre tu setur baddho yadṛcchayā
c rāmeṇa vismayaḥ ko 'tra yena te bhayam āgatam
a sa tu tīrtvārṇavaṃ rāmaḥ saha vānarasenayā
c pratijānāmi te satyaṃ na jīvan pratiyāsyati
a evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ saṃrabdhaṃ ruṣṭaṃ vijñāya rāvaṇam
