c vrīḍito mālyavān vākyaṃ nottaraṃ pratyapadyata
a jayāśiṣā ca rājānaṃ vardhayitvā yathocitam
c mālyavān abhyanujñāto jagāma svaṃ niveśanam
a rāvaṇas tu sahāmātyo mantrayitvā vimṛśya ca
c laṅkāyām atulāṃ guptiṃ kārayām āsa rākṣasaḥ
a vyādideśa ca pūrvasyāṃ prahastaṃ dvāri rākṣasaṃ
c dakṣiṇasyāṃ mahāvīryau mahāpārśva mahodarau
a paścimāyām atho dvāri putram indrajitaṃ tathā
c vyādideśa mahāmāyaṃ rākṣasair bahubhir vṛtam
a uttarasyāṃ puradvāri vyādiśya śukasāraṇau
c svayaṃ cātra bhaviṣyāmi mantriṇas tān uvāca ha
a rākṣasaṃ tu virūpākṣaṃ mahāvīryaparākramam
c madhyame 'sthāpayad gulme bahubhiḥ saha rākṣasaiḥ
a evaṃvidhānaṃ laṅkāyāṃ kṛtvā rākṣasapuṃgavaḥ
c mene kṛtārtham ātmānaṃ kṛtāntavaśam āgataḥ
a visarjayām āsa tataḥ sa mantriṇo
vidhānam ājñāpya purasya puṣkalam
c jayāśiṣā mantragaṇena pūjito
viveśa so 'ntaḥpuram ṛddhiman mahat
a naravānararājau tau sa ca vāyusutaḥ kapiḥ
c jāmbavān ṛkṣarājaś ca rākṣasaś ca vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a aṅgado vāliputraś ca saumitriḥ śarabhaḥ kapiḥ
c suṣeṇaḥ sahadāyādo maindo dvivida eva ca
a gajo gavākṣo kumudo nalo 'tha panasas tathā
c amitraviṣayaṃ prāptāḥ samavetāḥ samarthayan
a iyaṃ sā lakṣyate laṅkā purī rāvaṇapālitā
c sāsuroragagandharvair amarair api durjayā
a kāryasiddhiṃ puraskṛtya mantrayadhvaṃ vinirṇaye
c nityaṃ saṃnihito hy atra rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ
a tathā teṣu bruvāṇeṣu rāvaṇāvarajo 'bravīt
c vākyam agrāmyapadavat puṣkalārthaṃ vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a analaḥ śarabhaś caiva saṃpātiḥ praghasas tathā
c gatvā laṅkāṃ mamāmātyāḥ purīṃ punar ihāgatāḥ
a bhūtvā śakunayaḥ sarve praviṣṭāś ca ripor balam
c vidhānaṃ vihitaṃ yac ca tad dṛṣṭvā samupasthitāḥ
a saṃvidhānaṃ yathāhus te rāvaṇasya durātmanaḥ
c rāma tad bruvataḥ sarvaṃ yathātathyena me śṛṇu
a pūrvaṃ prahastaḥ sabalo dvāram āsādya tiṣṭhati
c dakṣiṇaṃ ca mahāvīryau mahāpārśvamahodarau
a indrajit paścimadvāraṃ rākṣasair bahubhir vṛtaḥ
c paṭṭasāsidhanuṣmadbhiḥ śūlamudgarapāṇibhiḥ
a nānāpraharaṇaiḥ śūrair āvṛto rāvaṇātmajaḥ
c rākṣasānāṃ sahasrais tu bahubhiḥ śastrapāṇibhiḥ
a yuktaḥ paramasaṃvigno rākṣasair bahubhir vṛtaḥ
c uttaraṃ nagaradvāraṃ rāvaṇaḥ svayam āsthitaḥ
a virūpākṣas tu mahatā śūlakhaḍgadhanuṣmatā
c balena rākṣasaiḥ sārdhaṃ madhyamaṃ gulmam āsthitaḥ
a etān evaṃvidhān gulmāṃl laṅkāyāṃ samudīkṣya te
c māmakāḥ sacivāḥ sarve śīghraṃ punar ihāgatāḥ
a gajānāṃ ca sahasraṃ ca rathānām ayutaṃ pure
c hayānām ayute dve ca sāgrakoṭī ca rakṣasām
a vikrāntā balavantaś ca saṃyugeṣv ātatāyinaḥ
c iṣṭā rākṣasarājasya nityam ete niśācarāḥ
a ekaikasyātra yuddhārthe rākṣasasya viśāṃ pate
c parivāraḥ sahasrāṇāṃ sahasram upatiṣṭhate
a etāṃ pravṛttiṃ laṅkāyāṃ mantriproktaṃ vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c rāmaṃ kamalapatrākṣam idam uttaram abravīt
a kuberaṃ tu yadā rāma rāvaṇaḥ pratyayudhyata
c ṣaṣṭiḥ śatasahasrāṇi tadā niryānti rākṣasāḥ
a parākrameṇa vīryeṇa tejasā sattvagauravāt
c sadṛśā yo 'tra darpeṇa rāvaṇasya durātmanaḥ
a atra manyur na kartavyo roṣaye tvāṃ na bhīṣaye
c samartho hy asi vīryeṇa surāṇām api nigrahe
a tad bhavāṃś caturaṅgeṇa balena mahatā vṛtaḥ
c vyūhyedaṃ vānarānīkaṃ nirmathiṣyasi rāvaṇam
a rāvaṇāvaraje vākyam evaṃ bruvati rāghavaḥ
c śatrūṇāṃ pratighātārtham idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a pūrvadvāre tu laṅkāyā nīlo vānarapuṃgavaḥ
c prahastaṃ pratiyoddhā syād vānarair bahubhir vṛtaḥ
a aṅgado vāliputras tu balena mahatā vṛtaḥ
c dakṣiṇe bādhatāṃ dvāre mahāpārśvamahodarau
a hanūmān paścimadvāraṃ nipīḍya pavanātmajaḥ
c praviśatv aprameyātmā bahubhiḥ kapibhir vṛtaḥ
a daityadānavasaṃghānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanām
c viprakārapriyaḥ kṣudro varadānabalānvitaḥ
a parikrāmati yaḥ sarvāṃl lokān saṃtāpayan prajāḥ
c tasyāhaṃ rākṣasendrasya svayam eva vadhe dhṛtaḥ
a uttaraṃ nagaradvāram ahaṃ saumitriṇā saha
c nipīḍyābhipravekṣyāmi sabalo yatra rāvaṇaḥ
a vānarendraś ca balavān ṛkṣarājaś ca jāmbavān
c rākṣasendrānujaś caiva gulme bhavatu madhyame
a na caiva mānuṣaṃ rūpaṃ kāryaṃ haribhir āhave
c eṣā bhavatu naḥ saṃjñā yuddhe 'smin vānare bale
a vānarā eva niścihnaṃ svajane 'smin bhaviṣyati
c vayaṃ tu mānuṣeṇaiva sapta yotsyāmahe parān
a aham eva saha bhrātrā lakṣmaṇena mahaujasā
c ātmanā pañcamaś cāyaṃ sakhā mama vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a sa rāmaḥ kāryasiddhyartham evam uktvā vibhīṣaṇam
c suvelārohaṇe buddhiṃ cakāra matimān matim
a tatas tu rāmo mahatā balena
pracchādya sarvāṃ pṛthivīṃ mahātmā
c prahṛṣṭarūpo 'bhijagāma laṅkāṃ
kṛtvā matiṃ so 'rivadhe mahātmā
a sa tu kṛtvā suvelasya matim ārohaṇaṃ prati
c lakṣmaṇānugato rāmaḥ sugrīvam idam abravīt
a vibhīṣaṇaṃ ca dharmajñam anuraktaṃ niśācaram
c mantrajñaṃ ca vidhijñaṃ ca ślakṣṇayā parayā girā
a suvelaṃ sādhu śailendram imaṃ dhātuśataiś citam
c adhyārohāmahe sarve vatsyāmo 'tra niśām imām
a laṅkāṃ cālokayiṣyāmo nilayaṃ tasya rakṣasaḥ
c yena me maraṇāntāya hṛtā bhāryā durātmanā
a yena dharmo na vijñāto na vṛttaṃ na kulaṃ tathā
c rākṣasyā nīcayā buddhyā yena tad garhitaṃ kṛtam
a yasmin me vardhate roṣaḥ kīrtite rākṣasādhame
c yasyāparādhān nīcasya vadhaṃ drakṣyāmi rakṣasām
a eko hi kurute pāpaṃ kālapāśavaśaṃ gataḥ
c nīcenātmāpacāreṇa kulaṃ tena vinaśyati
a evaṃ saṃmantrayann eva sakrodho rāvaṇaṃ prati
c rāmaḥ suvelaṃ vāsāya citrasānum upāruhat
a pṛṣṭhato lakṣmaṇa cainam anvagacchat samāhitaḥ
c saśaraṃ cāpam udyamya sumahad vikrame rataḥ
a tam anvarohat sugrīvaḥ sāmātyaḥ savibhīṣaṇaḥ
c hanūmān aṅgado nīlo maindo dvivida eva ca
a gajo gavākṣo gavayaḥ śarabho gandhamādanaḥ
c panasaḥ kumudaś caiva haro rambhaś ca yūthapaḥ
a ete cānye ca bahavo vānarāḥ śīghragāminaḥ
c te vāyuvegapravaṇās taṃ giriṃ giricāriṇaḥ
e adhyārohanta śataśaḥ suvelaṃ yatra rāghavaḥ
a te tv adīrgheṇa kālena girim āruhya sarvataḥ
c dadṛśuḥ śikhare tasya viṣaktām iva khe purīm
a tāṃ śubhāṃ pravaradvārāṃ prākāravaraśobhitām
c laṅkāṃ rākṣasasaṃpūrṇāṃ dadṛśur hariyūthapāḥ
a prākāracayasaṃsthaiś ca tathā nīlair niśācaraiḥ
c dadṛśus te hariśreṣṭhāḥ prākāram aparaṃ kṛtam
a te dṛṣṭvā vānarāḥ sarve rākṣasān yuddhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
c mumucur vipulān nādāṃs tatra rāmasya paśyataḥ
a tato 'stam agamat sūryaḥ saṃdhyayā pratirañjitaḥ
c pūrṇacandrapradīpā ca kṣapā samabhivartate
a tataḥ sa rāmo harivāhinīpatir
vibhīṣaṇena pratinandya satkṛtaḥ
c salakṣmaṇo yūthapayūthasaṃvṛtaḥ
suvela pṛṣṭhe nyavasad yathāsukham
a tāṃ rātrim uṣitās tatra suvele haripuṃgavāḥ
c laṅkāyāṃ dadṛśur vīrā vanāny upavanāni ca
a samasaumyāni ramyāṇi viśālāny āyatāni ca
c dṛṣṭiramyāṇi te dṛṣṭvā babhūvur jātavismayāḥ
a campakāśokapuṃnāgasālatālasamākulā
c tamālavanasaṃchannā nāgamālāsamāvṛtā
a hintālair arjunair nīpaiḥ saptaparṇaiś ca puṣpitaiḥ
c tilakaiḥ karṇikāraiś ca paṭālaiś ca samantataḥ
a śuśubhe puṣpitāgraiś ca latāparigatair drumaiḥ
c laṅkā bahuvidhair divyair yathendrasyāmarāvatī
a vicitrakusumopetai raktakomalapallavaiḥ
c śādvalaiś ca tathā nīlaiś citrābhir vanarājibhiḥ
a gandhāḍhyāny abhiramyāṇi puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca
c dhārayanty agamās tatra bhūṣaṇānīva mānavāḥ
a tac caitrarathasaṃkāśaṃ manojñaṃ nandanopamam
c vanaṃ sarvartukaṃ ramyaṃ śuśubhe ṣaṭpadāyutam
a natyūhakoyaṣṭibhakair nṛtyamānaiś ca barhibhiḥ
c rutaṃ parabhṛtānāṃ ca śuśruve vananirjhare
a nityamattavihaṃgāni bhramarācaritāni ca
c kokilākulaṣaṇḍāni vihagābhirutāni ca
a bhṛṅgarājābhigītāni bhramaraiḥ sevitāni ca
c koṇālakavighuṣṭāni sārasābhirutāni ca
a viviśus te tatas tāni vanāny upavanāni ca
c hṛṣṭāḥ pramuditā vīrā harayaḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
a teṣāṃ praviśatāṃ tatra vānarāṇāṃ mahaujasām
c puṣpasaṃsargasurabhir vavau ghrāṇasukho 'nilaḥ
a anye tu harivīrāṇāṃ yūthān niṣkramya yūthapāḥ
c sugrīveṇābhyanujñātā laṅkāṃ jagmuḥ patākinīm
a vitrāsayanto vihagāṃs trāsayanto mṛgadvipān
c kampayantaś ca tāṃ laṅkāṃ nādaiḥ svair nadatāṃ varāḥ
a kurvantas te mahāvegā mahīṃ cāraṇapīḍitām
c rajaś ca sahasaivordhvaṃ jagāma caraṇoddhatam
a ṛkṣāḥ siṃhā varāhāś ca mahiṣā vāraṇā mṛgāḥ
c tena śabdena vitrastā jagmur bhītā diśo daśa
a śikharaṃ tu trikūṭasya prāṃśu caikaṃ divispṛśam
c samantāt puṣpasaṃchannaṃ mahārajatasaṃnibham
a śatayojanavistīrṇaṃ vimalaṃ cārudarśanam
c ślakṣṇaṃ śrīman mahac caiva duṣprāpaṃ śakunair api
a manasāpi durārohaṃ kiṃ punaḥ karmaṇā janaiḥ
c niviṣṭā tatra śikhare laṅkā rāvaṇapālitā
a sā purī gopurair uccaiḥ pāṇḍurāmbudasaṃnibhaiḥ
c kāñcanena ca sālena rājatena ca śobhitā
a prāsādaiś ca vimānaiś ca laṅkā paramabhūṣitā
c ghanair ivātapāpāye madhyamaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ padam
a yasyāṃ stambhasahasreṇa prāsādaḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ
c kailāsaśikharākāro dṛśyate kham ivollikhan
a caityaḥ sa rākṣasendrasya babhūva purabhūṣaṇam
c śatena rakṣasāṃ nityaṃ yaḥ samagreṇa rakṣyate
a tāṃ samṛddhāṃ samṛddhārtho lakṣmīvāṃl lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥ
c rāvaṇasya purīṃ rāmo dadarśa saha vānaraiḥ
a tāṃ ratnapūrṇāṃ bahusaṃvidhānāṃ
prāsādamālābhir alaṃkṛtāṃ ca
c purīṃ mahāyantrakavāṭamukhyāṃ
dadarśa rāmo mahatā balena
a atha tasmin nimittāni dṛṣṭvā lakṣmaṇapūrvajaḥ
c lakṣmaṇaṃ lakṣmisaṃpannam idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a parigṛhyodakaṃ śītaṃ vanāni phalavanti ca
c balaughaṃ saṃvibhajyemaṃ vyūhya tiṣṭhema lakṣmaṇa
a lokakṣayakaraṃ bhīmaṃ bhayaṃ paśyāmy upasthitam
c nibarhaṇaṃ pravīrāṇām ṛkṣavānararakṣasām
a vātāś ca paruṣaṃ vānti kampate ca vasuṃdharā
c parvatāgrāṇi vepante patanti dharaṇīdharāḥ
a meghāḥ kravyādasaṃkāśāḥ paruṣāḥ paruṣasvanāḥ
c krūrāḥ krūraṃ pravarṣanti miśraṃ śoṇitabindubhiḥ
a raktacandanasaṃkāśā saṃdhyāparamadāruṇā
c jvalac ca nipataty etad ādityād agnimaṇḍalam
a ādityam abhivāśyante janayanto mahad bhayam
c dīnā dīnasvarā ghorā apraśastā mṛgadvijāḥ
a rajanyām aprakāśaś ca saṃtāpayati candramāḥ
c kṛṣṇaraktāṃśuparyanto yathā lokasya saṃkṣaye
a hrasvo rūkṣo 'praśastaś ca pariveṣaḥ sulohitaḥ
c ādityamaṇḍale nīlaṃ lakṣma lakṣmaṇa dṛśyate
a dṛśyante na yathāvac ca nakṣatrāṇy abhivartate
c yugāntam iva lokasya paśya lakṣmaṇa śaṃsati
a kākāḥ śyenās tathā gṛdhrā nīcaiḥ paripatanti ca
c śivāś cāpy aśivā vācaḥ pravadanti mahāsvanāḥ
a kṣipram adya durādharṣāṃ purīṃ rāvaṇapālitām
c abhiyāma javenaiva sarvato haribhir vṛtāḥ
a ity evaṃ tu vadan vīro lakṣmaṇaṃ lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥ
c tasmād avātarac chīghraṃ parvatāgrān mahābalaḥ
a avatīrya tu dharmātmā tasmāc chailāt sa rāghavaḥ
c paraiḥ paramadurdharṣaṃ dadarśa balam ātmanaḥ
a saṃnahya tu sasugrīvaḥ kapirājabalaṃ mahat
c kālajño rāghavaḥ kāle saṃyugāyābhyacodayat
a tataḥ kāle mahābāhur balena mahatā vṛtaḥ
c prasthitaḥ purato dhanvī laṅkām abhimukhaḥ purīm
a taṃ vibhīṣaṇa sugrīvau hanūmāñ jāmbavān nalaḥ
c ṛkṣarājas tathā nīlo lakṣmaṇaś cānyayus tadā
a tataḥ paścāt sumahatī pṛtanarkṣavanaukasām
c pracchādya mahatīṃ bhūmim anuyāti sma rāghavam
a śailaśṛṅgāṇi śataśaḥ pravṛddhāṃś ca mahīruhām
c jagṛhuḥ kuñjaraprakhyā vānarāḥ paravāraṇāḥ
a tau tv adīrgheṇa kālena bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau
c rāvaṇasya purīṃ laṅkām āsedatur ariṃdamau
a patākāmālinīṃ ramyām udyānavanaśobhitām
c citravaprāṃ suduṣprāpām uccaprākāratoraṇām
a tāṃ surair api durdharṣāṃ rāmavākyapracoditāḥ
c yathānideśaṃ saṃpīḍya nyaviśanta vanaukasaḥ
a laṅkāyās tūttaradvāraṃ śailaśṛṅgam ivonnatam
c rāmaḥ sahānujo dhanvī jugopa ca rurodha ca
a laṅkām upaniviṣṭaś ca rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ
c lakṣmaṇānucaro vīraḥ purīṃ rāvaṇapālitām
a uttaradvāram āsādya yatra tiṣṭhati rāvaṇaḥ
c nānyo rāmād dhi tad dvāraṃ samarthaḥ parirakṣitum
a rāvaṇādhiṣṭhitaṃ bhīmaṃ varuṇeneva sāgaram
c sāyudhau rākṣasair bhīmair abhiguptaṃ samantataḥ
e laghūnāṃ trāsajananaṃ pātālam iva dānavaiḥ
a vinyastāni ca yodhānāṃ bahūni vividhāni ca
c dadarśāyudhajālāni tathaiva kavacāni ca
a pūrvaṃ tu dvāram āsādya nīlo haricamūpatiḥ
c atiṣṭhat saha maindena dvividena ca vīryavān
a aṅgado dakṣiṇadvāraṃ jagrāha sumahābalaḥ
c ṛṣabheṇa gavākṣeṇa gajena gavayena ca
a hanūmān paścimadvāraṃ rarakṣa balavān kapiḥ
c pramāthi praghasābhyāṃ ca vīrair anyaiś ca saṃgataḥ
a madhyame ca svayaṃ gulme sugrīvaḥ samatiṣṭhata
c saha sarvair hariśreṣṭhaiḥ suparṇaśvasanopamaiḥ
a vānarāṇāṃ tu ṣaṭtriṃśat koṭyaḥ prakhyātayūthapāḥ
c nipīḍyopaniviṣṭāś ca sugrīvo yatra vānaraḥ
a śāsanena tu rāmasya lakṣmaṇaḥ savibhīṣaṇaḥ
c dvāre dvāre harīṇāṃ tu koṭiṃ koṭiṃ nyaveśayat
a paścimena tu rāmasya sugrīvaḥ saha jāmbavān
c adūrān madhyame gulme tasthau bahubalānugaḥ
a te tu vānaraśārdūlāḥ śārdūlā iva daṃṣṭriṇaḥ
c gṛhītvā drumaśailāgrān hṛṣṭā yuddhāya tasthire
a sarve vikṛtalāṅgūlāḥ sarve daṃṣṭrānakhāyudhāḥ
c sarve vikṛtacitrāṅgāḥ sarve ca vikṛtānanāḥ
a daśanāgabalāḥ ke cit ke cid daśaguṇottarāḥ
c ke cin nāgasahasrasya babhūvus tulyavikramāḥ
a santi caughā balāḥ ke cit ke cic chataguṇottarāḥ
c aprameyabalāś cānye tatrāsan hariyūthapāḥ
a adbhutaś ca vicitraś ca teṣām āsīt samāgamaḥ
c tatra vānarasainyānāṃ śalabhānām ivodgamaḥ
a paripūrṇam ivākāśaṃ saṃchanneva ca medinī
c laṅkām upaniviṣṭaiś ca saṃpatadbhiś ca vānaraiḥ
a śataṃ śatasahasrāṇāṃ pṛthag ṛkṣavanaukasām
c laṅkā dvārāṇy upājagmur anye yoddhuṃ samantataḥ
a āvṛtaḥ sa giriḥ sarvais taiḥ samantāt plavaṃgamaiḥ
c ayutānāṃ sahasraṃ ca purīṃ tām abhyavartata
a vānarair balavadbhiś ca babhūva drumapāṇibhiḥ
c sarvataḥ saṃvṛtā laṅkā duṣpraveśāpi vāyunā
a rākṣasā vismayaṃ jagmuḥ sahasābhinipīḍitāḥ
c vānarair meghasaṃkāśaiḥ śakratulyaparākramaiḥ
a mahāñ śabdo 'bhavat tatra balaughasyābhivartataḥ
c sāgarasyeva bhinnasya yathā syāt salilasvanaḥ
a tena śabdena mahatā saprākārā satoraṇā
c laṅkā pracalitā sarvā saśailavanakānanā
a rāmalakṣmaṇaguptā sā sugrīveṇa ca vāhinī
c babhūva durdharṣatarā sarvair api surāsuraiḥ
a rāghavaḥ saṃniveśyaivaṃ sainyaṃ svaṃ rakṣasāṃ vadhe
c saṃmantrya mantribhiḥ sārdhaṃ niścitya ca punaḥ punaḥ
a ānantaryam abhiprepsuḥ kramayogārthatattvavit
c vibhīṣaṇasyānumate rājadharmam anusmaran
e aṅgadaṃ vālitanayaṃ samāhūyedam abravīt
a gatvā saumya daśagrīvaṃ brūhi madvacanāt kape
c laṅghayitvā purīṃ laṅkāṃ bhayaṃ tyaktvā gatavyathaḥ
a bhraṣṭaśrīkagataiśvaryamumūrṣo naṣṭacetanaḥ
c ṛṣīṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca gandharvāpsarasāṃ tathā
a nāgānām atha yakṣāṇāṃ rājñāṃ ca rajanīcara
c yac ca pāpaṃ kṛtaṃ mohād avaliptena rākṣasa
a nūnam adya gato darpaḥ svayambhū varadānajaḥ
c yasya daṇḍadharas te 'haṃ dārāharaṇakarśitaḥ
e daṇḍaṃ dhārayamāṇas tu laṅkādvare vyavasthitaḥ
a padavīṃ devatānāṃ ca maharṣīṇāṃ ca rākṣasa
c rājarṣīṇāṃ ca sarveṇāṃ gamiṣyasi mayā hataḥ
a balena yena vai sītāṃ māyayā rākṣasādhama
c mām atikrāmayitvā tvaṃ hṛtavāṃs tad vidarśaya
a arākṣasam imaṃ lokaṃ kartāsmi niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c na cec charaṇam abhyeṣi mām upādāya maithilīm
a dharmātmā rakṣasāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ saṃprāpto 'yaṃ vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c laṅkaiśvaryaṃ dhruvaṃ śrīmān ayaṃ prāpnoty akaṇṭakam
a na hi rājyam adharmeṇa bhoktuṃ kṣaṇam api tvayā
c śakyaṃ mūrkhasahāyena pāpenāvijitātmanā
a yudhyasva vā dhṛtiṃ kṛtvā śauryam ālambya rākṣasa
c maccharais tvaṃ raṇe śāntas tataḥ pūto bhaviṣyasi
a yady āviśasi lokāṃs trīn pakṣibhūto manojavaḥ
c mama cakṣuṣpathaṃ prāpya na jīvan pratiyāsyasi
a bravīmi tvāṃ hitaṃ vākyaṃ kriyatām aurdhvadekikam
c sudṛṣṭā kriyatāṃ laṅkā jīvitaṃ te mayi sthitam
a ity uktaḥ sa tu tāreyo rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇā
c jagāmākāśam āviśya mūrtimān iva havyavāṭ
a so 'tipatya muhūrtena śrīmān rāvaṇamandiram
c dadarśāsīnam avyagraṃ rāvaṇaṃ sacivaiḥ saha
a tatas tasyāvidūreṇa nipatya haripuṃgavaḥ
c dīptāgnisadṛśas tasthāv aṅgadaḥ kanakāṅgadaḥ
a tad rāmavacanaṃ sarvam anyūnādhikam uttamam
c sāmātyaṃ śrāvayām āsa nivedyātmānam ātmanā
a dūto 'haṃ kosalendrasya rāmasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
c vāliputro 'ṅgado nāma yadi te śrotram āgataḥ
a āha tvāṃ rāghavo rāmaḥ kausalyānandavardhanaḥ
c niṣpatya pratiyudhyasva nṛśaṃsaṃ puruṣādhama
a hantāsmi tvāṃ sahāmātyaṃ saputrajñātibāndhavam
c nirudvignās trayo lokā bhaviṣyanti hate tvayi
a devadānavayakṣāṇāṃ gandharvoragarakṣasām
c śatrum adyoddhariṣyāmi tvām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca kaṇṭakam
a vibhīṣaṇasya caiśvaryaṃ bhaviṣyati hate tvayi
c na cet satkṛtya vaidehīṃ praṇipatya pradāsyasi
a ity evaṃ paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ bruvāṇe haripuṃgave
c amarṣavaśam āpanno niśācaragaṇeśvaraḥ
a tataḥ sa roṣatāmrākṣaḥ śaśāsa sacivāṃs tadā
c gṛhyatām eṣa durmedhā vadhyatām iti cāsakṛt
a rāvaṇasya vacaḥ śrutvā dīptāgnisamatejasaḥ
c jagṛhus taṃ tato ghorāś catvāro rajanīcarāḥ
a grāhayām āsa tāreyaḥ svayam ātmānam ātmanā
c balaṃ darśayituṃ vīro yātudhānagaṇe tadā
a sa tān bāhudvaye saktān ādāya patagān iva
c prāsādaṃ śailasaṃkāśam utpāpātāṅgadas tadā
a te 'ntarikṣād vinirdhūtās tasya vegena rākṣasāḥ
c bhumau nipatitāḥ sarve rākṣasendrasya paśyataḥ
a tataḥ prāsādaśikharaṃ śailaśṛṅgam ivonnatam
c tat paphāla tadākrāntaṃ daśagrīvasya paśyataḥ
a bhaṅktvā prāsādaśikharaṃ nāma viśrāvya cātmanaḥ
c vinadya sumahānādam utpapāta vihāyasā
a rāvaṇas tu paraṃ cakre krodhaṃ prāsādadharṣaṇāt
c vināśaṃ cātmanaḥ paśyan niḥśvāsaparamo 'bhavat
a rāmas tu bahubhir hṛṣṭair ninadadbhiḥ plavaṃgamaiḥ
c vṛto ripuvadhākāṅkṣī yuddhāyaivābhyavartata
a suṣeṇas tu mahāvīryo girikūṭopamo hariḥ
c bahubhiḥ saṃvṛtas tatra vānaraiḥ kāmarūpibhiḥ
a caturdvārāṇi sarvāṇi sugrīvavacanāt kapiḥ
c paryākramata durdharṣo nakṣatrāṇīva candramāḥ
a teṣām akṣauhiṇiśataṃ samavekṣya vanaukasām
c laṅkām upaniviṣṭānāṃ sāgaraṃ cātivartatām
a rākṣasā vismayaṃ jagmus trāsaṃ jagmus tathāpare
c apare samaroddharṣād dharṣam evopapedire
a kṛtsnaṃ hi kapibhir vyāptaṃ prākāraparikhāntaram
c dadṛśū rākṣasā dīnāḥ prākāraṃ vānarīkṛtam
a tasmin mahābhīṣaṇake pravṛtte
kolāhale rākṣasarājadhānyām
c pragṛhya rakṣāṃsi mahāyudhāni
yugāntavātā iva saṃviceruḥ
a tatas te rākṣasās tatra gatvā rāvaṇamandiram
c nyavedayan purīṃ ruddhāṃ rāmeṇa saha vānaraiḥ
a ruddhāṃ tu nagarīṃ śrutvā jātakrodho niśācaraḥ
c vidhānaṃ dviguṇaṃ śrutvā prāsādaṃ so 'dhyarohata
a sa dadarśāvṛtāṃ laṅkāṃ saśailavanakānanām
c asaṃkhyeyair harigaṇaiḥ sarvato yuddhakāṅkṣibhiḥ
a sa dṛṣṭvā vānaraiḥ sarvāṃ vasudhāṃ kavalīkṛtām
c kathaṃ kṣapayitavyāḥ syur iti cintāparo 'bhavat
a sa cintayitvā suciraṃ dhairyam ālambya rāvaṇaḥ
c rāghavaṃ hariyūthāṃś ca dadarśāyatalocanaḥ
a prekṣato rākṣasendrasya tāny anīkāni bhāgaśaḥ
c rāghavapriyakāmārthaṃ laṅkām āruruhus tadā
a te tāmravaktrā hemābhā rāmārthe tyaktajīvitāḥ
c laṅkām evāhyavartanta sālatālaśilāyudhāḥ
a te drumaiḥ parvatāgraiś ca muṣṭibhiś ca plavaṃgamāḥ
c prāsādāgrāṇi coccāni mamantus toraṇāni ca
a pārikhāḥ pūrayanti sma prasannasalilāyutāḥ
c pāṃsubhiḥ parvatāgraiś ca tṛṇaiḥ kāṣṭhaiś ca vānarāḥ
a tataḥ sahasrayūthāś ca koṭiyūthāś ca yūthapāḥ
c koṭīśatayutāś cānye laṅkām āruruhus tadā
a kāñcanāni pramṛdnantas toraṇāni plavaṃgamāḥ
c kailāsaśikharābhāni gopurāṇi pramathya ca
a āplavantaḥ plavantaś ca garjantaś ca plavaṃgamāḥ
c laṅkāṃ tām abhyavartanta mahāvāraṇasaṃnibhāḥ
a jayaty atibalo rāmo lakṣmaṇaś ca mahābalaḥ
c rājā jayati sugrīvo rāghaveṇābhipālitaḥ
a ity evaṃ ghoṣayantaś ca garjantaś ca plavaṃgamāḥ
c abhyadhāvanta laṅkāyāḥ prākāraṃ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
a vīrabāhuḥ subāhuś ca nalaś ca vanagocaraḥ
c nipīḍyopaniviṣṭās te prākāraṃ hariyūthapāḥ
a etasminn antare cakruḥ skandhāvāraniveśanam
a pūrvadvāraṃ tu kumudaḥ koṭibhir daśabhir vṛtaḥ
c āvṛtya balavāṃs tasthau haribhir jitakāśibhiḥ
a dakṣiṇadvāram āgamya vīraḥ śatabaliḥ kapiḥ
c āvṛtya balavāṃs tasthau viṃśatyā koṭibhir vṛtaḥ
a suṣeṇaḥ paścimadvāraṃ gatas tārā pitā hariḥ
c āvṛtya balavāṃs tasthau ṣaṣṭi koṭibhir āvṛtaḥ
a uttaradvāram āsādya rāmaḥ saumitriṇā saha
c āvṛtya balavāṃs tasthau sugrīvaś ca harīśvaraḥ
a golāṅgūlo mahākāyo gavākṣo bhīmadarśanaḥ
c vṛtaḥ koṭyā mahāvīryas tasthau rāmasya pārvataḥ
a ṛṣkāṇāṃ bhīmavegānāṃ dhūmraḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥ
c vṛtaḥ koṭyā mahāvīryas tasthau rāmasya pārśvataḥ
a saṃnaddhas tu mahāvīryo gadāpāṇir vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c vṛto yas tais tu sacivais tasthau tatra mahābalaḥ
a gajo gavākṣo gavayaḥ śarabho gandhamādanaḥ
c samantāt parighāvanto rarakṣur harivāhinīm
a tataḥ kopaparītātmā rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c niryāṇaṃ sarvasainyānāṃ drutam ājñāpayat tadā
a niṣpatanti tataḥ sainyā hṛṣṭā rāvaṇacoditāḥ
c samaye pūryamāṇasya vegā iva mahodadheḥ
a etasminn antare ghoraḥ saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyata
c rakṣasāṃ vānarāṇāṃ ca yathā devāsure purā
a te gadābhiḥ pradīptābhiḥ śaktiśūlaparaśvadhaiḥ
c nijaghnur vānarān ghorāḥ kathayantaḥ svavikramān
a tathā vṛkṣair mahākāyāḥ parvatāgraiś ca vānarāḥ
c rākṣasās tāni rakṣāṃsi nakhair dantaiś ca vegitāḥ
a rākṣasās tv apare bhīmāḥ prākārasthā mahīgatān
c bhiṇḍipālaiś ca khaḍgaiś ca śūlaiś caiva vyadārayan
a vānarāś cāpi saṃkruddhāḥ prākārasthān mahīgatāḥ
c rākṣasān pātayām āsuḥ samāplutya plavaṃgamāḥ
a sa saṃprahāras tumulo māṃsaśoṇitakardamaḥ
c rakṣasāṃ vānarāṇāṃ ca saṃbabhūvādbhutopamāḥ
a yudhyatāṃ tu tatas teṣāṃ vānarāṇāṃ mahātmanām
c rakṣasāṃ saṃbabhūvātha balakopaḥ sudāruṇaḥ
a te hayaiḥ kāñcanāpīḍair dhvajaiś cāgniśikhopamaiḥ
c rathaiś cādityasaṃkāśaiḥ kavacaiś ca manoramaiḥ
a niryayū rākṣasavyāghrā nādayanto diśo daśa
c rākṣasā bhīmakarmāṇo rāvaṇasya jayaiṣiṇaḥ
a vānarāṇām api camūr mahatī jayam iccatām
c abhyadhāvata tāṃ senāṃ rakṣasāṃ kāmarūpiṇām
a etasminn antare teṣām anyonyam abhidhāvatām
c rakṣasāṃ vānarāṇāṃ ca dvandvayuddham avartata
a aṅgadenendrajit sārdhaṃ vāliputreṇa rākṣasaḥ
c ayudhyata mahātejās tryambakeṇa yathāndhakaḥ
a prajaṅghena ca saṃpātir nityaṃ durmarṣaṇo raṇe
c jambūmālinam ārabdho hanūmān api vānaraḥ
a saṃgataḥ sumahākrodho rākṣaso rāvaṇānujaḥ
c samare tīkṣṇavegena mitraghnena vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a tapanena gajaḥ sārdhaṃ rākṣasena mahābalaḥ
c nikumbhena mahātejā nīlo 'pi samayudhyata
a vānarendras tu sugrīvaḥ praghasena samāgataḥ
c saṃgataḥ samare śrīmān virūpākṣeṇa lakṣmaṇaḥ
a agniketuś ca durdharṣo raśmiketuś ca rākṣasaḥ
c suptaghno yajñakopaś ca rāmeṇa saha saṃgatāḥ
a vajramuṣṭis tu maindena dvividenāśaniprabhaḥ
c rākṣasābhyāṃ sughorābhyāṃ kapimukhyau samāgatau
a vīraḥ pratapano ghoro rākṣaso raṇadurdharaḥ
c samare tīkṣṇavegena nalena samayudhyata
a dharmasya putro balavān suṣeṇa iti viśrutaḥ
c sa vidyunmālinā sārdham ayudhyata mahākapiḥ
a vānarāś cāpare bhīmā rākṣasair aparaiḥ saha
c dvandvaṃ samīyur bahudhā yuddhāya bahubhiḥ saha
a tatrāsīt sumahad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c rakṣasāṃ vānarāṇāṃ ca vīrāṇāṃ jayam icchatām
a harirākṣasadehebhyaḥ prasṛtāḥ keśaśāḍvalāḥ
c śarīrasaṃghāṭavahāḥ prasusruḥ śoṇitāpagāḥ
a ājaghānendrajit kruddho vajreṇeva śatakratuḥ
c aṅgadaṃ gadayā vīraṃ śatrusainyavidāraṇam
a tasya kāñcanacitrāṅgaṃ rathaṃ sāśvaṃ sasārathim
c jaghāna samare śrīmān aṅgado vegavān kapiḥ
a saṃpātis tu tribhir bāṇaiḥ prajaṅghena samāhataḥ
c nijaghānāśvakarṇena prajaṅghaṃ raṇamūrdhani
a jambūmālī rathasthas tu rathaśaktyā mahābalaḥ
c bibheda samare kruddho hanūmantaṃ stanāntare
a tasya taṃ ratham āsthāya hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
c pramamātha talenāśu saha tenaiva rakṣasā
a bhinnagātraḥ śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ kṣiprahastena rakṣasā
c prajaghānādriśṛṅgeṇa tapanaṃ muṣṭinā gajaḥ
a grasantam iva sainyāni praghasaṃ vānarādhipaḥ
c sugrīvaḥ saptaparṇena nirbibheda jaghāna ca
a prapīḍya śaravarṣeṇa rākṣasaṃ bhīmadarśanam
c nijaghāna virūpākṣaṃ śareṇaikena lakṣmaṇaḥ
a agniketuś ca durdharṣo raśmiketuś ca rākṣasaḥ
c suptighno yajñakopaś ca rāmaṃ nirbibhiduḥ śaraiḥ
a teṣāṃ caturṇāṃ rāmas tu śirāṃsi samare śaraiḥ
c kruddhaś caturbhiś ciccheda ghorair agniśikhopamaiḥ
a vajramuṣṭis tu maindena muṣṭinā nihato raṇe
c papāta sarathaḥ sāśvaḥ purāṭṭa iva bhūtale

c śarair aśanisaṃkāśaiḥ sa vivyādhāśaniprabhaḥ
a sa śarair atividdhāṅgo dvividaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
c sālena sarathaṃ sāśvaṃ nijaghānāśaniprabham
a nikumbhas tu raṇe nīlaṃ nīlāñjanacayaprabham
c nirbibheda śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ karair megham ivāṃśumān

c bibheda samare nīlaṃ nikumbhaḥ prajahāsa ca

c suṣeṇaṃ tāḍayām āsa nanāda ca muhur muhuḥ
a taṃ rathastham atho dṛṣṭvā suṣeṇo vānarottamaḥ
c giriśṛṅgeṇa mahatā ratham āśu nyapātayat

c apakramya rathāt tūrṇaṃ gadāpāṇiḥ kṣitau sthitaḥ

c śilāṃ sumahatīṃ gṛhya niśācaram abhidravat

c tāṃ śilāṃ pātayām āsa tasyorasi mahāmṛdhe
a śilāprahārābhihato vidyunmālī niśācaraḥ
c niṣpiṣṭahṛdayo bhūmau gatāsur nipapāta ha
a evaṃ tair vānaraiḥ śūraiḥ śūrās te rajanīcarāḥ
c dvandve vimṛditās tatra daityā iva divaukasaiḥ
a bhallaiḥ khaḍgair gadābhiś ca śaktitomara paṭṭasaiḥ
c apaviddhaś ca bhinnaś ca rathaiḥ sāṃgrāmikair hayaiḥ
a nihataiḥ kuñjarair mattais tathā vānararākṣasaiḥ
c cakrākṣayugadaṇḍaiś ca bhagnair dharaṇisaṃśritaiḥ
e babhūvāyodhanaṃ ghoraṃ gomāyugaṇasevitam

niśācarāḥ śoṇitadigdhagātrāḥ

a yudhyatām eva teṣāṃ tu tadā vānararakṣasām

a anyonyaṃ baddhavairāṇāṃ ghorāṇāṃ jayam icchatām
c saṃpravṛttaṃ niśāyuddhaṃ tadā vāraṇarakṣasām
a rākṣaso 'sīti harayo hariś cāsīti rākṣasāḥ
c anyonyaṃ samare jaghnus tasmiṃs tamasi dāruṇe
a jahi dāraya caitīti kathaṃ vidravasīti ca

c saṃprādṛśyanta śailendrā dīptauṣadhivanā iva

c paripetur mahāvegā bhakṣayantaḥ plavaṃgamān

c yuddhād apasṛtās tatra sāvaśeṣāyuṣo 'bhavan
a tataḥ kāñcanacitrāṅgaiḥ śarair agniśikhopamaiḥ
c diśaś cakāra vimalāḥ pradiśaś ca mahābalaḥ

c bibheda samare kruddhaḥ sarvagātreṣu rākṣasaḥ
a sa tasya gatim anvicchan rājaputraḥ pratāpavān

c aṅgadaṃ vāliputraṃ ca śarabhaṃ ca tarasvinam

c draṣṭum āsādituṃ vāpi na śaktaḥ kiṃ punar yuvām

a tataḥ puṣpakam āropya sītāṃ trijaṭayā saha
c rāvaṇo 'kārayal laṅkāṃ patākādhvajamālinīm
a prāghoṣayata hṛṣṭaś ca laṅkāyāṃ rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c rāghavo lakṣmaṇaś caiva hatāv indrajitā raṇe
a vimānenāpi sītā tu gatvā trijaṭayā saha
c dadarśa vānarāṇāṃ tu sarvaṃ sinyaṃ nipātitam
a prahṛṣṭamanasaś cāpi dadarśa piśitāśanān
c vānarāṃś cāpi duḥkhārtān rāmalakṣmaṇapārśvataḥ
a tataḥ sītā dadarśobhau śayānau śatatalpayoḥ
c lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva rāmaṃ ca visaṃjñau śarapīḍitau
a vidhvastakavacau vīrau vipraviddhaśarāsanau
c sāyakaiś chinnasarvāṅgau śarastambhamayau kṣitau
a tau dṛṣṭvā bhrātarau tatra vīrau sā puruṣarṣabhau
c duḥkhārtā subhṛśaṃ sītā karuṇaṃ vilalāpa ha
a sā bāṣpaśokābhihatā samīkṣya
tau bhrātarau devasamaprabhāvau
c vitarkayantī nidhanaṃ tayoḥ sā
duḥkhānvitā vākyam idaṃ jagāda
a bhartāraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā lakṣmaṇaṃ ca mahābalam
c vilalāpa bhṛśaṃ sītā karuṇaṃ śokakarśitā
a ūcur lakṣaṇikā ye māṃ putriṇy avidhaveti ca
c te 'sya sarve hate rāme 'jñānino 'nṛtavādinaḥ
a yajvano mahiṣīṃ ye mām ūcuḥ patnīṃ ca satriṇaḥ
c te 'dya sarve hate rāme 'jñānino 'nṛtavādinaḥ
a vīrapārthivapatnī tvaṃ ye dhanyeti ca māṃ viduḥ
c te 'dya sarve hate rāme 'jñānino 'nṛtavādinaḥ
a ūcuḥ saṃśravaṇe ye māṃ dvijāḥ kārtāntikāḥ śubhām
c te 'dya sarve hate rāme 'jñānino 'nṛtavādinaḥ
a imāni khalu padmāni pādayor yaiḥ kila striyaḥ
c adhirājye 'bhiṣicyante narendraiḥ patibhiḥ saha
a vaidhavyaṃ yānti yair nāryo 'lakṣaṇair bhāgyadurlabhāḥ
c nātmanas tāni paśyāmi paśyantī hatalakṣaṇā
a satyānīmāni padmāni strīṇām uktvāni lakṣaṇe
c tāny adya nihate rāme vitathāni bhavanti me
a keśāḥ sūkṣmāḥ samā nīlā bhruvau cāsaṃgate mama
c vṛtte cālomaśe jaṅghe dantāś cāviralā mama
a śaṅkhe netre karau pādau gulphāv ūrū ca me citau
c anuvṛttā nakhāḥ snigdhāḥ samāś cāṅgulayo mama
a stanau cāviralau pīnau mamemau magnacūcukau
c magnā cotsaṅginī nābhiḥ pārśvoraskaṃ ca me citam
a mama varṇo maṇinibho mṛdūny aṅgaruhāṇi ca
c pratiṣṭhitāṃ dvadaśabhir mām ūcuḥ śubhalakṣaṇām
a samagrayavam acchidraṃ pāṇipādaṃ ca varṇavat
c mandasmitety eva ca māṃ kanyālakṣaṇikā viduḥ
a adhirājye 'bhiṣeko me brāhmaṇaiḥ patinā saha
c kṛtāntakuśalair uktaṃ tat sarvaṃ vitathīkṛtam
a śodhayitvā janasthānaṃ pravṛttim upalabhya ca
c tīrtvā sāgaram akṣobhyaṃ bhrātarau goṣpade hatau
a nanu vāruṇam āgneyam aindraṃ vāyavyam eva ca
c astraṃ brahmaśiraś caiva rāghavau pratyapadyatām
a adṛśyamānena raṇe māyayā vāsavopamau
c mama nāthāv anāthāyā nihatau rāmalakṣmaṇau
a na hi dṛṣṭipathaṃ prāpya rāghavasya raṇe ripuḥ
c jīvan pratinivarteta yady api syān manojavaḥ
a na kālasyātibhāro 'sti kṛtāntaś ca sudurjayaḥ
c yatra rāmaḥ saha bhrātrā śete yudhi nipāthitaḥ
a nāhaṃ śocāmi bhartāraṃ nihataṃ na ca lakṣmaṇam
c nātmānaṃ jananī cāpi yathā śvaśrūṃ tapasvinīm
a sā hi cintayate nityaṃ samāptavratam āgatam
c kadā drakṣyāmi sītāṃ ca rāmaṃ ca sahalakṣmaṇam
a paridevayamānāṃ tāṃ rākṣasī trijaṭābravīt
c mā viṣādaṃ kṛthā devi bhartāyaṃ tava jīvati
a kāraṇāni ca vakṣyāmi mahānti sadṛśāni ca
c yathemau jīvato devi bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau
a na hi kopaparītāni harṣaparyutsukāni ca
c bhavanti yudhi yodhānāṃ mukhāni nihate patau
a idaṃ vimānaṃ vaidehi puṣpakaṃ nāma nāmataḥ
c divyaṃ tvāṃ dhārayen nedaṃ yady etau gajajīvitau
a hatavīrapradhānā hi hatotsāhā nirudyamā
c senā bhramati saṃkhyeṣu hatakarṇeva naur jale
a iyaṃ punar asaṃbhrāntā nirudvignā tarasvinī
c senā rakṣati kākutsthau māyayā nirjitau raṇe
a sā tvaṃ bhava suvisrabdhā anumānaiḥ sukhodayaiḥ
c ahatau paśya kākutsthau snehād etad bravīmi te
a anṛtaṃ noktapūrvaṃ me na ca vakṣye kadā cana
c cāritrasukhaśīlatvāt praviṣṭāsi mano mama
a nemau śakyau raṇe jetuṃ sendrair api surāsuraiḥ
c etayor ānanaṃ dṛṣṭvā mayā cāveditaṃ tava
a idaṃ ca sumahac cihnaṃ śanaiḥ paśyasva maithili
c niḥsaṃjñāv apy ubhāv etau naiva lakṣmīr viyujyate
a prāyeṇa gatasattvānāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ gatāyuṣām
c dṛśyamāneṣu vaktreṣu paraṃ bhavati vaikṛtam
a tyaja śokaṃ ca duḥkhaṃ ca mohaṃ ca janakātmaje
c rāmalakṣmaṇayor arthe nādya śakyam ajīvitum
a śrutvā tu vacanaṃ tasyāḥ sītā surasutopamā
c kṛtāñjalir uvācedam evam astv iti maithilī
a vimānaṃ puṣpakaṃ tat tu samivartya manojavam
c dīnā trijaṭayā sītā laṅkām eva praveśitā
a tatas trijaṭayā sārdhaṃ puṣpakād avaruhya sā
c aśokavanikām eva rakṣasībhiḥ praveśitā
a praviśya sītā bahuvṛkṣaṣaṇḍāṃ
tāṃ rākṣasendrasya vihārabhūmim
c saṃprekṣya saṃcintya ca rājaputrau
paraṃ viṣādaṃ samupājagāma
a ghoreṇa śarabandhena baddhau daśarathātmajau
c niśvasantau yathā nāgau śayānau rudhirokṣitau
a sarve te vānaraśreṣṭhāḥ sasugrīvā mahābalāḥ
c parivārya mahātmānau tasthuḥ śokapariplutāḥ
a etasminn antere rāmaḥ pratyabudhyata vīryavān
c sthiratvāt sattvayogāc ca śaraiḥ saṃdānito 'pi san
a tato dṛṣṭvā sarudhiraṃ viṣaṇṇaṃ gāḍham arpitam
c bhrātaraṃ dīnavadanaṃ paryadevayad āturaḥ
a kiṃ nu me sītayā kāryaṃ kiṃ kāryaṃ jīvitena vā
c śayānaṃ yo 'dya paśyāmi bhrātaraṃ yudhi nirjitam
a śakyā sītā samā nārī prāptuṃ loke vicinvatā
c na lakṣmaṇasamo bhrātā sacivaḥ sāmparāyikaḥ
a parityakṣyāmy ahaṃ prāṇān vānarāṇāṃ tu paśyatām
c yadi pañcatvam āpannaḥ sumitrānandavardhanaḥ
a kiṃ nu vakṣyāmi kausalyāṃ mātaraṃ kiṃ nu kaikayīm
c katham ambāṃ sumitrāṃca putradarśanalālasām
a vivatsāṃ vepamānāṃ ca krośantīṃ kurarīm iva
c katham āśvāsayiṣyāmi yadi yāsyāmi taṃ vinā
a kathaṃ vakṣyāmi śatrughnaṃ bharataṃ ca yaśasvinam
c mayā saha vanaṃ yāto vinā tenāgataḥ punaḥ
a upālambhaṃ na śakṣyāmi soḍhuṃ bata sumitrayā
c ihaiva dehaṃ tyakṣyāmi na hi jīvitum utsahe
a dhiṅ māṃ duṣkṛtakarmāṇam anāryaṃ yatkṛte hy asau
c lakṣmaṇaḥ patitaḥ śete śaratalpe gatāsuvat
a tvaṃ nityaṃ suviṣaṇṇaṃ mām āśvāsayasi lakṣmaṇa
c gatāsur nādya śaknoṣi mām ārtam abhibhāṣitum
a yenādya bahavo yuddhe rākṣasā nihatāḥ kṣitau
c tasyām eva kṣitau vīraḥ sa śete nihataḥ paraiḥ
a śayānaḥ śaratalpe 'smin svaśoṇitapariplutaḥ
c śarajālaiś cito bhāti bhāskaro 'stam iva vrajan
a bāṇābhihatamarmatvān na śaknoty abhivīkṣitum
c rujā cābruvato hy asya dṛṣṭirāgeṇa sūcyate
a yathaiva māṃ vanaṃ yāntam anuyāto mahādyutiḥ
c aham apy anuyāsyāmi tathaivainaṃ yamakṣayam
a iṣṭabandhujano nityaṃ māṃ ca nityam anuvrataḥ
c imām adya gato 'vasthāṃ mamānāryasya durnayaiḥ
a suruṣṭenāpi vīreṇa lakṣmaṇenā na saṃsmare
c paruṣaṃ vipriyaṃ vāpi śrāvitaṃ na kadā cana
a visasarjaikavegena pañcabāṇaśatāni yaḥ
c iṣvastreṣv adhikas tasmāt kārtavīryāc ca lakṣmaṇaḥ
a astrair astrāṇi yo hanyāc chakrasyāpi mahātmanaḥ
c so 'yam urvyāṃhataḥ śete mahārhaśayanocitaḥ
a tac ca mithyā pralaptaṃ māṃ pradhakṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
c yan mayā na kṛto rājā rākṣasānāṃ vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a asmin muhūrte sugrīva pratiyātum ito 'rhasi
c matvā hīnaṃ mayā rājan rāvaṇo 'bhidraved balī
a aṅgadaṃ tu puraskṛtya sasainyaḥ sasuhṛjjanaḥ
c sāgaraṃ tara sugrīva punas tenaiva setunā
a kṛtaṃ hanumatā kāryaṃ yad anyair duṣkaraṃ raṇe
c ṛkṣarājena tuṣyāmi golāṅgūlādhipena ca
a aṅgadena kṛtaṃ karma maindena dvividena ca
c yuddhaṃ kesariṇā saṃkhye ghoraṃ saṃpātinā kṛtam
a gavayena gavākṣeṇa śarabheṇa gajena ca
c anyaiś ca haribhir yuddhaṃ madārthe tyaktajīvitaiḥ
a na cātikramituṃ śakyaṃ daivaṃ sugrīva mānuṣaiḥ
c yat tu śakyaṃ vayasyena suhṛdā vā paraṃtapa
e kṛtaṃ sugrīva tat sarvaṃ bhavatādharmabhīruṇā
a mitrakāryaṃ kṛtam idaṃ bhavadbhir vānararṣabhāḥ
c anujñātā mayā sarve yatheṣṭaṃ gantum arhatha
a śuśruvus tasya te sarve vānarāḥ paridevitam
c vartayāṃ cakrur aśrūṇi netraiḥ kṛṣṇetarekṣaṇāḥ
a tataḥ sarvāṇy anīkāni sthāpayitvā vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c ājagāma gadāpāṇis tvarito yatra rāghavaḥ
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā tvaritaṃ yāntaṃ nīlāñjanacayopamam
c vānarā dudruvuḥ sarve manyamānās tu rāvaṇim
a athovāca mahātejā harirājo mahābalaḥ
c kim iyaṃ vyathitā senā mūḍhavāteva naur jale
a sugrīvasya vacaḥ śrutvā vāliputro 'ṅgado 'bravīt
c na tvaṃ paśyasi rāmaṃ ca lakṣmaṇaṃ ca mahābalam
a śarajālācitau vīrāv ubhau daśarathātmajau
c śaratalpe mahātmānau śayānāu rudhirokṣitau
a athābravīd vānarendraḥ sugrīvaḥ putram aṅgadam
c nānimittam idaṃ manye bhavitavyaṃ bhayena tu
a viṣaṇṇavadanā hy ete tyaktapraharaṇā diśaḥ
c prapalāyanti harayas trāsād utphullalocanāḥ
a anyonyasya na lajjante na nirīkṣanti pṛṣṭhataḥ
c viprakarṣanti cānyonyaṃ patitaṃ laṅghayanti ca
a etasminn antare vīro gadāpāṇir vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c sugrīvaṃ vardhayām āsa rāghavaṃ ca niraikṣata
a vibhīṣaṇaṃ taṃ sugrīvo dṛṣṭvā vānarabhīṣaṇam
c ṛkṣarājaṃ samīpasthaṃ jāmbavantam uvāca ha
a vibhīṣaṇo 'yaṃ saṃprāpto yaṃ dṛṣṭvā vānararṣabhāḥ
c vidravanti paritrastā rāvaṇātmajaśaṅkayā
a śīghram etān suvitrastān bahudhā vipradhāvitān
c paryavasthāpayākhyāhi vibhīṣaṇam upasthitam
a sugrīveṇaivam uktas tu jāmbavān ṛkṣapārthivaḥ
c vānarān sāntvayām āsa saṃnivartya prahāvataḥ
a te nivṛttāḥ punaḥ sarve vānarās tyaktasaṃbhramāḥ
c ṛkṣarājavacaḥ śrutvā taṃ ca dṛṣṭvā vibhīṣaṇam
a vibhīṣaṇas tu rāmasya dṛṣṭvā gātraṃ śaraiś citam
c lakṣmaṇasya ca dharmātmā babhūva vyathitendriyaḥ
a jalaklinnena hastena tayor netre pramṛjya ca
c śokasaṃpīḍitamanā ruroda vilalāpa ca
a imau tau sattvasaṃpannau vikrāntau priyasaṃyugau
c imām avasthāṃ gamitau rākasaiḥ kūṭayodhibhiḥ
a bhrātuḥ putreṇa me tena duṣputreṇa durātmanā
c rākṣasyā jihmayā buddhyā chalitāv ṛjuvikramau
a śarair imāv alaṃ viddhau rudhireṇa samukṣitau
c vasudhāyām ima suptau dṛśyete śalyakāv iva
a yayor vīryam upāśritya pratiṣṭhā kāṅkṣitā mayā
c tāv ubhau dehanāśāya prasuptau puruṣarṣabhau
a jīvann adya vipanno 'smi naṣṭarājyamanorathaḥ
c prāptapratijñaś ca ripuḥ sakāmo rāvaṇaḥ kṛtaḥ
a evaṃ vilapamānaṃ taṃ pariṣvajya vibhīṣaṇam
c sugrīvaḥ sattvasaṃpanno harirājo 'bravīd idam
a rājyaṃ prāpsyasi dharmajña laṅkāyāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
c rāvaṇaḥ saha putreṇa sa rājyaṃ neha lapsyate
a śarasaṃpīḍitāv etāv ubhau rāghavalakṣmaṇau
c tyaktvā mohaṃ vadhiṣyete sagaṇaṃ rāvaṇaṃ raṇe
a tam evaṃ sāntvayitvā tu samāśvāsya ca rākṣasaṃ
c suṣeṇaṃ śvaśuraṃ pārśve sugrīvas tam uvāca ha
a saha śūrair harigaṇair labdhasaṃjñāv ariṃdamau
c gaccha tvaṃ bhrātarau gṛhya kiṣkindhāṃ rāmalakṣmaṇau
a ahaṃ tu rāvaṇaṃ hatvā saputraṃ sahabāndhavam
c maithilīm ānayiṣyāmi śakro naṣṭām iva śriyam
a śrutvaitad vānarendrasya suṣeṇo vākyam abravīt
c devāsuraṃ mahāyuddham anubhūtaṃ sudāruṇam
a tadā sma dānavā devāñ śarasaṃsparśakovidāḥ
c nijaghnuḥ śastraviduṣaś chādayanto muhur muhuḥ
a tān ārtān naṣṭasaṃjñāṃś ca parāsūṃś ca bṛhaspatiḥ
c vidhyābhir mantrayuktābhir oṣadhībhiś cikitsati
a tāny auṣadhāny ānayituṃ kṣīrodaṃ yāntu sāgaram
c javena vānarāḥ śīghraṃ saṃpāti panasādayaḥ
a harayas tu vijānanti pārvatī te mahauṣadhī
c saṃjīvakaraṇīṃ divyāṃ viśalyāṃ devanirmitām
a candraś ca nāma droṇaś ca parvatau sāgarottame
c amṛtaṃ yatra mathitaṃ tatra te paramauṣadhī
a te tatra nihite devaiḥ parvate paramauṣadhī
c ayaṃ vāyusuto rājan hanūmāṃs tatra gacchatu
a etasminn antare vāyur meghāṃś cāpi savidyutaḥ
c paryasyan sāgare toyaṃ kampayann iva parvatān
a mahatā pakṣavātena sarve dvīpamahādrumāḥ
c nipetur bhagnaviṭapāḥ samūlā lavaṇāmbhasi
a abhavan pannagās trastā bhoginas tatravāsinaḥ
c śīghraṃ sarvāṇi yādāṃsi jagmuś ca lavaṇārṇavam
a tato muhūrtad garuḍaṃ vainateyaṃ mahābalam
c vānarā dadṛśuḥ sarve jvalantam iva pāvakam
a tam āgatam abhiprekṣya nāgās te vipradudruvuḥ
c yais tau satpuruṣau baddhau śarabhūtair mahābalau
a tataḥ suparṇaḥ kākutsthau dṛṣṭvā pratyabhinandya ca
c vimamarśa ca pāṇibhyāṃ mukhe candrasamaprabhe
a vainateyena saṃspṛṣṭās tayoḥ saṃruruhur vraṇāḥ
c suvarṇe ca tanū snigdhe tayor āśu babhūvatuḥ
a tejo vīryaṃ balaṃ cauja utsāhaś ca mahāguṇāḥ
c pradarśanaṃ ca buddhiś ca smṛtiś ca dviguṇaṃ tayoḥ
a tāv utthāpya mahāvīryau garuḍo vāsavopamau
c ubhau tau sasvaje hṛṣṭau rāmaś cainam uvāca ha
a bhavatprasādād vyasanaṃ rāvaṇiprabhavaṃ mahat
c āvām iha vyatikrāntau śīghraṃ ca balinau kṛtau
a yathā tātaṃ daśarathaṃ yathājaṃ ca pitāmaham
c tathā bhavantam āsādya hṛṣayaṃ me prasīdati
a ko bhavān rūpasaṃpanno divyasraganulepanaḥ
c vasāno viraje vastre divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ
a tam uvāca mahātejā vainateyo mahābalaḥ
c patatrirājaḥ prītātmā harṣaparyākulekṣaṇaḥ
a ahaṃ sakhā te kākutstha priyaḥ prāṇo bahiścaraḥ
c garutmān iha saṃprāpto yuvayoḥ sāhyakāraṇāt
a asurā vā mahāvīryā dānavā vā mahābalāḥ
c surāś cāpi sagandharvāḥ puraskṛtya śatakratum
a nemaṃ mokṣayituṃ śaktāḥ śarabandhaṃ sudāruṇam
c māyā balād indrajitā nirmitaṃ krūrakarmaṇā
a ete nāgāḥ kādraveyās tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāviṣolbaṇāḥ
c rakṣomāyā prabhāvena śarā bhūtvā tvadāśritāḥ
a sabhāgyaś cāsi dharmajña rāma satyaparākrama
c lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā samare ripughātinā
a imaṃ śrutvā tu vṛttāntaṃ tvaramāṇo 'ham āgataḥ
c sahasā yuvayoḥ snehāt sakhitvam anupālayan
a mokṣitau ca mahāghorād asmāt sāyakabandhanāt
c apramādaś ca kartavyo yuvābhyāṃ nityam eva hi
a prakṛtyā rākṣasāḥ sarve saṃgrāme kūṭayodhinaḥ
c śūrāṇāṃ śuddhabhāvānāṃ bhavatām ārjavaṃ balam
a tan na viśvasitavyaṃ vo rākṣasānāṃ raṇājire
c etenaivopamānena nityajihmā hi rākṣasāḥ
a evam uktvā tato rāmaṃ suparṇaḥ sumahābalaḥ
c pariṣvajya suhṛtsnigdham āpraṣṭum upacakrame
a sakhe rāghava dharmajña ripūṇām api vatsala
c abhyanujñātum icchāmi gamiṣyāmi yathāgatam
a bālavṛddhāvaśeṣāṃ tu laṅkāṃ kṛtvā śarormibhiḥ
c rāvaṇaṃ ca ripuṃ hatvā sītāṃ samupalapsyase
a ity evam uktvā vacanaṃ suparṇaḥ śīghravikramaḥ
c rāmaṃ ca virujaṃ kṛtvā madhye teṣāṃ vanaukasām
a pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pariṣvajya ca vīryavān
c jagāmākāśam āviśya suparṇaḥ pavano yathā
a virujau rāghavau dṛṣṭvā tato vānarayūthapāḥ
c siṃhanādāṃs tadā nedur lāṅgūlaṃ dudhuvuś ca te
a tato bherīḥ samājaghnur mṛdaṅgāṃś ca vyanādayan
c dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān saṃprahṛṣṭāḥ kṣvelanty api yathāpuram
a āsphoṭyāsphoṭya vikrāntā vānarā nagayodhinaḥ
c drumān utpāṭya vividhāṃs tasthuḥ śatasahasraśaḥ
a visṛjanto mahānādāṃs trāsayanto niśācarān
c laṅkādvārāṇy upājagmur yoddhukāmāḥ plavaṃgamāḥ
a tatas tu bhīmas tumulo ninādo
babhūva śākhāmṛgayūthapānām
c kṣaye nidāghasya yathā ghanānāṃ
nādaḥ subhīmo nadatāṃ niśīthe
a teṣāṃ sutumulaṃ śabdaṃ vānarāṇāṃ tarasvinām
c nardatāṃ rākṣasaiḥ sārdhaṃ tadā śuśrāva rāvaṇaḥ
a snigdhagambhīranirghoṣaṃ śrutvā sa ninadaṃ bhṛśam
c sacivānāṃ tatas teṣāṃ madhye vacanam abravīt
a yathāsau saṃprahṛṣṭānāṃ vānarāṇāṃ samutthitaḥ
c bahūnāṃ sumahān nādo meghānām iva garjatām
a vyaktaṃ sumahatī prītir eteṣāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
c tathā hi vipulair nādaiś cukṣubhe varuṇālayaḥ
a tau tu baddhau śarais tīṣkṇair bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau
c ayaṃ ca sumahān nādaḥ śaṅkāṃ janayatīva me
a etat tu vacanaṃ coktvā mantriṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c uvāca nairṛtāṃs tatra samīpaparivartinaḥ
a jñāyatāṃ tūrṇam etaṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ vanacāriṇām
c śokakāle samutpanne harṣakāraṇam utthitam
a tathoktās tena saṃbhrāntāḥ prākāram adhiruhya te
c dadṛśuḥ pālitāṃ senāṃ sugrīveṇa mahātmanā
a tau ca muktau sughoreṇa śarabandhena rāghavau
c samutthitau mahābhāgau viṣeduḥ prekṣya rākṣasāḥ
a saṃtrastahṛdayā sarve prākārād avaruhya te
c viṣaṇṇavadanāḥ sarve rākṣasendram upasthitāḥ
a tad apriyaṃ dīnamukhā rāvaṇasya niśācarāḥ
c kṛtsnaṃ nivedayām āsur yathāvad vākyakovidāḥ
a yau tāv indrajitā yuddhe bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau
c nibaddhau śarabandhena niṣprakampabhujau kṛtau
a vimuktau śarabandhena tau dṛśyete raṇājire
c pāśān iva gajāu chittvā gajendrasamavikramau
a tac chrutvā vacanaṃ teṣāṃ rākṣasendro mahābalaḥ
c cintāśokasamākrānto viṣaṇṇavadano 'bravīt
a ghorair dattavarair baddhau śarair āśīviṣomapaiḥ
c amoghaiḥ sūryasaṃkāśaiḥ pramathyendrajitā yudhi
a tam astrabandham āsādya yadi muktau ripū mama
c saṃśayastham idaṃ sarvam anupaśyāmy ahaṃ balam
a niṣphalāḥ khalu saṃvṛttāḥ śarā vāsukitejasaḥ
c ādattaṃ yais tu saṃgrāme ripūṇāṃ mama jīvitam
a evam uktvā tu saṃkruddho niśvasann urago yathā
c abravīd rakṣasāṃ madhye dhūmrākṣaṃ nāma rākasaṃ
a balena mahatā yukto rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām
c tvaṃ vadhāyābhiniryāhi rāmasya saha vānaraiḥ
a evam uktas tu dhūmrākṣo rākṣasendreṇa dhīmatā
c kṛtvā praṇāmaṃ saṃhṛṣṭo nirjagāma nṛpālayāt
a abhiniṣkramya taddvāraṃ balādhyakṣam uvāca ha
c tvarayasva balaṃ tūrṇaṃ kiṃ cireṇa yuyutsataḥ
a dhūmrākṣasya vacaḥ śrutvā balādhyakṣo balānugaḥ
c balam udyojayām āsa rāvaṇasyājñayā drutam
a te baddhaghaṇṭā balino ghorarūpā niśācarāḥ
c vinardamānāḥ saṃhṛṣṭā dhūmrākṣaṃ paryavārayan
a vividhāyudhahastāś ca śūlamudgarapāṇayaḥ
c gadābhiḥ paṭṭasair daṇḍair āyasair musalair bhṛśam
a parighair bhiṇḍipālaiś ca bhallaiḥ prāsaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ
c niryayū rākṣasā ghorā nardanto jaladā yathā
a rathaiḥ kavacinas tv anye dhvajaiś ca samalaṃkṛtaiḥ
c suvarṇajālavihitaiḥ kharaiś ca vividhānanaiḥ
a hayaiḥ paramaśīghraiś ca gajendraiś ca madotkaṭaiḥ
c niryayū rākṣasavyāghrā vyāghrā iva durāsadāḥ
a vṛkasiṃhamukhair yuktaṃ kharaiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c āruroha rathaṃ divyaṃ dhūmrākṣaḥ kharanisvanaḥ
a sa niryāto mahāvīryo dhūmrākṣo rākṣasair vṛtaḥ
c prahasan paścimadvāraṃ hanūmān yatra yūthapaḥ
a prayāntaṃ tu mahāghoraṃ rākṣasaṃ bhīmadarśanam
c antarikṣagatāḥ krūrāḥ śakunāḥ pratyavārayan
a rathaśīrṣe mahābhīmo gṛdhraś ca nipapāta ha
c dhvajāgre grathitāś caiva nipetuḥ kuṇapāśanāḥ
a rudhirārdro mahāñ śvetaḥ kabandhaḥ patito bhuvi
c visvaraṃ cotsṛjan nādaṃ dhūmrākṣasya samīpataḥ
a vavarṣa rudhiraṃ devaḥ saṃcacāla ca medinī
c pratilomaṃ vavau vāyur nirghātasamanisvanaḥ
e timiraughāvṛtās tatra diśaś ca na cakāśire
a sa tūtpātāṃs tato dṛṣṭvā rākṣasānāṃ bhayāvahān
c prādurbhūtān sughorāṃś ca dhūmrākṣo vyathito 'bhavat
a tataḥ subhīmo bahubhir niśācarair
vṛto 'bhiniṣkramya raṇotsuko balī
c dadarśa tāṃ rāghavabāhupālitāṃ
samudrakalpāṃ bahuvānarīṃ camūm
a dhūmrākṣaṃ prekṣya niryāntaṃ rākṣasaṃ bhīmanisvanam
c vinedur vānarāḥ sarve prahṛṣṭā yuddhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
a teṣāṃ tu tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ saṃjajñe harirakṣasām
c anyonyaṃ pādapair ghorair nighnataṃ śūlamudgaraiḥ
a rākṣasair vānarā ghorā vinikṛttāḥ samantataḥ
c vānarai rākṣasāś cāpi drumair bhūmau samīkṛtāḥ
a rākṣasāś cāpi saṃkruddhā vānarān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c vivyadhur ghorasaṃkāśaiḥ kaṅkapatrair ajihmagaiḥ
a te gadābhiś ca bhīmābhiḥ paṭṭasaiḥ kūṭamudgaraiḥ
c ghoraiś ca parighaiś citrais triśūlaiś cāpi saṃśitaiḥ
a vidāryamāṇā rakṣobhir vānarās te mahābalāḥ
c amarṣāj janitoddharṣāś cakruḥ karmāṇy abhītavat
a śaranirbhinnagātrās te śūlanirbhinnadehinaḥ
c jagṛhus te drumāṃs tatra śilāś ca hariyūthapāḥ
a te bhīmavegā harayo nardamānās tatas tataḥ
c mamanthū rākṣasān bhīmān nāmāni ca babhāṣire
a tad babhūvādbhutaṃ ghoraṃ yuddhaṃ vānararakṣasām
c śilābhir vividhābhiś ca bahuśākhaiś ca pādapaiḥ
a rākṣasā mathitāḥ ke cid vānarair jitakāśibhiḥ
c vavarṣū rudhiraṃ ke cin mukhai rudhirabhojanāḥ
a pārśveṣu dāritāḥ ke cit ke cid rāśīkṛtā drumaiḥ
c śilābhiś cūrṇitāḥ ke cit ke cid dantair vidāritāḥ
a dhvajair vimathitair bhagnaiḥ kharaiś ca vinipātitaiḥ
c rathair vidhvaṃsitaiś cāpi patitai rajanīcaraiḥ
a vānarair bhīmavikrāntair āplutyāplutya vegitaiḥ
c rākṣasāḥ karajais tīkṣṇair mukheṣu vinikartitāḥ
a vivarṇavadanā bhūyo viprakīrṇaśiroruhāḥ
c mūḍhāḥ śoṇitagandhena nipetur dharaṇītale
a naye tu paramakruddhā rākṣasā bhīmavikramāḥ
c talair evābhidhāvanti vajrasparśasamair harīn
a vanarair āpatantas te vegitā vegavattaraiḥ
c muṣṭibhiś caraṇair dantaiḥ pādapaiś cāpapothitāḥ
a sanyaṃ tu vidrutaṃ dṛṣṭvā dhūmrākṣo rākṣasarṣabhaḥ
c krodhena kadanaṃ cakre vānarāṇāṃ yuyutsatām
a prāsaiḥ pramathitāḥ ke cid vānarāḥ śoṇitasravāḥ
c mudgarair āhatāḥ ke cit patitā dharaṇītale
a parighair mathitaḥ ke cid bhiṇḍipālair vidāritāḥ
c paṭṭasair āhatāḥ ke cid vihvalanto gatāsavaḥ
a ke cid vinihatā bhūmau rudhirārdrā vanaukasaḥ
c ke cid vidrāvitā naṣṭāḥ saṃkruddhai rākṣasair yudhi
a vibhinnahṛdayāḥ ke cid ekapārśvena śāyitāḥ
c vidāritāstraśūlai ca ke cid āntrair vinisrutāḥ
a tat subhīmaṃ mahad yuddhaṃ harirākasa saṃkulam
c prababhau śastrabahulaṃ śilāpādapasaṃkulam
a dhanurjyātantrimadhuraṃ hikkātālasamanvitam
c mandrastanitasaṃgītaṃ yuddhagāndharvam ābabhau
a dhūmrākṣas tu dhanuṣpāṇir vānarān raṇamūrdhani
c hasan vidrāvayām āsa diśas tāñ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
a dhūmrākṣeṇārditaṃ sainyaṃ vyathitaṃ dṛśya mārutiḥ
c abhyavartata saṃkruddhaḥ pragṛhya vipulāṃ śilām
a krodhād dviguṇatāmrākṣaḥ pitṛtulyaparākramaḥ
c śilāṃ tāṃ pātayām āsa dhūmrākṣasya rathaṃ prati
a āpatantīṃ śilāṃ dṛṣṭvā gadām udyamya saṃbhramāt
c rathād āplutya vegena vasudhāyāṃ vyatiṣṭhata
a sā pramathya rathaṃ tasya nipapāta śilābhuvi
c sacakrakūbaraṃ sāśvaṃ sadhvajaṃ saśarāsanam
a sa bhaṅktvā tu rathaṃ tasya hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
c rakṣasāṃ kadanaṃ cakre saskandhaviṭapair drumaiḥ
a vibhinnaśiraso bhūtvā rākṣasāḥ śoṇitokṣitāḥ
c drumaiḥ pramathitāś cānye nipetur dharaṇītale
a vidrāvya rākṣasaṃ sainyaṃ hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
c gireḥ śikharam ādāya dhūmrākṣam abhidudruve
a tam āpatantaṃ dhūmrākṣo gadām udyamya vīryavān
c vinardamānaḥ sahasā hanūmantam abhidravat
a tataḥ kruddhas tu vegena gadāṃ tāṃ bahukaṇṭakām
c pātayām āsa dhūmrākṣo mastake tu hanūmataḥ
a tāḍitaḥ sa tayā tatra gadayā bhīmarūpayā
c sa kapir mārutabalas taṃ prahāram acintayan
e dhūmrākṣasya śiro madhye giriśṛṅgam apātayat
a sa vihvalitasarvāṅgo giriśṛṅgeṇa tāḍitaḥ
c papāta sahasā bhūmau vikīrṇa iva parvataḥ
a dhūmrākṣaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā hataśeṣā niśācarāḥ
c trastāḥ praviviśur laṅkāṃ vadhyamānāḥ plavaṃgamaiḥ
a sa tu pavanasuto nihatya śatruṃ
kṣatajavahāḥ saritaś ca saṃvikīrya
c ripuvadhajanitaśramo mahātmā
mudam agamat kapibhiś ca pūjyamānaḥ
a dhūmrākṣaṃ nihataṃ śrutvā rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c balādhyakṣam uvācedaṃ kṛtāñjalim upasthitam
a śīghraṃ niryāntu durdharṣā rākṣasā bhīmavikramāḥ
c akampanaṃ puraskṛtya sarvaśastraprakovidam
a tato nānāpraharaṇā bhīmākṣā bhīmadarśanāḥ
c niṣpetū rākṣasā mukhyā balādhyakṣapracoditāḥ
a ratham āsthāya vipulaṃ taptakāñcanakuṇḍalaḥ
c rākasaiḥ saṃvṛto ghorais tadā niryāty akampanaḥ
a na hi kampayituṃ śakyaḥ surair api mahāmṛdhe
c akampanas tatas teṣām āditya iva tejasā
a tasya nidhāvamānasya saṃrabdhasya yuyutsayā
c akasmād dainyam āgacchad dhayānāṃ rathavāhinām
a vyasphuran nayanaṃ cāsya savyaṃ yuddhābhinandinaḥ
c vivarṇo mukhavarṇaś ca gadgadaś cābhavat svaraḥ
a abhavat sudine cāpi durdine rūkṣamārutam
c ūcuḥ khagā mṛgāḥ sarve vācaḥ krūrā bhayāvahāḥ
a sa siṃhopacitaskandhaḥ śārdūlasamavikramaḥ
c tān utpātān acintyaiva nirjagāma raṇājiram
a tadā nirgacchatas tasya rakṣasaḥ saha rākṣasaiḥ
c babhūva sumahān nādaḥ kṣobhayann iva sāgaram
a tena śabdena vitrastā vānarāṇāṃ mahācamūḥ
c drumaśailapraharaṇā yoddhuṃ samavatiṣṭhata
a teṣāṃ yuddhaṃ mahāraudraṃ saṃjajñe kapirakṣasām
c rāmarāvaṇayor arthe samabhityaktajīvinām
a sarve hy atibalāḥ śūrāḥ sarve parvatasaṃnibhāḥ
c harayo rākṣasāś caiva parasparajighaṃsavaḥ
a teṣāṃ vinardātāṃ śabdaḥ saṃyuge 'titarasvinām
c śuśruve sumahān krodhād anyonyam abhigarjatām
a rajaś cāruṇavarṇābhaṃ subhīmam abhavad bhṛśam
c uddhūtaṃ harirakṣobhiḥ saṃrurodha diśo daśa
a anyonyaṃ rajasā tena kauśeyoddhūtapāṇḍunā
c saṃvṛtāni ca bhūtāni dadṛśur na raṇājire
a na dhvajo na patākāvā varma vā turago 'pi vā
c āyudhaṃ syandanaṃ vāpi dadṛśe tena reṇunā
a śabdaś ca sumahāṃs teṣāṃ nardatām abhidhāvatām
c śrūyate tumule yuddhe na rūpāṇi cakāśire
a harīn eva susaṃkruddhā harayo jaghnur āhave
c rākṣasāś cāpi rakṣāṃsi nijaghnus timire tadā
a parāṃś caiva vinighnantaḥ svāṃś ca vānararākṣasāḥ
c rudhirārdraṃ tadā cakrur mahīṃ paṅkānulepanām
a tatas tu rudhiraugheṇa siktaṃ vyapagataṃ rajaḥ
c śarīraśavasaṃkīrṇā babhūva ca vasuṃdharā
a drumaśaktiśilāprāsair gadāparighatomaraiḥ
c harayo rākṣasās tūrṇaṃ jaghnur anyonyam ojasā
a bāhubhiḥ parighākārair yudhyantaḥ parvatopamāḥ
c harayo bhīmakarmāṇo rākṣasāñ jaghnur āhave
a rākṣasāś cāpi saṃkruddhāḥ prāsatomarapāṇayaḥ
c kapīn nijaghnire tatra śastraiḥ paramadāruṇaiḥ
a harayas tv api rakṣāṃsi mahādrumamahāśmabhiḥ
c vidārayanty abhikramya śastrāṇy ācchidya vīryataḥ
a etasminn antare vīrā harayaḥ kumudo nalaḥ
c maindaś ca paramakruddhaś cakrur vegam anuttamam
a te tu vṛkṣair mahāvegā rākṣasānāṃ camūmukhe
c kadanaṃ sumaha cakrur līlayā hariyūthapāḥ
a tad dṛṣṭvā sumahat karma kṛtaṃ vānarasattamaiḥ
c krodham āhārayām āsa yudhi tīvram akampanaḥ
a krodhamūrchitarūpas tu dhnuvan paramakārmukam
c dṛṣṭvā tu karma śatrūṇāṃ sārathiṃ vākyam abravīt
a tatraiva tāvat tvaritaṃ rathaṃ prāpaya sārathe
c ete 'tra bahavo ghnanti subahūn rākṣasān raṇe
a ete 'tra balavanto hi bhīmakāyāś ca vānarāḥ
c drumaśailapraharaṇās tiṣṭhanti pramukhe mama
a etān nihantum icchāmi samaraślāghino hy aham
c etaiḥ pramathitaṃ sarvaṃ dṛśyate rākṣasaṃ balam
a tataḥ prajavitāśvena rathena rathināṃ varaḥ
c harīn abhyahanat krodhāc charajālair akampanaḥ
a na sthātuṃ vānarāḥ śekuḥ kiṃ punar yoddhum āhave
c akampanaśarair bhagnāḥ sarva eva pradudruvuḥ
a tān mṛtyuvaśam āpannān akampanavaśaṃ gatān
c samīkṣya hanumāñ jñātīn upatasthe mahābalaḥ
a taṃ mahāplavagaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve plavagayūthapāḥ
c sametya samare vīrāḥ sahitāḥ paryavārayan
a vyavasthitaṃ hanūmantaṃ te dṛṣṭvā hariyūthapāḥ
c babhūvur balavanto hi balavantam upāśritāḥ
a akampanas tu śailābhaṃ hanūmantam avasthitam
c mahendra iva dhārābhiḥ śarair abhivavarṣa ha
a acintayitvā bāṇaughāñ śarīre patitāñ śitān
c akampanavadhārthāya mano dadhre mahābalaḥ
a sa prahasya mahātejā hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
c abhidudrāva tad rakṣaḥ kampayann iva medinīm
a tasyābhinardamānasya dīpyamānasya tejasā
c babhūva rūpaṃ durdharṣaṃ dīptasyeva vibhāvasoḥ
a ātmānaṃ tv apraharaṇaṃ jñātvā krodhasamanvitaḥ
c śailam utpāṭayām āsa vegena haripuṃgavaḥ
a taṃ gṛhītvā mahāśailaṃ pāṇinaikena mārutiḥ
c vinadya sumahānādaṃ bhrāmayām āsa vīryavān
a tatas tam abhidudrāva rākṣasendram akampanam
c yathā hi namuciṃ saṃkhye vajreṇeva puraṃdaraḥ
a akampanas tu tad dṛṣṭvā giriśṛṅgaṃ samudyatam
c dūrād eva mahābāṇair ardhacandrair vyadārayat
a tat parvatāgram ākāśe rakṣobāṇavidāritam
c vikīrṇaṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā hanūmān krodhamūrchitaḥ
a so 'śvakarṇaṃ samāsādya roṣadarpānvito hariḥ
c tūrṇam utpāṭayām āsa mahāgirim ivocchritam
a taṃ gṛhītvā mahāskandhaṃ so 'śvakarṇaṃ mahādyutiḥ
c prahasya parayā prītyā bhrāmayām āsa saṃyuge
a pradhāvann uruvegena prabhañjaṃs tarasā drumān
c hanūmān paramakruddhaś caraṇair dārayat kṣitim
a gajāṃś ca sagajārohān sarathān rathinas tathā
c jaghāna hanumān dhīmān rākṣasāṃś ca padātikān
a tam antakam iva kruddhaṃ samare prāṇahāriṇam
c hanūmantam abhiprekṣya rākṣasā vipradudruvuḥ
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃkruddhaṃ rākṣasānāṃ bhayāvaham
c dadarśākampano vīraś cukrodha ca nanāda ca
a sa caturdaśabhir bāṇaiḥ śitair dehavidāraṇaiḥ
c nirbibheda hanūmantaṃ mahāvīryam akampanaḥ
a sa tathā pratividdhas tu bahvībhiḥ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
c hanūmān dadṛśe vīraḥ prarūḍha iva sānumān
a tato 'nyaṃ vṛkṣam utpāṭya kṛtvā vegam anuttamam
c śirasy abhijaghānāśu rākṣasendram akampanam
a sa vṛkṣeṇa hatas tena sakrodhena mahātmanā
c rākṣaso vānarendreṇa papāta sa mamāra ca
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā nihataṃ bhūmau rākṣasendram akampanam
c vyathitā rākṣasāḥ sarve kṣitikampa iva drumāḥ
a tyaktapraharaṇāḥ sarve rākṣasās te parājitāḥ
c laṅkām abhiyayus trastā vānarais tair abhidrutāḥ
a te muktakeśāḥ saṃbhrāntā bhagnamānāḥ parājitāḥ
c sravacchramajalair aṅgaiḥ śvasanto vipradudruvuḥ
a anyonyaṃ pramamantus te viviśur nagaraṃ bhayāt
c pṛṣṭhatas te susaṃmūḍhāḥ prekṣamāṇā muhur muhuḥ
a teṣu laṅkāṃ praviṣṭeṣu rākṣaseṣu mahābalāḥ
c sametya harayaḥ sarve hanūmantam apūjayan
a so 'pi prahṛṣṭas tān sarvān harīn saṃpratyapūjayat
c hanūmān sattvasaṃpanno yathārham anukūlataḥ
a vineduś ca yathā prāṇaṃ harayo jitakāśinaḥ
c cakarṣuś ca punas tatra saprāṇān eva rākṣasān
a sa vīraśobhām abhajan mahākapiḥ
sametya rakṣāṃsi nihatya mārutiḥ
c mahāsuraṃ bhīmam amitranāśanaṃ
yathaiva viṣṇur balinaṃ camūmukhe
a apūjayan devagaṇās tadā kapiṃ
svayaṃ ca rāmo 'tibalaś ca lakṣmaṇaḥ
c tathaiva sugrīvamukhāḥ plavaṃgamā
vibhīṣaṇaś caiva mahābalas tadā
a akampanavadhaṃ śrutvā kruddho vai rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c kiṃ cid dīnamukhaś cāpi sacivāṃs tān udaikṣata
a sa tu dhyātvā muhūrtaṃ tu mantribhiḥ saṃvicārya ca
c purīṃ pariyayau laṅkāṃ sarvān gulmān avekṣitum
a tāṃ rākṣasagaṇair guptāṃ gulmair bahubhir āvṛtām
c dadarśa nagarīṃ laṅkāṃ patākādhvajamālinīm
a ruddhāṃ tu nagarīṃ dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c uvācāmarṣitaḥ kāle prahastaṃ yuddhakovidam
a purasyopaniviṣṭasya sahasā pīḍitasya ca
c nānyaṃ yuddhāt prapaśyāmi mokṣaṃ yuddhaviśārada
a ahaṃ vā kumbhakarṇo vā tvaṃ vā senāpatir mama
c indrajid vā nikumbho vā vaheyur bhāram īdṛśam
a sa tvaṃ balam itaḥ śīghram ādāya parigṛhya ca
c vijayāyābhiniryāhi yatra sarve vanaukasaḥ
a niryāṇād eva te nūnaṃ capalā harivāhinī
c nardatāṃ rākṣasendrāṇāṃ śrutvā nādaṃ draviṣyati
a capalā hy avinītāś ca calacittāś ca vānarāḥ
c na sahiṣyanti te nādaṃ siṃhanādam iva dvipāḥ
a vidrute ca bale tasmin rāmaḥ saumitriṇā saha
c avaśaste nirālambaḥ prahastavaśam eṣyati
a āpatsaṃśayitā śreyo nātra niḥsaṃśayīkṛtā
c pratilomānulomaṃ vā yad vā no manyase hitam
a rāvaṇenaivam uktas tu prahasto vāhinīpatiḥ
c rākṣasendram uvācedam asurendram ivośanā
a rājan mantritapūrvaṃ naḥ kuśalaiḥ saha mantribhiḥ
c vivādaś cāpi no vṛttaḥ samavekṣya parasparam
a pradānena tu sītāyāḥ śreyo vyavasitaṃ mayā
c apradāne punar yuddhaṃ dṛṣṭam etat tathaiva naḥ
a so 'haṃ dānaiś ca mānaiś ca satataṃ pūjitas tvayā
c sāntvaiś ca vividhaiḥ kāle kiṃ na kuryāṃ priyaṃ tava
a na hi me jīvitaṃ rakṣyaṃ putradāradhanāni vā
c tvaṃ paśya māṃ juhūṣantaṃ tvadarthe jīvitaṃ yudhi
a evam uktvā tu bhartāraṃ rāvaṇaṃ vāhinīpatiḥ
c samānayata me śīghraṃ rākṣasānāṃ mahad balam
a madbāṇāśanivegena hatānāṃ tu raṇājire
c adya tṛpyantu māṃsena pakṣiṇaḥ kānanaukasām
a ity uktās te prahastena balādhyakṣāḥ kṛtatvarāḥ
c balam udyojayām āsus tasmin rākṣasamandire
a sā babhūva muhūrtena tigmanānāvidhāyudhaiḥ
c laṅkā rākṣasavīrais tair gajair iva samākulā
a hutāśanaṃ tarpayatāṃ brāhmaṇāṃś ca namasyatām
c ājyagandhaprativahaḥ surabhir māruto vavau
a srajaś ca vividhākārā jagṛhus tv abhimantritāḥ
c saṃgrāmasajjāḥ saṃhṛṣṭā dhārayan rākṣasās tadā
a sadhanuṣkāḥ kavacino vegād āplutya rākṣasāḥ
c rāvaṇaṃ prekṣya rājānaṃ prahastaṃ paryavārayan
a athāmantrya ca rājānaṃ bherīm āhatya bhairavām
c āruroha rathaṃ divyaṃ prahastaḥ sajjakalpitam
a hayair mahājavair yuktaṃ samyak sūtasusaṃyutam
c mahājaladanirghoṣaṃ sākṣāc candrārkabhāsvaram
a uragadhvajadurdharṣaṃ suvarūthaṃ svapaskaram
c suvarṇajālasaṃyuktaṃ prahasantam iva śriyā
a tatas taṃ ratham āsthāya rāvaṇārpitaśāsanaḥ
c laṅkāyā niryayau tūrṇaṃ balena mahatā vṛtaḥ
a tato duṃdubhinirghoṣaḥ parjanyaninadopamaḥ
c śuśruve śaṅkhaśabdaś ca prayāte vāhinīpatau
a ninadantaḥ svarān ghorān rākṣasā jagmur agrataḥ
c bhīmarūpā mahākāyāḥ prahastasya puraḥsarāḥ
a vyūḍhenaiva sughoreṇa pūrvadvārāt sa niryayau
c gajayūthanikāśena balena mahatā vṛtaḥ
a sāgarapratimaughena vṛtas tena balena saḥ
c prahasto niryayau tūrṇaṃ kruddhaḥ kālāntakopamaḥ
a tasya niryāṇa ghoṣeṇa rākṣasānāṃ ca nardatām
c laṅkāyāṃ sarvabhūtāni vinedur vikṛtaiḥ svaraiḥ
a vyabhram ākāśam āviśya māṃsaśoṇitabhojanāḥ
c maṇḍalāny apasavyāni khagāś cakrū rathaṃ prati
a vamantyaḥ pāvakajvālāḥ śivā ghorā vavāśire
a antarikṣāt papātolkā vāyuś ca paruṣo vavau
c anyonyam abhisaṃrabdhā grahāś ca na cakāśire
a vavarṣū rudhiraṃ cāsya siṣicuś ca puraḥsarān
c ketumūrdhani gṛdhro 'sya vilīno dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ
a sārather bahuśaś cāsya saṃgrāmam avagāhataḥ
c pratodo nyapatad dhastāt sūtasya hayasādinaḥ
a niryāṇa śrīś ca yāsyāsīd bhāsvarā ca sudurlabhā
c sā nanāśa muhūrtena same ca skhalitā hayāḥ
a prahastaṃ tv abhiniryāntaṃ prakhyāta balapauruṣam
c yudhi nānāpraharaṇā kapisenābhyavartata
a atha ghoṣaḥ sutumulo harīṇāṃ samajāyata
c vṛkṣān ārujatāṃ caiva gurvīś cāgṛhṇatāṃ śilāḥ
a ubhe pramudite sainye rakṣogaṇavanaukasām
c vegitānāṃ samarthānām anyonyavadhakāṅkṣiṇām
e parasparaṃ cāhvayatāṃ ninādaḥ śrūyate mahān
a tataḥ prahastaḥ kapirājavāhinīm
abhipratasthe vijayāya durmatiḥ
c vivṛddhavegāṃ ca viveśa tāṃ camūṃ
yathā mumūrṣuḥ śalabho vibhāvasum
a tataḥ prahastaṃ niryāntaṃ bhīmaṃ bhīmaparākramam
c garjantaṃ sumahākāyaṃ rākṣasair abhisaṃvṛtam
a dadarśa mahatī senā vānarāṇāṃ balīyasām
c atisaṃjātaroṣāṇāṃ prahastam abhigarjatām
a khaḍgaśaktyaṣṭibāṇāś ca śūlāni musalāni ca
c gadāś ca parighāḥ prāsā vividhāś ca paraśvadhāḥ
a dhanūṃṣi ca vicitrāṇi rākṣasānāṃ jayaiṣiṇām
c pragṛhītāny aśobhanta vānarān abhidhāvatām
a jagṛhuḥ pādapāṃś cāpi puṣpitān vānararṣabhāḥ
c śilāś ca vipulā dīrghā yoddhukāmāḥ plavaṃgamāḥ
a teṣām anyonyam āsādya saṃgrāmaḥ sumahān abhūt
c bahūnām aśmavṛṣṭiṃ ca śaravṛṣṭiṃ ca varṣatām
a bahavo rākṣasā yuddhe bahūn vānarayūthapān
c vānarā rākṣasāṃś cāpi nijaghnur bahavo bahūn
a śūlaiḥ pramathitāḥ ke cit ke cit tu paramāyudhaiḥ
c parighair āhatāḥ ke cit ke cic chinnāḥ paraśvadhaiḥ
a nirucchvāsāḥ punaḥ ke cit patitā dharaṇītale
c vibhinnahṛdayāḥ ke cid iṣusaṃtānasaṃditāḥ
a ke cid dvidhākṛtāḥ khaḍgaiḥ sphurantaḥ patitā bhuvi
c vānarā rākṣasaiḥ śūlaiḥ pārśvataś ca vidāritāḥ
a vānaraiś cāpi saṃkruddhai rākṣasaughāḥ samantataḥ
c pādapair giriśṛṅgaiś ca saṃpiṣṭā vasudhātale
a vajrasparśatalair hastair muṣṭibhiś ca hatā bhṛśam
c vemuḥ śoṇitam āsyebhyo viśīrṇadaśanekṣaṇaḥ
a ārtasvaraṃ ca svanatāṃ siṃhanādaṃ ca nardatām
c babhūva tumulaḥ śabdo harīṇāṃ rakṣasāṃ yudhi
a vānarā rākṣasāḥ kruddhā vīramārgam anuvratāḥ
c vivṛttanayanāḥ krūrāś cakruḥ karmāṇy abhītavat
a narāntakaḥ kumbhahanur mahānādaḥ samunnataḥ
c ete prahastasacivāḥ sarve jaghnur vanaukasaḥ
a teṣām āpatatāṃ śīghraṃ nighnatāṃ cāpi vānarān
c dvivido giriśṛṅgeṇa jaghānaikaṃ narāntakam
a durmukhaḥ punar utpāṭya kapiḥ sa vipuladrumam
c rākṣasaṃ kṣiprahastas tu samunnatam apothayat
a jāmbavāṃs tu susaṃkruddhaḥ pragṛhya mahatīṃ śilām
c pātayām āsa tejasvī mahānādasya vakṣasi
a atha kumbhahanus tatra tāreṇāsādya vīryavān
c vṛkṣeṇābhihato mūrdhni prāṇāṃs tatyāja rākṣasaḥ
a amṛṣyamāṇas tat karma prahasto ratham āsthitaḥ
c cakāra kadanaṃ ghoraṃ dhanuṣpāṇir vanaukasām
a āvarta iva saṃjajñe ubhayoḥ senayos tadā
c kṣubhitasyāprameyasya sāgarasyeva nisvanaḥ
a mahatā hi śaraugheṇa prahasto yuddhakovidaḥ
c ardayām āsa saṃkruddho vānarān paramāhave
a vānarāṇāṃ śarīrais tu rākṣasānāṃ ca medinī
c babhūva nicitā ghorā patitair iva parvataiḥ
a sā mahīrudhiraugheṇa pracchannā saṃprakāśate
c saṃchannā mādhave māsi palāśair iva puṣpitaiḥ
a hatavīraughavaprāṃ tu bhagnāyudhamahādrumām
c śoṇitaughamahātoyāṃ yamasāgaragāminīm
a yakṛtplīhamahāpaṅkāṃ vinikīrṇāntraśaivalām
c bhinnakāyaśiromīnām aṅgāvayavaśāḍvalām
a gṛdhrahaṃsagaṇākīrṇāṃ kaṅkasārasasevitām
c medhaḥphenasamākīrṇām ārtastanitanisvanām
a tāṃ kāpuruṣadustārāṃ yuddhabhūmimayīṃ nadīm
c nadīm iva ghanāpāye haṃsasārasasevitām
a rākṣasāḥ kapimukhyāś ca terus tāṃ dustarāṃ nadīm
c yathā padmarajodhvastāṃ nalinīṃ gajayūthapāḥ
a tataḥ sṛjantaṃ bāṇaughān prahastaṃ syandane sthitam
c dadarśa tarasā nīlo vinighnantaṃ plavaṃgamān
a sa taṃ paramadurdharṣam āpatantaṃ mahākapiḥ
c prahastaṃ tāḍayām āsa vṛkṣam utpāṭya vīryavān
a sa tenābhihataḥ kruddho nadan rākṣasapuṃgavaḥ
c vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi plavagānāṃ camūpatau
a apārayan vārayituṃ pratyagṛhṇān nimīlitaḥ
c yathaiva govṛṣo varṣaṃ śāradaṃ śīghram āgatam
a evam eva prahastasya śaravarṣaṃ durāsadam
c nimīlitākṣaḥ sahasā nīlaḥ sehe sudāruṇam
a roṣitaḥ śaravarṣeṇa sālena mahatā mahān
c prajaghāna hayān nīlaḥ prahastasya manojavān
a vidhanus tu kṛtas tena prahasto vāhinīpatiḥ
c pragṛhya musalaṃ ghoraṃ syandanād avapupluve
a tāv ubhau vāhinīmukhyau jātaroṣau tarasvinau
c sthitau kṣatajadigdhāṅgau prabhinnāv iva kuñjarau
a ullikhantau sutīkṣṇābhir daṃṣṭrābhir itaretaram
c siṃhaśārdūlasadṛśau siṃhaśārdūlaceṣṭitau
a vikrāntavijayau vīrau samareṣv anivartinau
c kāṅkṣamāṇau yaśaḥ prāptuṃ vṛtravāsavayoḥ samau
a ājaghāna tadā nīlaṃ lalāṭe musalena saḥ
c prahastaḥ paramāyastas tasya susrāva śoṇitam
a tataḥ śoṇitadigdhāṅgaḥ pragṛhya sumahātarum
c prahastasyorasi kruddho visasarja mahākapiḥ
a tam acintyaprahāraṃ sa pragṛhya musalaṃ mahat
c abhidudrāva balinaṃ balī nīlaṃ plavaṃgamam
a tam ugravegaṃ saṃrabdham āpatantaṃ mahākapiḥ
c tataḥ saṃprekṣya jagrāha mahāvego mahāśilām
a tasya yuddhābhikāmasya mṛdhe musalayodhinaḥ
c prahastasya śilāṃ nīlo mūrdhni tūrṇam apātayat
a sā tena kapimukhyena vimuktā mahatī śilā
c bibheda bahudhā ghorā prahastasya śiras tadā
a sa gatāsur gataśrīko gatasattvo gatendriyaḥ
c papāta sahasā bhūmau chinnamūla iva drumaḥ
a vibhinnaśirasas tasya bahu susrāvaśoṇitam
c śarīrād api susrāva gireḥ prasravaṇaṃ yathā
a hate prahaste nīlena tad akampyaṃ mahad balam
c rakṣasām aprahṛṣṭānāṃ laṅkām abhijagāma ha
a na śekuḥ samavasthātuṃ nihate vāhinīpatau
c setubandhaṃ samāsādya viśīrṇaṃ salilaṃ yathā
a hate tasmiṃś camūmukhye rākṣasas te nirudyamāḥ
c rakṣaḥpatigṛhaṃ gatvā dhyānamūkatvam āgatāḥ
a tatas tu nīlo vijayī mahābalaḥ
praśasyamānaḥ svakṛtena karmaṇā
c sametya rāmeṇa salakṣmaṇena
prahṛṣṭarūpas tu babhūva yūthapaḥ
a tasmin hate rākṣasasainyapāle
plavaṃgamānām ṛṣabheṇa yuddhe
c bhīmāyudhaṃ sāgaratulyavegaṃ
pradudruve rākṣasarājasainyam
a gatvā tu rakṣo'dhipateḥ śaśaṃsuḥ
senāpatiṃ pāvakasūnuśastam
c tac cāpi teṣāṃ vacanaṃ niśamya
rakṣo'dhipaḥ krodhavaśaṃ jagāma
a saṃkhye prahastaṃ nihataṃ niśamya
śokārditaḥ krodhaparītacetāḥ
c uvāca tān nairṛtayodhamukhyān
indro yathā cāmarayodhamukhyān
a nāvajñā ripave kāryā yair indrabalasūdanaḥ
c sūditaḥ sainyapālo me sānuyātraḥ sakuñjaraḥ
a so 'haṃ ripuvināśāya vijayāyāvicārayan
c svayam eva gamiṣyāmi raṇaśīrṣaṃ tad adbhutam
a adya tad vānarānīkaṃ rāmaṃ ca sahalakṣmaṇam
c nirdahiṣyāmi bāṇaughair vanaṃ dīptair ivāgnibhiḥ
a sa evam uktvā jvalanaprakāśaṃ
rathaṃ turaṃgottamarājiyuktam
c prakāśamānaṃ vapuṣā jvalantaṃ
samārurohāmararājaśatruḥ
a sa śaṅkhabherīpaṭaha praṇādair
āsphoṭitakṣveḍitasiṃhanādaiḥ
c puṇyaiḥ stavaiś cāpy abhipūjyamānas
tadā yayau rākṣasarājamukhyaḥ
a sa śailajīmūtanikāśa rūpair
māṃsāśanaiḥ pāvakadīptanetraiḥ
c babhau vṛto rākṣasarājamukhyair
bhūtair vṛto rudra ivāmareśaḥ
a tato nagaryāḥ sahasā mahaujā
niṣkramya tad vānarasainyam ugram
c mahārṇavābhrastanitaṃ dadarśa
samudyataṃ pādapaśailahastam
a tad rākṣasānīkam atipracaṇḍam
ālokya rāmo bhujagendrabāhuḥ
c vibhīṣaṇaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭham
uvāca senānugataḥ pṛthuśrīḥ
a nānāpatākādhvajaśastrajuṣṭaṃ
prāsāsiśūlāyudhacakrajuṣṭam
c sainyaṃ nagendropamanāgajuṣṭaṃ
kasyedam akṣobhyam abhīrujuṣṭam
a tatas tu rāmasya niśamya vākyaṃ
vibhīṣaṇaḥ śakrasamānavīryaḥ
c śaśaṃsa rāmasya balapravekaṃ
mahātmanāṃ rākṣasapuṃgavānām
a yo 'sau gajaskandhagato mahātmā
navoditārkopamatāmravaktraḥ
c prakampayan nāgaśiro 'bhyupaiti hy
akampanaṃ tv enam avehi rājan
a yo 'sau rathastho mṛgarājaketur
dhūnvan dhanuḥ śakradhanuḥprakāśam
c karīva bhāty ugravivṛttadaṃṣṭraḥ
sa indrajin nāma varapradhānaḥ
a yaś caiṣa vindhyāstamahendrakalpo
dhanvī rathastho 'tiratho 'tivīryaḥ
c visphārayaṃś cāpam atulyamānaṃ
nāmnātikāyo 'tivivṛddhakāyaḥ
a yo 'sau navārkoditatāmracakṣur
āruhya ghaṇṭāninadapraṇādam
c gajaṃ kharaṃ garjati vai mahātmā
mahodaro nāma sa eṣa vīraḥ
a yo 'sau hayaṃ kāñcanacitrabhāṇḍam
āruhya saṃdhyābhragiriprakāśam
c prāsaṃ samudyamya marīcinaddhaṃ
piśāca eṣāśanitulyavegaḥ
a yaś caiṣa śūlaṃ niśitaṃ pragṛhya
vidyutprabhaṃ kiṃkaravajravegam
c vṛṣendram āsthāya giriprakāśam
āyāti so 'sau triśirā yaśasvī
a asau ca jīmūtanikāśa rūpaḥ
kumbhaḥ pṛthuvyūḍhasujātavakṣāḥ
c samāhitaḥ pannagarājaketur
visphārayan bhāti dhanur vidhūnvan
a yaś caiṣa jāmbūnadavajrajuṣṭaṃ
dīptaṃ sadhūmaṃ parighaṃ pragṛhya
c āyāti rakṣobalaketubhūtaḥ
so 'sau nikumbho 'dbhutaghorakarmā
a yaś caiṣa cāpāsiśaraughajuṣṭaṃ
patākinaṃ pāvakadīptarūpam
c rathaṃ samāsthāya vibhāty udagro
narāntako 'sau nagaśṛṅgayodhī
a yaś caiṣa nānāvidhaghorarūpair
vyāghroṣṭranāgendramṛgendravaktraiḥ
c bhūtair vṛto bhāti vivṛttanetraiḥ
so 'sau surāṇām api darpahantā
a yatraitad indupratimaṃ vibhātic
chattraṃ sitaṃ sūkṣmaśalākam agryam
c atraiṣa rakṣo'dhipatir mahātmā
bhūtair vṛto rudra ivāvabhāti
a asau kirīṭī calakuṇḍalāsyo
nāgendravindhyopamabhīmakāyaḥ
c mahendravaivasvatadarpahantā
rakṣo'dhipaḥ sūrya ivāvabhāti
a pratyuvāca tato rāmo vibhīṣaṇam ariṃdamam
c aho dīpto mahātejā rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ
a āditya iva duṣprekṣyo raśmibhir bhāti rāvaṇaḥ
c suvyaktaṃ lakṣaye hy asya rūpaṃ tejaḥsamāvṛtam
a devadānavavīrāṇāṃ vapur naivaṃvidhaṃ bhavet
c yādṛśaṃ rākṣasendrasya vapur etat prakāśate
a sarve parvatasaṃkāśāḥ sarve parvatayodhinaḥ
c sarve dīptāyudhadharā yodhaś cāsya mahaujasaḥ
a bhāti rākṣasarājo 'sau pradīptair bhīmavikramaiḥ
c bhūtaiḥ parivṛtas tīkṣṇair dehavadbhir ivāntakaḥ
a evam uktvā tato rāmo dhanur ādāya vīryavān
c lakṣmaṇānucaras tasthau samuddhṛtya śarottamam
a tataḥ sa rakṣo'dhipatir mahātmā
rakṣāṃsi tāny āha mahābalāni
c dvāreṣu caryāgṛhagopureṣu
sunirvṛtās tiṣṭhata nirviśaṅkāḥ
a visarjayitvā sahasā tatas tān
gateṣu rakṣaḥsu yathāniyogam
c vyadārayad vānarasāgaraughaṃ
mahājhaṣaḥ pūrmam ivārṇavaugham
a tam āpatantaṃ sahasā samīkṣya
dīpteṣucāpaṃ yudhi rākṣasendram
c mahat samutpāṭya mahīdharāgraṃ
dudrāva rakṣo'dhipatiṃ harīśaḥ
a tac chailaśṛṅgaṃ bahuvṛkṣasānuṃ
pragṛhya cikṣepa niśācarāya
c tam āpatantaṃ sahasā samīkṣya
bibheda bāṇais tapanīyapuṅkhaiḥ
a tasmin pravṛddhottamasānuvṛkṣe
śṛṅge vikīrṇe patite pṛthivyām
c mahāhikalpaṃ śaram antakābhaṃ
samādade rākṣasalokanāthaḥ
a sa taṃ gṛhītvānilatulyavegaṃ
savisphuliṅgajvalanaprakāśam
c bāṇaṃ mahendrāśanitulyavegaṃ
cikṣepa sugrīvavadhāya ruṣṭaḥ
a sa sāyako rāvaṇabāhumuktaḥ
śakrāśaniprakhyavapuḥ śitāgraḥ
c sugrīvam āsādya bibheda vegād
guheritā kraucam ivograśaktiḥ
a sa sāyakārto viparītacetāḥ
kūjan pṛthivyāṃ nipapāta vīraḥ
c taṃ prekṣya bhūmau patitaṃ visaṃjmaṃ
neduḥ prahṛṣṭā yudhi yātudhānāḥ
a tato gavākṣo gavayaḥ sudaṃṣṭras
tatharṣabho jyotimukho nalaś ca
c śailān samudyamya vivṛddhakāyāḥ
pradudruvus taṃ prati rākṣasendram
a teṣāṃ prahārān sa cakāra meghān
rakṣo'dhipo bāṇagaṇaiḥ śitāgraiḥ
c tān vānarendrān api bāṇajālair
bibheda jāmbūnadacitrapuṅkhaiḥ
a te vānarendrās tridaśāribāṇair
bhinnā nipetur bhuvi bhīmarūpāḥ
c tatas tu tad vānarasainyam ugraṃ
pracchādayām āsa sa bāṇajālaiḥ
a te vadhyamānāḥ patitāgryavīrā
nānadyamānā bhayaśalyaviddhāḥ
c śākhāmṛgā rāvaṇasāyakārtā
jagmuḥ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ sma rāmam
a tato mahātmā sa dhanur dhanuṣmān
ādāya rāmaḥ saharā jagāma
c taṃ lakṣmaṇaḥ prāñjalir abhyupetya
uvāca vākyaṃ paramārthayuktam
a kāmam āryaḥ suparyāpto vadhāyāsya durātmanaḥ
c vidhamiṣyāmy ahaṃ nīcam anujānīhi māṃ vibho
a tam abravīn mahātejā rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
c gaccha yatnaparaś cāpi bhava lakṣmaṇa saṃyuge
a rāvaṇo hi mahāvīryo raṇe 'dbhutaparākramaḥ
c trailokyenāpi saṃkruddho duṣprasahyo na saṃśayaḥ
a tasya cchidrāṇi mārgasva svacchidrāṇi ca gopaya
c cakṣuṣā dhanuṣā yatnād rakṣātmānaṃ samāhitaḥ
a rāghavasya vacaḥ śrutvā saṃpariṣvajya pūjya ca
c abhivādya tato rāmaṃ yayau saumitrir āhavam
a sa rāvaṇaṃ vāraṇahastabāhur
dadarśa dīptodyatabhīmacāpam
c pracchādayantaṃ śaravṛṣṭijālais
tān vānarān bhinnavikīrṇadehān
a tam ālokya mahātejā hanūmān mārutātmajā
c nivārya śarajālāni pradudrāva sa rāvaṇam
a rathaṃ tasya samāsādya bhujam udyamya dakṣiṇam
c trāsayan rāvaṇaṃ dhīmān hanūmān vākyam abravīt
a devadānavagandharvā yakṣāś ca saha rākṣasaiḥ
c avadhyatvāt tvayā bhagnā vānarebhyas tu te bhayam
a eṣa me dakṣiṇo bāhuḥ pañcaśākhaḥ samudyataḥ
c vidhamiṣyati te dehād bhūtātmānaṃ ciroṣitam
a śrutvā hanūmato vākyaṃ rāvaṇo bhīmavikramaḥ
c saṃraktanayanaḥ krodhād idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a kṣipraṃ prahara niḥśaṅkaṃ sthirāṃ kīrtim avāpnuhi
c tatas tvāṃ jñātivikrāntaṃ nāśayiṣyāmi vānara
a rāvaṇasya vacaḥ śrutvā vāyusūnur vaco 'bravīt
c prahṛtaṃ hi mayā pūrvam akṣaṃ smara sutaṃ tava
a evam ukto mahātejā rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c ājaghānānilasutaṃ talenorasi vīryavān
a sa talābhihatas tena cacāla ca muhur muhuḥ
c ājaghānābhisaṃkruddhas talenaivāmaradviṣam
a tatas talenābhihato vānareṇa mahātmanā
c daśagrīvaḥ samādhūto yathā bhūmicale 'calaḥ
a saṃgrāme taṃ tathā dṛṣṭva rāvaṇaṃ talatāḍitam
c ṛṣayo vānarāḥ siddhā nedur devāḥ sahāsurāḥ
a athāśvasya mahātejā rāvaṇo vākyam abravīt
c sādhu vānaravīryeṇa ślāghanīyo 'si me ripuḥ
a rāvaṇenaivam uktas tu mārutir vākyam abravīt
c dhig astu mama vīryaṃ tu yat tvaṃ jīvasi rāvaṇa
a sakṛt tu praharedānīṃ durbuddhe kiṃ vikatthase
c tatas tvāṃ māmako muṣṭir nayiṣyāmi yathākṣayam
e tato mārutivākyena krodhas tasya tadājvalat
a saṃraktanayano yatnān muṣṭim udyamya dakṣiṇam
c pātayām āsa vegena vānarorasi vīryavān
e hanūmān vakṣasi vyūdhe saṃcacāla hataḥ punaḥ
a vihvalaṃ taṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā hanūmantaṃ mahābalam
c rathenātirathaḥ śīghraṃ nīlaṃ prati samabhyagāt
a pannagapratimair bhīmaiḥ paramarmātibhedibhiḥ
c śarair ādīpayām āsa nīlaṃ haricamūpatim
a sa śaraughasamāyasto nīlaḥ kapicamūpatiḥ
c kareṇaikena śailāgraṃ rakṣo'dhipataye 'sṛjat
a hanūmān api tejasvī samāśvasto mahāmanāḥ
c viprekṣamāṇo yuddhepsuḥ saroṣam idam abravīt
a nīlena saha saṃyuktaṃ rāvaṇaṃ rākṣaseśvaram
c anyena yudhyamānasya na yuktam abhidhāvanam
a rāvaṇo 'pi mahātejās tac chṛṅgaṃ saptabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c ājaghāna sutīkṣṇāgrais tad vikīrṇaṃ papāta ha
a tad vikīrṇaṃ gireḥ śṛṅgaṃ dṛṣṭvā haricamūpatiḥ
c kālāgnir iva jajvāla krodhena paravīrahā
a so 'śvakarṇān dhavān sālāṃś cūtāṃś cāpi supuṣpitān
c anyāṃś ca vividhān vṛkṣān nīlaś cikṣepa saṃyuge
a sa tān vṛkṣān samāsādya praticiccheda rāvaṇaḥ
c abhyavarṣat sughoreṇa śaravarṣeṇa pāvakim
a abhivṛṣṭaḥ śaraugheṇa megheneva mahācalaḥ
c hrasvaṃ kṛtvā tadā rūpaṃ dhvajāgre nipapāta ha
a pāvakātmajam ālokya dhvajāgre samavasthitam
c jajvāla rāvaṇaḥ krodhāt tato nīlo nanāda ha
a dhvajāgre dhanuṣaś cāgre kirīṭāgre ca taṃ harim
c lakṣmaṇo 'tha hanūmāṃś ca dṛṣṭvā rāmaś ca vismitāḥ
a rāvaṇo 'pi mahātejāḥ kapilāghavavismitaḥ
c astram āhārayām āsa dīptam āgneyam adbhutam
a tatas te cukruśur hṛṣṭā labdhalakṣyāḥ plavaṃgamāḥ
c nīlalāghavasaṃbhrāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇam āhave
a vānarāṇāṃ ca nādena saṃrabdho rāvaṇas tadā
c saṃbhramāviṣṭahṛdayo na kiṃ cit pratyapadyata
a āgneyenātha saṃyuktaṃ gṛhītvā rāvaṇaḥ śaram
c dhvajaśīrṣasthitaṃ nīlam udaikṣata niśācaraḥ
a tato 'bravīn mahātejā rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c kape lāghavayukto 'si māyayā parayānayā
a jīvitaṃ khalu rakṣasva yadi śaknoṣi vānara
c tāni tāny ātmarūpāṇi sṛjase tvam anekaśaḥ
a tathāpi tvāṃ mayā muktaḥ sāyako 'straprayojitaḥ
c jīvitaṃ parirakṣantaṃ jīvitād bhraṃśayiṣyati
a evam uktvā mahābāhū rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c saṃdhāya bāṇam astreṇa camūpatim atāḍayat
a so 'strayuktena bāṇena nīlo vakṣasi tāḍitaḥ
c nirdahyamānaḥ sahasā nipapāta mahītale
a pitṛmāhātmya saṃyogād ātmanaś cāpi tejasā
c jānubhyām apatad bhūmau na ca prāṇair vyayujyata
a visaṃjñaṃ vānaraṃ dṛṣṭvā daśagrīvo raṇotsukaḥ
c rathenāmbudanādena saumitrim abhidudruve
a tam āha saumitrir adīnasattvo
visphārayantaṃ dhanur aprameyam
c anvehi mām eva niśācarendra
na vānarāṃs tvaṃ prati yoddhum arhasi
a sa tasya vākyaṃ paripūrṇaghoṣaṃ
jyāśabdam ugraṃ ca niśamya rājā
c āsādya saumitrim avasthitaṃ taṃ
kopānvitaṃ vākyam uvāca rakṣaḥ
a diṣṭyāsi me rāghava dṛṣṭimārgaṃ
prāpto 'ntagāmī viparītabuddhiḥ
c asmin kṣaṇe yāsyasi mṛtyudeśaṃ
saṃsādyamāno mama bāṇajālaiḥ
a tam āha saumitrir avismayāno
garjantam udvṛttasitāgradaṃṣṭram
c rājan na garjanti mahāprabhāvā
vikatthase pāpakṛtāṃ variṣṭha
a jānāmi vīryaṃ tava rākṣasendra
balaṃ pratāpaṃ ca parākramaṃ ca
c avasthito 'haṃ śaracāpapāṇir
āgaccha kiṃ moghavikatthanena
a sa evam uktaḥ kupitaḥ sasarja
rakṣo'dhipaḥ saptaśarān supuṅkhān
c tāṃl lakṣmaṇaḥ kāñcanacitrapuṅkhaiś
ciccheda bāṇair niśitāgradhāraiḥ
a tān prekṣamāṇaḥ sahasā nikṛttān
nikṛttabhogān iva pannagendrān
c laṅkeśvaraḥ krodhavaśaṃ jagāma
sasarja cānyān niśitān pṛṣatkān
a sa bāṇavarṣaṃ tu vavarṣa tīvraṃ
rāmānujaḥ kārmukasaṃprayuktam
c kṣurārdhacandrottamakarṇibhallaiḥ
śarāṃś ca ciccheda na cukṣubhe ca
a sa lakṣmaṇaś cāśu śarāñ śitāgrān
mahendravajrāśanitulyavegān
c saṃdhāya cāpe jvalanaprakāśān
sasarja rakṣo'dhipater vadhāya
a sa tān praciccheda hi rākṣasendraś
chittvā ca tāṃl lakṣmaṇam ājaghāna
c śareṇa kālāgnisamaprabheṇa
svayambhudattena lalāṭadeśe
a sa lakṣmaṇo rāvaṇasāyakārtaś
cacāla cāpaṃ śithilaṃ pragṛhya
c punaś ca saṃjñāṃ pratilabhya kṛcchrāc
ciccheda cāpaṃ tridaśendraśatroḥ
a nikṛttacāpaṃ tribhir ājaghāna
bāṇais tadā dāśarathiḥ śitāgraiḥ
c sa sāyakārto vicacāla rājā
kṛcchrāc ca saṃjñāṃ punar āsasāda
a sa kṛttacāpaḥ śaratāḍitaś ca
svedārdragātro rudhirāvasiktaḥ
c jagrāha śaktiṃ samudagraśaktiḥ
svayambhudattāṃ yudhi devaśatruḥ
a sa tāṃ vidhūmānalasaṃnikāśāṃ
vitrāsanīṃ vānaravāhinīnām
c cikṣepa śaktiṃ tarasā jvalantīṃ
saumitraye rākṣasarāṣṭranāthaḥ
a tām āpatantīṃ bharatānujo 'strair
jaghāna bāṇaiś ca hutāgnikalpaiḥ
c tathāpi sā tasya viveśa śaktir
bhujāntaraṃ dāśarather viśālam
a śaktyā brāmyā tu saumitris tāḍitas tu stanāntare
c viṣṇor acintyaṃ svaṃ bhāgam ātmānaṃ pratyanusmarat
a tato dānavadarpaghnaṃ saumitriṃ devakaṇṭakaḥ
c taṃ pīḍayitvā bāhubhyām aprabhur laṅghane 'bhavat
a himavān mandaro merus trailokyaṃ vā sahāmaraiḥ
c śakyaṃ bhujābhyām uddhartuṃ na saṃkhye bharatānujaḥ
a athainaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ bhāgaṃ mānuṣaṃ deham āsthitam
c visaṃjñaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇo vismito 'bhavat
a atha vāyusutaḥ kruddho rāvaṇaṃ samabhidravat
c ājaghānorasi kruddho vajrakalpena muṣṭinā
a tena muṣṭiprahāreṇa rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c jānubhyām apatad bhūmau cacāla ca papāta ca
a visaṃjñaṃ rāvaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā samare bhīmavikramam
c ṛṣayo vānarāś caiva nedur devāḥ savāsavāḥ
a hanūmān api tejasvī lakṣmaṇaṃ rāvaṇārditam
c anayad rāghavābhyāśaṃ bāhubhyāṃ parigṛhya tam
a vāyusūnoḥ suhṛttvena bhaktyā paramayā ca saḥ
c śatrūṇām aprakampyo 'pi laghutvam agamat kapeḥ
a taṃ samutsṛjya sā śaktiḥ saumitriṃ yudhi durjayam
c rāvaṇasya rathe tasmin sthānaṃ punar upāgamat
a rāvaṇo 'pi mahātejāḥ prāpya saṃjñāṃ mahāhave
c ādade niśitān bāṇāñ jagrāha ca mahad dhanuḥ
a āśvastaś ca viśalyaś ca lakṣmaṇaḥ śatrusūdanaḥ
c viṣṇor bhāgam amīmāṃsyam ātmānaṃ pratyanusmaran
a nipātitamahāvīrāṃ vānarāṇāṃ mahācamūm
c rāghavas tu raṇe dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇaṃ samabhidravat
a athainam upasaṃgamya hanūmān vākyam abravīt
c mama pṛṣṭhaṃ samāruhya rakṣasaṃ śāstum arhasi
a tac chrutvā rāghavo vākyaṃ vāyuputreṇa bhāṣitam
c ārohat sahasā śūro hanūmantaṃ mahākapim
e rathasthaṃ rāvaṇaṃ saṃkhye dadarśa manujādhipaḥ
a tam ālokya mahātejāḥ pradudrāva sa rāghavaḥ
c vairocanam iva kruddho viṣṇur abhyudyatāyudhaḥ
a jyāśabdam akarot tīvraṃ vajraniṣpeṣanisvanam
c girā gambhīrayā rāmo rākṣasendram uvāca ha
a tiṣṭha tiṣṭha mama tvaṃ hi kṛtvā vipriyam īdṛśam
c kva nu rākṣasaśārdūla gato mokṣam avāpsyasi
a yadīndravaivasvata bhāskarān vā
svayambhuvaiśvānaraśaṃkarān vā
c gamiṣyasi tvaṃ daśa vā diśo vā
tathāpi me nādya gato vimokṣyase
a yaś caiṣa śaktyābhihatas tvayādya
icchan viṣādaṃ sahasābhyupetaḥ
c sa eṣa rakṣogaṇarāja mṛtyuḥ
saputradārasya tavādya yuddhe
a rāghavasya vacaḥ śrutvā rākṣasendro mahākapim
c ājaghāna śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ kālānalaśikhopamaiḥ
a rākṣasenāhave tasya tāḍitasyāpi sāyakaiḥ
c svabhāvatejoyuktasya bhūyas tejo vyavardhata
a tato rāmo mahātejā rāvaṇena kṛtavraṇam
c dṛṣṭvā plavagaśārdūlaṃ krodhasya vaśam eyivān
a tasyābhisaṃkramya rathaṃ sacakraṃ
sāśvadhvajacchatramahāpatākam
c sasārathiṃ sāśaniśūlakhaḍgaṃ
rāmaḥ praciccheda śaraiḥ supuṅkhaiḥ
a athendraśatruṃ tarasā jaghāna
bāṇena vajrāśanisaṃnibhena
c bhujāntare vyūḍhasujātarūpe
vajreṇa meruṃ bhagavān ivendraḥ
a yo vajrapātāśanisaṃnipātān
na cukṣubhe nāpi cacāla rājā
c sa rāmabāṇābhihato bhṛśārtaś
cacāla cāpaṃ ca mumoca vīraḥ
a taṃ vihvalantaṃ prasamīkṣya rāmaḥ
samādade dīptam athārdhacandram
c tenārkavarṇaṃ sahasā kirīṭaṃ
ciccheda rakṣo'dhipater mahātmāḥ
a taṃ nirviṣāśīviṣasaṃnikāśaṃ
śāntārciṣaṃ sūryam ivāprakāśam
c gataśriyaṃ kṛttakirīṭakūṭam
uvāca rāmo yudhi rākṣasendram
a kṛtaṃ tvayā karma mahat subhīmaṃ
hatapravīraś ca kṛtas tvayāham
c tasmāt pariśrānta iti vyavasya
na tvaṃ śarair mṛtyuvaśaṃ nayāmi
a sa evam ukto hatadarpaharṣo
nikṛttacāpaḥ sa hatāśvasūtaḥ
c śarārditaḥ kṛttamahākirīṭo
viveśa laṅkāṃ sahasā sma rājā
a tasmin praviṣṭe rajanīcarendre
mahābale dānavadevaśatrau
c harīn viśalyān sahalakṣmaṇena
cakāra rāmaḥ paramāhavāgre
a tasmin prabhagne tridaśendraśatrau
surāsurā bhūtagaṇā diśaś ca
c sasāgarāḥ sarṣimahoragāś ca
tathaiva bhūmyambucarāś ca hṛṣṭāḥ
a sa praviśya purīṃ laṅkāṃ rāmabāṇabhayārditaḥ
c bhagnadarpas tadā rājā babhūva vyathitendriyaḥ
a mātaṃga iva siṃhena garuḍeneva pannagaḥ
c abhibhūto 'bhavad rājā rāghaveṇa mahātmanā
a brahmadaṇḍaprakāśānāṃ vidyutsadṛśavarcasām
c smaran rāghavabāṇānāṃ vivyathe rākṣaseśvaraḥ
a sa kāñcanamayaṃ divyam āśritya paramāsanam
c vikprekṣamāṇo rakṣāṃsi rāvaṇo vākyam abravīt
a sarvaṃ tat khalu me moghaṃ yat taptaṃ paramaṃ tapaḥ
c yat samāno mahendreṇa mānuṣeṇāsmi nirjitaḥ
a idaṃ tad brahmaṇo ghoraṃ vākyaṃ mām abhyupasthitam
c mānuṣebhyo vijānīhi bhayaṃ tvam iti tat tathā
a devadānavagandharvair yakṣarākṣasapannagaiḥ
c avadhyatvaṃ mayā prāptaṃ mānuṣebhyo na yācitam
a etad evābhyupāgamya yatnaṃ kartum ihārhatha
c rākṣasāś cāpi tiṣṭhantu caryāgopuramūrdhasu
a sa cāpratimagambhīro devadānavadarpahā
c brahmaśāpābhibhūtas tu kumbhakarṇo vibodhyatām
a sa parājitam ātmānaṃ prahastaṃ ca niṣūditam
c jñātvā rakṣobalaṃ bhīmam ādideśa mahābalaḥ
a dvāreṣu yatnaḥ kriyatāṃ prākārāś cādhiruhyatām
c nidrāvaśasamāviṣṭaḥ kumbhakarṇo vibodhyatām
a nava ṣaṭ sapta cāṣṭau ca māsān svapiti rākṣasaḥ
c taṃ tu bodhayata kṣipraṃ kumbhakarṇaṃ mahābalam
a sa hi saṃkhye mahābāhuḥ kakudaṃ sarvarakṣasām
c vānarān rājaputrau ca kṣipram eva vadhiṣyati
a kumbhakarṇaḥ sadā śete mūḍho grāmyasukhe rataḥ
c rāmeṇābhinirastasya saṃgrāmo 'smin sudāruṇe
a bhaviṣyati na me śokaḥ kumbhakarṇe vibodhite
c kiṃ kariṣyāmy ahaṃ tena śakratulyabalena hi
a īdṛśe vyasane prāpte yo na sāhyāya kalpate
c te tu tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rākṣasendrasya rākṣasāḥ
a jagmuḥ paramasaṃbhrāntāḥ kumbhakarṇaniveśanam
c te rāvaṇasamādiṣṭā māṃsaśoṇitabhojanāḥ
a gandhamālyāṃs tathā bhakṣyān ādāya sahasā yayuḥ
c tāṃ praviśya mahādvārāṃ sarvato yojanāyatām
a kumbhakarṇaguhāṃ ramyāṃ sarvagandhapravāhinīm
c pratiṣṭhamānāḥ kṛcchreṇa yatnāt praviviśur guhām
a tāṃ praviśya guhāṃ ramyāṃ śubhāṃ kāñcanakuṭṭimām
c dadṛśur nairṛtavyāghraṃ śayānaṃ bhīmadarśanam
a te tu taṃ vikṛtaṃ suptaṃ vikīrṇam iva parvatam
c kumbhakarṇaṃ mahānidraṃ sahitāḥ pratyabodhayan
a ūrdhvaromāñcitatanuṃ śvasantam iva pannagam
c trāsayantaṃ mahāśvāsaiḥ śayānaṃ bhīmadarśanam
a bhīmanāsāpuṭaṃ taṃ tu pātālavipulānanam
c dadṛśur nairṛtavyāghraṃ kumbhakarṇaṃ mahābalam
a tataś cakrur mahātmānaḥ kumbhakarṇāgratas tadā
c māṃsānāṃ merusaṃkāśaṃ rāśiṃ paramatarpaṇam
a mṛgāṇāṃ mahiṣāṇāṃ ca varāhāṇāṃ ca saṃcayān
c cakrur nairṛtaśārdūlā rāśimann asya cādbhutam
a tataḥ śoṇitakumbhāṃś ca madyāni vividhāni ca
c purastāt kumbhakarṇasya cakrus tridaśaśatravaḥ
a lilipuś ca parārdhyena candanena paraṃtapam
c divyair ācchādayām āsur mālyair gandhaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ
a dhūpaṃ sugandhaṃ sasṛjus tuṣṭuvuś ca paraṃtapam
c jaladā iva conedur yātudhānāḥ sahasraśaḥ
a śaṅkhān āpūrayām āsuḥ śaśāṅkasadṛśaprabhān
c tumulaṃ yugapac cāpi vineduś cāpy amarṣitāḥ
a nedur āsphoṭayām āsuś cikṣipus te niśācarāḥ
c kumbhakarṇavibodhārthaṃ cakrus te vipulaṃ svanam
a saśaṅkhabherīpaṭahapraṇādam
āsphoṭitakṣveḍitasiṃhanādam
c diśo dravantas tridivaṃ kirantaḥ
śrutvā vihaṃgāḥ sahasā nipetuḥ
a yadā bhṛśaṃ tair ninadair mahātmā
na kumbhakarṇo bubudhe prasuptaḥ
c tato musuṇḍīmusalāni sarve
rakṣogaṇās te jagṛhur gadāś ca
a taṃ śailaśṛṅgair musalair gadābhir
vṛkṣais talair mudgaramuṣṭibhiś ca
c sukhaprasuptaṃ bhuvi kumbhakarṇaṃ
rakṣāṃsy udagrāṇi tadā nijaghnuḥ
a tasya niśvāsavātena kumbhakarṇasya rakṣasaḥ
c rākṣasā balavanto 'pi sthātuṃ nāśaknuvan puraḥ
a tato 'sya purato gāḍhaṃ rākṣasā bhīmavikramāḥ
c mṛdaṅgapaṇavān bherīḥ śaṅkhakumbhagaṇāṃs tathā
e daśarākṣasasāhasraṃ yugapat paryavādayan
a nīlāñjanacayākāraṃ te tu taṃ pratyabodhayan
c abhighnanto nadantaś ca naiva saṃvivide tu saḥ
a yadā cainaṃ na śekus te pratibodhayituṃ tadā
c tato gurutaraṃ yatnaṃ dāruṇaṃ samupākraman
a aśvān uṣṭrān kharān nāgāñ jaghnur daṇḍakaśāṅkuśaiḥ
c bherīśaṅkhamṛdaṅgāṃś ca sarvaprāṇair avādayan
a nijaghnuś cāsya gātrāṇi mahākāṣṭhakaṭaṃ karaiḥ
c mudgarair musalaiś caiva sarvaprāṇasamudyataiḥ
a tena śabdena mahatā laṅkā samabhipūritā
c saparvatavanā sarvā so 'pi naiva prabudhyate
a tataḥ sahasraṃ bherīṇāṃ yugapat samahanyata
c mṛṣṭakāñcanakoṇānām asaktānāṃ samantataḥ
a evam apy atinidras tu yadā naiva prabudhyata
c śāpasya vaśam āpannas tataḥ kruddhā niśācarāḥ
a mahākrodhasamāviṣṭāḥ sarve bhīmaparākramāḥ
c tad rakṣobodhayiṣyantaś cakrur anye parākramam
a anye bherīḥ samājaghnur anye cakrur mahāsvanam
c keśān anye pralulupuḥ karṇāv anye daśanti ca
e na kumbhakarṇaḥ paspande mahānidrāvaśaṃ gataḥ
a anye ca balinas tasya kūṭamudgarapāṇayaḥ
c mūrdhni vakṣasi gātreṣu pātayan kūṭamudgarān
a rajjubandhanabaddhābhiḥ śataghnībhiś ca sarvataḥ
c vadhyamāno mahākāyo na prābudhyata rākṣasaḥ
a vāraṇānāṃ sahasraṃ tu śarīre 'sya pradhāvitam
c kumbhakarṇas tato buddhaḥ sparśaṃ param abudhyata
a sa pātyamānair giriśṛṅgavṛkṣair
acintayaṃs tān vipulān prahārān
c nidrākṣayāt kṣudbhayapīḍitaś ca
vijṛmbhamāṇaḥ sahasotpapāta
a sa nāgabhogācalaśṛṅgakalpau
vikṣipya bāhū giriśṛṅgasārau
c vivṛtya vaktraṃ vaḍavāmukhābhaṃ
niśācaro 'sau vikṛtaṃ jajṛmbhe
a tasya jājṛmbhamāṇasya vaktraṃ pātālasaṃnibham
c dadṛśe meruśṛṅgāgre divākara ivoditaḥ
a vijṛmbhamāṇo 'tibalaḥ pratibuddho niśācaraḥ
c niśvāsaś cāsya saṃjajñe parvatād iva mārutaḥ
a rūpam uttiṣṭhatas tasya kumbhakarṇasya tad babhau
c tapānte sabalākasya meghasyeva vivarṣataḥ
a tasya dīptāgnisadṛśe vidyutsadṛśavarcasī
c dadṛśāte mahānetre dīptāv iva mahāgrahau
a ādad bubhukṣito māṃsaṃ śoṇitaṃ tṛṣito 'pibat
c medaḥ kumbhaṃ ca madyaṃ ca papau śakraripus tadā
a tatas tṛpta iti jñātvā samutpetur niśācarāḥ
c śirobhiś ca praṇamyainaṃ sarvataḥ paryavārayan
