a sa sarvān sāntvayām āsa nairṛtān nairṛtarṣabhaḥ
c bodhanād vismitaś cāpi rākṣasān idam abravīt
a kimartham aham āhatya bhavadbhiḥ pratibodhitaḥ
c kaccit sukuśalaṃ rājño bhayaṃ vā neha kiṃ cana
a atha vā dhruvam anyebhyo bhayaṃ param upasthitam
c yadartham eva tvaritair bhavadbhiḥ pratibodhitaḥ
a adya rākṣasarājasya bhayam utpāṭayāmy aham
c pātayiṣye mahendraṃ vā śātayiṣye tathānalam
a na hy alpakāraṇe suptaṃ bodhayiṣyati māṃ bhṛśam
c tad ākhyātārthatattvena matprabodhanakāraṇam
a evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ saṃrabdhaṃ kumbhakarṇam ariṃdamam
c yūpākṣaḥ sacivo rājñaḥ kṛtāñjalir uvāca ha
a na no devakṛtaṃ kiṃ cid bhayam asti kadā cana
c na daityadānavebhyo vā bhayam asti hi tādṛśam
e yādṛśaṃ mānuṣaṃ rājan bhayam asmān upasthitam
a vānaraiḥ parvatākārair laṅkeyaṃ parivāritā
c sītāharaṇasaṃtaptād rāmān nas tumulaṃ bhayam
a ekena vānareṇeyaṃ pūrvaṃ dagdhā mahāpurī
c kumāro nihataś cākṣaḥ sānuyātraḥ sakuñjaraḥ
a svayaṃ rakṣo'dhipaś cāpi paulastyo devakaṇṭakaḥ
c mṛteti saṃyuge muktārāmeṇādityatejasā
a yan na devaiḥ kṛto rājā nāpi daityair na dānavaiḥ
c kṛtaḥ sa iha rāmeṇa vimuktaḥ prāṇasaṃśayāt
a sa yūpākṣavacaḥ śrutvā bhrātur yudhi parājayam
c kumbhakarṇo vivṛttākṣo yūpākṣam idam abravīt
a sarvam adyaiva yūpākṣa harisainyaṃ salakṣmaṇam
c rāghavaṃ ca raṇe hatvā paścād drakṣyāmi rāvaṇam
a rākṣasāṃs tarpayiṣyāmi harīṇāṃ māṃsaśoṇitaiḥ
c rāmalakṣmaṇayoś cāpi svayaṃ pāsyāmi śoṇitam
a tat tasya vākyaṃ bruvato niśamya
sagarvitaṃ roṣavivṛddhadoṣam
c mahodaro nairṛtayodhamukhyaḥ
kṛtāñjalir vākyam idaṃ babhāṣe
a rāvaṇasya vacaḥ śrutvā guṇadoṣu vimṛśya ca
c paścād api mahābāho śatrūn yudhi vijeṣyasi
a mahodaravacaḥ śrutvā rākṣasaiḥ parivāritaḥ
c kumbhakarṇo mahātejāḥ saṃpratasthe mahābalaḥ
a taṃ samutthāpya bhīmākṣaṃ bhīmarūpaparākramam
c rākṣasās tvaritā jagmur daśagrīvaniveśanam
a tato gatvā daśagrīvam āsīnaṃ paramāsane
c ūcur baddhāñjalipuṭāḥ sarva eva niśācarāḥ
a prabuddhaḥ kumbhakarṇo 'sau bhrātā te rākṣasarṣabha
c kathaṃ tatraiva niryātu drakṣyase tam ihāgatam
a rāvaṇas tv abravīd dhṛṣṭo yathānyāyaṃ ca pūjitam
c draṣṭum enam ihecchāmi yathānyāyaṃ ca pūjitam
a tathety uktvā tu te sarve punar āgamya rākṣasāḥ
c kumbhakarṇam idaṃ vākyam ūcū rāvaṇacoditāḥ
a draṣṭuṃ tvāṃ kāṅkṣate rājā sarvarākṣasapuṃgavaḥ
c gamane kriyatāṃ buddhir bhrātaraṃ saṃpraharṣaya
a kumbhakarṇas tu durdharṣo bhrātur ājñāya śāsanam
c tathety uktvā mahāvīryaḥ śayanād utpapāta ha
a prakṣālya vadanaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ snātaḥ paramabhūṣitaḥ
c pipāsus tvarayām āsa pānaṃ balasamīraṇam
a tatas te tvaritās tasya rājṣasā rāvaṇājñayā
c madyaṃ bhakṣyāṃś ca vividhān kṣipram evopahārayan
a pītvā ghaṭasahasraṃ sa gamanāyopacakrame
a īṣatsamutkaṭo mattas tejobalasamanvitaḥ
c kumbhakarṇo babhau hṛṣṭaḥ kālāntakayamopamaḥ
a bhrātuḥ sa bhavanaṃ gacchan rakṣobalasamanvitaḥ
c kumbhakarṇaḥ padanyāsair akampayata medinīm
a sa rājamārgaṃ vapuṣā prakāśayan
sahasraraśmir dharaṇīm ivāṃśubhiḥ
c jagāma tatrāñjalimālayā vṛtaḥ
śatakratur geham iva svayambhuvaḥ
a ke cic charaṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ sma rāmaṃ
vrajanti ke cid vyathitāḥ patanti
c ke cid diśaḥ sma vyathitāḥ prayānti
ke cid bhayārtā bhuvi śerate sma
a tam adriśṛṅgapratimaṃ kirīṭinaṃ
spṛśantam ādityam ivātmatejasā
c vanaukasaḥ prekṣya vivṛddham adbhutaṃ
bhayārditā dudruvire tatas tataḥ
a tato rāmo mahātejā dhanur ādāya vīryavān
c kirīṭinaṃ mahākāyaṃ kumbhakarṇaṃ dadarśa ha
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasaśreṣṭhaṃ parvatākāradarśanam
c kramamāṇam ivākāśaṃ purā nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum
a satoyāmbudasaṃkāśaṃ kāñcanāṅgadabhūṣaṇam
c dṛṣṭvā punaḥ pradudrāva vānarāṇāṃ mahācamūḥ
a vidrutāṃ vāhinīṃ dṛṣṭvā vardhamānaṃ ca rākṣasaṃ
c savismayam idaṃ rāmo vibhīṣaṇam uvāca ha
a ko 'sau parvatasaṃkaśaḥ kirīṭī harilocanaḥ
c laṅkāyāṃ dṛśyate vīraḥ savidyud iva toyadaḥ
a pṛthivyāḥ ketubhūto 'sau mahān eko 'tra dṛśyate
c yaṃ dṛṣṭvā vānarāḥ sarve vidravanti tatas tataḥ
a ācakṣva me mahān ko 'sau rakṣo vā yadi vāsuraḥ
c na mayaivaṃvidhaṃ bhūtaṃ dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ kadā cana
a sa pṛṣṭo rājaputreṇa rāmeṇākliṣṭakāriṇā
c vibhīṣaṇo mahāprājñaḥ kākutstham idam abravīt
a yena vaivasvato yuddhe vāsavaś ca parājitaḥ
c saiṣa viśravasaḥ putraḥ kumbhakarṇaḥ pratāpavān
a etena devā yudhi dānavāś ca
yakṣā bhujaṃgāḥ piśitāśanāś ca
c gandharvavidyādharakiṃnarāś ca
sahasraśo rāghava saṃprabhagnāḥ
a śūlapāṇiṃ virūpākṣaṃ kumbhakarṇaṃ mahābalam
c hantuṃ na śekus tridaśāḥ kālo 'yam iti mohitāḥ
a prakṛtyā hy eṣa tejasvī kumbhakarṇo mahābalaḥ
c anyeṣāṃ rākṣasendrāṇāṃ varadānakṛtaṃ balam
a etena jātamātreṇa kṣudhārtena mahātmanā
c bhakṣitāni sahasrāṇi sattvānāṃ subahūny api
a teṣu saṃbhakṣyamāṇeṣu prajā bhayanipīḍitāḥ
c yānti sma śaraṇaṃ śakraṃ tam apy arthaṃ nyavedayan
a sa kumbhakarṇaṃ kupito mahendro
jaghāna vajreṇa śitena vajrī
c sa śakravajrābhihato mahātmā
cacāla kopāc ca bhṛśaṃ nanāda
a tasya nānadyamānasya kumbhakarṇasya dhīmataḥ
c śrutvā ninādaṃ vitrastā bhūyo bhūmir vitatrase
a tataḥ kopān mahendrasya kumbhakarṇo mahābalaḥ
c vikṛṣyairāvatād dantaṃ jaghānorasi vāsavam
a kumbhakarṇaprahārārto vicacāla sa vāsavaḥ
c tato viṣeduḥ sahasā devabrahmarṣidānavāḥ
a prajābhiḥ saha śakraś ca yayau sthānaṃ svayambhuvaḥ
c kumbhakarṇasya daurātmyaṃ śaśaṃsus te prajāpateḥ
e prajānāṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ cāpi devānāṃ cāpi dharṣaṇam
a evaṃ prajā yadi tv eṣa bhakṣayiṣyati nityaśaḥ
c acireṇaiva kālena śūnyo loko bhaviṣyati
a vāsavasya vacaḥ śrutvā sarvalokapitāmahaḥ
c rakṣāṃsy āvāhayām āsa kumbhakarṇaṃ dadarśa ha
a kumbhakarṇaṃ samīkṣyaiva vitatrāsa prajāpatiḥ
c dṛṣṭvā niśvasya caivedaṃ svayambhūr idam abravīt
a dhruvaṃ lokavināśāya paurastyenāsi nirmitaḥ
c tasmāt tvam adya prabhṛti mṛtakalpaḥ śayiṣyasi
e brahmaśāpābhibhūto 'tha nipapātāgrataḥ prabhoḥ
a tataḥ paramasaṃbhrānto rāvaṇo vākyam abravīt
c vivṛddhaḥ kāñcano vṛkṣaḥ phalakāle nikṛtyate
a na naptāraṃ svakaṃ nyāyyaṃ śaptum evaṃ prajāpate
c na mithyāvacanaś ca tvaṃ svapsyaty eṣa na saṃśayaḥ
e kālas tu kriyatām asya śayane jāgare tathā
a rāvaṇasya vacaḥ śrutvā svayambhūr idam abravīt
c śayitā hy eṣa ṣaṇ māsān ekāhaṃ jāgariṣyati
a ekenāhnā tv asau vīraś caran bhūmiṃ bubhukṣitaḥ
c vyāttāsyo bhakṣayel lokān saṃkruddha iva pāvakaḥ
a so 'sau vyasanam āpannaḥ kumbhakarṇam abodhayat
c tvatparākramabhītaś ca rājā saṃprati rāvaṇaḥ
a sa eṣa nirgato vīraḥ śibirād bhīmavikramaḥ
c vānarān bhṛśasaṃkruddho bhakṣayan paridhāvati
a kumbhakarṇaṃ samīkṣyaiva harayo vipradudruvuḥ
c katham enaṃ raṇe kruddhaṃ vārayiṣyanti vānarāḥ
a ucyantāṃ vānarāḥ sarve yantram etat samucchritam
c iti vijñāya harayo bhaviṣyantīha nirbhayāḥ
a vibhīṣaṇavacaḥ śrutvā hetumat sumukhodgatam
c uvāca rāghavo vākyaṃ nīlaṃ senāpatiṃ tadā
a gaccha sainyāni sarvāṇi vyūhya tiṣṭhasva pāvake
c dvārāṇy ādāya laṅkāyāś caryāś cāpy atha saṃkramān
a śailaśṛṅgāṇi vṛkṣāṃś ca śilāś cāpy upasaṃharan
c tiṣṭhantu vānarāḥ sarve sāyudhāḥ śailapāṇayaḥ
a rāghaveṇa samādiṣṭo nīlo haricamūpatiḥ
c śaśāsa vānarānīkaṃ yathāvat kapikuñjaraḥ
a tato gavākṣaḥ śarabho hanumān aṅgado nalaḥ
c śailaśṛṅgāṇi śailābhā gṛhītvā dvāram abhyayuḥ
a tato harīṇāṃ tad anīkam ugraṃ
rarāja śailodyatavṛkṣahastam
c gireḥ samīpānugataṃ yathaiva
mahan mahāmbhodharajālam ugram
a sa tu rākṣasaśārdūlo nidrāmadasamākulaḥ
c rājamārgaṃ śriyā juṣṭaṃ yayau vipulavikramaḥ
a rākṣasānāṃ sahasraiś ca vṛtaḥ paramadurjayaḥ
c gṛhebhyaḥ puṣpavarṣeṇa kāryamāṇas tadā yayau
a sa hemajālavitataṃ bhānubhāsvaradarśanam
c dadarśa vipulaṃ ramyaṃ rākṣasendraniveśanam
a sa tat tadā sūrya ivābhrajālaṃ
praviśya rakṣo'dhipater niveśanam
c dadarśa dūre 'grajam āsanasthaṃ
svayambhuvaṃ śakra ivāsanastham
a so 'bhigamya gṛhaṃ bhrātuḥ kakṣyām abhivigāhya ca
c dadarśodvignam āsīnaṃ vimāne puṣpake gurum
a atha dṛṣṭvā daśagrīvaḥ kumbhakarṇam upasthitam
c tūrṇam utthāya saṃhṛṣṭaḥ saṃnikarṣam upānayat
a athāsīnasya paryaṅke kumbhakarṇo mahābalaḥ
c bhrātur vavande caraṇāṃ kiṃ kṛtyam iti cābravīt
e utpatya cainaṃ mudito rāvaṇaḥ pariṣasvaje
a sa bhrātrā saṃpariṣvakto yathāvac cābhinanditaḥ
c kumbhakarṇaḥ śubhaṃ divyaṃ pratipede varāsanam
a sa tadāsanam āśritya kumbhakarṇo mahābalaḥ
c saṃraktanayanaḥ kopād rāvaṇaṃ vākyam abravīt
a kimartham aham ādṛtya tvayā rājan prabodhitaḥ
c śaṃsa kasmād bhayaṃ te 'sti ko 'dya preto bhaviṣyati
a bhrātaraṃ rāvaṇaḥ kruddhaṃ kumbhakarṇam avasthitam
c īṣat tu parivṛttābhyāṃ netrābhyāṃ vākyam abravīt
a adya te sumahān kālaḥ śayānasya mahābala
c sukhitas tvaṃ na jānīṣe mama rāmakṛtaṃ bhayam
a eṣa dāśarathī rāmaḥ sugrīvasahito balī
c samudraṃ sabalas tīrtvā mūlaṃ naḥ parikṛntati
a hanta paśyasva laṅkāyā vanāny upavanāni ca
c setunā sukham āgamya vānaraikārṇavaṃ kṛtam
a ye rākṣasā mukhyatamā hatās te vānarair yudhi
c vānarāṇāṃ kṣayaṃ yuddhe na paśyāmi kadā cana
a sarvakṣapitakośaṃ ca sa tvam abhyavapadya mām
c trāyasvemāṃ purīṃ laṅkāṃ bālavṛddhāvaśeṣitām
a bhrātur arthe mahābāho kuru karma suduṣkaram
c mayaivaṃ noktapūrvo hi kaś cid bhrātaḥ paraṃtapa
e tvayy asti mama ca snehaḥ parā saṃbhāvanā ca me
a devāsuravimardeṣu bahuśo rākṣasarṣabha
c tvayā devāḥ prativyūhya nirjitāś cāsurā yudhi
e na hi te sarvabhūteṣu dṛśyate sadṛśo balī
a kuruṣva me priyahitam etad uttamaṃ
yathāpriyaṃ priyaraṇabāndhavapriya
c svatejasā vidhama sapatnavāhinīṃ
śaradghanaṃ pavana ivodyato mahān
a tasya rākṣasarājasya niśamya paridevitam
c kumbhakarṇo babhāṣe 'tha vacanaṃ prajahāsa ca
a dṛṣṭo doṣo hi yo 'smābhiḥ purā mantravinirṇaye
c hiteṣv anabhiyuktena so 'yam āsāditas tvayā
a śīghraṃ khalv abhyupetaṃ tvāṃ phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ
c nirayeṣv eva patanaṃ yathā duṣkṛtakarmaṇaḥ
a prathamaṃ vai mahārāja kṛtyam etad acintitam
c kevalaṃ vīryadarpeṇa nānubandho vicāritaḥ
a yaḥ paścāt pūrvakāryāṇi kuryād aiśvaryam āsthitaḥ
c pūrvaṃ cottarakāryāṇi na sa veda nayānayau
a deśakālavihīnāni karmāṇi viparītavat
c kriyamāṇāni duṣyanti havīṃṣy aprayateṣv iva
a trayāṇāṃ pañcadhā yogaṃ karmaṇāṃ yaḥ prapaśyati
c sacivaiḥ samayaṃ kṛtvā sa sabhye vartate pathi
a yathāgamaṃ ca yo rājā samayaṃ vicikīrṣati
c budhyate sacivān buddhyā suhṛdaś cānupaśyati
a dharmam arthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca sarvān vā rakṣasāṃ pate
c bhajate puruṣaḥ kāle trīṇi dvandvāni vā punaḥ
a triṣu caiteṣu yac chreṣṭhaṃ śrutvā tan nāvabudhyate
c rājā vā rājamātro vā vyarthaṃ tasya bahuśrutam
a upapradānaṃ sāntvaṃ vā bhedaṃ kāle ca vikramam
c yogaṃ ca rakṣasāṃ śreṣṭha tāv ubhau ca nayānayau
a kāle dharmārthakāmān yaḥ saṃmantrya sacivaiḥ saha
c niṣevetātmavāṃl loke na sa vyasanam āpnuyāt
a hitānubandham ālokya kāryākāryam ihātmanaḥ
c rājā sahārthatattvajñaiḥ sacivaiḥ saha jīvati
a anabhijñāya śāstrārthān puruṣāḥ paśubuddhayaḥ
c prāgalbhyād vaktum icchanti mantreṣv abhyantarīkṛtāḥ
a aśāstraviduṣāṃ teṣāṃ na kāryam ahitaṃ vacaḥ
c arthaśāstrānabhijñānāṃ vipulāṃ śriyam icchatām
a ahitaṃ ca hitākāraṃ dhārṣṭyāj jalpanti ye narāḥ
c avekṣya mantrabāhyās te kartavyāḥ kṛtyadūṣaṇāḥ
a vināśayanto bhartāraṃ sahitāḥ śatrubhir budhaiḥ
c viparītāni kṛtyāni kārayantīha mantriṇaḥ
a tān bhartā mitrasaṃkāśān amitrān mantranirṇaye
c vyavahāreṇa jānīyāt sacivān upasaṃhitān
a capalasyeha kṛtyāni sahasānupradhāvataḥ
c chidram anye prapadyante krauñcasya kham iva dvijāḥ
a yo hi śatrum avajñāya nātmānam abhirakṣati
c avāpnoti hi so 'narthān sthānāc ca vyavaropyate
a tat tu śrutvā daśagrīvaḥ kumbhakarṇasya bhāṣitam
c bhrukuṭiṃ caiva saṃcakre kruddhaś cainam uvāca ha
a mānyo gurur ivācāryaḥ kiṃ māṃ tvam anuśāsati
c kim evaṃ vākśramaṃ kṛtvā kāle yuktaṃ vidhīyatām
a vibhramāc cittamohād vā balavīryāśrayeṇa vā
c nābhipannam idānīṃ yad vyarthās tasya punaḥ kṛthāḥ
a asmin kāle tu yad yuktaṃ tad idānīṃ vidhīyatām
c mamāpanayajaṃ doṣaṃ vikrameṇa samīkuru
a yadi khalv asti me sneho bhrātṛtvaṃ vāvagacchasi
c yadi vā kāryam etat te hṛdi kāryatamaṃ matam
a sa suhṛdyo vipannārthaṃ dīnam abhyavapadyate
c sa bandhur yo 'panīteṣu sāhāyyāyopakalpate
a tam athaivaṃ bruvāṇaṃ tu vacanaṃ dhīradāruṇam
c ruṣṭo 'yam iti vijñāya śanaiḥ ślakṣṇam uvāca ha
a atīva hi samālakṣya bhrātaraṃ kṣubhitendriyam
c kumbhakarṇaḥ śanair vākyaṃ babhāṣe parisāntvayan
a alaṃ rākṣasarājendra saṃtāpam upapadya te
c roṣaṃ ca saṃparityajya svastho bhavitum arhasi
a naitan manasi kartavvyaṃ mayi jīvati pārthiva
c tam ahaṃ nāśayiṣyāmi yatkṛte paritapyase
a avaśyaṃ tu hitaṃ vācyaṃ sarvāvasthaṃ mayā tava
c bandhubhāvād abhihitaṃ bhrātṛsnehāc ca pārthiva
a sadṛśaṃ yat tu kāle 'smin kartuṃ snigdhena bandhunā
c śatrūṇāṃ kadanaṃ paśya kriyamāṇaṃ mayā raṇe
a adya paśya mahābāho mayā samaramūrdhani
c hate rāme saha bhrātrā dravantīṃ harivāhinīm
a adya rāmasya tad dṛṣṭvā mayānītaṃ raṇāc chiraḥ
c sukhībhava mahābāho sītā bhavatu duḥkhitā
a adya rāmasya paśyantu nidhanaṃ sumahat priyam
c laṅkāyāṃ rākṣasāḥ sarve ye te nihatabāndhavāḥ
a adya śokaparītānāṃ svabandhuvadhakāraṇāt
c śatror yudhi vināśena karomy asrapramārjanam
a adya parvatasaṃkāśaṃ sasūryam iva toyadam
c vikīrṇaṃ paśya samare sugrīvaṃ plavageśvaram
a na paraḥ preṣaṇīyas te yuddhāyātula vikrama
c aham utsādayiṣyāmi śatrūṃs tava mahābala
a yadi śakro yadi yamo yadi pāvakamārutau
c tān ahaṃ yodhayiṣyāmi kubera varuṇāv api
a girimātraśarīrasya śitaśūladharasya me
c nardatas tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrasya bibhīyāc ca puraṃdaraḥ
a atha vā tyaktaśastrasya mṛdgatas tarasā ripūn
c na me pratimukhe kaś cic chaktaḥ sthātuṃ jijīviṣuḥ
a naiva śaktyā na gadayā nāsinā na śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c hastābhyām eva saṃrabdho haniṣyāmy api vajriṇam
a yadi me muṣṭivegaṃ sa rāghavo 'dya sahiṣyati
c tataḥ pāsyanti bāṇaughā rudhiraṃ rāghavasya te
a cintayā bādhyase rājan kimarthaṃ mayi tiṣṭhati
c so 'haṃ śatruvināśāya tava niryātum udyataḥ
a muñca rāmād bhayaṃ rājan haniṣyāmīha saṃyuge
c rāghavaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva sugrīvaṃ ca mahābalam
e asādhāraṇam icchāmi tava dātuṃ mahad yaśaḥ
a vadhena te dāśaratheḥ sukhāvahaṃ
sukhaṃ samāhartum ahaṃ vrajāmi
c nihatya rāmaṃ sahalakṣmaṇena
khādāmi sarvān hariyūthamukhyān
a ramasva kāmaṃ piba cāgryavāruṇīṃ
kuruṣva kṛtyāni vinīyatāṃ jvaraḥ
c mayādya rāme gamite yamakṣayaṃ
cirāya sītā vaśagā bhaviṣyati
a tad uktam atikāyasya balino bāhuśālinaḥ
c kumbhakarṇasya vacanaṃ śrutvovāca mahodaraḥ
a kumbhakarṇakule jāto dhṛṣṭaḥ prākṛtadarśanaḥ
c avalipto na śaknoṣi kṛtyaṃ sarvatra veditum
a na hi rājā na jānīte kumbhakarṇa nayānayau
c tvaṃ tu kaiśorakād dhṛṣṭaḥ kevalaṃ vaktum icchasi
a sthānaṃ vṛddhiṃ ca hāniṃ ca deśakālavibhāgavit
c ātmanaś ca pareṣāṃ ca budhyate rākṣasarṣabha
a yat tu śakyaṃ balavatā kartuṃ prākṛtabuddhinā
c anupāsitavṛddhena kaḥ kuryāt tādṛśaṃ budhaḥ
a yāṃs tu dharmārthakāmāṃs tvaṃ bravīṣi pṛthag āśrayān
c anuboddhuṃ svabhāvena na hi lakṣaṇam asti te
a karma caiva hi sarveṣāṃ kāraṇānāṃ prayojanam
c śreyaḥ pāpīyasāṃ cātra phalaṃ bhavati karmaṇām
a niḥśreyasa phalāv eva dharmārthāv itarāv api
c adharmānarthayoḥ prāptiḥ phalaṃ ca pratyavāyikam
a aihalaukikapāratryaṃ karma pumbhir niṣevyate
c karmāṇy api tu kalpyāni labhate kāmam āsthitaḥ
a tatra kḷptam idaṃ rājñā hṛdi kāryaṃ mataṃ ca naḥ
c śatrau hi sāhasaṃ yat syāt kim ivātrāpanīyate
a ekasyaivābhiyāne tu hetur yaḥ prakṛtas tvayā
c tatrāpy anupapannaṃ te vakṣyāmi yad asādhu ca
a yena pūrvaṃ janasthāne bahavo 'tibalā hatāḥ
c rākṣasā rāghavaṃ taṃ tvaṃ katham eko jayiṣyasi
a ye purā nirjitās tena janasthāne mahaujasaḥ
c rākṣasāṃs tān pure sarvān bhītān adyāpi paśyasi
a taṃ siṃham iva saṃkruddhaṃ rāmaṃ daśarathātmajam
c sarpaṃ suptam ivābuddhyā prabodhayitum icchasi
a jvalantaṃ tejasā nityaṃ krodhena ca durāsadam
c kas taṃ mṛtyum ivāsahyam āsādayitum arhati
a saṃśayastham idaṃ sarvaṃ śatroḥ pratisamāsane
c ekasya gamanaṃ tatra na hi me rocate tava
a hīnārthas tu samṛddhārthaṃ ko ripuṃ prākṛto yathā
c niścitaṃ jīvitatyāge vaśam ānetum icchati
a yasya nāsti manuṣyeṣu sadṛśo rākṣasottama
c katham āśaṃsase yoddhuṃ tulyenendravivasvatoḥ
a evam uktvā tu saṃrabdhaṃ kumbhakarṇaṃ mahodaraḥ
c uvāca rakṣasāṃ madhye rāvaṇo lokarāvaṇam
a labdhvā punas tāṃ vaidehīṃ kimarthaṃ tvaṃ prajalpasi
c yadecchasi tadā sītā vaśagā te bhaviṣyati
a dṛṣṭaḥ kaś cid upāyo me sītopasthānakārakaḥ
c rucitaś cet svayā buddhyā rākṣaseśvara taṃ śṛṇu
a ahaṃ dvijihvaḥ saṃhrādī kumbhakarṇo vitardanaḥ
c pañcarāmavadhāyaite niryāntīty avaghoṣaya
a tato gatvā vayaṃ yuddhaṃ dāsyāmas tasya yatnataḥ
c jeṣyāmo yadi te śatrūn nopāyaiḥ kṛtyam asti naḥ
a atha jīvati naḥ śatrur vayaṃ ca kṛtasaṃyugāḥ
c tataḥ samabhipatsyāmo manasā yat samīkṣitum
a vayaṃ yuddhād ihaiṣyāmo rudhireṇa samukṣitāḥ
c vidārya svatanuṃ bāṇai rāmanāmāṅkitaiḥ śitaiḥ
a bhakṣito rāghavo 'smābhir lakṣmaṇaś ceti vādinaḥ
c tava pādau grahīṣyāmas tvaṃ naḥ kāma prapūraya
a tato 'vaghoṣaya pure gajaskandhena pārthiva
c hato rāmaḥ saha bhrātrā sasainya iti sarvataḥ
a prīto nāma tato bhūtvā bhṛtyānāṃ tvam ariṃdama
c bhogāṃś ca parivārāṃś ca kāmāṃś ca vasudāpaya
a tato mālyāni vāsāṃsi vīrāṇām anulepanam
c peyaṃ ca bahu yodhebhyaḥ svayaṃ ca muditaḥ piba
a tato 'smin bahulībhūte kaulīne sarvato gate
c praviśyāśvāsya cāpi tvaṃ sītāṃ rahasi sāntvaya
e dhanadhānyaiś ca kāmaiś ca ratnaiś caināṃ pralobhaya
a anayopadhayā rājan bhayaśokānubandhayā
c akāmā tvadvaśaṃ sītā naṣṭanāthā gamiṣyati
a rañjanīyaṃ hi bhartāraṃ vinaṣṭam avagamya sā
c nairāśyāt strīlaghutvāc ca tvadvaśaṃ pratipatsyate
a sā purā sukhasaṃvṛddhā sukhārhā duḥkhakarṣitā
c tvayy adhīnaḥ sukhaṃ jñātvā sarvathopagamiṣyati
a etat sunītaṃ mama darśanena
rāmaṃ hi dṛṣṭvaiva bhaved anarthaḥ
c ihaiva te setsyati motsuko bhūr
mahān ayuddhena sukhasya lābhaḥ
a anaṣṭasainyo hy anavāptasaṃśayo
ripūn ayuddhena jayañ janādhipa
c yaśaś ca puṇyaṃ ca mahan mahīpate
śriyaṃ ca kīrtiṃ ca ciraṃ samaśnute
a sa tathoktas tu nirbhartsya kumbhakarṇo mahodaram
c abravīd rākṣasaśreṣṭhaṃ bhrātaraṃ rāvaṇaṃ tataḥ
a so 'haṃ tava bhayaṃ ghoraṃ vadhāt tasya durātmanaḥ
c rāmasyādya pramārjāmi nirvairas tvaṃ sukhībhava
a garjanti na vṛthā śūra nirjalā iva toyadāḥ
c paśya saṃpādyamānaṃ tu garjitaṃ yudhi karmaṇā
a na marṣayati cātmānaṃ saṃbhāvayati nātmanā
c adarśayitvā śūrās tu karma kurvanti duṣkaram
a viklavānām abuddhīnāṃ rājñāṃ paṇḍitamāninām
c śṛṇvatām ādita idaṃ tvadvidhānāṃ mahodara
a yuddhe kāpuruṣair nityaṃ bhavadbhiḥ priyavādibhiḥ
c rājānam anugacchadbhiḥ kṛtyam etad vināśitam
a rājaśeṣā kṛtā laṅkā kṣīṇaḥ kośo balaṃ hatam
c rājānam imam āsādya suhṛccihnam amitrakam
a eṣa niryāmy ahaṃ yuddham udyataḥ śatrunirjaye
c durnayaṃ bhavatām adya samīkartuṃ mahāhave
a evam uktavato vākyaṃ kumbhakarṇasya dhīmataḥ
c pratyuvāca tato vākyaṃ prahasan rākṣasādhipaḥ
a mahodaro 'yaṃ rāmāt tu paritrasto na saṃśayaḥ
c na hi rocayate tāta yuddhaṃ yuddhaviśārada
a kaś cin me tvatsamo nāsti sauhṛdena balena ca
c gaccha śatruvadhāya tvaṃ kumbhakarṇajayāya ca
a ādade niśitaṃ śūlaṃ vegāc chatrunibarhaṇaḥ
c sarvakālāyasaṃ dīptaṃ taptakāñcanabhūṣaṇam
a indrāśanisamaṃ bhīmaṃ vajrapratimagauravam
c devadānavagandharvayakṣakiṃnarasūdanam
a raktamālya mahādāma svataś codgatapāvakam
c ādāya niśitaṃ śūlaṃ śatruśoṇitarañjitam
e kumbhakarṇo mahātejā rāvaṇaṃ vākyam abravīt
a gamiṣyāmy aham ekākī tiṣṭhatv iha balaṃ mahat
c adya tān kṣudhitaḥ kruddho bhakṣayiṣyāmi vānarān
a kumbhakarṇavacaḥ śrutvā rāvaṇo vākyam abravīt
c sainyaiḥ parivṛto gaccha śūlamudgalapāṇibhiḥ
a vānarā hi mahātmānaḥ śīghrāś ca vyavasāyinaḥ
c ekākinaṃ pramattaṃ vā nayeyur daśanaiḥ kṣayam
a tasmāt paramadurdharṣaiḥ sainyaiḥ parivṛto vraja
c rakṣasām ahitaṃ sarvaṃ śatrupakṣaṃ nisūdaya
a athāsanāt samutpatya srajaṃ maṇikṛtāntarām
c ābabandha mahātejāḥ kumbhakarṇasya rāvaṇaḥ
a aṅgadān aṅgulīveṣṭān varāṇy ābharaṇāni ca
c hāraṃ ca śaśisaṃkāśam ābabandha mahātmanaḥ
a divyāni ca sugandhīni mālyadāmāni rāvaṇaḥ
c śrotre cāsajjayām āsa śrīmatī cāsya kuṇḍale
a kāñcanāṅgadakeyūro niṣkābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ
c kumbhakarṇo bṛhatkarṇaḥ suhuto 'gnir ivābabhau
a śroṇīsūtreṇa mahatā mecakena virājitaḥ
c amṛtotpādane naddho bhujaṃgeneva mandaraḥ
a sa kāñcanaṃ bhārasahaṃ nivātaṃ
vidyutprabhaṃ dīptam ivātmabhāsā
c ābadhyamānaḥ kavacaṃ rarāja
saṃdhyābhrasaṃvīta ivādrirājaḥ
a sarvābharaṇanaddhāṅgaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ sa rākṣasaḥ
c trivikramakṛtotsāho nārāyaṇa ivābabhau
a bhrātaraṃ saṃpariṣvajya kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇam
c praṇamya śirasā tasmai saṃpratasthe mahābaliḥ
e tam āśīrbhiḥ praśastābhiḥ preṣayām āsa rāvaṇaḥ
a śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣaiḥ sainyaiś cāpi varāyudhaiḥ
c taṃ gajaiś ca turaṃgaiś ca syandanaiś cāmbudasvanaiḥ
e anujagmur mahātmānaṃ rathino rathināṃ varam
a sarpair uṣṭraiḥ kharair aśvaiḥ siṃhadvipamṛgadvijaiḥ
c anujagmuś ca taṃ ghoraṃ kumbhakarṇaṃ mahābalam
a sa puṣpavarṇair avakīryamāṇo
dhṛtātapatraḥ śitaśūlapāṇiḥ
c madotkaṭaḥ śoṇitagandhamatto
viniryayau dānavadevaśatruḥ
a padātayaś a bahavo mahānādā mahābalāḥ
c anvayū rākṣasā bhīmā bhīmākṣāḥ śastrapāṇayaḥ
a raktākṣāḥ sumahākāyā nīlāñjanacayopamāḥ
c śūrān udyamya khaḍgāṃś ca niśitāṃś ca paraśvadhān
a bahuvyāmāṃś ca vipulān kṣepaṇīyān durāsadān
c tālaskandhāṃś ca vipulān kṣepaṇīyān durāsadān
a athānyad vapur ādāya dāruṇaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c niṣpapāta mahātejāḥ kumbhakarṇo mahābalaḥ
a dhanuḥśataparīṇāhaḥ sa ṣaṭśatasamucchitaḥ
c raudraḥ śakaṭacakrākṣo mahāparvatasaṃnibhaḥ
a saṃnipatya ca rakṣāṃsi dagdhaśailopamo mahān
c kumbhakarṇo mahāvaktraḥ prahasann idam abravīt
a adya vānaramukhyānāṃ tāni yūthāni bhāgaśaḥ
c nirdahiṣyāmi saṃkruddhaḥ śalabhān iva pāvakaḥ
a nāparādhyanti me kāmaṃ vānarā vanacāriṇaḥ
c jātir asmadvidhānāṃ sā purodyānavibhūṣaṇam
a purarodhasya mūlaṃ tu rāghavaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
c hate tasmin hataṃ sarvaṃ taṃ vadhiṣyāmi saṃyuge
a evaṃ tasya bruvāṇasya kumbhakarṇasya rākṣasāḥ
c nādaṃ cakrur mahāghoraṃ kampayanta ivārṇavam
a tasya niṣpatatas tūrṇaṃ kumbhakarṇasya dhīmataḥ
c babhūvur ghorarūpāṇi nimittāni samantataḥ
a ulkāśaniyutā meghā vineduś ca sudāruṇāḥ
c sasāgaravanā caiva vasudhā samakampata
a ghorarūpāḥ śivā neduḥ sajvālakavalair mukhaiḥ
c maṇḍalāny apasavyāni babandhuś ca vihaṃgamāḥ
a niṣpapāta ca gṛdhre 'sya śūle vai pathi gacchataḥ
c prāsphuran nayanaṃ cāsya savyo bāhur akampata
a niṣpapāta tadā coklā jvalantī bhīmanisvanā
c ādityo niṣprabhaś cāsīn na pravāti sukho 'nilaḥ
a acintayan mahotpātān utthitāṃl lomaharṣaṇān
c niryayau kumbhakarṇas tu kṛtāntabalacoditaḥ
a sa laṅghayitvā prākāraṃ padbhyāṃ parvatasaṃnibhaḥ
c dadarśābhraghanaprakhyaṃ vānarānīkam adbhutam
a te dṛṣṭvā rākṣasaśreṣṭhaṃ vānarāḥ parvatopamam
c vāyununnā iva ghanā yayuḥ sarvā diśas tadā
a tad vānarānīkam atipracaṇḍaṃ
diśo dravad bhinnam ivābhrajālam
c sa kumbhakarṇaḥ samavekṣya harṣān
nanāda bhūyo ghanavad ghanābhaḥ
a te tasya ghoraṃ ninadaṃ niśamya
yathā ninādaṃ divi vāridasya
c petur dharaṇyāṃ bahavaḥ plavaṃgā
nikṛttamūlā iva sālavṛkṣāḥ
a vipulaparighavān sa kumbhakarṇo
ripunidhanāya viniḥsṛto mahātmā
c kapi gaṇabhayam ādadat subhīmaṃ
prabhur iva kiṃkaradaṇḍavān yugānte
a sa nanāda mahānādaṃ samudram abhinādayan
c janayann iva nirghātān vidhamann iva parvatān
a tam avadhyaṃ maghavatā yamena varuṇena ca
c prekṣya bhīmākṣam āyāntaṃ vānarā vipradudruvuḥ
a tāṃs tu vidravato dṛṣṭvā vāliputro 'ṅgado 'bravīt
c nalaṃ nīlaṃ gavākṣaṃ ca kumudaṃ ca mahābalam
a ātmānam atra vismṛtya vīryāṇy abhijanāni ca
c kva gacchata bhayatrastāḥ prākṛtā harayo yathā
a sādhu saumyā nivartadhvaṃ kiṃ prāṇān parirakṣatha
c nālaṃ yuddhāya vai rakṣo mahatīyaṃ vibhīṣikāḥ
a mahatīm utthitām enāṃ rākṣasānāṃ vibhīṣikām
c vikramād vidhamiṣyāmo nivartadhvaṃ plavaṃgamāḥ
a kṛcchreṇa tu samāśvāsya saṃgamya ca tatas tataḥ
c vṛkṣādrihastā harayaḥ saṃpratasthū raṇājiram
a te nivṛtya tu saṃkruddhāḥ kumbhakarṇaṃ vanaukasaḥ
c nijaghnuḥ paramakruddhāḥ samadā iva kuñjarāḥ
e prāṃśubhir giriśṛṅgaiś ca śilābhiś ca mahābalāḥ
a pādapaiḥ puṣpitāgraiś ca hanyamāno na kampate
c tasya gātreṣu patitā bhidyante śataśaḥ śilāḥ
e pādapāḥ puṣpitāgrāś ca bhagnāḥ petur mahītale
a so 'pi sainyāni saṃkruddho vānarāṇāṃ mahaujasām
c mamantha paramāyatto vanāny agnir ivotthitaḥ
a lohitārdrās tu bahavaḥ śerate vānararṣabhāḥ
c nirastāḥ patitā bhūmau tāmrapuṣpā iva drumāḥ
a laṅghayantaḥ pradhāvanto vānarā nāvalokayan
c ke cit samudre patitāḥ ke cid gaganam āśritāḥ
a vadhyamānās tu te vīrā rākṣasena balīyasā
c sāgaraṃ yena te tīrṇāḥ pathā tenaiva dudruvuḥ
a te sthalāni tathā nimnaṃ viṣaṇṇavadanā bhayāt
c ṛkṣā vṛkṣān samārūḍhāḥ ke cit parvatam āśritāḥ
a mamajjur arṇave ke cid guhāḥ ke cit samāśritāḥ
c niṣeduḥ plavagāḥ ke cit ke cin naivāvatasthire
a tān samīkṣyāṅgado bhaṅgān vānarān idam abravīt
c avatiṣṭhata yudhyāmo nivartadhvaṃ plavaṃgamāḥ
a bhagnānāṃ vo na paśyāmi parigamya mahīm imām
c sthānaṃ sarve nivartadhvaṃ kiṃ prāṇān parirakṣatha
a nirāyudhānāṃ dravatām asaṃgagatipauruṣāḥ
c dārā hy apahasiṣyanti sa vai ghātas tu jīvitām
a kuleṣu jātāḥ sarve sma vistīrṇeṣu mahatsu ca
c anāryāḥ khalu yad bhītās tyaktvā vīryaṃ pradhāvata
a vikatthanāni vo yāni yadā vai janasaṃsadi
c tāni vaḥ kva ca yatāni sodagrāṇi mahānti ca
a bhīrupravādāḥ śrūyante yas tu jīvati dhikkṛtaḥ
c mārgaḥ satpuruṣair juṣṭaḥ sevyatāṃ tyajyatāṃ bhayam
a śayāmahe vā nihatāḥ pṛthivyām alpajīvitāḥ
c duṣprāpaṃ brahmalokaṃ vā prāpnumo yudhi sūditāḥ
e saṃprāpnuyāmaḥ kīrtiṃ vā nihatya śatrum āhave
a na kumbhakarṇaḥ kākutsthaṃ dṛṣṭvā jīvan gamiṣyati
c dīpyamānam ivāsādya pataṃgo jvalanaṃ yathā
a palāyanena coddiṣṭāḥ prāṇān rakṣāmahe vayam
c ekena bahavo bhagnā yaśo nāśaṃ gamiṣyati
a evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ taṃ śūram aṅgadaṃ kanakāṅgadam
c dravamāṇās tato vākyam ūcuḥ śūravigarhitam
a kṛtaṃ naḥ kadanaṃ ghoraṃ kumbhakarṇena rakṣasā
c na sthānakālo gacchāmo dayitaṃ jīvitaṃ hi naḥ
a etāvad uktvā vacanaṃ sarve te bhejire diśaḥ
c bhīmaṃ bhīmākṣam āyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā vānarayūthapāḥ
a dravamāṇās tu te vīrā aṅgadena valīmukhāḥ
c sāntvaiś ca bahumānaiś ca tataḥ sarve nivartitāḥ
a ṛṣabhaśarabhamaindadhūmranīlāḥ
kumudasuṣeṇagavākṣarambhatārāḥ
c dvividapanasavāyuputramukhyās
tvaritatarābhimukhaṃ raṇaṃ prayātāḥ
a te nivṛttā mahākāyāḥ śrutvāṅgadavacas tadā
c naiṣṭhikīṃ buddhim āsthāya sarve saṃgrāmakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
a samudīritavīryās te samāropitavikramāḥ
c paryavasthāpitā vākyair aṅgadena valīmukhāḥ
a prayātāś ca gatā harṣaṃ maraṇe kṛtaniścayāḥ
c cakruḥ sutumulaṃ yuddhaṃ vānarās tyaktajīvitāḥ
a atha vṛkṣān mahākāyāḥ sānūni sumahānti ca
c vānarās tūrṇam udyamya kumbhakarṇam abhidravan
a sa kumbhakarṇaḥ saṃkruddho gadām udyamya vīryavān
c ardayan sumahākāyaḥ samantād vyākṣipad ripūn
a śatāni sapta cāṣṭau ca sahasrāṇi ca vānarāḥ
c prakīrṇāḥ śerate bhūmau kumbhakarṇena pothitāḥ
a ṣoḍaśāṣṭau ca daśa ca viṃśat triṃśat tathaiva ca
c parikṣipya ca bāhubhyāṃ khādan viparidhāvati
e bhakṣayan bhṛśasaṃkruddho garuḍaḥ pannagān iva
a hanūmāñ śailaśṛṅgāṇi vṛkṣāṃś ca vividhān bahūn
c vavarṣa kumbhakarṇasya śirasy ambaram āsthitaḥ
a tāni parvataśṛṅgāṇi śūlena tu bibheda ha
c babhañja vṛkṣavarṣaṃ ca kumbhakarṇo mahābalaḥ
a tato harīṇāṃ tad anīkam ugraṃ
dudrāva śūlaṃ niśitaṃ pragṛhya
c tasthau tato 'syāpatataḥ purastān
mahīdharāgraṃ hanumān pragṛhya
a sa kumbhakarṇaṃ kupito jaghāna
vegena śailottamabhīmakāyam
c sa cukṣubhe tena tadābhibūto
medārdragātro rudhirāvasiktaḥ
a sa śūlam āvidhya taḍitprakāśaṃ
giriṃ yathā prajvalitāgraśṛṅgam
c bāhvantare mārutim ājaghāna
guho 'calaṃ krauñcam ivograśaktyā
a sa śūlanirbhinna mahābhujāntaraḥ
pravihvalaḥ śoṇitam udvaman mukhāt
c nanāda bhīmaṃ hanumān mahāhave
yugāntameghastanitasvanopamam
a tato vineduḥ sahasā prahṛṣṭā
rakṣogaṇās taṃ vyathitaṃ samīkṣya
c plavaṃgamās tu vyathitā bhayārtāḥ
pradudruvuḥ saṃyati kumbhakarṇāt
a nīlaś cikṣepa śailāgraṃ kumbhakarṇāya dhīmate
c tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya muṣṭinābhijaghāna ha
a muṣṭiprahārābhihataṃ tac chailāgraṃ vyaśīryata
c savisphuliṅgaṃ sajvālaṃ nipapāta mahītale
a ṛṣabhaḥ śarabho nīlo gavākṣo gandhamādanaḥ
c pañcavānaraśārdūlāḥ kumbhakarṇam upādravan
a śailair vṛkṣais talaiḥ pādair muṣṭibhiś ca mahābalāḥ
c kumbhakarṇaṃ mahākāyaṃ sarvato 'bhinijaghnire
a sparśān iva prahārāṃs tān vedayāno na vivyathe
c ṛṣabhaṃ tu mahāvegaṃ bāhubhyāṃ pariṣasvaje
a kumbhakarṇabhujābhyāṃ tu pīḍito vānararṣabhaḥ
c nipapātarṣabho bhīmaḥ pramukhāgataśoṇitaḥ
a muṣṭinā śarabhaṃ hatvā jānunā nīlam āhave
c ājaghāna gavākṣaṃ ca talenendraripus tadā
a dattapraharavyathitā mumuhuḥ śoṇitokṣitāḥ
c nipetus te tu medinyāṃ nikṛttā iva kiṃśukāḥ
a teṣu vānaramukhyeṣu patiteṣu mahātmasu
c vānarāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi kumbhakarṇaṃ pradudruvuḥ
a taṃ śailam iva śailābhāḥ sarve tu plavagarṣabhāḥ
c samāruhya samutpatya dadaṃśuś ca mahābalāḥ
a taṃ nakhair daśanaiś cāpi muṣṭibhir jānubhis tathā
c kumbhakarṇaṃ mahākāyaṃ te jaghnuḥ plavagarṣabhāḥ
a sa vānarasahasrais tair ācitaḥ parvatopamaḥ
c rarāja rākṣasavyāghro girir ātmaruhair iva
a bāhubhyāṃ vānarān sarvān pragṛhya sa mahābalaḥ
c bhakṣayām āsa saṃkruddho garuḍaḥ pannagān iva
a prakṣiptāḥ kumbhakarṇena vaktre pātālasaṃnibhe
c nāsā puṭābhyāṃ nirjagmuḥ karṇābhyāṃ caiva vānarāḥ
a bhakṣayan bhṛśasaṃkruddho harīn parvatasaṃnibhaḥ
c babhañja vānarān sarvān saṃkruddho rākṣasottamaḥ
a māṃsaśoṇitasaṃkledāṃ bhūmiṃ kurvan sa rākṣasaḥ
c cacāra harisainyeṣu kālāgnir iva mūrchitaḥ
a vajrahasto yathā śakraḥ pāśahasta ivāntakaḥ
c śūlahasto babhau tasmin kumbhakarṇo mahābalaḥ
a yathā śuṣkāṇy araṇyāni grīṣme dahati pāvakaḥ
c tathā vānarasainyāni kumbhakarṇo vinirdahat
a tatas te vadhyamānās tu hatayūthā vināyakāḥ
c vānarā bhayasaṃvignā vinedur visvaraṃ bhṛśam
a anekaśo vadhyamānāḥ kumbhakarṇena vānarāḥ
c rāghavaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagmur vyathitāḥ khinnacetasaḥ
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya kumbhakarṇaṃ mahābalam
c utpapāta tadā vīraḥ sugrīvo vānarādhipaḥ
a sa parvatāgram utkṣipya samāvidhya mahākapiḥ
c abhidudrāva vegena kumbhakarṇaṃ mahābalam
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya kumbhakarṇaḥ plavaṃgamam
c tasthau vivṛtasarvāṅgo vānarendrasya saṃmukhaḥ
a kapiśoṇitadigdhāṅgaṃ bhakṣayantaṃ mahākapīn
c kumbhakarṇaṃ sthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sugrīvo vākyam abravīt
a pātitāś ca tvayā vīrāḥ kṛtaṃ karma suduṣkaram
c bhakṣitāni ca sainyāni prāptaṃ te paramaṃ yaśaḥ
a tyaja tad vānarānīkaṃ prākṛtaiḥ kiṃ kariṣyasi
c sahasvaikaṃ nipātaṃ me parvatasyāsya rākṣasa
a tad vākyaṃ harirājasya sattvadhairyasamanvitam
c śrutvā rākṣasaśārdūlaḥ kumbhakarṇo 'bravīd vacaḥ
a prajāpates tu pautras tvaṃ tathaivarkṣarajaḥsutaḥ
c śrutapauruṣasaṃpannas tasmād garjasi vānara
a sa kumbhakarṇasya vaco niśamya
vyāvidhya śailaṃ sahasā mumoca
c tenājaghānorasi kumbhakarṇaṃ
śailena vajrāśanisaṃnibhena
a tac chailaśṛṅgaṃ sahasā vikīrṇaṃ
bhujāntare tasya tadā viśāle
c tato viṣeduḥ sahasā plavaṃgamā
rakṣogaṇāś cāpi mudā vineduḥ
a sa śailaśṛṅgābhihataś cukopa
nanāda kopāc ca vivṛtya vaktram
c vyāvidhya śūlaṃ ca taḍitprakāśaṃ
cikṣepa haryṛkṣapater vadhāya
a tat kumbhakarṇasya bhujapraviddhaṃ
śūlaṃ śitaṃ kāñcanadāmajuṣṭam
c kṣipraṃ samutpatya nigṛhya dorbhyāṃ
babhañja vegena suto 'nilasya
a kṛtaṃ bhārasahasrasya śūlaṃ kālāyasaṃ mahat
c babhañja janaum āropya prahṛṣṭaḥ plavagarṣabhaḥ
a sa tat tadā bhagnam avekṣya śūlaṃ
cukopa rakṣo'dhipatir mahātmā
c utpāṭya laṅkāmalayāt sa śṛṅgaṃ
jaghāna sugrīvam upetya tena
a sa śailaśṛṅgābhihato visaṃjñaḥ
papāta bhūmau yudhi vānarendraḥ
c taṃ prekṣya bhūmau patitaṃ visaṃjñaṃ
neduḥ prahṛṣṭā yudhi yātudhānāḥ
a tam abhyupetyādbhutaghoravīryaṃ
sa kumbhakarṇo yudhi vānarendram
c jahāra sugrīvam abhipragṛhya
yathānilo megham atipracaṇḍaḥ
a sa taṃ mahāmeghanikāśarūpam
utpāṭya gacchan yudhi kumbhakarṇaḥ
c rarāja merupratimānarūpo
merur yathātyucchritaghoraśṛṅgaḥ
a tataḥ samutpāṭya jagāma vīraḥ
saṃstūyamāno yudhi rākṣasendraiḥ
c śṛṇvan ninādaṃ tridaśālayānāṃ
plavaṃgarājagrahavismitānām
a tatas tam ādāya tadā sa mene
harīndram indropamam indravīryaḥ
c asmin hṛte sarvam idaṃ hṛtaṃ syāt
sarāghavaṃ sainyam itīndraśatruḥ
a vidrutāṃ vāhinīṃ dṛṣṭvā vānarāṇāṃ tatas tataḥ
c kumbhakarṇena sugrīvaṃ gṛhītaṃ cāpi vānaram
a hanūmāṃś cintayām āsa matimān mārutātmajaḥ
c evaṃ gṛhīte sugrīve kiṃ kartavyaṃ mayā bhavet
a yad vai nyāyyaṃ mayā kartuṃ tat kariṣyāmi sarvathā
c bhūtvā parvatasaṃkāśo nāśayiṣyāmi rākṣasaṃ
a mayā hate saṃyati kumbhakarṇe
mahābale muṣṭiviśīrṇadehe
c vimocite vānarapārthive ca
bhavantu hṛṣṭāḥ pravagāḥ samagrāḥ
a atha vā svayam apy eṣa mokṣaṃ prāpsyati pārthivaḥ
c gṛhīto 'yaṃ yadi bhavet tridaśaiḥ sāsuroragaiḥ
a manye na tāvad ātmānaṃ budhyate vānarādhipaḥ
c śailaprahārābhihataḥ kumbhakarṇena saṃyuge
a ayaṃ muhūrtāt sugrīvo labdhasaṃjño mahāhave
c ātmano vānarāṇāṃ ca yat pathyaṃ tat kariṣyati
a mayā tu mokṣitasyāsya sugrīvasya mahātmanaḥ
c aprītaś ca bhavet kaṣṭā kīrtināśaś ca śāśvataḥ
a tasmān muhūrtaṃ kāṅkṣiṣye vikramaṃ pārthivasya naḥ
c bhinnaṃ ca vānarānīkaṃ tāvad āśvāsayāmy aham
a ity evaṃ cintayitvā tu hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
c bhūyaḥ saṃstambhayām āsa vānarāṇāṃ mahācamūm
a sa kumbhakarṇo 'tha viveśa laṅkāṃ
sphurantam ādāya mahāhariṃ tam
c vimānacaryāgṛhagopurasthaiḥ
puṣpāgryavarṣair avakīryamāṇaḥ
a tataḥ sa saṃjñām upalabhya kṛcchrād
balīyasas tasya bhujāntarasthaḥ
c avekṣamāṇaḥ purarājamārgaṃ
vicintayām āsa muhur mahātmā
a evaṃ gṛhītena kathaṃ nu nāma
śakyaṃ mayā saṃprati kartum adya
c tathā kariṣyāmi yathā harīṇāṃ
bhaviṣyatīṣṭaṃ ca hitaṃ ca kāryam
a tataḥ karāgraiḥ sahasā sametya
rājā harīṇām amarendraśatroḥ
c nakhaiś ca karṇau daśanaiś ca nāsāṃ
dadaṃśa pārśveṣu ca kumbhakarṇam
a sa kumbhakarṇau hṛtakarṇanāso
vidāritas tena vimarditaś ca
c roṣābhibhūtaḥ kṣatajārdragātraḥ
sugrīvam āvidhya pipeṣa bhūmau
a sa bhūtale bhīmabalābhipiṣṭaḥ
surāribhis tair abhihanyamānaḥ
c jagāma khaṃ vegavad abhyupetya
punaś ca rāmeṇa samājagāma
a karṇanāsā vihīnasya kumbhakarṇo mahābalaḥ
c rarāja śoṇitotsikto giriḥ prasravaṇair iva
a tataḥ sa puryāḥ sahasā mahātmā
niṣkramya tad vānarasainyam ugram
c babhakṣa rakṣo yudhi kumbhakarṇaḥ
prajā yugāntāgnir iva pradīptaḥ
a bubhukṣitaḥ śoṇitamāṃsagṛdhnuḥ
praviśya tad vānarasainyam ugram
c cakhāda rakṣāṃsi harīn piśācān
ṛkṣāṃś ca mohād yudhi kumbhakarṇaḥ
a ekaṃ dvau trīn bahūn kruddho vānarān saha rākṣasaiḥ
c samādāyaikahastena pracikṣepa tvaran mukhe
a saṃprasravaṃs tadā medaḥ śoṇitaṃ ca mahābalaḥ
c vadhyamāno nagendrāgrair bhakṣayām āsa vānarān
e te bhakṣyamāṇā harayo rāmaṃ jagmus tadā gatim
a tasmin kāle sumitrāyāḥ putraḥ parabalārdanaḥ
c cakāra lakṣmaṇaḥ kruddho yuddhaṃ parapuraṃjayaḥ
a sa kumbhakarṇasya śarāñ śarīre sapta vīryavān
c nicakhānādade cānyān visasarja ca lakṣmaṇaḥ
a atikramya ca saumitriṃ kumbhakarṇo mahābalaḥ
c rāmam evābhidudrāva dārayann iva medinīm
a atha dāśarathī rāmo raudram astraṃ prayojayan
c kumbhakarṇasya hṛdaye sasarja niśitāñ śarān
a tasya rāmeṇa viddhasya sahasābhipradhāvataḥ
c aṅgāramiśrāḥ kruddhasya mukhān niścerur arciṣaḥ
a tasyorasi nimagnāś ca śarā barhiṇavāsasaḥ
c hastāc cāsya paribhraṣṭā papātorvyāṃ mahāgadā
a sa nirāyudham ātmānaṃ yadā mene mahābalaḥ
c muṣṭibhyāṃ cāraṇābhyāṃ ca cakāra kadanaṃ mahat
a sa bāṇair atividdhāṅgaḥ kṣatajena samukṣitaḥ
c rudhiraṃ parisusrāva giriḥ prasravaṇān iva
a sa tīvreṇa ca kopena rudhireṇa ca mūrchitaḥ
c vānarān rākṣasān ṛkṣān khādan viparidhāvati
a tasmin kāle sa dharmātmā lakṣmaṇo rāmam abravīt
c kumbhakarṇavadhe yukto yogān parimṛśan bahūn
a naivāyaṃ vānarān rājan na vijānāti rākṣasān
c mattaḥ śoṇitagandhena svān parāṃś caiva khādati
a sādhv enam adhirohantu sarvato vānararṣabhāḥ
c yūthapāś ca yathāmukhyās tiṣṭhantv asya samantataḥ
a apy ayaṃ durmatiḥ kāle gurubhāraprapīḍitaḥ
c prapatan rākṣaso bhūmau nānyān hanyāt plavaṃgamān
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rājaputrasya dhīmataḥ
c te samāruruhur hṛṣṭāḥ kumbhakarṇaṃ plavaṃgamāḥ
a kumbhakarṇas tu saṃkruddhaḥ samārūḍhaḥ plavaṃgamaiḥ
c vyadhūnayat tān vegena duṣṭahastīva hastipān
a tān dṛṣṭvā nirdhūtān rāmo ruṣṭo 'yam iti rākṣasaḥ
c samutpapāta vegena dhanur uttamam ādade
a sa cāpam ādāya bhujaṃgakalpaṃ
dṛḍhajyam ugraṃ tapanīyacitram
c harīn samāśvāsya samutpapāta
rāmo nibaddhottamatūṇabāṇaḥ
a sa vānaragaṇais tais tu vṛtaḥ paramadurjayaḥ
c lakṣmaṇānucaro rāmaḥ saṃpratasthe mahābalaḥ
a sa dadarśa mahātmānaṃ kirīṭinam ariṃdamam
c śoṇitāplutasarvāṅgaṃ kumbhakarṇaṃ mahābalam
a sarvān samabhidhāvantaṃ yathāruṣṭaṃ diśā gajam
c mārgamāṇaṃ harīn kruddhaṃ rākṣasaiḥ parivāritam
a vindhyamandarasaṃkāśaṃ kāñcanāṅgadabhūṣaṇam
c sravantaṃ rudhiraṃ vaktrād varṣamegham ivotthitam
a jihvayā parilihyantaṃ śoṇitaṃ śoṇitokṣitam
c mṛdnantaṃ vānarānīkaṃ kālāntakayamopamam
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasaśreṣṭhaṃ pradīptānalavarcasaṃ
c visphārayām āsa tadā kārmukaṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
a sa tasya cāpanirghoṣāt kupito nairṛtarṣabhaḥ
c amṛṣyamāṇas taṃ ghoṣam abhidudrāva rāghavam
a tatas tu vātoddhatameghakalpaṃ
bhujaṃgarājottamabhogabāhum
c tam āpatantaṃ dharaṇīdharābham
uvāca rāmo yudhi kumbhakarṇam
a āgaccha rakṣo'dhipamā viṣādam
avasthito 'haṃ pragṛhītacāpaḥ
c avehi māṃ śakrasapatna rāmam
ayaṃ muhūrtād bhavitā vicetāḥ
a rāmo 'yam iti vijñāya jahāsa vikṛtasvanam
c pātayann iva sarveṣāṃ hṛdayāni vanaukasām
a prahasya vikṛtaṃ bhīmaṃ sa meghasvanitopamam
c kumbhakarṇo mahātejā rāghavaṃ vākyam abravīt
a nāhaṃ virādho vijñeyo na kabandhaḥ kharo na ca
c na vālī na ca mārīcaḥ kumbhakarṇo 'ham āgataḥ
a paśya me mudgaraṃ ghoraṃ sarvakālāyasaṃ mahat
c anena nirjitā devā dānavāś ca mayā purā
a vikarṇanāsa iti māṃ nāvajñātuṃ tvam arhasi
c svalpāpi hi na me pīḍā karṇanāsāvināśanāt
a darśayekṣvākuśārdūla vīryaṃ gātreṣu me laghu
c tatas tvāṃ bhakṣayiṣyāmi dṛṣṭapauruṣavikramam
a sa kumbhakarṇasya vaco niśamya
rāmaḥ supuṅkhān visasarja bāṇān
c tair āhato vajrasamapravegair
na cukṣubhe na vyathate surāriḥ
a yaiḥ sāyakaiḥ sālavarā nikṛttā
vālī hato vānarapuṃgavaś ca
c te kumbhakarṇasya tadā śarīraṃ
vajropamā na vyathayāṃ pracakruḥ
a sa vāridhārā iva sāyakāṃs tān
pibañ śarīreṇa mahendraśatruḥ
c jaghāna rāmasya śarapravegaṃ
vyāvidhya taṃ mudgaram ugravegam
a tatas tu rakṣaḥ kṣatajānuliptaṃ
vitrāsanaṃ devamahācamūnām
c vyāvidhya taṃ mudgaram ugravegaṃ
vidrāvayām āsa camūṃ harīṇām
a vāyavyam ādāya tato varāstraṃ
rāmaḥ pracikṣepa niśācarāya
c samudgaraṃ tena jahāra bāhuṃ
sa kṛttabāhus tumulaṃ nanāda
a sa tasya bāhur giriśṛṅgakalpaḥ
samudgaro rāghavabāṇakṛttaḥ
c papāta tasmin harirājasainye
jaghāna tāṃ vānaravāhinīṃ ca
a te vānarā bhagnahatāvaśeṣāḥ
paryantam āśritya tadā viṣaṇṇāḥ
c pravepitāṅgā dadṛśuḥ sughoraṃ
narendrarakṣo'dhipasaṃnipātam
a sa kumbhakarṇo 'stranikṛttabāhur
mahān nikṛttāgra ivācalendraḥ
c utpāṭayām āsa kareṇa vṛkṣaṃ
tato 'bhidudrāva raṇe narendram
a taṃ tasya bāhuṃ saha sālavṛkṣaṃ
samudyataṃ pannagabhogakalpam
c aindrāstrayuktena jahāra rāmo
bāṇena jāmbūnadacitritena
a sa kumbhakarṇasya bhujo nikṛttaḥ
papāta bhūmau girisaṃnikāśaḥ
c viveṣṭamāno nijaghāna vṛkṣāñ
śailāñ śilāvānararākṣasāṃś ca
a taṃ chinnabāhuṃ samavekṣya rāmaḥ
samāpatantaṃ sahasā nadantam
c dvāv ardhacandrau niśitau pragṛhya
ciccheda pādau yudhi rākṣasasya
a nikṛttabāhur vinikṛttapādo
vidārya vaktraṃ vaḍavāmukhābham
c dudrāva rāmaṃ sahasābhigarjan
rāhur yathā candram ivāntarikṣe
a apūrayat tasya mukhaṃ śitāgrai
rāmaḥ śarair hemapinaddhapuṅkhaiḥ
c sa pūrṇavaktro na śaśāka vaktuṃ
cukūja kṛcchreṇa mumoha cāpi
a athādade sūryamarīcikalpaṃ
sa brahmadaṇḍāntakakālakalpam
c ariṣṭam aindraṃ niśitaṃ supuṅkhaṃ
rāmaḥ śaraṃ mārutatulyavegam
a taṃ vajrajāmbūnadacārupuṅkhaṃ
pradīptasūryajvalanaprakāśam
c mahendravajrāśanitulyavegaṃ
rāmaḥ pracikṣepa niśācarāya
a sa sāyako rāghavabāhucodito
diśaḥ svabhāsā daśa saṃprakāśayan
c vidhūmavaiśvānaradīptadarśano
jagāma śakrāśanitulyavikramaḥ
a sa tan mahāparvatakūṭasaṃnibhaṃ
vivṛttadaṃṣṭraṃ calacārukuṇḍalam
c cakarta rakṣo'dhipateḥ śiras tadā
yathaiva vṛtrasya purā puraṃdaraḥ
a tad rāmabāṇābhihataṃ papāta
rakṣaḥśiraḥ parvatasaṃnikāśam
c babhañja caryāgṛhagopurāṇi
prākāram uccaṃ tam apātayac ca
a tac cātikāyaṃ himavatprakāśaṃ
rakṣas tadā toyanidhau papāta
c grāhān mahāmīnacayān bhujaṃgamān
mamarda bhūmiṃ ca tathā viveśa
a tasmir hate brāhmaṇadevaśatrau
mahābale saṃyati kumbhakarṇe
c cacāla bhūr bhūmidharāś ca sarve
harṣāc ca devās tumulaṃ praṇeduḥ
a tatas tu devarṣimaharṣipannagāḥ
surāś ca bhūtāni suparṇaguhyakāḥ
c sayakṣagandharvagaṇā nabhogatāḥ
praharṣitā rāma parākrameṇa
a praharṣam īyur bahavas tu vānarāḥ
prabuddhapadmapratimair ivānanaiḥ
c apūjayan rāghavam iṣṭabhāginaṃ
hate ripau bhīmabale durāsade
a sa kumbhakarṇaṃ surasainyamardanaṃ
mahatsu yuddheṣv aparājitaśramam
c nananda hatvā bharatāgrajo raṇe
mahāsuraṃ vṛtram ivāmarādhipaḥ
a kumbhakarṇaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā rāghaveṇa mahātmanā
c rākṣasā rākṣasendrāya rāvaṇāya nyavedayan
a śrutvā vinihataṃ saṃkhye kumbhakarṇaṃ mahābalam
c rāvaṇaḥ śokasaṃtapto mumoha ca papāta ca
a pitṛvyaṃ nihataṃ śrutvā devāntakanarāntakau
c triśirāś cātikāyaś ca ruruduḥ śokapīḍitāḥ
a bhrātaraṃ nihataṃ śrutvā rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇā
c mahodaramahāpārśvau śokākrāntau babhūvatuḥ
a tataḥ kṛcchrāt samāsādya saṃjñāṃ rākṣasapuṃgavaḥ
c kumbhakarṇavadhād dīno vilalāpa sa rāvaṇaḥ
a hā vīra ripudarpaghna kumbhakarṇa mahābala
c śatrusainyaṃ pratāpyaikaḥ kva māṃ saṃtyajya gacchasi
a idānīṃ khalv ahaṃ nāsmi yasya me patito bhujaḥ
c dakṣiṇo yaṃ samāśritya na bibhemi surāsurān
a katham evaṃvidho vīro devadānavadarpahā
c kālāgnipratimo hy adya rāghaveṇa raṇe hataḥ
a yasya te vajraniṣpeṣo na kuryād vyasanaṃ sadā
c sa kathaṃ rāmabāṇārtaḥ prasupto 'si mahītale
a ete devagaṇāḥ sārdham ṛṣibhir gagane sthitāḥ
c nihataṃ tvāṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā ninadanti praharṣitāḥ
a dhruvam adyaiva saṃhṛṣṭā labdhalakṣyāḥ plavaṃgamāḥ
c ārokṣyantīha durgāṇi laṅkādvārāṇi sarvaśaḥ
a rājyena nāsti me kāryaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi sītayā
c kumbhakarṇavihīnasya jīvite nāsti me ratiḥ
a yady ahaṃ bhrātṛhantāraṃ na hanmi yudhi rāghavam
c nanu me maraṇaṃ śreyo na cedaṃ vyarthajīvitam
a adyaiva taṃ gamiṣyāmi deśaṃ yatrānujo mama
c na hi bhrātṝn samutsṛjya kṣaṇaṃ jīvitum utsahe
a devā hi māṃ hasiṣyanti dṛṣṭvā pūrvāpakāriṇam
c katham indraṃ jayiṣyāmi kumbhakarṇahate tvayi
a tad idaṃ mām anuprāptaṃ vibhīṣaṇavacaḥ śubham
c yad ajñānān mayā tasya na gṛhītaṃ mahātmanaḥ
a vibhīṣaṇavaco yāvat kumbhakarṇaprahastayoḥ
c vināśo 'yaṃ samutpanno māṃ vrīḍayati dāruṇaḥ
a tasyāyaṃ karmaṇaḥ prāto vipāko mama śokadaḥ
c yan mayā dhārmikaḥ śrīmān sa nirasto vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a iti bahuvidham ākulāntarātmā
kṛpaṇam atīva vilapya kumbhakarṇam
c nyapatad atha daśānano bhṛśārtas
tam anujam indraripuṃ hataṃ viditvā
a evaṃ vilapamānasya rāvaṇasya durātmanaḥ
c śrutvā śokābhitaptasya triśirā vākyam abravīt
a evam eva mahāvīryo hato nas tāta madhyamaḥ
c na tu satpuruṣā rājan vilapanti yathā bhavān
a nūnaṃ tribhuvaṇasyāpi paryāptas tvam asi prabho
c sa kasmāt prākṛta iva śokasyātmānam īdṛśam
a brahmadattāsti te śaktiḥ kavacaḥ sāyako dhanuḥ
c sahasrakharasaṃyukto ratho meghasamasvanaḥ
a tvayāsakṛd viśastreṇa viśastā devadānavāḥ
c sa sarvāyudhasaṃpanno rāghavaṃ śāstum arhasi
a kāmaṃ tiṣṭha mahārājanirgamiṣyāmy ahaṃ raṇam
c uddhariṣyāmi te śatrūn garuḍaḥ pannagān iha
a śambaro devarājena narako viṣṇunā yathā
c tathādya śayitā rāmo mayā yudhi nipātitaḥ
a śrutvā triśiraso vākyaṃ rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ
c punar jātam ivātmānaṃ manyate kālacoditaḥ
a śrutvā triśiraso vākyaṃ devāntakanarāntakau
c atikāyaś ca tejasvī babhūvur yuddhaharṣitāḥ
a tato 'ham aham ity evaṃ garjanto nairṛtarṣabhāḥ
c rāvaṇasya sutā vīrāḥ śakratulyaparākramāḥ
a antarikṣacarāḥ sarve sarve māyā viśāradāḥ
c sarve tridaśadarpaghnāḥ sarve ca raṇadurmadāḥ
a sarve 'strabalasaṃpannāḥ sarve vistīrṇa kīrtayaḥ
c sarve samaram āsādya na śrūyante sma nirjitāḥ
a sarve 'straviduṣo vīrāḥ sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥ
c sarve pravarajijñānāḥ sarve labdhavarās tathā
a sa tais tathā bhāskaratulyavarcasaiḥ
sutair vṛtaḥ śatrubalapramardanaiḥ
c rarāja rājā maghavān yathāmarair
vṛto mahādānavadarpanāśanaiḥ
a sa putrān saṃpariṣvajya bhūṣayitvā ca bhūṣaṇaiḥ
c āśīrbhiś ca praśastābhiḥ preṣayām āsa saṃyuge
a mahodaramahāpārśvau bhrātarau cāpi rāvaṇaḥ
c rakṣaṇārthaṃ kumārāṇāṃ preṣayām āsa saṃyuge
a te 'bhivādya mahātmānaṃ rāvaṇaṃ ripurāvaṇam
c kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ caiva mahākāyāḥ pratasthire
a sarvauṣadhībhir gandhaiś ca samālabhya mahābalāḥ
c nirjagmur nairṛtaśreṣṭhāḥ ṣaḍ ete yuddhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
a tataḥ sudarśanaṃ nāma nīlajīmūtasaṃnibham
c airāvatakule jātam āruroha mahodaraḥ
a sarvāyudhasamāyuktaṃ tūṇībhiś ca svalaṃkṛtam
c rarāja gajam āsthāya savitevāstamūrdhani
a hayottamasamāyuktaṃ sarvāyudhasamākulam
c āruroha rathaśreṣṭhaṃ triśirā rāvaṇātmajaḥ
a triśirā ratham āsthāya virarāja dhanurdharaḥ
c savidyudulkaḥ sajvālaḥ sendracāpa ivāmbudaḥ
a tribhiḥ kirīṭais triśirāḥ śuśubhe sa rathottame
c himavān iva śailendras tribhiḥ kāñcanaparvataiḥ
a atikāyo 'pi tejasvī rākṣasendrasutas tadā
c āruroha rathaśreṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvadhanuṣmatām
a sucakrākṣaṃ susaṃyuktaṃ sānukarṣaṃ sakūbaram
c tūṇībāṇāsanair dīptaṃ prāsāsi parighākulam
a sa kāñcanavicitreṇa kirīṭena virājatā
c bhūṣaṇaiś ca babhau meruḥ prabhābhir iva bhāsvaraḥ
a sa rarāja rathe tasmin rājasūnur mahābalaḥ
c vṛto nairṛtaśārdūlair vajrapāṇir ivāmaraiḥ
a hayam uccaiḥśravaḥ prakhyaṃ śvetaṃ kanakabhūṣaṇam
c manojavaṃ mahākāyam āruroha narāntakaḥ
a gṛhītvā prāsam uklābhaṃ virarāja narāntakaḥ
c śaktim ādāya tejasvī guhaḥ śatruṣv ivāhave
a devāntakaḥ samādāya parighaṃ vajrabhūṣaṇam
c parigṛhya giriṃ dorbhyāṃ vapur viṣṇor viḍambayan
a mahāpārśvo mahātejā gadām ādāya vīryavān
c virarāja gadāpāṇiḥ kubera iva saṃyuge
a te pratasthur mahātmāno balair apratimair vṛtāḥ
c surā ivāmarāvatyāṃ balair apratimair vṛtāḥ
a tān gajaiś ca turaṃgaiś ca rathaiś cāmbudanisvanaiḥ
c anujagmur mahātmāno rākṣasāḥ pravarāyudhāḥ
a te virejur mahātmāno kumārāḥ sūryavarcasaḥ
c kirīṭinaḥ śriyā juṣṭā grahā dīptā ivāmbare
a pragṛhītā babhau teṣāṃ chatrāṇām āvaliḥ sitā
c śāradābhrapratīkāśāṃ haṃsāvalir ivāmbare
a maraṇaṃ vāpi niścitya śatrūṇāṃ vā parājayam
c iti kṛtvā matiṃ vīrā nirjagmuḥ saṃyugārthinaḥ
a jagarjuś ca praṇeduś ca cikṣipuś cāpi sāyakān
c jahṛṣuś ca mahātmāno niryānto yuddhadurmadāḥ
a kṣveḍitāsphoṭaninadaiḥ saṃcacāleva medinī
c rakṣasāṃ siṃhanādaiś ca pusphoṭeva tadāmbaram
a te 'bhiniṣkramya muditā rākṣasendrā mahābalāḥ
c dadṛśur vānarānīkaṃ samudyataśilānagam
a harayo 'pi mahātmāno dadṛśur nairṛtaṃ balam
c hastyaśvarathasaṃbādhaṃ kiṅkiṇīśatanāditam
a nīlajīmūtasaṃkāśaṃ samudyatamahāyudham
c dīptānalaraviprakhyair nairṛtaiḥ sarvato vṛtam
a tad dṛṣṭvā balam āyāntaṃ labdhalakṣyāḥ plavaṃgamāḥ
c samudyatamahāśailāḥ saṃpraṇedur muhur muhuḥ
a tataḥ samudghuṣṭaravaṃ niśamya
rakṣogaṇā vānarayūthapānām
c amṛṣyamāṇāḥ paraharṣam ugraṃ
mahābalā bhīmataraṃ vineduḥ
a te rākṣasabalaṃ ghoraṃ praviśya hariyūthapāḥ
c vicerur udyataiḥ śailair nagāḥ śikhariṇo yathā
a ke cid ākāśam āviśya ke cid urvyāṃ plavaṃgamāḥ
c rakṣaḥsainyeṣu saṃkruddhāś cerur drumaśilāyudhāḥ
a te pādapaśilāśailaiś cakrur vṛṣṭim anuttamām
c bāṇaughair vāryamāṇāś ca harayo bhīmavikramāḥ
a siṃhanādān vineduś ca raṇe rākṣasavānarāḥ
c śilābhiś cūrṇayām āsur yātudhānān plavaṃgamāḥ
a nijaghnuḥ saṃyuge kruddhāḥ kavacābharaṇāvṛtān
c ke cid rathagatān vīrān gajavājigatān api
a nijaghnuḥ sahasāplutya yātudhānān plavaṃgamāḥ
c śailaśṛṅganipātaiś ca muṣṭibhir vāntalocanāḥ
e celuḥ petuś ca neduś ca tatra rākṣasapuṃgavāḥ
a tataḥ śailaiś ca khaḍgaiś ca visṛṣṭair harirākṣasaiḥ
c muhūrtenāvṛtā bhūmir abhavac choṇitāplutā
a vikīrṇaparvatākārai rakṣobhir arimardanaiḥ
c ākṣiptāḥ kṣipyamāṇāś ca bhagnaśūlāś ca vānaraiḥ
a vānarān vānarair eva jagnus te rajanīcarāḥ
c rākṣasān rākṣasair eva jaghnus te vānarā api
a ākṣipya ca śilās teṣāṃ nijaghnū rākṣasā harīn
c teṣāṃ cācchidya śastrāṇi jaghnū rakṣāṃsi vānarāḥ
a nijaghnuḥ śailaśūlāstrair vibhiduś ca parasparam
c siṃhanādān vineduś ca raṇe vānararākṣasāḥ
a chinnavarmatanutrāṇā rākṣasā vānarair hatāḥ
c rudhiraṃ prasrutās tatra rasasāram iva drumāḥ
a rathena ca rathaṃ cāpi vāraṇena ca vāraṇam
c hayena ca hayaṃ ke cin nijaghnur vānarā raṇe
a kṣuraprair ardhacandraiś ca bhallaiś ca niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c rākṣasā vānarendrāṇāṃ cicchiduḥ pādapāñ śilāḥ
a vikīrṇaiḥ parvatāgraiś ca drumaiś chinnaiś ca saṃyuge
c hataiś ca kapirakṣobhir durgamā vasudhābhavat
a tasmin pravṛtte tumule vimarde
prahṛṣyamāṇeṣu valī mukheṣu
c nipātyamāneṣu ca rākṣaseṣu
maharṣayo devagaṇāś ca neduḥ
a tato hayaṃ mārutatulyavegam
āruhya śaktiṃ niśitāṃ pragṛhya
c narāntako vānararājasainyaṃ
mahārṇavaṃ mīna ivāviveśa
a sa vānarān saptaśatāni vīraḥ
prāsena dīptena vinirbibheda
c ekaḥ kṣaṇenendraripur mahātmā
jaghāna sainyaṃ haripuṃgavānām
a dadṛśuś ca mahātmānaṃ hayapṛṣṭhe pratiṣṭhitam
c carantaṃ harisainyeṣu vidyādharamaharṣayaḥ
a sa tasya dadṛśe mārgo māṃsaśoṇitakardamaḥ
c patitaiḥ parvatākārair vānarair abhisaṃvṛtaḥ
a yāvad vikramituṃ buddhiṃ cakruḥ plavagapuṃgavāḥ
c tāvad etān atikramya nirbibheda narāntakaḥ
a jvalantaṃ prāsam udyamya saṃgrāmānte narāntakaḥ
c dadāha harisainyāni vanānīva vibhāvasuḥ
a yāvad utpāṭayām āsur vṛkṣāñ śailān vanaukasaḥ
c tāvat prāsahatāḥ petur vajrakṛttā ivācalāḥ
a dikṣu sarvāsu balavān vicacāra narāntakaḥ
c pramṛdnan sarvato yuddhe prāvṛṭkāle yathānilaḥ
a na śekur dhāvituṃ vīrā na sthātuṃ spandituṃ kutaḥ
c utpatantaṃ sthitaṃ yāntaṃ sarvān vivyādha vīryavān
a ekenāntakakalpena prāsenādityatejasā
c bhinnāni harisainyāni nipetur dharaṇītale
a vajraniṣpeṣasadṛśaṃ prāsasyābhinipātanam
c na śekur vānarāḥ soḍhuṃ te vinedur mahāsvanam
a patatāṃ harivīrāṇāṃ rūpāṇi pracakāśire
c vajrabhinnāgrakūṭānāṃ śailānāṃ patatām iva
a ye tu pūrvaṃ mahātmānaḥ kumbhakarṇena pātitāḥ
c te 'svasthā vānaraśreṣṭhāḥ sugrīvam upatasthire
a viprekṣamāṇaḥ sugrīvo dadarśa harivāhinīm
c narāntakabhayatrastāṃ vidravantīm itas tataḥ
a vidrutāṃ vāhinīṃ dṛṣṭvā sa dadarśa narāntakam
c gṛhītaprāsam āyāntaṃ hayapṛṣṭhe pratiṣṭhitam
a athovāca mahātejāḥ sugrīvo vānarādhipaḥ
c kumāram aṅgadaṃ vīraṃ śakratulyaparākramam
a gacchainaṃ rākṣasaṃ vīra yo 'sau turagam āsthitaḥ
c kṣobhayantaṃ haribalaṃ kṣipraṃ prāṇair viyojaya
a sa bhartur vacanaṃ śrutvā niṣpapātāṅgadas tadā
c anīkān meghasaṃkāśān meghānīkād ivāṃśumān
a śailasaṃghātasaṃkāśo harīṇām uttamo 'ṅgadaḥ
c rarājāṅgadasaṃnaddhaḥ sadhātur iva parvataḥ
a nirāyudho mahātejāḥ kevalaṃ nakhadaṃṣṭravān
c narāntakam abhikramya vāliputro 'bravīd vacaḥ
a tiṣṭha kiṃ prākṛtair ebhir haribhis tvaṃ kariṣyasi
c asmin vajrasamasparśe prāsaṃ kṣipa mamorasi
a aṅgadasya vacaḥ śrutvā pracukrodha narāntakaḥ
c saṃdaśya daśanair oṣṭhaṃ niśvasya ca bhujaṃgavat
a sa prāsam āvidhya tadāṅgadāya
samujjvalantaṃ sahasotsasarja
c sa vāliputrorasi vajrakalpe
babhūva bhagno nyapatac ca bhūmau
a taṃ prāsam ālokya tadā vibhagnaṃ
suparṇakṛttoragabhogakalpam
c talaṃ samudyamya sa vāliputras
turaṃgamasyābhijaghāna mūrdhni
a nimagnapādaḥ sphuṭitākṣi tāro
niṣkrāntajihvo 'calasaṃnikāśaḥ
c sa tasya vājī nipapāta bhūmau
talaprahāreṇa vikīrṇamūrdhā
a narāntakaḥ krodhavaśaṃ jagāma
hataṃ turagaṃ patitaṃ nirīkṣya
c sa muṣṭim udyamya mahāprabhāvo
jaghāna śīrṣe yudhi vāliputram
a athāṅgado muṣṭivibhinnamūrdhā
susrāva tīvraṃ rudhiraṃ bhṛśoṣṇam
c muhur vijajvāla mumoha cāpi
saṃjñāṃ samāsādya visiṣmiye ca
a athāṅgado vajrasamānavegaṃ
saṃvartya muṣṭiṃ giriśṛṅgakalpam
c nipātayām āsa tadā mahātmā
narāntakasyorasi vāliputraḥ
a sa muṣṭiniṣpiṣṭavibhinnavakṣā
jvālāṃ vamañ śoṇitadigdhagātraḥ
c narāntako bhūmitale papāta
yathācalo vajranipātabhagnaḥ
a athāntarikṣe tridaśottamānāṃ
vanaukasāṃ caiva mahāpraṇādaḥ
c babhūva tasmin nihate 'gryavīre
narāntake vālisutena saṃkhye
a athāṅgado rāmamanaḥ praharṣaṇaṃ
suduṣkaraṃ taṃ kṛtavān hi vikramam
c visiṣmiye so 'py ativīrya vikramaḥ
punaś ca yuddhe sa babhūva harṣitaḥ
a narāntakaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā cukruśur nairṛtarṣabhāḥ
c devāntakas trimūrdhā ca paulastyaś ca mahodaraḥ
a ārūḍho meghasaṃkāśaṃ vāraṇendraṃ mahodaraḥ
c vāliputraṃ mahāvīryam abhidudrāva vīryavān
a bhrātṛvyasanasaṃtaptas tadā devāntako balī
c ādāya parighaṃ dīptam aṅgadaṃ samabhidravat
a ratham ādityasaṃkāśaṃ yuktaṃ paramavājibhiḥ
c āsthāya triśirā vīro vāliputram athābhyayāt
a sa tribhir devadarpaghnair nairṛtendrair abhidrutaḥ
c vṛkṣam utpāṭayām āsa mahāviṭapam aṅgadaḥ
a devāntakāya taṃ vīraś cikṣepa sahasāṅgadaḥ
c mahāvṛkṣaṃ mahāśākhaṃ śakro dīptam ivāśanim
a triśirās taṃ praciccheda śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥ
c sa vṛkṣaṃ kṛttam ālokya utpapāta tato 'ṅgadaḥ
a sa vavarṣa tato vṛkṣāñ śilāś ca kapikuñjaraḥ
c tān praciccheda saṃkruddhas triśirā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a parighāgreṇa tān vṛkṣān babhañja ca surāntakaḥ
c triśirāś cāṅgadaṃ vīram abhidudrāva sāyakaiḥ
a gajena samabhidrutya vāliputraṃ mahodaraḥ
c jaghānorasi saṃkruddhas tomarair vajrasaṃnibhaiḥ
a devāntakaś ca saṃkruddhaḥ parigheṇa tadāṅgadam
c upagamyābhihatyāśu vyapacakrāma vegavān
a sa tribhir nairṛtaśreṣṭhair yugapat samabhidrutaḥ
c na vivyathe mahātejā vāliputraḥ pratāpavān
a talena bhṛśam utpatya jaghānāsya mahāgajam
c petatur locane tasya vinanāda sa vāraṇaḥ
a viṣāṇaṃ cāsya niṣkṛṣya vāliputro mahābalaḥ
c devāntakam abhidrutya tāḍayām āsa saṃyuge
a sa vihvalitasarvāṅgo vātoddhata iva drumaḥ
c lākṣārasasavarṇaṃ ca susrāva rudhiraṃ mukhāt
a athāśvāsya mahātejāḥ kṛcchrād devāntako balī
c āvidhya parighaṃ ghoram ājaghāna tadāṅgadam
a parighābhihataś cāpi vānarendrātmajas tadā
c jānubhyāṃ patito bhūmau punar evotpapāta ha
a samutpatantaṃ triśirās tribhir āśīviṣopamaiḥ
c ghorair haripateḥ putraṃ lalāṭe 'bhijaghāna ha
a tato 'ṅgadaṃ parikṣiptaṃ tribhir nairṛtapuṃgavaiḥ
c hanūmān api vijñāya nīlaś cāpi pratasthatuḥ
a tataś cikṣepa śailāgraṃ nīlas triśirase tadā
c tad rāvaṇasuto dhīmān bibheda niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tad bāṇaśatanirbhinnaṃ vidāritaśilātalam
c savisphuliṅgaṃ sajvālaṃ nipapāta gireḥ śiraḥ
a tato jṛmbhitam ālokya harṣād devāntakas tadā
c parigheṇābhidudrāva mārutātmajam āhave
a tam āpatantam utpatya hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
c ājaghāna tadā mūrdhni vajravegena muṣṭinā
a sa muṣṭiniṣpiṣṭavikīrṇamūrdhā
nirvāntadantākṣivilambijihvaḥ
c devāntako rākṣasarājasūnur
gatāsur urvyāṃ sahasā papāta
a tasmin hate rākṣasayodhamukhye
mahābale saṃyati devaśatrau
c kruddhas trimūrdhā niśitāgram ugraṃ
vavarṣa nīlorasi bāṇavarṣam
a sa taiḥ śaraughair abhivarṣyamāṇo
vibhinnagātraḥ kapisainyapālaḥ
c nīlo babhūvātha visṛṣṭagātro
viṣṭambhitas tena mahābalena
a tatas tu nīlaḥ pratilabhya saṃjñāṃ
śailaṃ samutpāṭya savṛkṣaṣaṇḍam
c tataḥ samutpatya bhṛśogravego
mahodaraṃ tena jaghāna mūrdhni
a tataḥ sa śailābhinipātabhagno
mahodaras tena saha dvipena
c vipothito bhūmitale gatāsuḥ
papāta varjābhihato yathādriḥ
a pitṛvyaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā triśirāś cāpam ādade
c hanūmantaṃ ca saṃkruddho vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a hanūmāṃs tu samutpatya hayāṃs triśirasas tadā
c vidadāra nakhaiḥ kruddho gajendraṃ mṛgarāḍ iva
a atha śaktiṃ samādāya kālarātrim ivāntakaḥ
c cikṣepānilaputrāya triśirā rāvaṇātmajaḥ
a divi kṣiptām ivolkāṃ tāṃ śaktiṃ kṣiptām asaṃgatām
c gṛhītvā hariśārdūlo babhañja ca nanāda ca
a tāṃ dṛṣṭvā ghorasaṃkāśāṃ śaktiṃ bhagnāṃ hanūmatā
c prahṛṣṭā vānaragaṇā vinedur jaladā iva
a tataḥ khaḍgaṃ samudyamya triśirā rākṣasottamaḥ
c nicakhāna tadā roṣād vānarendrasya vakṣasi
a khaḍgaprahārābhihato hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
c ājaghāna trimūrdhānaṃ talenorasi vīryavān
a sa talabhihatas tena srastahastāmbaro bhuvi
c nipapāta mahātejās triśirās tyaktacetanaḥ
a sa tasya patataḥ khaḍgaṃ samācchidya mahākapiḥ
c nanāda girisaṃkāśas trāsayan sarvanairṛtān
a amṛṣyamāṇas taṃ ghoṣam utpapāta niśācaraḥ
c utpatya ca hanūmantaṃ tāḍayām āsa muṣṭinā
a tena muṣṭiprahāreṇa saṃcukopa mahākapiḥ
c kupitaś ca nijagrāha kirīṭe rākṣasarṣabham
a sa tasya śīrṣāṇy asinā śitena
kirīṭajuṣṭāni sakuṇḍalāni
c kruddhaḥ praciccheda suto 'nilasya
tvaṣṭuḥ sutasyeva śirāṃsi śakraḥ
a tāny āyatākṣāṇy agasaṃnibhāni
pradīptavaiśvānaralocanāni
c petuḥ śirāṃsīndraripor dharaṇyāṃ
jyotīṃṣi muktāni yathārkamārgāt
a tasmin hate devaripau triśīrṣe
hanūmata śakraparākrameṇa
c neduḥ plavaṃgāḥ pracacāla bhūmī
rakṣāṃsy atho dudruvire samantāt
a hataṃ triśirasaṃ dṛṣṭvā tathaiva ca mahodaram
c hatau prekṣya durādharṣau devāntakanarāntakau
a cukopa paramāmarṣī mahāpārśvo mahābalaḥ
c jagrāhārciṣmatīṃ cāpi gadāṃ sarvāyasīṃ śubhām
a hemapaṭṭaparikṣiptāṃ māṃsaśoṇitalepanām
c virājamānāṃ vapuṣā śatruśoṇitarañjitām
a tejasā saṃpradīptāgrāṃ raktamālyavibhūṣitām
c airāvatamahāpadmasārvabhauma bhayāvahām
a gadām ādāya saṃkruddho mahāpārśvo mahābalaḥ
c harīn samabhidudrāva yugāntāgnir iva jvalan
a atharṣayaḥ samutpatya vānaro ravaṇānujam
c mahāpārśvam upāgamya tasthau tasyāgrato balī
a taṃ purastāt sthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā vānaraṃ parvatopamam
c ājaghānorasi kruddho gadayā vajrakalpayā
a sa tayābhihatas tena gadayā vānararṣabhaḥ
c bhinnavakṣāḥ samādhūtaḥ susrāva rudhiraṃ bahu
a sa saṃprāpya cirāt saṃjñām ṛṣabho vānararṣabhaḥ
c kruddho visphuramāṇauṣṭho mahāpārśvam udaikṣata
a tāṃ gṛhītvā gadāṃ bhīmām āvidhya ca punaḥ punaḥ
c mattānīkaṃ mahāpārśvaṃ jaghāna raṇamūrdhani
a sa svayā gadayā bhinno vikīrṇadaśanekṣaṇaḥ
c nipapāta mahāpārśvo vajrāhata ivācalaḥ
a tasmin hate bhrātari rāvaṇasya
tan nairṛtānāṃ balam arṇavābham
c tyaktāyudhaṃ kevalajīvitārthaṃ
dudrāva bhinnārṇavasaṃnikāśam
a svabalaṃ vyathitaṃ dṛṣṭvā tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c bhrātṝṃś ca nihatān dṛṣṭvā śakratulyaparākramān
a pitṛvyau cāpi saṃdṛśya samare saṃniṣūditau
c mahodaramahāpārśvau bhrātarau rākṣasarṣabhau
a cukopa ca mahātejā brahmadattavaro yudhi
c atikāyo 'drisaṃkāśo devadānavadarpahā
a sa bhāskarasahasrasya saṃghātam iva bhāsvaram
c ratham āsthāya śakrārir abhidudrāva vānarān
a sa visphārya mahac cāpaṃ kirīṭī mṛṣṭakuṇḍalaḥ
c nāma viśrāvayām āsa nanāda ca mahāsvanam
a tena siṃhapraṇādena nāmaviśrāvaṇena ca
c jyāśabdena ca bhīmena trāsayām āsa vānarān
a te tasya rūpam ālokya yathā viṣṇos trivikrame
c bhayārtā vānarāḥ sarve vidravanti diśo daśa
a te 'tikāyaṃ samāsādya vānarā mūḍhacetasaḥ
c śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagmur lakṣmaṇāgrajam āhave
a tato 'tikāyaṃ kākutstho rathasthaṃ parvatopamam
c dadarśa dhanvinaṃ dūrād garjantaṃ kālameghavat
a sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā mahātmānaṃ rāghavas tu suvismitaḥ
c vānarān sāntvayitvā tu vibhīṣaṇam uvāca ha
a ko 'sau parvatasaṃkāśo dhanuṣmān harilocanaḥ
c yukte hayasahasreṇa viśāle syandane sthitaḥ
a ya eṣa niśitaiḥ śūlaiḥ sutīkṣṇaiḥ prāsatomaraiḥ
c arciṣmadbhir vṛto bhāti bhūtair iva maheśvaraḥ
a kālajihvāprakāśābhir ya eṣo 'bhivirājate
c āvṛto rathaśaktībhir vidyudbhir iva toyadaḥ
a dhanūṃsi cāsya sajyāni hemapṛṣṭhāni sarvaśaḥ
c śobhayanti rathaśreṣṭhaṃ śakrapātam ivāmbaram
a ka eṣa rakṣaḥ śārdūlo raṇabhūmiṃ virājayan
c abhyeti rathināṃ śreṣṭho rathenādityatejasā
a dhvajaśṛṅgapratiṣṭhena rāhuṇābhivirājate
c sūryaraśmiprabhair bāṇair diśo daśa virājayan
a triṇataṃ meghanirhrādaṃ hemapṛṣṭham alaṃkṛtam
c śatakratudhanuḥprakhyaṃ dhanuś cāsya virājate
a sadhvajaḥ sapatākaś ca sānukarṣo mahārathaḥ
c catuḥsādisamāyukto meghastanitanisvanaḥ
a viṃśatir daśa cāṣṭau ca tūṇīraratham āsthitāḥ
c kārmukāṇi ca bhīmāni jyāś ca kāñcanapiṅgalāḥ
a dvau ca khaḍgau rathagatau pārśvasthau pārśvaśobhinau
c caturhastatsarucitau vyaktahastadaśāyatau
a raktakaṇṭhaguṇo dhīro mahāparvatasaṃnibhaḥ
c kālaḥ kālamahāvaktro meghastha iva bhāskaraḥ
a kāñcanāṅgadanaddhābhyāṃ bhujābhyām eṣa śobhate
c śṛṅgābhyām iva tuṅgābhyāṃ himavān parvatottamaḥ
a kuṇḍalābhyāṃ tu yasyaitad bhāti vaktraṃ śubhekṣaṇam
c punarvasvantaragataṃ pūrṇabimbam ivaindavam
a ācakṣva me mahābāho tvam enaṃ rākṣasottamam
c yaṃ dṛṣṭvā vānarāḥ sarve bhayārtā vidrutā diśaḥ
a sa pṛṣṭho rājaputreṇa rāmeṇāmitatejasā
c ācacakṣe mahātejā rāghavāya vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a daśagrīvo mahātejā rājā vaiśravaṇānujaḥ
c bhīmakarmā mahotsāho rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ
a tasyāsīd vīryavān putro rāvaṇapratimo raṇe
c vṛddhasevī śrutadharaḥ sarvāstraviduṣāṃ varaḥ
a aśvapṛṣṭhe rathe nāge khaḍge dhanuṣi karṣaṇe
c bhede sāntve ca dāne ca naye mantre ca saṃmataḥ
a yasya bāhuṃ samāśritya laṅkā bhavati nirbhayā
c tanayaṃ dhānyamālinyā atikāyam imaṃ viduḥ
a etenārādhito brahmā tapasā bhāvitātmanā
c astrāṇi cāpy avāptāni ripavaś ca parājitāḥ
a surāsurair avadhyatvaṃ dattam asmai svayambhuvā
c etac ca kavacaṃ divyaṃ rathaś caiṣo 'rkabhāskaraḥ
a etena śataśo devā dānavāś ca parājitāḥ
c rakṣitāni ca rakṣāmi yakṣāś cāpi niṣūditāḥ
a vajraṃ viṣṭambhitaṃ yena bāṇair indrasya dhīmataḥ
c pāśaḥ salilarājasya yuddhe pratihatas tathā
a eṣo 'tikāyo balavān rākṣasānām atharṣabhaḥ
c rāvaṇasya suto dhīmān devadanava darpahā
a tad asmin kriyatāṃ yatnaḥ kṣipraṃ puruṣapuṃgava
c purā vānarasainyāni kṣayaṃ nayati sāyakaiḥ
a tato 'tikāyo balavān praviśya harivāhinīm
c visphārayām āsa dhanur nanāda ca punaḥ punaḥ
a taṃ bhīmavapuṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā rathasthaṃ rathināṃ varam
c abhipetur mahātmāno ye pradhānāḥ plavaṃgamāḥ
a kumudo dvivido maindo nīlaḥ śarabha eva ca
c pādapair giriśṛṅgaiś ca yugapat samabhidravan
a teṣāṃ vṛkṣāṃś ca śailāṃś ca śaraiḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c atikāyo mahātejāś cicchedāstravidāṃ varaḥ
a tāṃś caiva sarān sa harīñ śaraiḥ sarvāyasair balī
c vivyādhābhimukhaḥ saṃkhye bhīmakāyo niśācaraḥ
a te 'rditā bāṇabarṣeṇa bhinnagātrāḥ plavaṃgamāḥ
c na śekur atikāyasya pratikartuṃ mahāraṇe
a tat sainyaṃ harivīrāṇāṃ trāsayām āsa rākṣasaḥ
c mṛgayūtham iva kruddho harir yauvanam āsthitaḥ
a sa rāṣasendro harisainyamadhye
nāyudhyamānaṃ nijaghāna kaṃ cit
c upetya rāmaṃ sadhanuḥ kalāpī
sagarvitaṃ vākyam idaṃ babhāṣe
a rathe sthito 'haṃ śaracāpapāṇir
na prākṛtaṃ kaṃ cana yodhayāmi
c yasyāsti śaktir vyavasāya yuktā
dadātuṃ me kṣipram ihādya yuddham
a tat tasya vākyaṃ bruvato niśamya
cukopa saumitrir amitrahantā
c amṛṣyamāṇaś ca samutpapāta
jagrāha cāpaṃ ca tataḥ smayitvā
a kruddhaḥ saumitrir utpatya tūṇād ākṣipya sāyakam
c purastād atikāyasya vicakarṣa mahad dhanuḥ
a pūrayan sa mahīṃ śailān ākāśaṃ sāgaraṃ diśaḥ
c jyāśabdo lakṣmaṇasyogras trāsayan rajanīcarān
a saumitreś cāpanirghoṣaṃ śrutvā pratibhayaṃ tadā
c visiṣmiye mahātejā rākṣasendrātmajo balī
a athātikāyaḥ kupito dṛṣṭvā lakṣmaṇam utthitam
c ādāya niśitaṃ bāṇam idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a bālas tvam asi saumitre vikrameṣv avicakṣaṇaḥ
c gaccha kiṃ kālasadṛśaṃ māṃ yodhayitum icchasi
a na hi madbāhusṛṣṭānām astrāṇāṃ himavān api
c soḍhum utsahate vegam antarikṣam atho mahī
a sukhaprasuptaṃ kālāgniṃ prabodhayitum icchasi
c nyasya cāpaṃ nivartasva mā prāṇāñ jahi madgataḥ
a atha vā tvaṃ pratiṣṭabdho na nivartitum icchasi
c tiṣṭha prāṇān parityajya gamiṣyasi yamakṣayam
a paśya me niśitān bāṇān aridarpaniṣūdanān
c īśvarāyudhasaṃkāśāṃs taptakāñcanabhūṣaṇān
a eṣa te sarpasaṃkāśo bāṇaḥ pāsyati śoṇitam
c mṛgarāja iva kruddho nāgarājasya śoṇitam
a śrutvātikāyasya vacaḥ saroṣaṃ
sagarvitaṃ saṃyati rājaputraḥ
c sa saṃcukopātibalo bṛhacchrīr
uvāca vākyaṃ ca tato mahārtham
a na vākyamātreṇa bhavān pradhāno
na katthanāt satpuruṣā bhavanti
c mayi sthite dhanvini bāṇapāṇau
vidarśayasvātmabalaṃ durātman
a karmaṇā sūcayātmānaṃ na vikatthitum arhasi
c pauruṣeṇa tu yo yuktaḥ sa tu śūra iti smṛtaḥ
a sarvāyudhasamāyukto dhanvī tvaṃ ratham āsthitaḥ
c śarair vā yadi vāpy astrair darśayasva parākramam
a tataḥ śiras te niśitaiḥ pātayiṣyāmy ahaṃ śaraiḥ
c mārutaḥ kālasaṃpakvaṃ vṛntāt tālaphalaṃ yathā
a adya te māmakā bāṇās taptakāñcanabhūṣaṇāḥ
c pāsyanti rudhiraṃ gātrād bāṇaśalyāntarotthitam
a bālo 'yam iti vijñāya na māvajñātum arhasi
c bālo vā yadi vā vṛddho mṛtyuṃ jānīhi saṃyuge
a lakṣmaṇasya vacaḥ śrutvā hetumat paramārthavat
c atikāyaḥ pracukrodha bāṇaṃ cottamam ādade
a tato vidyādharā bhūtā devā daityā maharṣayaḥ
c guhyakāś ca mahātmānas tad yuddhaṃ dadṛśus tadā
a tato 'tikāyaḥ kupitaś cāpam āropya sāyakam
c lakṣmaṇasya pracikṣepa saṃkṣipann iva cāmbaram
a tam āpatantaṃ niśitaṃ śaram āśīviṣopamam
c ardhacandreṇa ciccheda lakṣmaṇaḥ paravīrahā
a taṃ nikṛttaṃ śaraṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛttabhogam ivoragam
c atikāyo bhṛśaṃ kruddhaḥ pañcabāṇān samādade
a tāñ śarān saṃpracikṣepa lakṣmaṇāya niśācaraḥ
c tān aprāptāñ śarais tīkṣṇaiś ciccheda bharatānujaḥ
a sa tāṃś chittvā śarais tīkṣṇair lakṣmaṇaḥ paravīrahā
c ādade niśitaṃ bāṇaṃ jvalantam iva tejasā
a tam ādāya dhanuḥ śreṣṭhe yojayām āsa lakṣmaṇaḥ
c vicakarṣa ca vegena visasarja ca sāyakam
a pūrṇāyatavisṛṣṭena śareṇānata parvaṇā
c lalāṭe rākṣasaśreṣṭham ājaghāna sa vīryavān
a sa lalāṭe śaro magnas tasya bhīmasya rakṣasaḥ
c dadṛśe śoṇitenāktaḥ pannagendra ivāhave
a rākṣasaḥ pracakampe ca lakṣmaṇeṣu prakampitaḥ
c rudrabāṇahataṃ bhīmaṃ yathā tripuragopuram
a cintayām āsa cāśvasya vimṛśya ca mahābalaḥ
c sādhu bāṇanipātena śvāghanīyo 'si me ripuḥ
a vicāryaivaṃ vinamyāsyaṃ vinamya ca bhujāv ubhau
c sa rathopastham āsthāya rathena pracacāra ha
a ekaṃ trīn pañca sapteti sāyakān rākṣasarṣabhaḥ
c ādade saṃdadhe cāpi vicakarṣotsasarja ca
a te bāṇāḥ kālasaṃkāśā rākṣasendradhanuś cyutāḥ
c hemapuṅkhā raviprakhyāś cakrur dīptam ivāmbaram
a tatas tān rākṣasotsṛṣṭāñ śaraughān rāvaṇānujaḥ
c asaṃbhrāntaḥ praciccheda niśitair bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ
a tāñ śarān yudhi saṃprekṣya nikṛttān rāvaṇātmajaḥ
c cukopa tridaśendrārir jagrāha niśitaṃ śaram
a sa saṃdhāya mahātejās taṃ bāṇaṃ sahasotsṛjat
c tataḥ saumitrim āyāntam ājaghāna stanāntare
a atikāyena saumitris tāḍito yudhi vakṣasi
c susrāva rudhiraṃ tīvraṃ madaṃ matta iva dvipaḥ
a sa cakāra tadātmānaṃ viśalyaṃ sahasā vibhuḥ
c jagrāha ca śaraṃ tīṣṇam astreṇāpi samādadhe
a āgneyena tadāstreṇa yojayām āsa sāyakam
c sa jajvāla tadā bāṇo dhanuś cāsya mahātmanaḥ
a atikāyo 'titejasvī sauram astraṃ samādade
c tena bāṇaṃ bhujaṃgābhaṃ hemapuṅkham ayojayat
a tatas taṃ jvalitaṃ ghoraṃ lakṣmaṇaḥ śaram āhitam
c atikāyāya cikṣepa kāladaṇḍam ivāntakaḥ
a āgneyenābhisaṃyuktaṃ dṛṣṭvā bāṇaṃ niśācaraḥ
c utsasarja tadā bāṇaṃ dīptaṃ sūryāstrayojitam
a tāv ubhāv ambare bāṇāv anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ
c tejasā saṃpradīptāgrau kruddhāv iva bhujaṃ gamau
a tāv anyonyaṃ vinirdahya petatur dharaṇītale
c nirarciṣau bhasmakṛtau na bhrājete śarottamau
a tato 'tikāyaḥ saṃkruddhas tv astram aiṣīkam utsṛjat
c tat praciccheda saumitrir astram aindreṇa vīryavān
a aiṣīkaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā kumāro rāvaṇātmajaḥ
c yāmyenāstreṇa saṃkruddho yojayām āsa sāyakam
a tatas tad astraṃ cikṣepa lakṣmaṇāya niśācaraḥ
c vāyavyena tad astraṃ tu nijaghāna sa lakṣmaṇaḥ
a athainaṃ śaradhārābhir dhārābhir iva toyadaḥ
c abhyavarṣata saṃkruddho lakṣmaṇo rāvaṇātmajam
a te 'tikāyaṃ samāsādya kavace vajrabhūṣite
c bhagnāgraśalyāḥ sahasā petur bāṇā mahītale
a tān moghān abhisaṃprekṣya lakṣmaṇaḥ paravīrahā
c abhyavarṣata bāṇānāṃ sahasreṇa mahāyaśāḥ
a sa varṣyamāṇo bāṇaughair atikāyo mahābalaḥ
c avadhyakavacaḥ saṃkhye rākṣaso naiva vivyathe
a na śaśāka rujaṃ kartuṃ yudhi tasya narottamaḥ
c athainam abhyupāgamya vāyur vākyam uvāca ha
a brahmadattavaro hy eṣa avadhya kavacāvṛtaḥ
c brāhmeṇāstreṇa bhindhy enam eṣa vadhyo hi nānyathā
a tataḥ sa vāyor vacanaṃ niśamya
saumitrir indrapratimānavīryaḥ
c samādade bāṇam amoghavegaṃ
tad brāhmam astraṃ sahasā niyojya
a tasmin varāstre tu niyujyamāne
saumitriṇā bāṇavare śitāgre
c diśaḥ sacandrārkamahāgrahāś ca
nabhaś ca tatrāsa rarāsa corvī
a taṃ brahmaṇo 'streṇa niyujya cāpe
śaraṃ supuṅkhaṃ yamadūtakalpam
c saumitrir indrārisutasya tasya
sasarja bāṇaṃ yudhi vajrakalpam
a taṃ lakṣmaṇotsṛṣṭam amoghavegaṃ
samāpatantaṃ jvalanaprakāśam
c suvarṇavajrottamacitrapuṅkhaṃ
tadātikāyaḥ samare dadarśa
a taṃ prekṣamāṇaḥ sahasātikāyo
jaghāna bāṇair niśitair anekaiḥ
c sa sāyakas tasya suparṇavegas
tadātivegena jagāma pārśvam
a tam āgataṃ prekṣya tadātikāyo
bāṇaṃ pradīptāntakakālakalpam
c jaghāna śaktyṛṣṭigadākuṭhāraiḥ
śūlair halaiś cāpy avipannaceṣṭaḥ
a tāny āyudhāny adbhutavigrahāṇi
moghāni kṛtvā sa śaro 'gnidīptaḥ
c prasahya tasyaiva kirīṭajuṣṭaṃ
tadātikāyasya śiro jahāra
a tac chiraḥ saśiras trāṇaṃ lakṣmaṇeṣuprapīḍitam
c papāta sahasā bhūmau śṛṅgaṃ himavato yathā
a praharṣayuktā bahavas tu vānarā
prabuddhapadmapratimānanās tadā
c apūjayaṃl lakṣmaṇam iṣṭabhāginaṃ
hate ripau bhīmabale durāsade
a tato hatān rākṣasapuṃgavāṃs tān
devāntakāditriśiro 'tikāyān
c rakṣogaṇās tatra hatāvaśiṣṭās
te rāvaṇāya tvaritaṃ śaśaṃsuḥ
a tato hatāṃs tān sahasā niśamya
rājā mumohāśrupariplutākṣaḥ
c putrakṣayaṃ bhrātṛvadhaṃ ca ghoraṃ
vicintya rājā vipulaṃ pradadhyau
a tatas tu rājānam udīkṣya dīnaṃ
śokārṇave saṃparipupluvānam
c atharṣabho rākṣasarājasūnur
athendrajid vākyam idaṃ babhāṣe
a na tāta mohaṃ pratigantum arhasi
yatrendrajij jīvati rākṣasendra
c nendrāribāṇābhihato hi kaś cit
prāṇān samarthaḥ samare 'bhidhartum
a paśyādya rāmaṃ sahalakṣmaṇena
madbāṇanirbhinnavikīrṇadeham
c gatāyuṣaṃ bhūmitale śayānaṃ
śaraiḥ śitair ācitasarvagātram
a imāṃ pratijñāṃ śṛṇu śakraśatroḥ
suniścitāṃ pauruṣadaivayuktām
c adyaiva rāmaṃ sahalakṣmaṇena
saṃtāpayiṣyāmi śarair amoghaiḥ
a adyendravaivasvataviṣṇumitra
sādhyāśvivaiśvānaracandrasūryāḥ
c drakṣyanti me vikramam aprameyaṃ
viṣṇor ivograṃ baliyajñavāṭe
a sa evam uktvā tridaśendraśatrur
āpṛcchya rājānam adīnasattvaḥ
c samārurohānilatulyavegaṃ
rathaṃ kharaśreṣṭhasamādhiyuktam
a samāsthāya mahātejā rathaṃ harirathopamam
c jagāma sahasā tatra yatra yuddham ariṃdama
a taṃ prasthitaṃ mahātmānam anujagmur mahābalāḥ
c saṃharṣamāṇā bahavo dhanuḥpravarapāṇayaḥ
a gajaskandhagatāḥ ke cit ke cit paramavājibhiḥ
c prāsamudgaranistriṃśa paraśvadhagadādharāḥ
a sa śaṅkhaninadair bhīmair bherīṇāṃ ca mahāsvanaiḥ
c jagāma tridaśendrāriḥ stūyamāno niśācaraiḥ
a sa śaṅkhaśaśivarṇena chatreṇa ripusādanaḥ
c rarāja paripūrṇena nabhaś candramasā yathā
a avījyata tato vīro haimair hemavibhūṣitaiḥ
c cārucāmaramukhyaiś ca mukhyaḥ sarvadhanuṣmatām
a tatas tv indrajitā laṅkā sūryapratimatejasā
c rarājāprativīryeṇa dyaur ivārkeṇa bhāsvatā
a sa tu dṛṣṭvā viniryāntaṃ balena mahatā vṛtam
c rākṣasādhipatiḥ śrīmān rāvaṇaḥ putram abravīt
a tvam apratirathaḥ putra jitas te yudhi vāsavaḥ
c kiṃ punar mānuṣaṃ dhṛṣyaṃ na vadhiṣyasi rāghavam
a tathokto rākṣasendreṇa pratigṛhya mahāśiṣaḥ
c rathenāśvayujā vīraḥ śīghraṃ gatvā nikumbhilām
a sa saṃprāpya mahātejā yuddhabhūmim ariṃdamaḥ
c sthāpayām āsa rakṣāṃsi rathaṃ prati samantataḥ
a tatas tu hutabhoktāraṃ hutabhuk sadṛśaprabhaḥ
c juhuve rākṣasaśreṣṭho mantravad vidhivat tadā
a sa havirjālasaṃskārair mālyagandhapuraskṛtaiḥ
c juhuve pāvakaṃ tatra rākṣasendraḥ pratāpavān
a śastrāṇi śarapatrāṇi samidho 'tha vibhītakaḥ
c lohitāni ca vāsāṃsi sruvaṃ kārṣṇāyasaṃ tathā
a sa tatrāgniṃ samāstīrya śarapatraiḥ satomaraiḥ
c chāgasya sarvakṛṣṇasya galaṃ jagrāha jīvataḥ
a sakṛd eva samiddhasya vidhūmasya mahārciṣaḥ
c babhūvus tāni liṅgāni vijayaṃ yāny adarśayan
a pradakṣiṇāvartaśikhas taptakāñcanasaṃnibhaḥ
c havis tat pratijagrāha pāvakaḥ svayam utthitaḥ
a so 'stram āhārayām āsa brāhmam astravidāṃ varaḥ
c dhanuś cātmarathaṃ caiva sarvaṃ tatrābhyamantrayat
a tasminn āhūyamāne 'stre hūyamāne ca pāvake
c sārkagrahendu nakṣatraṃ vitatrāsa nabhastalam
a sa pāvakaṃ pāvakadīptatejā
hutvā mahendrapratimaprabhāvaḥ
c sacāpabāṇāsirathāśvasūtaḥ
khe 'ntardadha ātmānam acintyarūpaḥ
a sa sainyam utsṛjya sametya tūrṇaṃ
mahāraṇe vānaravāhinīṣu
c adṛśyamānaḥ śarajālam ugraṃ
vavarṣa nīlāmbudharo yathāmbu
a te śakrajidbāṇaviśīrṇadehā
māyāhatā visvaram unnadantaḥ
c raṇe nipetur harayo 'drikalpā
yathendravajrābhihatā nagendrāḥ
a te kevalaṃ saṃdadṛśuḥ śitāgrān
bāṇān raṇe vānaravāhinīṣu
c māyā nigūḍhaṃ ca surendraśatruṃ
na cātra taṃ rākṣasam abhyapaśyan
a tataḥ sa rakṣo'dhipatir mahātmā
sarvā diśo bāṇagaṇaiḥ śitāgraiḥ
c pracchādayām āsa raviprakāśair
viṣādayām āsa ca vānarendrān
a sa śūlanistriṃśa paraśvadhāni
vyāvidhya dīptānalasaṃnibhāni
c savisphuliṅgojjvalapāvakāni
vavarṣa tīvraṃ plavagendrasainye
a tato jvalanasaṃkāśaiḥ śitair vānarayūthapāḥ
c tāḍitāḥ śakrajidbāṇaiḥ praphullā iva kiṃśukāḥ
a anyonyam abhisarpanto ninadantaś ca visvaram
c rākṣasendrāstranirbhinnā nipetur vānararṣabhāḥ
a udīkṣamāṇā gaganaṃ ke cin netreṣu tāḍitāḥ
c śarair viviśur anyonyaṃ petuś ca jagatītale
a hanūmantaṃ ca sugrīvam aṅgadaṃ gandhamādanam
c jāmbavantaṃ suṣeṇaṃ ca vegadarśinam eva ca
a maindaṃ ca dvividaṃ nīlaṃ gavākṣaṃ gajagomukhau
c kesariṃ harilomānaṃ vidyuddaṃṣṭraṃ ca vānaram
a sūryānanaṃ jyotimukhaṃ tathā dadhimukhaṃ harim
c pāvakākṣaṃ nalaṃ caiva kumudaṃ caiva vānaram
a prāsaiḥ śūlaiḥ śitair bāṇair indrajinmantrasaṃhitaiḥ
c vivyādha hariśārdūlān sarvāṃs tān rākṣasottamaḥ
a sa vai gadābhir hariyūthamukhyān
nirbhidya bāṇais tapanīyapuṅkhaiḥ
c vavarṣa rāmaṃ śaravṛṣṭijālaiḥ
salakṣmaṇaṃ bhāskararaśmikalpaiḥ
a sa bāṇavarṣair abhivarṣyamāṇo
dhārānipātān iva tān vicintya
c samīkṣamāṇaḥ paramādbhutaśrī
rāmas tadā lakṣmaṇam ity uvāca
a asau punar lakṣmaṇa rākṣasendro
brahmāstram āśritya surendraśatruḥ
c nipātayitvā harisainyam ugram
asmāñ śarair ardayati prasaktam
a svayambhuvā dattavaro mahātmā
kham āsthito 'ntarhitabhīmakāyaḥ
c kathaṃ nu śakyo yudhi naṣṭadeho
nihantum adyendrajid udyatāstraḥ
a manye svayambhūr bhagavān acintyo
yasyaitad astraṃ prabhavaś ca yo 'sya
c bāṇāvapātāṃs tvam ihādya dhīman
mayā sahāvyagramanāḥ sahasva
a pracchādayaty eṣa hi rākṣasendraḥ
sarvā diśaḥ sāyakavṛṣṭijālaiḥ
c etac ca sarvaṃ patitāgryavīraṃ
na bhrājate vānararājasainyam
a āvāṃ tu dṛṣṭvā patitau visaṃjñau
nivṛttayuddhau hataroṣaharṣau
c dhruvaṃ pravekṣyaty amarārivāsaṃ
asau samādāya raṇāgralakṣmīm
a tatas tu tāv indrajid astrajālair
babhūvatus tatra tadā viśastau
c sa cāpi tau tatra viṣādayitvā
nanāda harṣād yudhi rākṣasendraḥ
a sa tat tadā vānararājasainyaṃ
rāmaṃ ca saṃkhye sahalakṣmaṇena
c viṣādayitvā sahasā viveśa
purīṃ daśagrīvabhujābhiguptām
a tayos tadā sāditayo raṇāgre
mumoha sainyaṃ hariyūthapānām
c sugrīvanīlāṅgadajāmbavanto
na cāpi kiṃ cit pratipedire te
a tato viṣaṇṇaṃ samavekṣya sainyaṃ
vibhīṣaṇo buddhimatāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
c uvāca śākhāmṛgarājavīrān
āśvāsayann apratimair vacobhiḥ
a mā bhaiṣṭa nāsty atra viṣādakālo
yad āryaputrāv avaśau viṣaṇṇau
c svayambhuvo vākyam athodvahantau
yat sāditāv indrajidastrajālaiḥ
a tasmai tu dattaṃ paramāstram etat
svayambhuvā brāhmam amoghavegam
c tan mānayantau yadi rājaputrau
nipātitau ko 'tra viṣādakālaḥ
a brāhmam astraṃ tadā dhīmān mānayitvā tu mārutiḥ
c vibhīṣaṇavacaḥ śrutvā hanūmāṃs tam athābravīt
a etasmin nihate sainye vānarāṇāṃ tarasvinām
c yo yo dhārayate prāṇāṃs taṃ tam āśvāsayāvahe
a tāv ubhau yugapad vīrau hanūmad rākṣasottamau
c ulkāhastau tadā rātrau raṇaśīrṣe viceratuḥ
a chinnalāṅgūlahastorupādāṅguli śiro dharaiḥ
c sravadbhiḥ kṣatajaṃ gātraiḥ prasravadbhiḥ samantataḥ
a patitaiḥ parvatākārair vānarair abhisaṃkulām
c śastraiś ca patitair dīptair dadṛśāte vasuṃdharām
a sugrīvam aṅgadaṃ nīlaṃ śarabhaṃ gandhamādanam
c jāmbavantaṃ suṣeṇaṃ ca vegadarśanam āhukam
a maindaṃ nalaṃ jyotimukhaṃ dvividaṃ panasaṃ tathā
c vibhīṣaṇo hanūmāṃś ca dadṛśāte hatān raṇe
a saptaṣaṣṭir hatāḥ koṭyo vānarāṇāṃ tarasvinām
c ahnaḥ pañcamaśeṣeṇa vallabhena svayambhuvaḥ
a sāgaraughanibhaṃ bhīmaṃ dṛṣṭvā bāṇārditaṃ balam
c mārgate jāmbavantaṃ sma hanūmān savibhīṣaṇaḥ
a svabhāvajarayā yuktaṃ vṛddhaṃ śaraśataiś citam
c prajāpatisutaṃ vīraṃ śāmyantam iva pāvakam
a dṛṣṭvā tam upasaṃgamya paulastyo vākyam abravīt
c kaccid āryaśarais tīrṣṇair na prāṇā dhvaṃsitās tava
a vibhīṣaṇavacaḥ śrutvā jāmbavān ṛkṣapuṃgavaḥ
c kṛcchrād abhyudgiran vākyam idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a nairṛtendramahāvīryasvareṇa tvābhilakṣaye
c pīḍyamānaḥ śitair bāṇair na tvāṃ paśyāmi cakṣuṣā
a añjanā suprajā yena mātariśvā ca nairṛta
c hanūmān vānaraśreṣṭhaḥ prāṇān dhārayate kva cit
a śrutvā jāmbavato vākyam uvācedaṃ vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c āryaputrāv atikramya kasmāt pṛcchasi mārutim
a naiva rājani sugrīve nāṅgade nāpi rāghave
c ārya saṃdarśitaḥ sneho yathā vāyusute paraḥ
a vibhīṣaṇavacaḥ śrutvā jāmbavān vākyam abravīt
c śṛṇu nairṛtaśārdūla yasmāt pṛcchāmi mārutim
a tasmiñ jīvati vīre tu hatam apy ahataṃ balam
c hanūmaty ujjhitaprāṇe jīvanto 'pi vayaṃ hatāḥ
a dhriyate mārutis tāta mārutapratimo yadi
c vaiśvānarasamo vīrye jīvitāśā tato bhavet
a tato vṛddham upāgamya niyamenābhyavādayat
c gṛhya jāmbavataḥ pādau hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
a śrutvā hanumato vākyaṃ tathāpi vyathitendriyaḥ
c punarjātam ivātmānaṃ sa mene ṛkṣapuṃgavaḥ
a tato 'bravīn mahātejā hanūmantaṃ sa jāmbavān
c āgaccha hariśārdūlavānarāṃs trātum arhasi
a nānyo vikramaparyāptas tvam eṣāṃ paramaḥ sakhā
c tvatparākramakālo 'yaṃ nānyaṃ paśyāmi kañ cana
a ṛkṣavānaravīrāṇām anīkāni praharṣaya
c viśalyau kuru cāpy etau sāditau rāmalakṣmaṇau
a gatvā paramam adhvānam upary upari sāgaram
c himavantaṃ nagaśreṣṭhaṃ hanūman gantum arhasi
a tataḥ kāñcanam atyugram ṛṣabhaṃ parvatottamam
c kailāsaśikharaṃ cāpi drakṣyasy ariniṣūdana
a tayoḥ śikharayor madhye pradīptam atulaprabham
c sarvauṣadhiyutaṃ vīra drakṣyasy auṣadhiparvatam
a tasya vānaraśārdūlacatasro mūrdhni saṃbhavāḥ
c drakṣyasy oṣadhayo dīptā dīpayantyo diśo daśa
a mṛtasaṃjīvanīṃ caiva viśalyakaraṇīm api
c sauvarṇakaraṇīṃ caiva saṃdhānīṃ ca mahauṣadhīm
a tāḥ sarvā hanuman gṛhya kṣipram āgantum arhasi
c āśvāsaya harīn prāṇair yojya gandhavahātmajaḥ
a śrutvā jāmbavato vākyaṃ hanūmān haripuṃgavaḥ
c āpūryata baloddharṣais toyavegair ivārṇavaḥ
a sa parvatataṭāgrasthaḥ pīḍayan parvatottaram
c hanūmān dṛśyate vīro dvitīya iva parvataḥ
a haripādavinirbhinno niṣasāda sa parvataḥ
c na śaśāka tadātmānaṃ soḍhuṃ bhṛśanipīḍitaḥ
a tasya petur nagā bhūmau harivegāc ca jajvaluḥ
c śṛṅgāṇi ca vyakīryanta pīḍitasya hanūmatā
a tasmin saṃpīḍyamāne tu bhagnadrumaśilātale
c na śekur vānarāḥ sthātuṃ ghūrṇamāne nagottame
a sa ghūrṇitamahādvārā prabhagnagṛhagopurā
c laṅkā trāsākulā rātrau pranṛttevābhavat tadā
a pṛthivīdharasaṃkāśo nipīḍya dharaṇīdharam
c pṛthivīṃ kṣobhayām āsa sārṇavāṃ mārutātmajaḥ
a padbhyāṃ tu śailam āpīḍya vaḍavāmukhavan mukham
c vivṛtyograṃ nanādoccais trāsayann iva rākṣasān
a tasya nānadyamānasya śrutvā ninadam adbhutam
c laṅkāsthā rākṣasāḥ sarve na śekuḥ spandituṃ bhayāt
a namaskṛtvātha rāmāya mārutir bhīmavikramaḥ
c rāghavārthe paraṃ karma samaihata paraṃtapaḥ
a sa puccham udyamya bhujaṃgakalpaṃ
vinamya pṛṣṭhaṃ śravaṇe nikuñcya
c vivṛtya vaktraṃ vaḍavāmukhābham
āpupluve vyomni sa caṇḍavegaḥ
a sa vṛkṣaṣaṇḍāṃs tarasā jahāra
śailāñ śilāḥ prākṛtavānarāṃś ca
c bāhūruvegoddhatasaṃpraṇunnās
te kṣīṇavegāḥ salile nipetuḥ
a sa tau prasāryoragabhogakalpau
bhujau bhujaṃgārinikāśavīryaḥ
c jagāma meruṃ nagarājam agryaṃ
diśaḥ prakarṣann iva vāyusūnuḥ
a sa sāgaraṃ ghūrṇitavīcimālaṃ
tadā bhṛśaṃ bhrāmitasarvasattvam
c samīkṣamāṇaḥ sahasā jagāma
cakraṃ yathā viṣṇukarāgramuktam
a sa parvatān vṛkṣagaṇān sarāṃsi
nadīs taṭākāni purottamāni
c sphītāñjanāṃs tān api saṃprapaśyañ
jagāma vegāt pitṛtulyavegaḥ
a ādityapatham āśritya jagāma sa gataśramaḥ
c sa dadarśa hariśreṣṭho himavantaṃ nagottamam
a nānāprasravaṇopetaṃ bahukaṃdaranirjharam
c śvetābhracayasaṃkāśaiḥ śikharaiś cārudarśanaiḥ
a sa taṃ samāsādya mahānagendram
atipravṛddhottamaghoraśṛṅgam
c dadarśa puṇyāni mahāśramāṇi
surarṣisaṃghottamasevitāni
a sa brahmakośaṃ rajatālayaṃ ca
śakrālayaṃ rudraśarapramokṣam
c hayānanaṃ brahmaśiraś ca dīptaṃ
dadarśa vaivasvata kiṃkarāṃś ca
a vajrālayaṃ vaiśvaraṇālayaṃ ca
sūryaprabhaṃ sūryanibandhanaṃ ca
c brahmāsanaṃ śaṃkarakārmukaṃ ca
dadarśa nābhiṃ ca vasuṃdharāyāḥ
a kailāsam agryaṃ himavacchilāṃ ca
tatharṣabhaṃ kāñcanaśailam agryam
c sa dīptasarvauṣadhisaṃpradīptaṃ
dadarśa sarvauṣadhiparvatendram
a sa taṃ samīkṣyānalaraśmidīptaṃ
visiṣmiye vāsavadūtasūnuḥ
c āplutya taṃ cauṣadhiparvatendraṃ
tatrauṣadhīnāṃ vicayaṃ cakāra
a sa yojanasahasrāṇi samatītya mahākapiḥ
c divyauṣadhidharaṃ śailaṃ vyacaran mārutātmajaḥ
a mahauṣadhyas tu tāḥ sarvās tasmin parvatasattame
c vijñāyārthinam āyāntaṃ tato jagmur adarśanam
a sa tā mahātmā hanumān apaśyaṃś
cukopa kopāc ca bhṛśaṃ nanāda
c amṛṣyamāṇo 'gninikāśacakṣur
mahīdharendraṃ tam uvāca vākyam
a kim etad evaṃ suviniścitaṃ te
yad rāghave nāsi kṛtānukampaḥ
c paśyādya madbāhubalābhibhūto
vikīrṇam ātmānam atho nagendra
a sa tasya śṛṅgaṃ sanagaṃ sanāgaṃ
sakāñcanaṃ dhātusahasrajuṣṭam
c vikīrṇakūṭaṃ calitāgrasānuṃ
pragṛhya vegāt sahasonmamātha
a sa taṃ samutpāṭya kham utpapāta
vitrāsya lokān sasurān surendrān
c saṃstūyamānaḥ khacarair anekair
jagāma vegād garuḍogravīryaḥ
a sa bhāskarādhvānam anuprapannas
tad bhāskarābhaṃ śikharaṃ pragṛhya
c babhau tadā bhāskarasaṃnikāśo
raveḥ samīpe pratibhāskarābhaḥ
a sa tena śailena bhṛśaṃ rarāja
śailopamo gandhavahātmajas tu
c sahasradhāreṇa sapāvakena
cakreṇa khe viṣṇur ivoddhṛtena
a taṃ vānarāḥ prekṣya tadā vineduḥ
sa tān api prekṣya mudā nanāda
c teṣāṃ samudghuṣṭaravaṃ niśamya
laṅkālayā bhīmataraṃ vineduḥ
a tato mahātmā nipapāta tasmiñ
śailottame vānarasainyamadhye
c haryuttamebhyaḥ śirasābhivādya
vibhīṣaṇaṃ tatra ca sasvaje saḥ
a tāv apy ubhau mānuṣarājaputrau
taṃ gandham āghrāya mahauṣadhīnām
c babhūvatus tatra tadā viśalyāv
uttasthur anye ca haripravīrāḥ
a tato harir gandhavahātmajas tu
tam oṣadhīśailam udagravīryaḥ
c nināya vegād dhimavantam eva
punaś ca rāmeṇa samājagāma
a tato 'bravīn mahātejāḥ sugrīvo vānarādhipaḥ
c arthyaṃ vijāpayaṃś cāpi hanūmantaṃ mahābalam
a yato hataḥ kumbhakarṇaḥ kumārāś ca niṣūditāḥ
c nedānīim upanirhāraṃ rāvaṇo dātum arhati
a ye ye mahābalāḥ santi laghavaś ca plavaṃgamāḥ
c laṅkām abhyutpatantv āśu gṛhyolkāḥ plavagarṣabhāḥ
a tato 'staṃ gata āditye raudre tasmin niśāmukhe
c laṅkām abhimukhāḥ solkā jagmus te plavagarṣabhāḥ
a ulkāhastair harigaṇaiḥ sarvataḥ samabhidrutāḥ
c ārakṣasthā virūpākṣāḥ sahasā vipradudruvuḥ
a gopurāṭṭa pratolīṣu caryāsu vividhāsu ca
c prāsādeṣu ca saṃhṛṣṭāḥ sasṛjus te hutāśanam
a teṣāṃ gṛhasahasrāṇi dadāha hutabhuk tadā
c āvāsān rākṣasānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ gṛhamedhinām
a hemacitratanutrāṇāṃ sragdāmāmbaradhāriṇām
c sīdhupānacalākṣāṇāṃ madavihvalagāminām
a kāntālambitavastrāṇāṃ śatrusaṃjātamanyunām
c gadāśūlāsi hastānāṃ khādatāṃ pibatām api
a śayaneṣu mahārheṣu prasuptānāṃ priyaiḥ saha
c trastānāṃ gacchatāṃ tūrṇaṃ putrān ādāya sarvataḥ
a teṣāṃ gṛhasahasrāṇi tadā laṅkānivāsinām
c adahat pāvakas tatra jajvāla ca punaḥ punaḥ
a sāravanti mahārhāṇi gambhīraguṇavanti ca
c hemacandrārdhacandrāṇi candraśālonnatāni ca
a ratnacitragavākṣāṇi sādhiṣṭhānāni sarvaśaḥ
c maṇividrumacitrāṇi spṛśantīva ca bhāskaram
a krauñcabarhiṇavīṇānāṃ bhūṣaṇānāṃ ca nisvanaiḥ
c nāditāny acalābhāni veśmāny agnir dadāha saḥ
a jvalanena parītāni toraṇāni cakāśire
c vidyudbhir iva naddhāni meghajālāni gharmage
a vimāneṣu prasuptāś ca dahyamānā varāṅganāḥ
c tyaktābharaṇasaṃyogā hāhety uccair vicukruśaḥ
a tatra cāgniparītāni nipetur bhavanāny api
c vajrivajrahatānīva śikharāṇi mahāgireḥ
a tāni nirdahyamānāni dūrataḥ pracakāśire
c himavacchikharāṇīva dīptauṣadhivanāni ca
a harmyāgrair dahyamānaiś ca jvālāprajvalitair api
c rātrau sā dṛśyate laṅkā puṣpitair iva kiṃśukaiḥ
a hastyadhyakṣair gajair muktair muktaiś ca turagair api
c babhūva laṅkā lokānte bhrāntagrāha ivārṇavaḥ
a aśvaṃ muktaṃ gajo dṛṣṭvā kaccid bhīto 'pasarpati
c bhīto bhītaṃ gajaṃ dṛṣṭvā kva cid aśvo nivartate
a sā babhūva muhūrtena haribhir dīpitā purī
c lokasyāsya kṣaye ghore pradīpteva vasuṃdharā
a nārī janasya dhūmena vyāptasyoccair vineduṣaḥ
