c svano jvalanataptasya śuśruve daśayojanam
a pradagdhakāyān aparān rākṣasān nirgatān bahiḥ
c sahasābhyutpatanti sma harayo 'tha yuyutsavaḥ
a udghuṣṭaṃ vānarāṇāṃ ca rākṣasānāṃ ca nisvanaḥ
c diśo daśa samudraṃ ca pṛthivīṃ cānvanādayat
a viśalyau tu mahātmānau tāv ubhau rāmalakṣmaṇau
c asaṃbhrāntau jagṛhatus tāv ubhau dhanuṣī vare
a tato visphārayāṇasya rāmasya dhanur uttamam
c babhūva tumulaḥ śabdo rākṣasānāṃ bhayāvahaḥ
a aśobhata tadā rāmo dhanur visphārayan mahat
c bhagavān iva saṃkruddho bhavo vedamayaṃ dhanuḥ
a vānarodghuṣṭaghoṣaś ca rākṣasānāṃ ca nisvanaḥ
c jyāśabdaś cāpi rāmasya trayaṃ vyāpa diśo daśa
a tasya kārmukamuktaiś ca śarais tatpuragopuram
c kailāsaśṛṅgapratimaṃ vikīrṇam apatad bhuvi
a tato rāmaśarān dṛṣṭvā vimāneṣu gṛheṣu ca
c saṃnāho rākṣasendrāṇāṃ tumulaḥ samapadyata
a teṣāṃ saṃnahyamānānāṃ siṃhanādaṃ ca kurvatām
c śarvarī rākṣasendrāṇāṃ raudrīva samapadyata
a ādiṣṭā vānarendrās te sugrīveṇa mahātmanā
c āsannā dvāram āsādya yudhyadhvaṃ plavagarṣabhāḥ
a yaś ca vo vitathaṃ kuryāt tatra tatra vyavasthitaḥ
c sa hantavyo 'bhisaṃplutya rājaśāsanadūṣakaḥ
a teṣu vānaramukhyeṣu dīptolkojjvalapāṇiṣu
c sthiteṣu dvāram āsādya rāvaṇaṃ manyur āviśat
a tasya jṛmbhitavikṣepād vyāmiśrā vai diśo daśa
c rūpavān iva rudrasya manyur gātreṣv adṛśyata
a sa nikumbhaṃ ca kumbhaṃ ca kumbhakarṇātmajāv ubhau
c preṣayām āsa saṃkruddho rākṣasair bahubhiḥ saha
a śaśāsa caiva tān sarvān rākṣasān rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c rākṣasā gacchatātraiva siṃhanādaṃ ca nādayan
a tatas tu coditās tena rākṣasā jvalitāyudhāḥ
c laṅkāyā niryayur vīrāḥ praṇadantaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
a bhīmāśvarathamātaṃgaṃ nānāpatti samākulam
c dīptaśūlagadākhaḍgaprāsatomarakārmukam
a tad rākṣasabalaṃ ghoraṃ bhīmavikramapauruṣam
c dadṛśe jvalitaprāsaṃ kiṅkiṇīśatanāditam
a hemajālācitabhujaṃ vyāveṣṭitaparaśvadham
c vyāghūrṇitamahāśastraṃ bāṇasaṃsaktakārmukam
a gandhamālyamadhūtsekasaṃmodita mahānilam
c ghoraṃ śūrajanākīrṇaṃ mahāmbudharanisvanam
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā balam āyāntaṃ rākṣasānāṃ sudāruṇam
c saṃcacāla plavaṃgānāṃ balam uccair nanāda ca
a javenāplutya ca punas tad rākṣasabalaṃ mahat
c abhyayāt pratyaribalaṃ pataṃga iva pāvakam
a teṣāṃ bhujaparāmarśavyāmṛṣṭaparighāśani
c rākṣasānāṃ balaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ bhūyastaram aśobhata
a tathaivāpy apare teṣāṃ kapīnām asibhiḥ śitaiḥ
c pravīrān abhito jaghnur ghorarūpā niśācarāḥ
a ghnantam anyaṃ jaghānānyaḥ pātayantam apātayat
c garhamāṇaṃ jagarhānye daśantam apare 'daśat
a dehīty anye dadāty anyo dadāmīty aparaḥ punaḥ
c kiṃ kleśayasi tiṣṭheti tatrānyonyaṃ babhāṣire
a samudyatamahāprāsaṃ muṣṭiśūlāsisaṃkulam
c prāvartata mahāraudraṃ yuddhaṃ vānararakṣasām
a vānarān daśa sapteti rākṣasā abhyapātayan
c rākṣasān daśasapteti vānarā jaghnur āhave
a visrastakeśarasanaṃ vimuktakavacadhvajam
c balaṃ rākṣasam ālambya vānarāḥ paryavārayan
a pravṛtte saṃkule tasmin ghore vīrajanakṣaye
c aṅgadaḥ kampanaṃ vīram āsasāda raṇotsukaḥ
a āhūya so 'ṅgadaṃ kopāt tāḍayām āsa vegitaḥ
c gadayā kampanaḥ pūrvaṃ sa cacāla bhṛśāhataḥ
a sa saṃjñāṃ prāpya tejasvī cikṣepa śikharaṃ gireḥ
c arditaś ca prahāreṇa kampanaḥ patito bhuvi
a hatapravīrā vyathitā rākṣasendracamūs tadā
c jagāmābhimukhī sā tu kumbhakarṇasuto yataḥ
e āpatantīṃ ca vegena kumbhas tāṃ sāntvayac camūm
a sa dhanur dhanvināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pragṛhya susamāhitaḥ
c mumocāśīviṣaprakhyāñ śarān dehavidāraṇān
a tasya tac chuśubhe bhūyaḥ saśaraṃ dhanur uttamam
c vidyudairāvatārciṣmad dvitīyendradhanur yathā
a ākarṇakṛṣṭamuktena jaghāna dvividaṃ tadā
c tena hāṭakapuṅkhena patriṇā patravāsasā
a sahasābhihatas tena vipramuktapadaḥ sphuran
c nipapātādrikūṭābho vihvalaḥ plavagottamaḥ
a maindas tu bhrātaraṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagnaṃ tatra mahāhave
c abhidudrāva vegena pragṛhya mahatīṃ śilām
a tāṃ śilāṃ tu pracikṣepa rākṣasāya mahābalaḥ
c bibheda tāṃ śilāṃ kumbhaḥ prasannaiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a saṃdhāya cānyaṃ sumukhaṃ śaram āśīviṣopamam
c ājaghāna mahātejā vakṣasi dvividāgrajam
a sa tu tena prahāreṇa maindo vānarayūthapaḥ
c marmaṇy abhihatas tena papāta bhuvi mūrchitaḥ
a aṅgado mātulau dṛṣṭvā patitau tau mahābalau
c abhidudrāva vegena kumbham udyatakārmukam
a tam āpatantaṃ vivyādha kumbhaḥ pañcabhir āyasaiḥ
c tribhiś cānyaiḥ śitair bāṇair mātaṃgam iva tomaraiḥ
a so 'ṅgadaṃ vividhair bāṇaiḥ kumbho vivyādha vīryavān
c akuṇṭhadhārair niśitais tīkṣṇaiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥ
a aṅgadaḥ pratividdhāṅgo vāliputro na kampate
c śilāpādapavarṣāṇi tasya mūrdhni vavarṣa ha
a sa praciccheda tān sarvān bibheda ca punaḥ śilāḥ
c kumbhakarṇātmajaḥ śrīmān vāliputrasamīritān
a āpatantaṃ ca saṃprekṣya kumbho vānarayūthapam
c bhruvor vivyādha bāṇābhyām ulkābhyām iva kuñjaram
a aṅgadaḥ pāṇinā netre pidhāya rudhirokṣite
c sālam āsannam ekena parijagrāha pāṇinā
a tam indraketupratimaṃ vṛkṣaṃ mandarasaṃnibham
c samutsṛjantaṃ vegena paśyatāṃ sarvarakṣasām
a sa ciccheda śitair bāṇaiḥ saptabhiḥ kāyabhedanaiḥ
c aṅgado vivyathe 'bhīkṣṇaṃ sasāda ca mumoha ca
a aṅgadaṃ vyathitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sīdantam iva sāgare
c durāsadaṃ hariśreṣṭhā rāghavāya nyavedayan
a rāmas tu vyathitaṃ śrutvā vāliputraṃ mahāhave
c vyādideśa hariśreṣṭhāñ jāmbavatpramukhāṃs tataḥ
a te tu vānaraśārdūlāḥ śrutvā rāmasya śāsanam
c abhipetuḥ susaṃkruddhāḥ kumbham udyatakārmukam
a tato drumaśilāhastāḥ kopasaṃraktalocanāḥ
c rirakṣiṣanto 'bhyapatann aṅgadaṃ vānararṣabhāḥ
a jāmbavāṃś ca suṣeṇaś ca vegadarśī ca vānaraḥ
c kumbhakarṇātmajaṃ vīraṃ kruddhāḥ samabhidudruvuḥ
a samīkṣyātatatas tāṃs tu vānarendrān mahābalān
c āvavāra śaraugheṇa nageneva jalāśayam
a tasya bāṇacayaṃ prāpya na śoker ativartitum
c vānarendrā mahātmāno velām iva mahodadhiḥ
a tāṃs tu dṛṣṭvā harigaṇāñ śaravṛṣṭibhir arditān
c aṅgadaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā bhrātṛjaṃ plavageśvaraḥ
a abhidudrāva vegena sugrīvaḥ kumbham āhave
c śailasānu caraṃ nāgaṃ vegavān iva kesarī
a utpāṭya ca mahāśailān aśvakarṇān dhavān bahūn
c anyāṃś ca vividhān vṛkṣāṃś cikṣepa ca mahābalaḥ
a tāṃ chādayantīm ākāśaṃ vṛkṣavṛṣṭiṃ durāsadām
c kumbhakarṇātmajaḥ śrīmāṃś ciccheda niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a abhilakṣyeṇa tīvreṇa kumbhena niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c ācitās te drumā rejur yathā ghorāḥ śataghnayaḥ
a drumavarṣaṃ tu tac chinnaṃ dṛṣṭvā kumbhena vīryavān
c vānarādhipatiḥ śrīmān mahāsattvo na vivyathe
a nirbhidyamānaḥ sahasā sahamānaś ca tāñ śarān
c kumbhasya dhanur ākṣipya babhañjendradhanuḥprabham
a avaplutya tataḥ śīghraṃ kṛtvā karma suduṣkaram
c abravīt kupitaḥ kumbhaṃ bhagnaśṛṅgam iva dvipam
a nikumbhāgraja vīryaṃ te bāṇavegaṃ tad adbhutam
c saṃnatiś ca prabhāvaś ca tava vā rāvaṇasya vā
a prahrādabalivṛtraghnakuberavaruṇopama
c ekas tvam anujāto 'si pitaraṃ balavattaraḥ
a tvām evaikaṃ mahābāhuṃ śūlahastam ariṃdamam
c tridaśā nātivartante jitendriyam ivādhayaḥ
a varadānāt pitṛvyas te sahate devadānavān
c kumbhakarṇas tu vīryeṇa sahate ca surāsurān
a dhanuṣīndrajitas tulyaḥ pratāpe rāvaṇasya ca
c tvam adya rakṣasāṃ loke śreṣṭho 'si balavīryataḥ
a mahāvimardaṃ samare mayā saha tavādbhutam
c adya bhūtāni paśyantu śakraśambarayor iva
a kṛtam apratimaṃ karma darśitaṃ cāstrakauśalam
c pātitā harivīrāś ca tvayaite bhīmavikramāḥ
a upālambhabhayāc cāpi nāsi vīra mayā hataḥ
c kṛtakarmā pariśrānto viśrāntaḥ paśya me balam
a tena sugrīvavākyena sāvamānena mānitaḥ
c agner ājyahutasyeva tejas tasyābhyavardhata
a tataḥ kumbhaḥ samutpatya sugrīvam abhipadya ca
c ājaghānorasi kruddho vajravegena muṣṭinā
a tasya carma ca pusphoṭa saṃjajñe cāsya śoṇitam
c sa ca muṣṭir mahāvegaḥ pratijaghne 'sthimaṇḍale
a tadā vegena tatrāsīt tejaḥ prajvālitaṃ muhuḥ
c vajraniṣpeṣasaṃjātajvālā merau yathā girau
a sa tatrābhihatas tena sugrīvo vānararṣabhaḥ
c muṣṭiṃ saṃvartayām āsa vajrakalpaṃ mahābalaḥ
a arciḥsahasravikacaṃ ravimaṇḍalasaprabham
c sa muṣṭiṃ pātayām āsa kumbhasyorasi vīryavān
a muṣṭinābhihatas tena nipapātāśu rākṣasaḥ
c lohitāṅga ivākāśād dīptaraśmir yadṛcchayā
a kumbhasya patato rūpaṃ bhagnasyorasi muṣṭinā
c babhau rudrābhipannasya yathārūpaṃ gavāṃ pateḥ
a tasmin hate bhīmaparākrameṇa
plavaṃgamānām ṛṣabheṇa yuddhe
c mahī saśailā savanā cacāla
bhayaṃ ca rakṣāṃsy adhikaṃ viveśa
a nikumbho bhrātaraṃ dṛṣṭvā sugrīveṇa nipātitam
c pradahann iva kopena vānarendram avaikṣata
a tataḥ sragdāmasaṃnaddhaṃ dattapañcāṅgulaṃ śubham
c ādade parighaṃ vīro nagendraśikharopamam
a hemapaṭṭaparikṣiptaṃ vajravidrumabhūṣitam
c yamadaṇḍopamaṃ bhīmaṃ rakṣasāṃ bhayanāśanam
a tam āvidhya mahātejāḥ śakradhvajasamaṃ raṇe
c vinanāda vivṛttāsyo nikumbho bhīmavikramaḥ
a urogatena niṣkeṇa bhujasthair aṅgadair api
c kuṇḍalābhyāṃ ca mṛṣṭābhyāṃ mālayā ca vicitrayā
a nikumbho bhūṣaṇair bhāti tena sma parigheṇa ca
c yathendradhanuṣā meghaḥ savidyutstanayitnumān
a parighāgreṇa pusphoṭa vātagranthir mahātmanaḥ
c prajajvāla saghoṣaś ca vidhūma iva pāvakaḥ
a nagaryā viṭapāvatyā gandharvabhavanottamaiḥ
c saha caivāmarāvatyā sarvaiś ca bhavanaiḥ saha
a satārāgaṇanakṣatraṃ sacandraṃ samahāgraham
c nikumbhaparighāghūrṇaṃ bhramatīva nabhastalam
a durāsadaś ca saṃjajñe parighābharaṇaprabhaḥ
c krodhendhano nikumbhāgnir yugāntāgnir ivotthitaḥ
a rākṣasā vānarāś cāpi na śekuḥ spandituṃ bhayāt
c hanūmaṃs tu vivṛtyoras tasthau pramukhato balī
a parighopamabāhus tu parighaṃ bhāskaraprabham
c balī balavatas tasya pātayām āsa vakṣasi
a sthire tasyorasi vyūḍhe parighaḥ śatadhā kṛtaḥ
c viśīryamāṇaḥ sahasā ulkā śatam ivāmbare
a sa tu tena prahāreṇa cacāla ca mahākapiḥ
c parigheṇa samādhūto yathā bhūmicale 'calaḥ
a sa tathābhihatas tena hanūmān plavagottamaḥ
c muṣṭiṃ saṃvartayām āsa balenātimahābalaḥ
a tam udyamya mahātejā nikumbhorasi vīryavān
c abhicikṣepa vegena vegavān vāyuvikramaḥ
a tataḥ pusphoṭa carmāsya prasusrāva ca śoṇitam
c muṣṭinā tena saṃjajñe jvālā vidyud ivotthitā
a sa tu tena prahāreṇa nikumbho vicacāla ha
c svasthaś cāpi nijagrāha hanūmantaṃ mahābalam
a vicukruśus tadā saṃkhye bhīmaṃ laṅkānivāsinaḥ
c nikumbhenoddhṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā hanūmantaṃ mahābalam
a sa tathā hriyamāṇo 'pi kumbhakarṇātmajena hi
c ājaghānānilasuto vajravegena muṣṭinā
a ātmānaṃ mocayitvātha kṣitāv abhyavapadyata
c hanūmān unmamathāśu nikumbhaṃ mārutātmajaḥ
a nikṣipya paramāyatto nikumbhaṃ niṣpipeṣa ca
c utpatya cāsya vegena papātorasi vīryavān
a parigṛhya ca bāhubhyāṃ parivṛtya śirodharām
c utpāṭayām āsa śiro bhairavaṃ nadato mahat
a atha vinadati sādite nikumbhe
pavanasutena raṇe babhūva yuddham
c daśarathasutarākṣasendracamvor
bhṛśataram āgataroṣayoḥ subhīmam
a nikumbhaṃ ca hataṃ śrutvā kumbhaṃ ca vinipātitam
c rāvaṇaḥ paramāmarṣī prajajvālānalo yathā
a nairṛtaḥ krodhaśokābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ tu parimūrchitaḥ
c kharaputraṃ viśālākṣaṃ makarākṣam acodayat
a gaccha putra mayājñapto balenābhisamanvitaḥ
c rāghavaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva jahi tau savanaukasau
a rāvaṇasya vacaḥ śrutvā śūro mānī kharātmajaḥ
c bāḍham ity abravīd dhṛṣṭo makarākṣo niśācaraḥ
a so 'bhivādya daśagrīvaṃ kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇam
c nirjagāma gṛhāc chubhrād rāvaṇasyājñayā balī
a samīpasthaṃ balādhyakṣaṃ kharaputro 'bravīd idam
c ratham ānīyatāṃ śīghraṃ sainyaṃ cānīyatāṃ tvarāt
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā balādhyakṣo niśācaraḥ
c syandanaṃ ca balaṃ caiva samīpaṃ pratyapādayat
a pradakṣiṇaṃ rathaṃ kṛtvā āruroha niśācaraḥ
c sūtaṃ saṃcodayām āsa śīghraṃ me ratham āvaha
a atha tān rākṣasān sarvān makarākṣo 'bravīd idam
c yūyaṃ sarve prayudhyadhvaṃ purastān mama rākṣasāḥ
a ahaṃ rākṣasarājena rāvaṇena mahātmanā
c ājñaptaḥ samare hantuṃ tāv ubhau rāmalakṣmaṇau
a adya rāmaṃ vadhiṣyāmi lakṣmaṇaṃ ca niśācarāḥ
c śākhāmṛgaṃ ca sugrīvaṃ vānarāṃś ca śarottamaiḥ
a adya śūlanipātaiś ca vānarāṇāṃ mahācamūm
c pradahiṣyāmi saṃprāptāṃ śuṣkendhanam ivānalaḥ
a makarākṣasya tac chrutvā vacanaṃ te niśācarāḥ
c sarve nānāyudhopetā balavantaḥ samāhitāḥ
a te kāmarūpiṇaḥ śūrā daṃṣṭriṇaḥ piṅgalekṣaṇāḥ
c mātaṃgā iva nardanto dhvastakeśā bhayānakāḥ
a parivārya mahākāyā mahākāyaṃ kharātmajam
c abhijagmus tadā hṛṣṭāś cālayanto vasuṃdharām
a śaṅkhabherīsahasrāṇām āhatānāṃ samantataḥ
c kṣveḍitāsphoṭitānāṃ ca tataḥ śabdo mahān abhūt
a prabhraṣṭo 'tha karāt tasya pratodaḥ sārathes tadā
c papāta sahasā caiva dhvajas tasya ca rakṣasaḥ
a tasya te rathasaṃyuktā hayā vikramavarjitāḥ
c caraṇair ākulair gatvā dīnāḥ sāsramukhā yayuḥ
a pravāti pavanas tasya sapāṃsuḥ kharadāruṇaḥ
c niryāṇe tasya raudrasya makarākṣasya durmateḥ
a tāni dṛṣṭvā nimittāni rākṣasā vīryavattamāḥ
c acintyanirgatāḥ sarve yatra tau rāmalakṣmaṇau
a ghanagajamahiṣāṅgatulyavarṇāḥ
samaramukheṣv asakṛd gadāsibhinnāḥ
c aham aham iti yuddhakauśalās te
rajanicarāḥ paribabhramur nadantaḥ
a nirgataṃ makarākṣaṃ te dṛṣṭvā vānarapuṃgavāḥ
c āplutya sahasā sarve yoddhukāmā vyavasthitāḥ
a tataḥ pravṛttaṃ sumahat tad yuddhaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c niśācaraiḥ plavaṃgānāṃ devānāṃ dānavair iva
a vṛkṣaśūlanipātaiś ca śilāparighapātanaiḥ
c anyonyaṃ mardayanti sma tadā kapiniśācarāḥ
a śaktiśūlagadākhaḍgais tomaraiś ca niśācarāḥ
c paṭṭasair bhindipālaiś ca bāṇapātaiḥ samantataḥ
a pāśamudgaradaṇḍaiś ca nirghātaiś cāparais tathā
c kadanaṃ kapisiṃhānāṃ cakrus te rajanīcarāḥ
a bāṇaughair arditāś cāpi kharaputreṇa vānarāḥ
c saṃbhrāntamanasaḥ sarve dudruvur bhayapīḍitāḥ
a tān dṛṣṭvā rākṣasāḥ sarve dravamāṇān vanaukasaḥ
c nedus te siṃhavad dhṛṣṭā rākṣasā jitakāśinaḥ
a vidravatsu tadā teṣu vānareṣu samantataḥ
c rāmas tān vārayām āsa śaravarṣeṇa rākṣasān
a vāritān rākṣasān dṛṣṭvā makarākṣo niśācaraḥ
c krodhān alasam āviṣṭo vacanaṃ cedam abravīt
a tiṣṭha rāma mayā sārdhaṃ dvandvayuddhaṃ dadāmi te
c tyājayiṣyāmi te prāṇān dhanurmuktaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a yat tadā daṇḍakāraṇye pitaraṃ hatavān mama
c madagrataḥ svakarmasthaṃ smṛtvā roṣo 'bhivardhate
a dahyante bhṛśam aṅgāni durātman mama rāghava
c yan mayāsi na dṛṣṭas tvaṃ tasmin kāle mahāvane
a diṣṭyāsi darśanaṃ rāma mama tvaṃ prāptavān iha
c kāṅkṣito 'si kṣudhārtasya siṃhasyevetaro mṛgaḥ
a adya madbāṇavegena pretarāḍ viṣayaṃ gataḥ
c ye tvayā nihatāḥ śūrāḥ saha tais tvaṃ sameṣyasi
a bahunātra kim uktena śṛṇu rāma vaco mama
c paśyantu sakalā lokās tvāṃ māṃ caiva raṇājire
a astrair vā gadayā vāpi bāhubhyāṃ vā mahāhave
c abhyastaṃ yena vā rāma tena vā vartatāṃ yudhi
a makarākṣavacaḥ śrutvā rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ
c abravīt prahasan vākyam uttarottaravādinam
a caturdaśasahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ tvatpitā ca yaḥ
c triśirā dūṣaṇaś cāpi daṇḍake nihatā mayā
a svāśitās tava māṃsena gṛdhragomāyuvāyasāḥ
c bhaviṣyanty adya vai pāpa tīkṣṇatuṇḍanakhāṅkuśāḥ
a evam uktas tu rāmeṇa kharaputro niśācaraḥ
c bāṇaughān asṛjat tasmai rāghavāya raṇājire
a tāñ śarāñ śaravarṣeṇa rāmaś ciccheda naikadhā
c nipetur bhuvi te chinnā rukmapuṅkhāḥ sahasraśaḥ
a tad yuddham abhavat tatra sametyānyonyam ojasā
c khara rākṣasaputrasya sūnor daśarathasya ca
a jīmūtayor ivākāśe śabdo jyātalayos tadā
c dhanur muktaḥ svanotkṛṣṭaḥ śrūyate ca raṇājire
a devadānavagandharvāḥ kiṃnarāś ca mahoragāḥ
c antarikṣagatāḥ sarve draṣṭukāmās tad adbhutam
a viddham anyonyagātreṣu dviguṇaṃ vardhate balam
c kṛtapratikṛtānyonyaṃ kurvāte tau raṇājire
a rāmam uktās tu bāṇaughān rākṣasas tv acchinad raṇe
c rakṣomuktāṃs tu rāmo vai naikadhā prācchinac charaiḥ
a bāṇaughavitatāḥ sarvā diśaś ca vidiśas tathā
c saṃchannā vasudhā caiva samantān na prakāśate
a tataḥ kruddho mahābāhur dhanuś ciccheda rakṣasaḥ
c aṣṭābhir atha nārācaiḥ sūtaṃ vivyādha rāghavaḥ
e bhittvā śarai rathaṃ rāmo rathāśvān samapātayat
a viratho vasudhāṃ tiṣṭhan makarākṣo niśācaraḥ
c atiṣṭhad vasudhāṃ rakṣaḥ śūlaṃ jagrāha pāṇinā
e trāsanaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ yugāntāgnisamaprabham
a vibhrāmya ca mahac chūlaṃ prajvalantaṃ niśācaraḥ
c sa krodhāt prāhiṇot tasmai rāghavāya mahāhave
a tam āpatantaṃ jvalitaṃ kharaputrakarāc cyutam
c bāṇais tu tribhir ākāśe śūlaṃ ciccheda rāghavaḥ
a sacchinno naikadhā śūlo divyahāṭakamaṇḍitaḥ
c vyaśīryata mahokleva rāmabāṇārdito bhuvi
a tac chūlaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmeṇādbhutakarmaṇā
c sādhu sādhv iti bhūtāni vyāharanti nabhogatāḥ
a tad dṛṣṭvā nihataṃ śūlaṃ makarākṣo niśācaraḥ
c muṣṭim udyamya kākutsthaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā patantaṃ vai prahasya raghunandanaḥ
c pāvakāstraṃ tato rāmaḥ saṃdadhe svaśarāsane
a tenāstreṇa hataṃ rakṣaḥ kākutsthena tadā raṇe
c saṃchinnahṛdayaṃ tatra papāta ca mamāra ca
a dṛṣṭvā te rākṣasāḥ sarve makarākṣasya pātanam
c laṅkām eva pradhāvanta rāmabālārditās tadā
a daśarathanṛpaputrabāṇavegai
rajanicaraṃ nihataṃ kharātmajaṃ tam
c dadṛśur atha ca devatāḥ prahṛṣṭā
girim iva vajrahataṃ yathā viśīrṇam
a makarākṣaṃ hataṃ śrutvā rāvaṇaḥ samitiṃjayaḥ
c ādideśātha saṃkruddho raṇāyendrajitaṃ sutam
a jahi vīra mahāvīryau bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau
c adṛśyo dṛśyamāno vā sarvathā tvaṃ balādhikaḥ
a tvam apratimakarmāṇam indraṃ jayasi saṃyuge
c kiṃ punar mānuṣau dṛṣṭvā na vadhiṣyasi saṃyuge
a tathokto rākṣasendreṇa pratigṛhya pitur vacaḥ
c yajñabhūmau sa vidhivat pāvakaṃ juhuve ndrajit
a juhvataś cāpi tatrāgniṃ raktoṣṇīṣadharāḥ striyaḥ
c ājagmus tatra saṃbhrāntā rākṣasyo yatra rāvaṇiḥ
a śastrāṇi śarapatrāṇi samidho 'tha vibhītakāḥ
c lohitāni ca vāsāṃsi sruvaṃ kārṣṇāyasaṃ tathā
a sarvato 'gniṃ samāstīrya śarapatraiḥ samantataḥ
c chāgasya sarvakṛṣṇasya galaṃ jagrāha jīvataḥ
a caruhomasamiddhasya vidhūmasya mahārciṣaḥ
c babhūvus tāni liṅgāni vijayaṃ darśayanti ca
a pradakṣiṇāvartaśikhas taptahāṭakasaṃnibhaḥ
c havis tat pratijagrāha pāvakaḥ svayam utthitaḥ
a hutvāgniṃ tarpayitvātha devadānavarākṣasān
c āruroha rathaśreṣṭham antardhānagataṃ śubham
a sa vājibhiś caturbhis tu bāṇaiś ca niśitair yutaḥ
c āropitamahācāpaḥ śuśubhe syandanottame
a jājvalyamāno vapuṣā tapanīyaparicchadaḥ
c śaraiś candrārdhacandraiś ca sa rathaḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ
a jāmbūnadamahākambur dīptapāvakasaṃnibhaḥ
c babhūvendrajitaḥ ketur vaidūryasamalaṃkṛtaḥ
a tena cādityakalpena brahmāstreṇa ca pālitaḥ
c sa babhūva durādharṣo rāvaṇiḥ sumahābalaḥ
a so 'bhiniryāya nagarād indrajit samitiṃjayaḥ
c hutvāgniṃ rākṣasair mantrair antardhānagato 'bravīt
a adya hatvāhave yau tau mithyā pravrajitau vane
c jayaṃ pitre pradāsyāmi rāvaṇāya raṇādhikam
a kṛtvā nirvānarām urvīṃ hatvā rāmaṃ salakṣmaṇam
c kariṣye paramāṃ prītim ity uktvāntaradhīyata
a āpapātātha saṃkruddho daśagrīveṇa coditaḥ
c tīkṣṇakārmukanārācais tīkṣṇas tv indraripū raṇe
a sa dadarśa mahāvīryau nāgau triśirasāv iva
c sṛjantāv iṣujālāni vīrau vānaramadhyagau
a imau tāv iti saṃcintya sajyaṃ kṛtvā ca kārmukam
c saṃtatāneṣudhārābhiḥ parjanya iva vṛṣṭimān
a sa tu vaihāyasaṃ prāpya saratho rāmalakṣmaṇau
c acakṣur viṣaye tiṣṭhan vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tau tasya śaravegena parītau rāmalakṣmaṇau
c dhanuṣī saśare kṛtvā divyam astraṃ pracakratuḥ
a pracchādayantau gaganaṃ śarajālair mahābalau
c tam astraiḥ surasaṃkāśau naiva pasparśatuḥ śaraiḥ
a sa hi dhūmāndhakāraṃ ca cakre pracchādayan nabhaḥ
c diśaś cāntardadhe śrīmān nīhāratamasāvṛtaḥ
a naiva jyātalanirghoṣo na ca nemikhurasvanaḥ
c śuśruve caratas tasya na ca rūpaṃ prakāśate
a ghanāndhakāre timire śaravarṣam ivādbhutam
c sa vavarṣa mahābāhur nārācaśaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
a sa rāmaṃ sūryasaṃkāśaiḥ śarair dattavaro bhṛśam
c vivyādha samare kruddhaḥ sarvagātreṣu rāvaṇiḥ
a tau hanyamānau nārācair dhārābhir iva parvatau
c hemapuṅkhān naravyāghrau tigmān mumucatuḥ śarān
a antarikṣaṃ samāsādya rāvaṇiṃ kaṅkapatriṇaḥ
c nikṛtya patagā bhūmau petus te śoṇitokṣitāḥ
a atimātraṃ śaraugheṇa pīḍyamānau narottamau
c tān iṣūn patato bhallair anekair nicakartatuḥ
a yato hi dadṛśāte tau śarān nipatitāñ śitān
c tatas tato dāśarathī sasṛjāte 'stram uttamam
a rāvaṇis tu diśaḥ sarvā rathenātirathaḥ patan
c vivyādha tau dāśarathī laghv astro niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tenātividdhau tau vīrau rukmapuṅkhaiḥ susaṃhataiḥ
c babhūvatur dāśarathī puṣpitāv iva kiṃśukau
a nāsya veda gatiṃ kaś cin na ca rūpaṃ dhanuḥ śarān
c na cānyad viditaṃ kiṃ cit sūryasyevābhrasaṃplave
a tena viddhāś ca harayo nihatāś ca gatāsavaḥ
c babhūvuḥ śataśas tatra patitā dharaṇītale
a lakṣmaṇas tu susaṃkruddho bhrātaraṃ vākyam abravīt
c brāhmam astraṃ prayokṣyāmi vadhārthaṃ sarvarakṣasām
a tam uvāca tato rāmo lakṣmaṇaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam
c naikasya heto rakṣāṃsi pṛthivyāṃ hantum arhasi
a ayudhyamānaṃ pracchannaṃ prāñjaliṃ śaraṇāgatam
c palāyantaṃ pramattaṃ vā na tvaṃ hantum ihārhasi
a asyaiva tu vadhe yatnaṃ kariṣyāvo mahābala
c ādekṣyāvo mahāvegān astrān āśīviṣopamān
a tam enaṃ māyinaṃ kṣudram antarhitarathaṃ balāt
c rākṣasaṃ nihaniṣyanti dṛṣṭvā vānarayūthapāḥ
a yady eṣa bhūmiṃ viśate divaṃ vā
rasātalaṃ vāpi nabhastalaṃ vā
c evaṃ nigūḍho 'pi mamāstradagdhaḥ
patiṣyate bhūmitale gatāsuḥ
a ity evam uktvā vacanaṃ mahātmā
raghupravīraḥ plavagarṣabhair vṛtaḥ
c vadhāya raudrasya nṛśaṃsakarmaṇas
tadā mahātmā tvaritaṃ nirīkṣate
a vijñāya tu manas tasya rāghavasya mahātmanaḥ
c saṃnivṛtyāhavāt tasmāt praviveśa puraṃ tataḥ
a so 'nusmṛtya vadhaṃ teṣāṃ rākṣasānāṃ tarasvinām
c krodhatāmrekṣaṇaḥ śūro nirjagāma mahādyutiḥ
a sa paścimena dvāreṇa niryayau rākṣasair vṛtaḥ
c indrajit tu mahāvīryaḥ paulastyo devakaṇṭakaḥ
a indrajit tu tato dṛṣṭvā bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau
c raṇāyābhyudyatau vīrau māyāṃ prāduṣkarot tadā
a indrajit tu rathe sthāpya sītāṃ māyāmayīṃ tadā
c balena mahatāvṛtya tasyā vadham arocayat
a mohanārthaṃ tu sarveṣāṃ buddhiṃ kṛtvā sudurmatiḥ
c hantuṃ sītāṃ vyavasito vānarābhimukho yayau
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā tv abhiniryāntaṃ nagaryāḥ kānanaukasaḥ
c utpetur abhisaṃkruddhāḥ śilāhastā yuyutsavaḥ
a hanūmān puratas teṣāṃ jagāma kapikuñjaraḥ
c pragṛhya sumahac chṛṅgaṃ parvatasya durāsadam
a sa dadarśa hatānandāṃ sītām indrajito rathe
c ekaveṇīdharāṃ dīnām upavāsakṛśānanām
a parikliṣṭaikavasanām amṛjāṃ rāghavapriyām
c rajomalābhyām āliptaiḥ sarvagātrair varastriyam
a tāṃ nirīkṣya muhūrtaṃ tu maithilīm adhyavasya ca
c bāṣpaparyākulamukho hanūmān vyathito 'bhavat
a abravīt tāṃ tu śokārtāṃ nirānandāṃ tapasvinām
c dṛṣṭvā rathe stitāṃ sītāṃ rākṣasendrasutāśritām
a kiṃ samarthitam asyeti cintayan sa mahākapiḥ
c saha tair vānaraśreṣṭhair abhyadhāvata rāvaṇim
a tad vānarabalaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇiḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
c kṛtvā viśokaṃ nistriṃśaṃ mūrdhni sītāṃ parāmṛśat
a taṃ striyaṃ paśyatāṃ teṣāṃ tāḍayām āsa rāvaṇiḥ
c krośantīṃ rāma rāmeti māyayā yojitāṃ rathe
a gṛhītamūrdhajāṃ dṛṣṭvā hanūmān dainyam āgataḥ
c duḥkhajaṃ vārinetrābhyām utsṛjan mārutātmajaḥ
e abravīt paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ krodhād rakṣo'dhipātmajam
a durātmann ātmanāśāya keśapakṣe parāmṛśaḥ
c brahmarṣīṇāṃ kule jāto rākṣasīṃ yonim āśritaḥ
e dhik tvāṃ pāpasamācāraṃ yasya te matir īdṛśī
a nṛśaṃsānārya durvṛtta kṣudra pāpaparākrama
c anāryasyedṛśaṃ karma ghṛṇā te nāsti nirghṛṇa
a cyutā gṛhāc ca rājyāc ca rāmahastāc ca maithilī
c kiṃ tavaiṣāparāddhā hi yad enāṃ hantum icchasi
a sītāṃ ca hatvā na ciraṃ jīviṣyasi kathaṃ cana
c vadhārhakarmaṇānena mama hastagato hy asi
a ye ca strīghātināṃ lokā lokavadhyaiś ca kutsitāḥ
c iha jīvitam utsṛjya pretya tān pratilapsyase
a iti bruvāṇo hanumān sāyudhair haribhir vṛtaḥ
c abhyadhāvata saṃkruddho rākṣasendrasutaṃ prati
a āpatantaṃ mahāvīryaṃ tad anīkaṃ vanaukasām
c rakṣasāṃ bhīmavegānām anīkena nyavārayat
a sa tāṃ bāṇasahasreṇa vikṣobhya harivāhinīm
c hariśreṣṭhaṃ hanūmantam indrajit pratyuvāca ha
a sugrīvas tvaṃ ca rāmaś ca yannimittam ihāgatāḥ
c tāṃ haniṣyāmi vaidehīm adyaiva tava paśyataḥ
a imāṃ hatvā tato rāmaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ tvāṃ ca vānara
c sugrīvaṃ ca vadhiṣyāmi taṃ cānāryaṃ vibhīṣaṇam
a na hantavyāḥ striyaś ceti yad bravīṣi plavaṃgama
c pīḍā karam amitrāṇāṃ yat syāt kartavyam eta tat
a tam evam uktvā rudatīṃ sītāṃ māyāmayīṃ tataḥ
c śitadhāreṇa khaḍgena nijaghānendrajit svayam
a yajñopavītamārgeṇa chinnā tena tapasvinī
c sā pṛthivyāṃ pṛthuśroṇī papāta priyadarśanā
a tām indrajitstriyaṃ hatvā hanūmantam uvāca ha
c mayā rāmasya paśyemāṃ kopena ca niṣūditām
a tataḥ khaḍgena mahatā hatvā tām indrajit svayam
c hṛṣṭaḥ sa ratham āsthāya vinanāda mahāsvanam
a vānarāḥ śuśruvuḥ śabdam adūre pratyavasthitāḥ
c vyāditāsyasya nadatas tad durgaṃ saṃśritasya tu
a tathā tu sītāṃ vinihatya durmatiḥ
prahṛṣṭacetāḥ sa babhūva rāvaṇiḥ
c taṃ hṛṣṭarūpaṃ samudīkṣya vānarā
viṣaṇṇarūpāḥ samabhipradudruvuḥ
a śrutvā taṃ bhīmanirhrādaṃ śakrāśanisamasvanam
c vīkṣamāṇā diśaḥ sarvā dudruvur vānararṣabhāḥ
a tān uvāca tataḥ sarvān hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
c viṣaṇṇavadanān dīnāṃs trastān vidravataḥ pṛthak
a kasmād viṣaṇṇavadanā vidravadhvaṃ plavaṃgamāḥ
c tyaktayuddhasamutsāhāḥ śūratvaṃ kva nu vo gatam
a pṛṣṭhato 'nuvrajadhvaṃ mām agrato yāntam āhave
c śūrair abhijanopetair ayuktaṃ hi nivartitum
a evam uktāḥ susaṃkruddhā vāyuputreṇa dhīmatā
c śailaśṛṅgān drumāṃś caiva jagṛhur hṛṣṭamānasāḥ
a abhipetuś ca garjanto rākṣasān vānararṣabhāḥ
c parivārya hanūmantam anvayuś ca mahāhave
a sa tair vānaramukhyais tu hanūmān sarvato vṛtaḥ
c hutāśana ivārciṣmān adahac chatruvāhinīm
a sa rākṣasānāṃ kadanaṃ cakāra sumahākapiḥ
c vṛto vānarasainyena kālāntakayamopamaḥ
a sa tu śokena cāviṣṭaḥ krodhena ca mahākapiḥ
c hanūmān rāvaṇi rathe mahatīṃ pātayac chilām
a tām āpatantīṃ dṛṣṭvaiva rathaḥ sārathinā tadā
c vidheyāśva samāyuktaḥ sudūram apavāhitaḥ
a tam indrajitam aprāpya rathathaṃ sahasārathim
c viveśa dharaṇīṃ bhittvā sā śilāvyartham udyatā
a patitāyāṃ śilāyāṃ tu rakṣasāṃ vyathitā camūḥ
c tam abhyadhāvañ śataśo nadantaḥ kānanaukasaḥ
a te drumāṃś ca mahākāyā giriśṛṅgāṇi codyatāḥ
c cikṣipur dviṣatāṃ madhye vānarā bhīmavikramāḥ
a vānarair tair mahāvīryair ghorarūpā niśācarāḥ
c vīryād abhihatā vṛkṣair vyaveṣṭanta raṇakṣitau
a svasainyam abhivīkṣyātha vānarārditam indrajit
c pragṛhītāyudhaḥ kruddhaḥ parān abhimukho yayau
a sa śaraughān avasṛjan svasainyenābhisaṃvṛtaḥ
c jaghāna kapiśārdūlān subahūn dṛṣṭavikramaḥ
a śūlair aśanibhiḥ khaḍgaiḥ paṭṭasaiḥ kūṭamudgaraiḥ
c te cāpy anucarāṃs tasya vānarā jaghnur āhave
a saskandhaviṭapaiḥ sālaiḥ śilābhiś ca mahābalaiḥ
c hanūmān kadanaṃ cakre rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām
a sa nivārya parānīkam abravīt tān vanaukasaḥ
c hanūmān saṃnivartadhvaṃ na naḥ sādhyam idaṃ balam
a tyaktvā prāṇān viceṣṭanto rāma priyacikīrṣavaḥ
c yannimittaṃ hi yudhyāmo hatā sā janakātmajā
a imam arthaṃ hi vijñāpya rāmaṃ sugrīvam eva ca
c tau yat pratividhāsyete tat kariṣyāmahe vayam
a ity uktvā vānaraśreṣṭho vārayan sarvavānarān
c śanaiḥ śanair asaṃtrastaḥ sabalaḥ sa nyavartata
a sa tu prekṣya hanūmantaṃ vrajantaṃ yatra rāghavaḥ
c nikumbhilām adhiṣṭhāya pāvakaṃ juhuve ndrajit
a yajñabhūmyāṃ tu vidhivat pāvakas tena rakṣasā
c hūyamānaḥ prajajvāla homaśoṇitabhuk tadā
a so 'rciḥ pinaddho dadṛśe homaśoṇitatarpitaḥ
c saṃdhyāgata ivādityaḥ sa tīvrāgniḥ samutthitaḥ
a athendrajid rākṣasabhūtaye tu
juhāva havyaṃ vidhinā vidhānavat
c dṛṣṭvā vyatiṣṭhanta ca rākṣasās te
mahāsamūheṣu nayānayajñāḥ
a rāghavaś cāpi vipulaṃ taṃ rākṣasavanaukasām
c śrutvā saṃgrāmanirghoṣaṃ jāmbavantam uvāca ha
a saumya nūnaṃ hanumatā kṛtaṃ karma suduṣkaram
c śrūyate hi yathā bhīmaḥ sumahān āyudhasvanaḥ
a tad gaccha kuru sāhāyyaṃ svabalenābhisaṃvṛtaḥ
c kṣipram ṛṣkapate tasya kapiśreṣṭhasya yudhyataḥ
a ṛkṣarājas tathety uktvā svenānīkena saṃvṛtaḥ
c āgacchat paścimadvāraṃ hanūmān yatra vānaraḥ
a athāyāntaṃ hanūmantaṃ dadarśarkṣapatiḥ pathi
c vānaraiḥ kṛtasaṃgrāmaiḥ śvasadbhir abhisaṃvṛtam
a dṛṣṭvā pathi hanūmāṃś ca tad ṛṣkabalam udyatam
c nīlameghanibhaṃ bhīmaṃ saṃnivārya nyavartata
a sa tena harisainyena saṃnikarṣaṃ mahāyaśāḥ
c śīghram āgamya rāmāya duḥkhito vākyam abravīt
a samare yudhyamānānām asmākaṃ prekṣatāṃ ca saḥ
c jaghāna rudatīṃ sītām indrajid rāvaṇātmajaḥ
a udbhrāntacittas tāṃ dṛṣṭvā viṣaṇṇo 'ham ariṃdama
c tad ahaṃ bhavato vṛttaṃ vijñāpayitum āgataḥ
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rāghavaḥ śokamūrchitaḥ
c nipapāta tadā bhūmau chinnamūla iva drumaḥ
a taṃ bhūmau devasaṃkāśaṃ patitaṃ dṛśya rāghavam
c abhipetuḥ samutpatya sarvataḥ kapisattamāḥ
a asiñcan salilaiś cainaṃ padmotpalasugandhibhiḥ
c pradahantam asahyaṃ ca sahasāgnim ivotthitam
a taṃ lakṣmaṇo 'tha bāhubhyāṃ pariṣvajya suduḥkhitaḥ
c uvāca rāmam asvasthaṃ vākyaṃ hetvarthasaṃhitam
a śubhe vartmani tiṣṭhantaṃ tvām āryavijitendriyam
c anarthebhyo na śaknoti trātuṃ dharmo nirarthakaḥ
a bhūtānāṃ sthāvarāṇāṃ ca jaṅgamānāṃ ca darśanam
c yathāsti na tathā dharmas tena nāstīti me matiḥ
a yathaiva sthāvaraṃ vyaktaṃ jaṅgamaṃ ca tathāvidham
c nāyam arthas tathā yuktas tvadvidho na vipadyate
a yady adharmo bhaved bhūto rāvaṇo narakaṃ vrajet
c bhavāṃś ca dharmasaṃyukto naivaṃ vyasanam āpnuyāt
a tasya ca vyasanābhāvād vyasanaṃ ca gate tvayi
c dharmeṇopalabhed dharmam adharmaṃ cāpy adharmataḥ
a yadi dharmeṇa yujyeran nādharmarucayo janāḥ
c dharmeṇa caratāṃ dharmas tathā caiṣāṃ phalaṃ bhavet
a yasmād arthā vivardhante yeṣv adharmaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
c kliśyante dharmaśīlāś ca tasmād etau nirarthakau
a vadhyante pāpakarmāṇo yady adharmeṇa rāghava
c vadhakarmahato dharmaḥ sa hataḥ kaṃ vadhiṣyati
a atha vā vihitenāyaṃ hanyate hanti vā param
c vidhir ālipyate tena na sa pāpena karmaṇā
a adṛṣṭapratikāreṇa avyaktenāsatā satā
c kathaṃ śakyaṃ paraṃ prāptuṃ dharmeṇārivikarśana
a yadi sat syāt satāṃ mukhya nāsat syāt tava kiṃ cana
c tvayā yadīdṛśaṃ prāptaṃ tasmāt san nopapadyate
a atha vā durbalaḥ klībo balaṃ dharmo 'nuvartate
c durbalo hṛtamaryādo na sevya iti me matiḥ
a balasya yadi ced dharmo guṇabhūtaḥ parākrame
c dharmam utsṛjya vartasva yathā dharme tathā bale
a atha cet satyavacanaṃ dharmaḥ kila paraṃtapa
c anṛtas tvayy akaruṇaḥ kiṃ na baddhas tvayā pitā
a yadi dharmo bhaved bhūta adharmo vā paraṃtapa
c na sma hatvā muniṃ vajrī kuryād ijyāṃ śatakratuḥ
a adharmasaṃśrito dharmo vināśayati rāghava
c sarvam etad yathākāmaṃ kākutstha kurute naraḥ
a mama cedaṃ mataṃ tāta dharmo 'yam iti rāghava
c dharmamūlaṃ tvayā chinnaṃ rājyam utsṛjatā tadā
a arthebhyo hi vivṛddhebhyaḥ saṃvṛddhebhyas tatas tataḥ
c kriyāḥ sarvāḥ pravartante parvatebhya ivāpagāḥ
a arthena hi viyuktasya puruṣasyālpatejasaḥ
c vyucchidyante kriyāḥ sarvā grīṣme kusarito yathā
a so 'yam arthaṃ parityajya sukhakāmaḥ sukhaidhitaḥ
c pāpam ārabhate kartuṃ tathā doṣaḥ pravartate
a yasyārthās tasya mitrāṇi yasyārthās tasya bāndhavaḥ
c yasyārthāḥ sa pumāṃl loke yasyārthāḥ sa ca paṇḍitaḥ
a yasyārthāḥ sa ca vikrānto yasyārthāḥ sa ca buddhimān
c yasyārthāḥ sa mahābhāgo yasyārthāḥ sa mahāguṇaḥ
a arthasyaite parityāge doṣāḥ pravyāhṛtā mayā
c rājyam utsṛjatā vīra yena buddhis tvayā kṛtā
a yasyārthā dharmakāmārthās tasya sarvaṃ pradakṣiṇam
c adhanenārthakāmena nārthaḥ śakyo vicinvatā
a harṣaḥ kāmaś ca darpaś ca dharmaḥ krodhaḥ śamo damaḥ
c arthād etāni sarvāṇi pravartante narādhipa
a yeṣāṃ naśyaty ayaṃ lokaś caratāṃ dharmacāriṇām
c te 'rthās tvayi na dṛśyante durdineṣu yathā grahāḥ
a tvayi pravrajite vīra guroś ca vacane sthite
c rakṣasāpahṛtā bhāryā prāṇaiḥ priyatarā tava
a tad adya vipulaṃ vīra duḥkham indrajitā kṛtam
c karmaṇā vyapaneṣyāmi tasmād uttiṣṭha rāghava
a ayam anagha tavoditaḥ priyārthaṃ
janakasutā nidhanaṃ nirīkṣya ruṣṭaḥ
c sahayagajarathāṃ sarākṣasendrāṃ
bhṛśam iṣubhir vinipātayāmi laṅkām
a rāmam āśvāsayāne tu lakṣmaṇe bhrātṛvatsale
c nikṣipya gulmān svasthāne tatrāgacchad vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a nānāpraharaṇair vīraiś caturbhiḥ sacivair vṛtaḥ
c nīlāñjanacayākārair mātaṃgair iva yūthapaḥ
a so 'bhigamya mahātmānaṃ rāghavaṃ śokalālasaṃ
c vānarāṃś caiva dadṛśe bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇān
a rāghavaṃ ca mahātmānam ikṣvākukulanandanam
c dadarśa moham āpannaṃ lakṣmaṇasyāṅkam āśritam
a vrīḍitaṃ śokasaṃtaptaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmaṃ vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c antarduḥkhena dīnātmā kim etad iti so 'bravīt
a vibhīṣaṇa mukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā sugrīvaṃ tāṃś ca vānarān
c uvāca lakṣmaṇo vākyam idaṃ bāṣpapariplutaḥ
a hatām indrajitā sītām iha śrutvaiva rāghavaḥ
c hanūmad vacanāt saumya tato moham upāgataḥ
a kathayantaṃ tu saumitriṃ saṃnivārya vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c puṣkalārtham idaṃ vākyaṃ visaṃjñaṃ rāmam abravīt
a manujendrārtarūpeṇa yad uktas tvaṃ hanūmatā
c tad ayuktam ahaṃ manye sāgarasyeva śoṣaṇam
a abhiprāyaṃ tu jānāmi rāvaṇasya durātmanaḥ
c sītāṃ prati mahābāho na ca ghātaṃ kariṣyati
a yācyamānaḥ subahuśo mayā hitacikīrṣuṇā
c vaidehīm utsṛjasveti na ca tat kṛtavān vacaḥ
a naiva sāmnā na bhedena na dānena kuto yudhā
c sā draṣṭum api śakyeta naiva cānyena kena cit
a vānarān mohayitvā tu pratiyātaḥ sa rākṣasaḥ
c caityaṃ nikumbhilāṃ nāma yatra homaṃ kariṣyati
a hutavān upayāto hi devair api savāsavaiḥ
c durādharṣo bhavaty eṣa saṃgrāme rāvaṇātmajaḥ
a tena mohayatā nūnam eṣā māyā prayojitā
c vighnam anvicchatā tāta vānarāṇāṃ parākrame
e sasainyās tatra gacchāmo yāvat tan na samāpyate
a tyajemaṃ naraśārdūlamithyā saṃtāpam āgatam
c sīdate hi balaṃ sarvaṃ dṛṣṭvā tvāṃ śokakarśitam
a iha tvaṃ svastha hṛdayas tiṣṭha sattvasamucchritaḥ
c lakṣmaṇaṃ preṣayāsmābhiḥ saha sainyānukarṣibhiḥ
a eṣa taṃ naraśārdūlo rāvaṇiṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c tyājayiṣyati tat karma tato vadhyo bhaviṣyati
a tasyaite niśitās tīkṣṇāḥ patripatrāṅgavājinaḥ
c patatriṇa ivāsaumyāḥ śarāḥ pāsyanti śoṇitam
a tat saṃdiśa mahābāho lakṣmaṇaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam
c rākṣasasya vināśāya vajraṃ vajradharo yathā
a manujavara na kālaviprakarṣo
ripunidhanaṃ prati yat kṣamo 'dya kartum
c tvam atisṛja ripor vadhāya bāṇīm
asurapuronmathane yathā mahendraḥ
a samāptakarmā hi sa rākṣasendro
bhavaty adṛśyaḥ samare surāsuraiḥ
c yuyutsatā tena samāptakarmaṇā
bhavet surāṇām api saṃśayo mahān
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rāghavaḥ śokakarśitaḥ
c nopadhārayate vyaktaṃ yad uktaṃ tena rakṣasā
a tato dhairyam avaṣṭabhya rāmaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
c vibhīṣaṇam upāsīnam uvāca kapisaṃnidhau
a nairṛtādhipate vākyaṃ yad uktaṃ te vibhīṣaṇa
c bhūyas tac chrotum icchāmi brūhi yat te vivakṣitam
a rāghavasya vacaḥ śrutvā vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ
c yat tat punar idaṃ vākyaṃ babhāṣe sa vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a yathājñaptaṃ mahābāho tvayā gulmaniveśanam
c tat tathānuṣṭhitaṃ vīra tvadvākyasamanantaram
a tāny anīkāni sarvāṇi vibhaktāni samantataḥ
c vinyastā yūthapāś caiva yathānyāyaṃ vibhāgaśaḥ
a bhūyas tu mama vijāpyaṃ tac chṛṇuṣva mahāyaśaḥ
c tvayy akāraṇasaṃtapte saṃtaptahṛdayā vayam
a tyaja rājann imaṃ śokaṃ mithyā saṃtāpam āgatam
c tad iyaṃ tyajyatāṃ cintā śatruharṣavivardhanī
a udyamaḥ kriyatāṃ vīra harṣaḥ samupasevyatām
c prāptavyā yadi te sītā hantavyaś vca niśācarāḥ
a raghunandana vakṣyāmi śrūyatāṃ me hitaṃ vacaḥ
c sādhv ayaṃ yātu saumitrir balena mahatā vṛtaḥ
e nikumbhilāyāṃ saṃprāpya hantuṃ rāvaṇim āhave
a dhanurmaṇḍalanirmuktair āśīviṣaviṣopamaiḥ
c śarair hantuṃ maheṣvāso rāvaṇiṃ samitiṃjayaḥ
a tena vīreṇa tapasā varadānāt svayambhutaḥ
c astraṃ brahmaśiraḥ prāptaṃ kāmagāś ca turaṃgamāḥ
a nikumbhilām asaṃprāptam ahutāgniṃ ca yo ripuḥ
c tvām ātatāyinaṃ hanyād indraśatro sa te vadhaḥ
e ity evaṃ vihito rājan vadhas tasyaiva dhīmataḥ
a vadhāyendrajito rāma taṃ diśasva mahābalam
c hate tasmin hataṃ viddhi rāvaṇaṃ sasuhṛjjanam
a vibhīṣaṇavacaḥ śrutva rāmo vākyam athābravīt
c jānāmi tasya raudrasya māyāṃ satyaparākrama
a sa hi brahmāstravit prājño mahāmāyo mahābalaḥ
c karoty asaṃjñān saṃgrāme devān savaruṇān api
a tasyāntarikṣe carato rathasthasya mahāyaśaḥ
c na gatir jñāyate vīrasūryasyevābhrasaṃplave
a rāghavas tu ripor jñātvā māyāvīryaṃ durātmanaḥ
c lakṣmaṇaṃ kīrtisaṃpannam idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a yad vānarendrasya balaṃ tena sarveṇa saṃvṛtaḥ
c hanūmatpramukhaiś caiva yūthapaiḥ sahalakṣmaṇa
a jāmbavenarkṣapatinā saha sainyena saṃvṛtaḥ
c jahi taṃ rākṣasasutaṃ māyābalaviśāradam
a ayaṃ tvāṃ sacivaiḥ sārdhaṃ mahātmā rajanīcaraḥ
c abhijñas tasya deśasya pṛṣṭhato 'nugamiṣyati
a rāghavasya vacaḥ śrutvā lakṣmaṇaḥ savibhīṣaṇaḥ
c jagrāha kārmukaṃ śreṣṭham anyad bhīmaparākramaḥ
a saṃnaddhaḥ kavacī khaḍgī sa śarī hemacāpadhṛk
c rāmapādāv upaspṛśya hṛṣṭaḥ saumitrir abravīt
a adya matkārmukonmukhāḥ śarā nirbhidya rāvaṇim
c laṅkām abhipatiṣyanti haṃsāḥ puṣkariṇīm iva
a adyaiva tasya raudrasya śarīraṃ māmakāḥ śarāḥ
c vidhamiṣyanti hatvā taṃ mahācāpaguṇacyutāḥ
a sa evam uktvā dyutimān vacanaṃ bhrātur agrataḥ
c sa rāvaṇivadhākāṅkṣī lakṣmaṇas tvarito yayau
a so 'bhivādya guroḥ pādau kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇam
c nikumbhilām abhiyayau caityaṃ rāvaṇipālitam
a vibhīṣaṇena sahito rājaputraḥ pratāpavān
c kṛtasvastyayano bhrātrā lakṣmaṇas tvarito yayau
a vānarāṇāṃ sahasrais tu hanūmān bahubhir vṛtaḥ
c vibhīṣaṇaḥ sahāmātyas tadā lakṣmaṇam anvagāt
a mahatā harisainyena savegam abhisaṃvṛtaḥ
c ṛkṣarājabalaṃ caiva dadarśa pathi viṣṭhitam
a sa gatvā dūram adhvānaṃ saumitrir mitranandanaḥ
c rākṣasendrabalaṃ dūrād apaśyad vyūham āsthitam
a sa saṃprāpya dhanuṣpāṇir māyāyogam ariṃdama
c tasthau brahmavidhānena vijetuṃ raghunandanaḥ
a vividham amalaśastrabhāsvaraṃ tad
dhvajagahanaṃ vipulaṃ mahārathaiś ca
c pratibhayatamam aprameyavegaṃ
timiram iva dviṣatāṃ balaṃ viveśa
a atha tasyām avasthāyāṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ rāvaṇānujaḥ
c pareṣām ahitaṃ vākyam arthasādhakam abravīt
a asyānīkasya mahato bhedane yatalakṣmaṇa
c rākṣasendrasuto 'py atra bhinne dṛśyo bhaviṣyati
a sa tvam indrāśaniprakhyaiḥ śarair avakiran parān
c abhidravāśu yāvad vai naitat karma samāpyate
a jahi vīradurātmānaṃ māyāparam adhārmikam
c rāvaṇiṃ krūrakarmāṇaṃ sarvalokabhayāvaham
a vibhīṣaṇavacaḥ śrutvā lakṣmaṇaḥ śubhalakṣaṇaḥ
c vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi rākṣasendrasutaṃ prati
a ṛkṣāḥ śākhāmṛgāś caiva drumādrivarayodhinaḥ
c abhyadhāvanta sahitās tad anīkam avasthitam
a rākṣasāś ca śitair bāṇair asibhiḥ śaktitomaraiḥ
c udyataiḥ samavartanta kapisainyajighāṃsavaḥ
a sa saṃprahāras tumulaḥ saṃjajñe kapirakṣasām
c śabdena mahatā laṅkāṃ nādayan vai samantataḥ
a śastrair bahuvidhākāraiḥ śitair bāṇaiś ca pādapaiḥ
c udyatair giriśṛṅgaiś ca ghorair ākāśam āvṛtam
a te rākṣasā vānareṣu vikṛtānanabāhavaḥ
c niveśayantaḥ śastrāṇi cakrus te sumahad bhayam
a tathaiva sakalair vṛkṣair giriśṛṅgaiś ca vānarāḥ
c abhijaghnur nijaghnuś ca samare rākṣasarṣabhān
a ṛkṣavānaramukhyaiś ca mahākāyair mahābalaiḥ
c rakṣasāṃ vadhyamānānāṃ mahad bhayam ajāyata
a svam anīkaṃ viṣaṇṇaṃ tu śrutvā śatrubhir arditam
c udatiṣṭhata durdharṣas tat karmaṇy ananuṣṭhite
a vṛkṣāndhakārān niṣkramya jātakrodhaḥ sa rāvaṇiḥ
c āruroha rathaṃ sajjaṃ pūrvayuktaṃ sa rākṣasaḥ
a sa bhīmakārmukaśaraḥ kṛṣṇāñjanacayopamaḥ
c raktāsyanayanaḥ krūro babhau mṛtyur ivāntakaḥ
a dṛṣṭvaiva tu rathasthaṃ taṃ paryavartata tad balam
c rakṣasāṃ bhīmavegānāṃ lakṣmaṇena yuyutsatām
a tasmin kāle tu hanumān udyamya sudurāsadam
c dharaṇīdharasaṃkāśī mahāvṛkṣam ariṃdamaḥ
a sa rākṣasānāṃ tat sainyaṃ kālāgnir iva nirdahan
c cakāra bahubhir vṛkṣair niḥsaṃjñaṃ yudhi vānaraḥ
a vidhvaṃsayantaṃ tarasā dṛṣṭvaiva pavanātmajam
c rākṣasānāṃ sahasrāṇi hanūmantam avākiran
a śitaśūladharāḥ śūlair asibhiś cāsipāṇayaḥ
c śaktibhiḥ śaktihastāś ca paṭṭasaiḥ paṭṭasāyudhāḥ
a parighaiś ca gadābhiś ca kuntaiś ca śubhadarśanaiḥ
c śataśaś ca śataghnībhir āyasair api mudgaraiḥ
a ghoraiḥ paraśubhiś caiva bhiṇḍipālaiś ca rākṣasāḥ
c muṣṭibhir vajravegaiś ca talair aśanisaṃnibhaiḥ
a abhijaghnuḥ samāsādya samantāt parvatopamam
c teṣām api ca saṃkruddhaś cakāra kadanaṃ mahat
a sa dadarśa kapiśreṣṭham acalopamam indrajit
c sūdayānam amitraghnam amitrān pavanātmajam
a sa sārathim uvācedaṃ yāhi yatraiṣa vānaraḥ
c kṣayam eva hi naḥ kuryād rākṣasānām upekṣitaḥ
a ity uktaḥ sārathis tena yayau yatra sa mārutiḥ
c vahan paramadurdharṣaṃ sthitam indrajitaṃ rathe
a so 'bhyupetya śarān khaḍgān paṭṭasāsiparaśvadhān
c abhyavarṣata durdharṣaḥ kapimūrdhni sa rākṣasaḥ
a tāni śastrāṇi ghorāṇi pratigṛhya sa mārutiḥ
c roṣeṇa mahatāviṣo vākyaṃ cedam uvāca ha
a yudhyasva yadi śūro 'si rāvaṇātmaja durmate
c vāyuputraṃ samāsādya na jīvan pratiyāsyasi
a bāhubhyāṃ saṃprayudhyasva yadi me dvandvam āhave
c vegaṃ sahasva durbuddhe tatas tvaṃ rakṣasāṃ varaḥ
a hanūmantaṃ jighāṃsantaṃ samudyataśarāsanam
c rāvaṇātmajam ācaṣṭe lakṣmaṇāya vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a yas tu vāsavanirjetā rāvaṇasyātmasaṃbhavaḥ
c sa eṣa ratham āsthāya hanūmantaṃ jighāṃsati
a tam apratimasaṃsthānaiḥ śaraiḥ śatruvidāraṇaiḥ
c jīvitāntakarair ghoraiḥ saumitre rāvaṇiṃ jahi
a ity evam uktas tu tadā mahātmā
vibhīṣaṇenārivibhīṣaṇena
c dadarśa taṃ parvatasaṃnikāśaṃ
rathasthitaṃ bhīmabalaṃ durāsadam
a evam uktvā tu saumitriṃ jātaharṣo vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c dhanuṣpāṇinam ādāya tvaramāṇo jagāma saḥ
a avidūraṃ tato gatvā praviśya ca mahad vanam
c darśayām āsa tat karma lakṣmaṇāya vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a nīlajīmūtasaṃkāśaṃ nyagrodhaṃ bhīmadarśanam
c tejasvī rāvaṇabhrātā lakṣmaṇāya nyavedayat
a ihopahāraṃ bhūtānāṃ balavān rāvaṇātajaḥ
c upahṛtya tataḥ paścāt saṃgrāmam abhivartate
a adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tato bhavati rākṣasaḥ
c nihanti samare śatrūn badhnāti ca śarottamaiḥ
a tam apraviṣṭaṃ nyagrodhaṃ balinaṃ rāvaṇātmajam
c vidhvaṃsaya śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ sarathaṃ sāśvasārathim
a tathety uktvā mahātejāḥ saumitrir mitranandanaḥ
c babhūvāvasthitas tatra citraṃ visphārayan dhanuḥ
a sa rathenāgnivarṇena balavān rāvaṇātmajaḥ
c indrajit kavacī khaḍgī sadhvajaḥ pratyadṛśyata
a tam uvāca mahātejāḥ paulastyam aparājitam
c samāhvaye tvāṃ samare samyag yuddhaṃ prayaccha me
a evam ukto mahātejā manasvī rāvaṇātmajaḥ
c abravīt paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ tatra dṛṣṭvā vibhīṣaṇam
a iha tvaṃ jātasaṃvṛddhaḥ sākṣād bhrātā pitur mama
c kathaṃ druhyasi putrasya pitṛvyo mama rākṣasa
a na jñātitvaṃ na sauhārdaṃ na jātis tava durmate
c pramāṇaṃ na ca sodaryaṃ na dharmo dharmadūṣaṇa
a śocyas tvam asi durbuddhe nindanīyaś ca sādhubhiḥ
c yas tvaṃ svajanam utsṛjya parabhṛtyatvam āgataḥ
a naitac chithilayā buddhyā tvaṃ vetsi mahad antaram
c kva ca svajanasaṃvāsaḥ kva ca nīcaparāśrayaḥ
a guṇavān vā parajanaḥ svajano nirguṇo 'pi vā
c nirguṇaḥ svajanaḥ śreyān yaḥ paraḥ para eva saḥ
a niranukrośatā ceyaṃ yādṛśī te niśācara
c svajanena tvayā śakyaṃ paruṣaṃ rāvaṇānuja
a ity ukto bhrātṛputreṇa pratyuvāca vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c ajānann iva macchīlaṃ kiṃ rākṣasa vikatthase
a rākṣasendrasutāsādho pāruṣyaṃ tyaja gauravāt
c kule yady apy ahaṃ jāto rakṣasāṃ krūrakarmaṇām
e guṇo 'yaṃ prathamo nṝṇāṃ tan me śīlam arākṣasaṃ
a na rame dāruṇenāhaṃ na cādharmeṇa vai rame
c bhrātrā viṣamaśīlena kathaṃ bhrātā nirasyate
a parasvānāṃ ca haraṇaṃ paradārābhimarśanam
c suhṛdām atiśaṅkāṃ ca trayo doṣāḥ kṣayāvahāḥ
a maharṣīṇāṃ vadho ghoraḥ sarvadevaiś ca vigrahaḥ
c abhimānaś ca kopaś ca vairitvaṃ pratikūlatā
a ete doṣā mama bhrātur jīvitaiśvaryanāśanāḥ
c guṇān pracchādayām āsuḥ parvatān iva toyadāḥ
a doṣair etaiḥ parityakto mayā bhrātā pitā tava
c neyam asti purī laṅkā na ca tvaṃ na ca te pitā
a atimānī ca bālaś ca durvinītaś ca rākṣasa
c baddhas tvaṃ kālapāśena brūhi māṃ yad yad icchasi
a adya te vyasanaṃ prāptaṃ kim iha tvaṃ tu vakṣyasi
c praveṣṭuṃ na tvayā śakyo nyagrodho rākṣasādhama
a dharṣayitvā tu kākutsthau na śakyaṃ jīvituṃ tvayā
c yudhyasva naradevena lakṣmaṇena raṇe saha
e hatas tvaṃ devatā kāryaṃ kariṣyasi yamakṣaye
a nidarśayasvātmabalaṃ samudyataṃ
kuruṣva sarvāyudhasāyakavyayam
c na lakṣmaṇasyaitya hi bāṇagocaraṃ
tvam adya jīvan sabalo gamiṣyasi
a vibhīṣaṇa vacaḥ śrutvā rāvaṇiḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
c abravīt paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ vegenābhyutpapāta ha
a udyatāyudhanistriṃśo rathe tu samalaṃkṛte
c kālāśvayukte mahati sthitaḥ kālāntakopamaḥ
a mahāpramāṇam udyamya vipulaṃ vegavad dṛḍham
c dhanur bhīmaṃ parāmṛśya śarāṃś cāmitranāśanān
a uvācainaṃ samārabdhaḥ saumitriṃ savibhīṣaṇam
c tāṃś ca vānaraśārdūlān paśyadhvaṃ me parākramam
a adya matkārmukotsṛṣṭaṃ śaravarṣaṃ durāsadam
c muktaṃ varṣam ivākāśe vārayiṣyatha saṃyuge
a adya vo māmakā bāṇā mahākārmukaniḥsṛtāḥ
c vidhamiṣyanti gātrāṇi tūlarāśim ivānalaḥ
a tīkṣṇasāyakanirbhinnāñ śūlaśaktyṛṣṭitomaraiḥ
c adya vo gamayiṣyāmi sarvān eva yamakṣayam
a kṣipataḥ śaravarṣāṇi kṣiprahastasya me yudhi
c jīmūtasyeva nadataḥ kaḥ sthāsyati mamāgrataḥ
a tac chrutvā rākṣasendrasya garjitaṃ lakṣmaṇas tadā
c abhītavadanaḥ kruddho rāvaṇiṃ vākyam abravīt
a uktaś ca durgamaḥ pāraḥ kāryāṇāṃ rākṣasa tvayā
c kāryāṇāṃ karmaṇā pāraṃ yo gacchati sa buddhimān
a sa tvam arthasya hīnārtho duravāpasya kena cit
c vaco vyāhṛtya jānīṣe kṛtārtho 'smīti durmate
a antardhānagatenājau yas tvayācaritas tadā
c taskarācarito mārgo naiṣa vīraniṣevitaḥ
a yathā bāṇapathaṃ prāpya sthito 'haṃ tava rākṣasa
c darśayasvādya tat tejo vācā tvaṃ kiṃ vikatthase
a evam ukto dhanur bhīmaṃ parāmṛśya mahābalaḥ
c sasarje niśitān bāṇān indrajit samijiṃjaya
a te nisṛṣṭā mahāvegāḥ śarāḥ sarpaviṣopamāḥ
c saṃprāpya lakṣmaṇaṃ petuḥ śvasanta iva pannagāḥ
a śarair atimahāvegair vegavān rāvaṇātmajaḥ
c saumitrim indrajid yuddhe vivyādha śubhalakṣaṇam
a sa śarair atividdhāṅgo rudhireṇa samukṣitaḥ
c śuśubhe lakṣmaṇaḥ śrīmān vidhūma iva pāvakaḥ
a indrajit tv ātmanaḥ karma prasamīkṣyādhigamya ca
c vinadya sumahānādam idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a patriṇaḥ śitadhārās te śarā matkārmukacyutāḥ
c ādāsyante 'dya saumitre jīvitaṃ jīvitāntagāḥ
a adya gomāyusaṃghāś ca śyenasaṃghāś ca lakṣmaṇa
c gṛdhrāś ca nipatantu tvāṃ gatāsuṃ nihataṃ mayā
a kṣatrabandhuḥ sadānāryo rāmaḥ paramadurmatiḥ
c bhaktaṃ bhrātaram adyaiva tvāṃ drakṣyati mayā hatam
a viśastakavacaṃ bhūmau vyapaviddhaśarāsanam
c hṛtottamāṅgaṃ saumitre tvām adya nihataṃ mayā
a iti bruvāṇaṃ saṃrabdhaṃ paruṣaṃ rāvaṇātmajam
c hetumadvākyam atyarthaṃ lakṣmaṇaḥ pratyuvāca ha
a akṛtvā katthase karma kimartham iha rākṣasa
c kuru tat karma yenāhaṃ śraddadhyāṃ tava katthanam
a anuktvā paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ kiṃ cid apy anavakṣipan
c avikatthan vadhiṣyāmi tvāṃ paśya puruṣādana
a ity uktvā pañcanārācān ākarṇāpūritāñ śarān
c nicakhāna mahāvegāṃl lakṣmaṇo rākṣasorasi
a sa śarair āhatas tena saroṣo rāvaṇātmajaḥ
c suprayuktais tribhir bāṇaiḥ prativivyādha lakṣmaṇam
a sa babhūva mahābhīmo nararākṣasasiṃhayoḥ
c vimardas tumulo yuddhe parasparavadhaiṣiṇoḥ
a ubhau hi balasaṃpannāv ubhau vikramaśālinau
c ubhāv api suvikrāntau sarvaśastrāstrakovidau
a ubhau paramadurjeyāv atulyabalatejasau
c yuyudhāte mahāvīrau grahāv iva nabho gatau
a balavṛtrāv iva hi tau yudhi vai duṣpradharṣaṇau
c yuyudhāte mahātmānau tadā kesariṇāv iva
a bahūn avasṛjantau hi mārgaṇaughān avasthitau
c nararākṣasasiṃhau tau prahṛṣṭāv abhyayudhyatām
a susaṃprahṛṣṭau nararākṣasottamau
jayaiṣiṇau mārgaṇacāpadhāriṇau
c parasparaṃ tau pravavarṣatur bhṛśaṃ
śaraughavarṣeṇa balāhakāv iva
a tataḥ śaraṃ dāśarathiḥ saṃdhāyāmitrakarśanaḥ
c sasarja rākṣasendrāya kruddhaḥ sarpa iva śvasan
a tasya jyātalanirghoṣaṃ sa śrutvā rāvaṇātmajaḥ
c vivarṇavadano bhūtvā lakṣmaṇaṃ samudaikṣata
a taṃ viṣaṇṇamukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasaṃ rāvaṇātmajam
c saumitriṃ yuddhasaṃsaktaṃ pratyuvāca vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a nimittāny anupaśyāmi yāny asmin rāvaṇātmaje
c tvara tena mahābāho bhagna eṣa na saṃśayaḥ
a tataḥ saṃdhāya saumitriḥ śarān agniśikhopamān
c mumoca niśitāṃs tasmai sarvān iva viṣolbaṇān
a śakrāśanisamasparśair lakṣmaṇenāhataḥ śaraiḥ
c muhūrtam abhavan mūḍhaḥ sarvasaṃkṣubhitendriyaḥ
a upalabhya muhūrtena saṃjñāṃ pratyāgatendriyaḥ
c dadarśāvasthitaṃ vīraṃ vīro daśarathātmajam
a so 'bhicakrāma saumitriṃ roṣāt saṃraktalocanaḥ
c abravīc cainam āsādya punaḥ sa paruṣaṃ vacaḥ
a kiṃ na smarasi tad yuddhe prathame matparākramam
c nibaddhas tvaṃ saha bhrātrā yadā yudhi viceṣṭase
a yuvā khalu mahāyuddhe śakrāśanisamaiḥ śaraiḥ
c śāyinau prathamaṃ bhūmau visaṃjñau sapuraḥsarau
a smṛtir vā nāsti te manye vyaktaṃ vā yamasādanam
c gantum icchasi yasmāt tvaṃ māṃ dharṣayitum icchasi
a yadi te prathame yuddhe na dṛṣṭo matparākramaḥ
c adya tvāṃ darśayiṣyāmi tiṣṭhedānīṃ vyavasthitaḥ
a ity uktvā saptabhir bāṇair abhivivyādha lakṣmaṇam
c daśabhiś ca hanūmantaṃ tīkṣṇadhāraiḥ śarottamaiḥ
a tataḥ śaraśatenaiva suprayuktena vīryavān
c krodhād dviguṇasaṃrabdho nirbibheda vibhīṣaṇam
a tad dṛṣṭvendrajitaḥ karma kṛtaṃ rāmānujas tadā
c acintayitvā prahasan naitat kiṃ cid iti bruvan
a mumoca sa śarān ghorān saṃgṛhya narapuṃgavaḥ
c abhītavadanaḥ kruddho rāvaṇiṃ lakṣmaṇo yudhi
a naivaṃ raṇagataḥ śūrāḥ praharanti niśācara
c laghavaś cālpavīryāś ca sukhā hīme śarās tava
a naivaṃ śūrās tu yudhyante samare jayakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
c ity evaṃ taṃ bruvāṇas tu śaravarṣair avākirat
a tasya bāṇais tu vidhvastaṃ kavacaṃ hemabhūṣitam
c vyaśīryata rathopasthe tārājālam ivāmbarāt
a vidhūtavarmā nārācair babhūva sa kṛtavraṇaḥ
c indrajit samare śūraḥ prarūḍha iva sānumān
a abhīkṣṇaṃ niśvasantau hi yudhyetāṃ tumulaṃ yudhi
c śarasaṃkṛttasarvāṅgo sarvato rudhirokṣitau
a astrāṇy astravidāṃ śreṣṭhau darśayantau punaḥ punaḥ
c śarān uccāvacākārān antarikṣe babandhatuḥ
a vyapetadoṣam asyantau laghucitraṃ ca suṣṭhu ca
c ubhau tu tumulaṃ ghoraṃ cakratur nararākṣasau
a tayoḥ pṛthakpṛthag bhīmaḥ śuśruve talanisvanaḥ
c sughorayor niṣṭanator gagane meghayor iva
a te gātrayor nipatitā rukmapuṅkhāḥ śarā yudhi
c asṛgdigdhā viniṣpetur viviśur dharaṇītalam
a anyaiḥ suniśitaiḥ śastrair ākāśe saṃjaghaṭṭire
c babhañjuś cicchiduś cāpi tayor bāṇāḥ sahasraśaḥ
a sa babhūva raṇe ghoras tayor bāṇamayaś cayaḥ
c agnibhyām iva dīptābhyāṃ satre kuśamayaś cayaḥ
a tayoḥ kṛtavraṇau dehau śuśubhāte mahātmanoḥ
c sapuṣpāv iva niṣpatrau vane śālmalikuṃśukau
a cakratus tumulaṃ ghoraṃ saṃnipātaṃ muhur muhuḥ
c indrajil lakṣmaṇaś caiva parasparajayaiṣiṇau
a lakṣmaṇo rāvaṇiṃ yuddhe rāvaṇiś cāpi lakṣmaṇam
c anyonyaṃ tāv abhighnantau na śramaṃ pratyapadyatām
a bāṇajālaiḥ śarīrasthair avagāḍhais tarasvinau
c śuśubhāte mahāvīrau virūḍhāv iva parvatau
a tayo rudhirasiktāni saṃvṛtāni śarair bhṛśam
c babhrājuḥ sarvagātrāṇi jvalanta iva pāvakāḥ
a tayor atha mahān kālo vyatīyād yudhyamānayoḥ
c na ca tau yuddhavaimukhyaṃ śramaṃ vāpy upajagmatuḥ
a atha samarapariśramaṃ nihantuṃ
samaramukheṣv ajitasya lakṣmaṇasya
c priyahitam upapādayan mahaujāḥ
samaram upetya vibhīṣaṇo 'vatasthe
a yudhyamānau tu tau dṛṣṭvā prasaktau nararākṣasau
c śūraḥ sa rāvaṇabhrātā tasthau saṃgrāmamūrdhani
a tato visphārayām āsa mahad dhanur avasthitaḥ
c utsasarja ca tīkṣṇāgrān rākṣaseṣu mahāśarān
a te śarāḥ śikhisaṃkāśā nipatantaḥ samāhitāḥ
c rākṣasān dārayām āsur vajrā iva mahāgirīn
a vibhīṣaṇasyānucarās te 'pi śūlāsipaṭṭasaiḥ
c ciccheduḥ samare vīrān rākṣasān rākṣasottamāḥ
a rākṣasais taiḥ parivṛtaḥ sa tadā tu vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c babhau madhye prahṛṣṭānāṃ kalabhānām iva dvipaḥ
a tataḥ saṃcodayāno vai harīn rakṣoraṇapriyān
c uvāca vacanaṃ kāle kālajño rakṣasāṃ varaḥ
a eko 'yaṃ rākṣasendrasya parāyaṇam iva sthitaḥ
c etac cheṣaṃ balaṃ tasya kiṃ tiṣṭhata harīśvarāḥ
a asmin vinihate pāpe rākṣase raṇamūrdhani
c rāvaṇaṃ varjayitvā tu śeṣam asya balaṃ hatam
a prahasto nihato vīro nikumbhaś ca mahābalaḥ
c kumbhakarṇaś ca kumbhaś ca dhūmrākṣaś ca niśācaraḥ
a akampanaḥ supārśvaś ca cakramālī ca rākṣasaḥ
c kampanaḥ sattvavantaś ca devāntakanarāntakau
a etān nihatyātibalān bahūn rākṣasasattamān
c bāhubhyāṃ sāgaraṃ tīrtvā laṅghyatāṃ goṣpadaṃ laghu
a etāvad iha śeṣaṃ vo jetavyam iha vānarāḥ
c hatāḥ sarve samāgamya rākṣasā baladarpitāḥ
a ayuktaṃ nidhanaṃ kartuṃ putrasya janitur mama
c ghṛṇām apāsya rāmārthe nihanyāṃ bhrātur ātmajam
a hantukāmasya me bāṣpaṃ cakśuś caiva nirudhyate
c tad evaiṣa mahābāhur lakṣmaṇaḥ śamayiṣyati
e vānarā ghnantuṃ saṃbhūya bhṛtyān asya samīpagān
a iti tenātiyaśasā rākṣasenābhicoditāḥ
c vānarendrā jahṛṣire lāṅgalāni ca vivyadhuḥ
a tatas te kapiśārdūlāḥ kṣveḍantaś ca muhur muhuḥ
c mumucur vividhān nādān meghān dṛṣṭveva barhiṇaḥ
a jāmbavān api taiḥ sarvaiḥ svayūthair abhisaṃvṛtaḥ
c aśmabhis tāḍayām āsa nakhair dantaiś ca rākṣasān
a nighnantam ṛkṣādhipatiṃ rākṣasās te mahābalāḥ
c parivavrur bhayaṃ tyaktvā tam anekavidhāyudhāḥ
a śaraiḥ paraśubhis tīkṣṇaiḥ paṭṭasair yaṣṭitomaraiḥ
c jāmbavantaṃ mṛdhe jaghnur nighnantaṃ rākṣasīṃ camūm
a sa saṃprahāras tumulaḥ saṃjajñe kapirākṣasām
c devāsurāṇāṃ kruddhānāṃ yathā bhīmo mahāsvanaḥ
a hanūmān api saṃkruddhaḥ sālam utpāṭya parvatāt
c rakṣasāṃ kadanaṃ cakre samāsādya sahasraśaḥ
a sa dattvā tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ pitṛvyasyendrajid yudhi
c lakṣmaṇaṃ paravīraghnaṃ punar evābhyadhāvata
a tau prayuddhau tadā vīrau mṛdhe lakṣmaṇarākṣasau
c śaraughān abhivarṣantau jaghnatus tau parasparam
a abhīkṣṇam antardadhatuḥ śarajālair mahābalau
c candrādityāv ivoṣṇānte yathā meghais tarasvinau
a na hy ādānaṃ na saṃdhānaṃ dhanuṣo vā parigrahaḥ
c na vipramokṣo bāṇānāṃ na vikarṣo na vigrahaḥ
a na muṣṭipratisaṃdhānaṃ na lakṣyapratipādanam
c adṛśyata tayos tatra yudhyatoḥ pāṇilāghavāt
a cāpavegapramuktaiś ca bāṇajālaiḥ samantataḥ
c antarikṣe 'bhisaṃchanne na rūpāṇi cakāśire
e tamasā pihitaṃ sarvam āsīd bhīmataraṃ mahat
a na tadānīiṃ vavau vāyur na jajvāla ca pāvakaḥ
c svastyas tu lokebhya iti jajalpaś ca maharṣayaḥ
e saṃpetuś cātra saṃprāptā gandharvāḥ saha cāraṇaiḥ
a atha rākṣasasiṃhasya kṛṣṇān kanakabhūṣaṇān
c śaraiś caturbhiḥ saumitrir vivyādha caturo hayān
a tato 'pareṇa bhallena sūtasya vicariṣyataḥ
c lāghavād rāghavaḥ śrīmāñ śiraḥ kāyād apāharat
a nihataṃ sārathiṃ dṛṣṭvā samare rāvaṇātmajaḥ
c prajahau samaroddharṣaṃ viṣaṇṇaḥ sa babhūva ha
a viṣaṇṇavadanaṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasaṃ hariyūthapāḥ
c tataḥ paramasaṃhṛṣṭo lakṣmaṇaṃ cābhyapūjayan
a tataḥ pramāthī śarabho rabhaso gandhamādanaḥ
c amṛṣyamāṇāś catvāraś cakrur vegaṃ harīśvarāḥ
a te cāsya hayamukhyeṣu tūrṇam utpatya vānarāḥ
c caturṣu sumahāvīryā nipetur bhīmavikramāḥ
a teṣām adhiṣṭhitānāṃ tair vānaraiḥ parvatopamaiḥ
c mukhebhyo rudhiraṃ vyaktaṃ hayānāṃ samavartata
a te nihatya hayāṃs tasya pramathya ca mahāratham
c punar utpatya vegena tasthur lakṣmaṇapārśvataḥ
a sa hatāśvād avaplutya rathān mathitasāratheḥ
c śaravarṣeṇa saumitrim abhyadhāvata rāvaṇiḥ
a tato mahendrapratimaṃh sa lakṣmaṇaḥ
padātinaṃ taṃ niśitaiḥ śarottamaiḥ
c sṛjantam ādau niśitāñ śarottamān
bhṛśaṃ tadā bāṇagaṇair nyavārayat
a sa hatāśvo mahātejā bhūmau tiṣṭhan niśācaraḥ
c indrajit paramakruddhaḥ saṃprajajvāla tejasā
a tau dhanvinau jighāṃsantāv anyonyam iṣubhir bhṛśam
c vijayenābhiniṣkrāntau vane gajavṛṣāv iva
a nibarhayantaś cānyonyaṃ te rākṣasavanaukasaḥ
c bhartāraṃ na jahur yuddhe saṃpatantas tatas tataḥ
a sa lakṣmaṇaṃ samuddiśya paraṃ lāghavam āsthitaḥ
c vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi varṣāṇīva puraṃdaraḥ
a muktam indrajitā tat tu śaravarṣam ariṃdamaḥ
c avārayad asaṃbhrānto lakṣmaṇaḥ sudurāsadam
a abhedyakacanaṃ matvā lakṣmaṇaṃ rāvaṇātmajaḥ
c lalāṭe lakṣmaṇaṃ bāṇaiḥ supuṅkhais tribhir indrajit
e avidhyat paramakruddhaḥ śīghram astraṃ pradarśayan
a taiḥ pṛṣatkair lalāṭasthaiḥ śuśubhe raghunandanaḥ
c raṇāgre samaraślāghī triśṛṅga iva parvataḥ
a sa tathāpy ardito bāṇai rākṣasena mahāmṛdhe
c tam āśu prativivyādha lakṣmaṇaḥ panabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a lakṣmaṇendrajitau vīrau mahābalaśarāsanau
c anyonyaṃ jaghnatur bāṇair viśikhair bhīmavikramau
a tau parasparam abhyetya sarvagātreṣu dhanvinau
c ghorair vivyadhatur bāṇaiḥ kṛtabhāvāv ubhau jaye
a tasmai dṛḍhataraṃ kruddho hatāśvāya vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c vajrasparśasamān pañca sasarjorasi mārgaṇān
a te tasya kāyaṃ nirbhidya rukmapuṅkhā nimittagāḥ
c babhūvur lohitādigdhā rakṭā iva mahoragāḥ
a sa pitṛvyasya saṃkruddha indrajic charam ādade
c uttamaṃ rakṣasāṃ madhye yamadattaṃ mahābalaḥ
a taṃ samīkṣya mahātejā maheṣuṃ tena saṃhitam
c lakṣmaṇo 'py ādade bāṇam anyaṃ bhīmaparākramaḥ
a kubereṇa svayaṃ svapne yad dattam amitātmanā
c durjayaṃ durviṣahyaṃ ca sendrair api surāsuraiḥ
a tābhyāṃ tau dhanuṣi śreṣṭhe saṃhitau sāyakottamau
c vikṛṣyamāṇau vīrābhyāṃ bhṛśaṃ jajvalatuḥ śriyā
a tau bhāsayantāv ākāśaṃ dhanurbhyāṃ viśikhau cyutau
c mukhena mukham āhatya saṃnipetatur ojasā
a tau mahāgrahasaṃkāśāv anyonyaṃ saṃnipatya ca
c saṃgrāme śatadhā yātau medinyāṃ vinipetatuḥ
a śarau pratihatau dṛṣṭvā tāv ubhau raṇamūrdhani
c vrīḍito jātaroṣau ca lakṣmaṇendrajitāv ubhau
a susaṃrabdhas tu saumitrir astraṃ vāruṇam ādade
c raudraṃ mahedrajid yuddhe vyasṛjad yudhi viṣṭhitaḥ
a tayoḥ sutumulaṃ yuddhaṃ saṃbabhūvādbhutopamam
c gaganasthāni bhūtāni lakṣmaṇaṃ paryavārayan
a bhairavābhirute bhīme yuddhe vānararākṣasām
c bhūtair bahubhir ākāśaṃ vismitair āvṛtaṃ babhau
a ṛṣayaḥ pitaro devā gandharvā garuṇoragāḥ
c śatakratuṃ puraskṛtya rarakṣur lakṣmaṇaṃ raṇe
a athānyaṃ mārgaṇaśreṣṭhaṃ saṃdadhe rāvaṇānujaḥ
c hutāśanasamasparśaṃ rāvaṇātmajadāruṇam
a supatram anuvṛttāṅgaṃ suparvāṇaṃ susaṃsthitam
c suvarṇavikṛtaṃ vīraḥ śarīrāntakaraṃ śaram
a durāvāraṃ durviṣahaṃ rākṣasānāṃ bhayāvaham
c āśīviṣaviṣaprakhyaṃ devasaṃghaiḥ samarcitam
a yena śakro mahātejā dānavān ajayat prabhuḥ
c purā devāsure yuddhe vīryavān harivāhanaḥ
a tad aindram astraṃ saumitriḥ saṃyugeṣv aparājitam
c śaraśreṣṭhaṃ dhanuḥ śreṣṭhe naraśreṣṭho 'bhisaṃdadhe
a saṃdhāyāmitradalanaṃ vicakarṣa śarāsanam
c sajyam āyamya durdharśaḥ kālo lokakṣaye yathā
a saṃdhāya dhanuṣi śreṣṭhe vikarṣann idam abravīt
c lakṣmīvāṃl lakṣmaṇo vākyam arthasādhakam ātmanaḥ
a dharmātmā satyasaṃdhaś ca rāmo dāśarathir yadi
c pauruṣe cāpratidvandvas tad enaṃ jahi rāvaṇim
a ity uktvā bāṇam ākarṇaṃ vikṛṣya tam ajihmagam
c lakṣmaṇaḥ samare vīraḥ sasarjendrajitaṃ prati
e aindrāstreṇa samāyujya lakṣmaṇaḥ paravīrahā
a tac chiraḥ saśiras trāṇaṃ śrīmaj jvalitakuṇḍalam
c pramathyendrajitaḥ kāyāt papāta dharaṇītale
a tad rākṣasatanūjasya chinnaskandhaṃ śiro mahat
c tapanīyanibhaṃ bhūmau dadṛśe rudhirokṣitam
a hatas tu nipapātāśu dharaṇyāṃ rāvaṇātmajaḥ
c kavacī saśirastrāṇo vidhvastaḥ saśarāsanaḥ
a cukruśus te tataḥ sarve vānarāḥ savibhīṣaṇāḥ
c hṛṣyanto nihate tasmin devā vṛtravadhe yathā
a athāntarikṣe bhūtānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanām
c abhijajñe ca saṃnādo gandharvāpsarasām api
a patitaṃ samabhijñāya rākṣasī sā mahācamūḥ
c vadhyamānā diśo bheje haribhir jitakāśibhiḥ
a vanarair vadhyamānās te śastrāṇy utsṛjya rākṣasāḥ
c laṅkām abhimukhāḥ sarve naṣṭasaṃjñāḥ pradhāvitāḥ
a dudruvur bahudhā bhītā rākṣasāḥ śataśo diśaḥ
c tyaktvā praharaṇān sarve paṭṭasāsiparaśvadhān
a ke cil laṅkāṃ paritrastāḥ praviṣṭā vānarārditāḥ
c samudre patitāḥ ke cit ke cit parvatam āśritāḥ
a hatam indrajitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śayānaṃ samarakṣitau
c rākṣasānāṃ sahasreṣu na kaś cit pratyadṛśyata
a yathāstaṃ gata āditye nāvatiṣṭhanti raśmayaḥ
c tathā tasmin nipatite rākṣasās te gatā diśaḥ
a śāntarakśmir ivādityo nirvāṇa iva pāvakaḥ
c sa babhūva mahātejā vyapāsta gatajīvitaḥ
a praśāntapīḍā bahulo vinaṣṭāriḥ praharṣavān
c babhūva lokaḥ patite rākṣasendrasute tadā
a harṣaṃ ca śakro bhagavān saha sarvaiḥ surarṣabhaiḥ
c jagāma nihate tasmin rākṣase pāpakarmaṇi
a śuddhā āpo nabhaś caiva jahṛṣur daityadānavāḥ
c ājagmuḥ patite tasmin sarvalokabhayāvahe
a ūcuś ca sahitāḥ sarve devagandharvadānavāḥ
c vijvarāḥ śāntakaluṣā brāhmaṇā vicarantv iti
a tato 'bhyanandan saṃhṛṣṭāḥ samare hariyūthapāḥ
c tam apratibalaṃ dṛṣṭvā hataṃ nairṛtapuṃgavam
a vibhīṣaṇo hanūmāṃś ca jāmbavāṃś carkṣayūthapaḥ
c vijayenābhinandantas tuṣṭuvuś cāpi lakṣmaṇam
a kṣveḍantaś ca nadantaś ca garjantaś ca plavaṃgamāḥ
c labdhalakṣā raghusutaṃ parivāryopatasthire
a lāṅgūlāni pravidhyantaḥ sphoṭayantaś ca vānarāḥ
c lakṣmaṇo jayatīty evaṃ vākyaṃ vyaśrāvayaṃs tadā
a anyonyaṃ ca samāśliṣya kapayo hṛṣṭamānasāḥ
c cakrur uccāvacaguṇā rāghavāśrayajāḥ kathāḥ
a tad asukaram athābhivīkṣya hṛṣṭāḥ
priyasuhṛdo yudhi lakṣmaṇasya karma
c paramam upalabhan manaḥpraharṣaṃ
vinihatam indraripuṃ niśamya devāḥ
a rudhiraklinnagātras tu lakṣmaṇaḥ śubhalakṣaṇaḥ
c babhūva hṛṣṭas taṃ hatvā śakrajetāram āhave
a tataḥ sa jāmbavantaṃ ca hanūmantaṃ ca vīryavān
c saṃnivartya mahātejās tāṃś ca sarvān vanaukasaḥ
a ājagāma tataḥ śīghraṃ yatra sugrīvarāghavau
c vibhīṣaṇam avaṣṭabhya hanūmantaṃ ca lakṣmaṇaḥ
a tato rāmam abhikramya saumitrir abhivādya ca
c tasthau bhrātṛsamīpasthaḥ śakrasyendrānujo yathā
e ācacakṣe tadā vīro ghoram indrajito vadham
a rāvaṇas tu śiraś chinnaṃ lakṣmaṇena mahātmanā
c nyavedayata rāmāya tadā hṛṣṭo vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a upaveśya tam utsaṅge pariṣvajyāvapīḍitam
c mūrdhni cainam upāghrāya bhūyaḥ saṃspṛśya ca tvaran
e uvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ vākyam āśvāsya puruṣarṣabhaḥ
a kṛtaṃ paramakalyāṇaṃ karma duṣkarakāriṇā
c niramitraḥ kṛto 'smy adya niryāsyati hi rāvaṇaḥ
e balavyūhena mahatā śrutvā putraṃ nipātitam
a taṃ putravadhasaṃtaptaṃ niryāntaṃ rākṣasādhipam
c balenāvṛtya mahatā nihaniṣyāmi durjayam
a tvayā lakṣmaṇa nāthena sītā ca pṛthivī ca me
c na duṣprāpā hate tv adya śakrajetari cāhave
a sa taṃ bhrātaram āśvāsya pāriṣvajya ca rāghavaḥ
c rāmaḥ suṣeṇaṃ muditaḥ samābhāṣyedam abravīt
a saśalyo 'yaṃ mahāprājñaḥ saumitrir mitravatsalaḥ
c yathā bhavati susvasthas tathā tvaṃ samupācara
e viśalyaḥ kriyatāṃ kṣipraṃ saumitriḥ savibhīṣaṇaḥ
a kṛṣa vānarasainyānāṃ śūrāṇāṃ drumayodhinām
c ye cānye 'tra ca yudhyantaḥ saśalyā vraṇinas tathā
e te 'pi sarve prayatnena kriyantāṃ sukhinas tvayā
a evam uktaḥ sa rāmeṇa mahātmā hariyūthapaḥ
c lakṣmaṇāya dadau nastaḥ suṣeṇaḥ paramauṣadham
a sa tasya gandham āghrāya viśalyaḥ samapadyata
c tadā nirvedanaś caiva saṃrūḍhavraṇa eva ca
a vibhīṣaṇa mukhānāṃ ca suhṛdāṃ rāghavājñayā
c sarvavānaramukhyānāṃ cikitsāṃ sa tadākarot
a tataḥ prakṛtim āpanno hṛtaśalyo gatavyathaḥ
c saumitrir muditas tatra kṣaṇena vigatajvaraḥ
a tathaiva rāmaḥ plavagādhipas tadā
vibhīṣaṇaś carkṣapatiś ca jāmbavān
c avekṣya saumitrim arogam utthitaṃ
mudā sasainyaḥ suciraṃ jaharṣire
a apūjayat karma sa lakṣmaṇasya
suduṣkaraṃ dāśarathir mahātmā
c hṛṣṭā babhūvur yudhi yūthapendrā
niśamya taṃ śakrajitaṃ nipātitam
a tataḥ paulastya sacivāḥ śrutvā cendrajitaṃ hatam
c ācacakṣur abhijñāya daśagrīvāya savyathāḥ
a yuddhe hato mahārāja lakṣmaṇena tavātmajaḥ
c vibhīṣaṇasahāyena miṣatāṃ no mahādyute
a śūraḥ śūreṇa saṃgamya saṃyugeṣv aparājitaḥ
c lakṣṇanena hataḥ śūraḥ putras te vibudhendrajit
a sa taṃ pratibhayaṃ śrutvā vadhaṃ putrasya dāruṇam
c ghoram indrajitaḥ saṃkhye kaśmalaṃ prāviśan mahat
a upalabhya cirāt saṃjñāṃ rājā rākṣasapuṃgavaḥ
c putraśokārdito dīno vilalāpākulendriyaḥ
a hā rākṣasacamūmukhya mama vatsa mahāratha
c jitvendraṃ katham adya tvaṃ lakṣmaṇasya vaśaṃ gataḥ
a nanu tvam iṣubhiḥ kruddho bhindyāḥ kālāntakāv api
c mandarasyāpi śṛṅgāṇi kiṃ punar lakṣmaṇaṃ raṇe
a adya vaivasvato rājā bhūyo bahumato mama
c yenādya tvaṃ mahābāho saṃyuktaḥ kāladharmaṇā
a eṣa panthāḥ suyodhānāṃ sarvāmaragaṇeṣv api
c yaḥ kṛte hanyate bhartuḥ sa pumān svargam ṛcchati
a adya devagaṇāḥ sarve lokapālās tatharṣayaḥ
c hatam indrajitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sukhaṃ svapsyanti nirbhayāḥ
a adya lokās trayaḥ kṛtsnāḥ pṛthivī ca sakānanā
c ekenendrajitā hīnā śūṇyeva pratibhāti me
a adya nairṛtakanyāyāṃ śroṣyāmy antaḥpure ravam
c kareṇusaṃghasya yathā ninādaṃ girigahvare
a yauvarājyaṃ ca laṅkāṃ ca rakṣāṃsi ca paraṃtapa
c mātaraṃ māṃ ca bhāryāṃ ca kva gato 'si vihāya naḥ
a mama nāma tvayā vīra gatasya yamasādanam
c pretakāryāṇi kāryāṇi viparīte hi vartase
a sa tvaṃ jīvati sugrīve rāghave ca salakṣmaṇe
c mama śalyam anuddhṛtya kva gato 'si vihāya naḥ
a evamādivilāpārtaṃ rāvaṇaṃ rākṣasādhipam
c āviveśa mahān kopaḥ putravyasanasaṃbhavaḥ
a ghoraṃ prakṛtyā rūpaṃ tat tasya krodhāgnimūrchitam
c babhūva rūpaṃ rudrasya kruddhasyeva durāsadam
a tasya kruddhasya netrābhyāṃ prāpatann asrabindavaḥ
c dīptābhyām iva dīpābhyāṃ sārciṣaḥ snehabindavaḥ
a dantān vidaśatas tasya śrūyate daśanasvanaḥ
c yantrasyāveṣṭyamānasya mahato dānavair iva
a kālāgnir iva saṃkruddho yāṃ yāṃ diśam avaikṣata
c tasyāṃ tasyāṃ bhayatrastā rākṣasāḥ saṃnililyire
a tam antakam iva kruddhaṃ carācaracikhādiṣum
c vīkṣamāṇaṃ diśaḥ sarvā rākṣasā nopacakramuḥ
a tataḥ paramasaṃkruddho rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ
c abravīd rakṣasāṃ madhye saṃstambhayiṣur āhave
a mayā varṣasahasrāṇi caritvā duścaraṃ tapaḥ
c teṣu teṣv avakāśeṣu svayambhūḥ paritoṣitaḥ
a tasyaiva tapaso vyuṣṭyā prasādāc ca svayambhuvaḥ
c nāsurebhyo na devebhyo bhayaṃ mama kadā cana
a kavacaṃ brahmadattaṃ me yad ādityasamaprabham
c devāsuravimardeṣu na bhinnaṃ vajraśaktibhiḥ
a tena mām adya saṃyuktaṃ rathastham iha saṃyuge
c pratīyāt ko 'dya mām ājau sākṣād api puraṃdaraḥ
a yat tadābhiprasannena saśaraṃ kārmukaṃ mahat
c devāsuravimardeṣu mama dattaṃ svayambhuvā
a adya tūryaśatair bhīmaṃ dhanur utthāpyatāṃ mahat
c rāmalakṣmaṇayor eva vadhāya paramāhave
a sa putravadhasaṃtaptaḥ śūraḥ krodhavaśaṃ gataḥ
c samīkṣya rāvaṇo buddhyā sītāṃ hantuṃ vyavasyata
a pratyavekṣya tu tāmrākṣaḥ sughoro ghoradarśanān
c dīno dīnasvarān sarvāṃs tān uvāca niśācarān
a māyayā mama vatsena vañcanārthaṃ vanaukasām
c kiṃ cid eva hataṃ tatra sīteyam iti darśitam
a tad idaṃ satyam evāhaṃ kariṣye priyam ātmanaḥ
c vaidehīṃ nāśayiṣyāmi kṣatrabandhum anuvratām
e ity evam uktvā sacivān khaḍgam āśu parāmṛśat
a uddhṛtya guṇasaṃpannaṃ vimalāmbaravarcasaṃ
c niṣpapāta sa vegena sabhāyāḥ sacivair vṛtaḥ
a rāvaṇaḥ putraśokena bhṛśam ākulacetanaḥ
c saṃkruddhaḥ khaḍgam ādāya sahasā yatra maithilī
a vrajantaṃ rākṣasaṃ prekṣya siṃhanādaṃ pracukruśuḥ
c ūcuś cānyonyam āśliṣya saṃkruddhaṃ prekṣya rākṣasāḥ
a adyainaṃ tāv ubhau dṛṣṭvā bhrātarau pravyathiṣyataḥ
c lokapālā hi catvāraḥ kruddhenānena nirjitāḥ
e bahavaḥ śatravaś cānye saṃyugeṣv abhipātitāḥ
a teṣāṃ saṃjalpamānānām aśokavanikāṃ gatām
c abhidudrāva vaidehīṃ rāvaṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
a vāryamāṇaḥ susaṃkruddhaḥ suhṛdbhir hitabuddhibhiḥ
c abhyadhāvata saṃkruddhaḥ khe graho rohiṇīm iva
a maithilī rakṣyamāṇā tu rākṣasībhir aninditā
c dadarśa rākṣasaṃ kruddhaṃ nistriṃśavaradhāriṇam
a taṃ niśāmya sanistriṃśaṃ vyathitā janakātmajā
c nivāryamāṇaṃ bahuśaḥ suhṛdbhir anivartinam
a yathāyaṃ mām abhikruddhaḥ samabhidravati svayam
c vadhiṣyati sanāthāṃ mām anāthām iva durmatiḥ
a bahuśaś codayām āsa bhartāraṃ mām anuvratām
c bhāryā bhava ramasyeti pratyākhyāto 'bhavan mayā
a so 'yaṃ mām anupasthānād vyaktaṃ nairāśyam āgataḥ
c krodhamohasamāviṣṭo nihantuṃ māṃ samudyataḥ
a atha vā tau naravyāghrau bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau
c mannimittam anāryeṇa samare 'dya nipātitau
e aho dhin mannimitto 'yaṃ vināśo rājaputrayoḥ
a hanūmato hi tadvākyaṃ na kṛtaṃ kṣudrayā mayā
c yady ahaṃ tasya pṛṣṭhena tadāyāsam aninditā
e nādyaivam anuśoceyaṃ bhartur aṅkagatā satī
a manye tu hṛdayaṃ tasyāḥ kausalyāyāḥ phaliṣyati
c ekaputrā yadā putraṃ vinaṣṭaṃ śroṣyate yudhi
a sā hi janma ca bālyaṃ ca yauvanaṃ ca mahātmanaḥ
c dharmakāryāṇi rūpaṃ ca rudatī saṃsramiṣyati
a nirāśā nihate putre dattvā śrāddham acetanā
c agnim ārokṣyate nūnam apo vāpi pravekṣyati
a dhig astu kubjām asatīṃ mantharāṃ pāpaniścayām
c yannimittam idaṃ duḥkhaṃ kausalyā pratipatsyate
a ity evaṃ maithilīṃ dṛṣṭvā vilapantīṃ tapasvinīm
c rohiṇīm iva candreṇa vinā grahavaśaṃ gatām
a supārśvo nāma medhāvī rāvaṇaṃ rākṣaseśvaram
c nivāryamāṇaṃ sacivair idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a kathaṃ nāma daśagrīva sākṣād vaiśravaṇānuja
c hantum icchasi vaidehīṃ krodhād dharmam apāsya hi
a veda vidyāvrata snātaḥ svadharmanirataḥ sadā
c striyāḥ kasmād vadhaṃ vīra manyase rākṣaseśvara
a maithilīṃ rūpasaṃpannāṃ pratyavekṣasva pārthiva
c tvam eva tu sahāsmābhī rāghave krodham utsṛja
a abhyutthānaṃ tvam adyaiva kṛṣṇapakṣacaturdaśīm
c kṛtvā niryāhy amāvāsyāṃ vijayāya balair vṛtaḥ
a śūro dhīmān rathī khaḍgī rathapravaram āsthitaḥ
c hatvā dāśarathiṃ rāmaṃ bhavān prāpsyati maithilīm
a sa tad durātmā suhṛdā niveditaṃ
vacaḥ sudharmyaṃ pratigṛhya rāvaṇaḥ
c gṛhaṃ jagāmātha tataś ca vīryavān
punaḥ sabhāṃ ca prayayau suhṛdvṛtaḥ
a sa praviśya sabhāṃ rājā dīnaḥ paramaduḥkhitaḥ
c niṣasādāsane mukhye siṃhaḥ kruddha iva śvasan
a abravīc ca tadā sarvān balamukhyān mahābalaḥ
c rāvaṇaḥ prāñjalīn vākyaṃ putravyasanakarśitaḥ
a sarve bhavantaḥ sarveṇa hastyaśvena samāvṛtāḥ
c niryāntu rathasaṃghaiś ca pādātaiś copaśobhitāḥ
a ekaṃ rāmaṃ parikṣipya samare hantum arhatha
c prahṛṣṭā śaravarṣeṇa prāvṛṭkāla ivāmbudāḥ
a atha vāhaṃ śarair tīṣkṇair bhinnagātraṃ mahāraṇe
c bhavadbhiḥ śvo nihantāsmi rāmaṃ lokasya paśyataḥ
a ity evaṃ rākṣasendrasya vākyam ādāya rākṣasāḥ
c niryayus te rathaiḥ śīghraṃ nāgānīkaiś ca saṃvṛtāḥ
a sa saṃgrāmo mahābhīmaḥ sūryasyodayanaṃ prati
c rakṣasāṃ vānarāṇāṃ ca tumulaḥ samapadyata
a te gadābhir vicitrābhiḥ prāsaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ
c anyonyaṃ samare jaghnus tadā vānararākṣasāḥ
a mātaṃgarathakūlasya vājimatsyā dhvajadrumāḥ
c śarīrasaṃghāṭavahāḥ prasasruḥ śoṇitāpagāḥ
a dhvajavarmarathān aśvān nānāpraharaṇāni ca
c āplutyāplutya samare vānarendrā babhañjire
a keśān karṇalalāṭāṃś ca nāsikāś ca plavaṃgamāḥ
c rakṣasāṃ daśanais tīkṣṇair nakhaiś cāpi vyakartayan
a ekaikaṃ rākṣasaṃ saṃkhye śataṃ vānarapuṃgavāḥ
c abhyadhāvanta phalinaṃ vṛkṣaṃ śakunayo yathā
a tathā gadābhir gurvībhiḥ prāsaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ
c nirjaghnur vānarān ghorān rākṣasāḥ parvatopamāḥ
a rākṣasair vadhyamānānāṃ vānarāṇāṃ mahācamūḥ
c śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ yātā rāmaṃ daśarathātmajam
a tato rāmo mahātejā dhanur ādāya vīryavān
c praviśya rākṣasaṃ sainyaṃ śaravarṣaṃ vavarṣa ha
a praviṣṭaṃ tu tadā rāmaṃ meghāḥ sūryam ivāmbare
c nābhijagmur mahāghoraṃ nirdahantaṃ śarāgninā
a kṛtāny eva sughorāṇi rāmeṇa rajanīcarāḥ
c raṇe rāmasya dadṛśuḥ karmāṇy asukarāṇi ca
a cālayantaṃ mahānīkaṃ vidhamantaṃ mahārathān
c dadṛśus te na vai rāmaṃ vātaṃ vanagataṃ yathā
a chinnaṃ bhinnaṃ śarair dagdhaṃ prabhagnaṃ śastrapīḍitam
c balaṃ rāmeṇa dadṛśur na ramaṃ śīghrakāriṇam
a praharantaṃ śarīreṣu na te paśyanti rābhavam
c indriyārtheṣu tiṣṭhantaṃ bhūtātmānam iva prajāḥ
a eṣa hanti gajānīkam eṣa hanti mahārathān
c eṣa hanti śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ padātīn vājibhiḥ saha
a iti te rākṣasāḥ sarve rāmasya sadṛśān raṇe
c anyonyakupitā jaghnuḥ sādṛśyād rāghavasya te
a na te dadṛśire rāmaṃ dahantam arivāhinīm
c mohitāḥ paramāstreṇa gāndharveṇa mahātmanā
a te tu rāma sahasrāṇi raṇe paśyanti rākṣasāḥ
c punaḥ paśyanti kākutstham ekam eva mahāhave
a bhramantīṃ kāñcanīṃ koṭiṃ kārmukasya mahātmanaḥ
c alātacakrapratimāṃ dadṛśus te na rāghavam
a śarīranābhisattvārciḥ śarāraṃ nemikārmukam
c jyāghoṣatalanirghoṣaṃ tejobuddhiguṇaprabham
a divyāstraguṇaparyantaṃ nighnantaṃ yudhi rākṣasān
c dadṛśū rāmacakraṃ tat kālacakram iva prajāḥ
a anīkaṃ daśasāhasraṃ rathānāṃ vātaraṃhasām
c aṣṭādaśasahasrāṇi kuñjarāṇāṃ tarasvinām
a caturdaśasahasrāṇi sārohāṇāṃ ca vājinām
c pūrṇe śatasahasre dve rākṣasānāṃ padātinām
a divasasyāṣṭame bhāge śarair agniśikhopamaiḥ
c hatāny ekena rāmeṇa rakṣasāṃ kāmarūpiṇām
a te hatāśvā hatarathāḥ śrāntā vimathitadhvajāḥ
c abhipetuḥ purīṃ laṅkāṃ hataśeṣā niśācarāḥ
a hatair gajapadāty aśvais tad babhūva raṇājiram
c ākrīḍabhūmī rudrasya kruddhasyeva pinākinaḥ
a tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
c sādhu sādhv iti rāmasya tat karma samapūjayan
a abravīc ca tadā rāmaḥ sugrīvaṃ pratyanantaram
c etad astrabalaṃ divyaṃ mama vā tryambakasya vā
a nihatya tāṃ rākṣasavāhinīṃ tu
rāmas tadā śakrasamo mahātmā
c astreṣu śastreṣu jitaklamaś ca
saṃstūyate devagaṇaiḥ prahṛṣṭaiḥ
a tāni nāgasahasrāṇi sārohāṇāṃ ca vājinām
c rathānāṃ cāgnivarṇānāṃ sadhvajānāṃ sahasraśaḥ
a rākṣasānāṃ sahasrāṇi gadāparighayodhinām
c kāñcanadhvajacitrāṇāṃ śūrāṇāṃ kāmarūpiṇām
a nihatāni śarais tīkṣṇais taptakāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c rāvaṇena prayuktāni rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇā
a dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca saṃbhrāntā hataśeṣā niśācarāḥ
c rākṣasyaś ca samāgamya dīnāś cintāpariplutāḥ
a vidhavā hataputrāś ca krośantyo hatabāndhavāḥ
c rākṣasyaḥ saha saṃgamya duḥkhārtāḥ paryadevayan
a kathaṃ śūrpaṇakhā vṛddhā karālā nirṇatodarī
c āsasāda vane rāmaṃ kandarpam iva rūpiṇam
a sukumāraṃ mahāsattvaṃ sarvabhūtahite ratam
c taṃ dṛṣṭvā lokavadhyā sā hīnarūpā prakāmitā
a kathaṃ sarvaguṇair hīnā guṇavantaṃ mahaujasaṃ
c sumukhaṃ durmukhī rāmaṃ kāmayām āsa rākṣasī
a janasyāsyālpabhāgyatvāt palinī śvetamūrdhajā
c akāryam apahāsyaṃ ca sarvalokavigarhitam
a rākṣasānāṃ vināśāya dūṣaṇasya kharasya ca
c cakārāpratirūpā sā rāghavasya pradharṣaṇam
a tan nimittam idaṃ vairaṃ rāvaṇena kṛtaṃ mahat
c vadhāya nītā sā sītā daśagrīveṇa rakṣasā
a na ca sītāṃ daśagrīvaḥ prāpnoti janakātmajām
c baddhaṃ balavatā vairam akṣayaṃ rāghaveṇa ha
a vaidehīṃ prārthayānaṃ taṃ virādhaṃ prekṣya rākṣasaṃ
c hatam ekena rāmeṇa paryāptaṃ tannidarśanam
a caturdaśasahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām
c nihatāni janasthāne śarair agniśikhopamaiḥ
a kharaś ca nihataḥ saṃkhye dūṣaṇas triśirās tathā
c śarair ādityasaṃkāśaiḥ paryāptaṃ tannidarśanam
a hato yojanabāhuś ca kabandho rudhirāśanaḥ
c krodhārto vinadan so 'tha paryāptaṃ tannidarśanam
a jaghāna balinaṃ rāmaḥ sahasranayanātmajam
c bālinaṃ meghasaṃkāśaṃ paryāptaṃ tannidarśanam
a ṛśyamūke vasañ śaile dīno bhagnamanorathaḥ
c sugrīvaḥ sthāpito rājye paryāptaṃ tannidarśanam
a dharmārthasahitaṃ vākyaṃ sarveṣāṃ rakṣasāṃ hitam
c yuktaṃ vibhīṣaṇenoktaṃ mohāt tasya na rocate
a vibhīṣaṇavacaḥ kuryād yadi sma dhanadānujaḥ
c śmaśānabhūtā duḥkhārtā neyaṃ laṅkā purī bhavet
a kumbhakarṇaṃ hataṃ śrutvā rāghaveṇa mahābalam
c priyaṃ cendrajitaṃ putraṃ rāvaṇo nāvabudhyate
a mama putro mama bhrātā mama bhartā raṇe hataḥ
c ity evaṃ śrūyate śabdo rākṣasānāṃ kule kule
a rathāś cāśvāś ca nāgāś ca hatāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ
c raṇe rāmeṇa śūreṇa rākṣasāś ca padātayaḥ
a rudro vā yadi vā viṣṇur mahendro vā śatakratuḥ
c hanti no rāmarūpeṇa yadi vā svayam antakaḥ
a hatapravīrā rāmeṇa nirāśā jīvite vayam
c apaśyantyo bhayasyāntam anāthā vilapāmahe
a rāmahastād daśagrīvaḥ śūro dattavaro yudhi
c idaṃ bhayaṃ mahāghoram utpannaṃ nāvabudhyate
a na devā na ca gandharvā na piśācā na rākasāḥ
c upasṛṣṭaṃ paritrātuṃ śaktā rāmeṇa saṃyuge
a utpātāś cāpi dṛśyante rāvaṇasya raṇe raṇe
c kathayiṣyanti rāmeṇa rāvaṇasya nibarhaṇam
a pitāmahena prītena devadānavarākṣasaiḥ
c rāvaṇasyābhayaṃ dattaṃ mānuṣebhyo na yācitam
a tad idaṃ mānuṣān manye prāptaṃ niḥsaṃśayaṃ bhayam
c jīvitāntakaraṃ ghoraṃ rakṣasāṃ rāvaṇasya ca
a pīḍyamānās tu balinā varadānena rakṣasā
c dīptais tapobhir vibudhāḥ pitāmaham apūjayan
a devatānāṃ hitārthāya mahātmā vai pitāmahaḥ
c uvāca devatāḥ sarvā idaṃ tuṣṭo mahad vacaḥ
a adya prabhṛti lokāṃs trīn sarve dānavarākṣasāḥ
c bhayena prāvṛtā nityaṃ vicariṣyanti śāśvatam
a daivatais tu samāgamya sarvaiś cendrapurogamaiḥ
c vṛṣadhvajas tripurahā mahādevaḥ prasāditaḥ
a prasannas tu mahādevo devān etad vaco 'bravīt
c utpatsyati hitārthaṃ vo nārī rakṣaḥkṣayāvahā
a eṣā devaiḥ prayuktā tu kṣud yathā dānavān purā
c bhakṣayiṣyati naḥ sītā rākṣasaghnī sarāvaṇān
a rāvaṇasyāpanītena durvinītasya durmateḥ
c ayaṃ niṣṭānako ghoraḥ śokena samabhiplutaḥ
a taṃ na paśyāmahe loke yo naḥ śaraṇado bhavet
c rāghaveṇopasṛṣṭānāṃ kāleneva yugakṣaye
a itīva sarvā rajanīcarastriyaḥ
parasparaṃ saṃparirabhya bāhubhiḥ
c viṣedur ārtātibhayābhipīḍitā
vinedur uccaiś ca tadā sudāruṇam
a ārtānāṃ rākṣasīnāṃ tu laṅkāyāṃ vai kule kule
c rāvaṇaḥ karuṇaṃ śabdaṃ śuśrāva pariveditam
a sa tu dīrghaṃ viniśvasya muhūrtaṃ dhyānam āsthitaḥ
c babhūva paramakruddho rāvaṇo bhīmadarśanaḥ
a saṃdaśya daśanair oṣṭhaṃ krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ
c rākṣasair api durdarśaḥ kālāgnir iva mūrchitaḥ
a uvāca ca samīpasthān rākṣasān rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c bhayāvyaktakathāṃs tatra nirdahann iva cakṣuṣā
a mahodaraṃ mahāpārśvaṃ virūpākṣaṃ ca rākṣasaṃ
c śīghraṃ vadata sainyāni niryāteti mamājñayā
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rākṣasās te bhayārditāḥ
c codayām āsur avyagrān rākṣasāṃs tān nṛpājñayā
a te tu sarve tathety uktvā rākṣasā ghoradarśanāḥ
c kṛtasvastyayanāḥ sarve rāvaṇābhimukhā yayuḥ
a pratipūjya yathānyāyaṃ rāvaṇaṃ te mahārathāḥ
c tasthuḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve bhartur vijayakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
a athovāca prahasyaitān rāvaṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
c mahodaramahāpārśvau virūpākṣaṃ ca rākṣasaṃ
a adya bāṇair dhanurmuktair yugāntādityasaṃnibhaiḥ
c rāghavaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva neṣyāmi yamasādhanam
a kharasya kumbhakarṇasya prahastendrajitos tathā
c kariṣyāmi pratīkāram adya śatruvadhād aham
a naivāntarikṣaṃ na diśo na nadyo nāpi sāgaraḥ
c prakāśatvaṃ gamiṣyāmi madbāṇajaladāvṛtāḥ
a adya vānarayūthānāṃ tāni yūthāni bhāgaśaḥ
c dhanuḥsamudrād udbhūtair mathiṣyāmi śarormibhiḥ
a vyākośapadmacakrāṇi padmakesaravarcasām
c adya yūthataṭākāni gajavat pramathāmy aham
a saśarair adya vadanaiḥ saṃkhye vānarayūthapāḥ
c maṇḍayiṣyanti vasudhāṃ sanālair iva paṅkalaiḥ
a adya yuddhapracaṇḍānāṃ harīṇāṃ drumayodhinām
c muktenaikeṣuṇā yuddhe bhetsyāmi ca śataṃśatam
a hato bhartā hato bhrātā yāsāṃ ca tanayā hatāḥ
c vadhenādya ripos tāsāṃ karmomy asrapramārjanam
a adya madbāṇanirbhinnaiḥ prakīrṇair gatacetanaiḥ
c karomi vānarair yuddhe yatnāvekṣya talāṃ mahīm
a adya gomāyavo gṛdhrā ye ca māṃsāśino 'pare
c sarvāṃs tāṃs tarpayiṣyāmi śatrumāṃsaiḥ śarārditaiḥ
a kalpyatāṃ me rathaśīghraṃ kṣipram ānīyatāṃ dhanuḥ
c anuprayāntu māṃ yuddhe ye 'vaśiṣṭā niśācarāḥ
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā mahāpārśvo 'bravīd vacaḥ
c balādhyakṣān sthitāṃs tatra balaṃ saṃtvaryatām iti
a balādhyakṣās tu saṃrabdhā rākṣasāṃs tān gṛhād gṛhāt
c codayantaḥ pariyayur laṅkāṃ laghuparākramāḥ
a tato muhūrtān niṣpetū rākṣasā bhīmavikramāḥ
c nardanto bhīmavadanā nānāpraharaṇair bhujaiḥ
a asibhiḥ paṭṭasaiḥ śūlair galābhir musalair halaiḥ
c śaktibhis tīkṣṇadhārābhir mahadbhiḥ kūṭamudgaraiḥ
a yaṣṭibhir vimalaiś cakrair niśitaiś ca paraśvadhaiḥ
c bhiṇḍipālaiḥ śataghnībhir anyaiś cāpi varāyudhaiḥ
a athānayan balādhyakṣāś catvāro rāvaṇājñayā
c drutaṃ sūtasamāyuktaṃ yuktāṣṭaturagaṃ ratham
a āruroha rathaṃ divyaṃ dīpyamānaṃ svatejasā
c rāvaṇaḥ sattvagāmbhīryād dārayann iva medinīm
a rāvaṇenābhyanujñātau mahāpārśvamahodarau
c virūpākṣaś ca durdharṣo rathān āruruhus tadā
a te tu hṛṣṭā vinardanto bhindata iva medinīm
c nādaṃ ghoraṃ vimuñcanto niryayur jayakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
a tato yuddhāya tejasvī rakṣogaṇabalair vṛtaḥ
c niryayāv udyatadhanuḥ kālāntakayamomapaḥ
a tataḥ prajavanāśvena rathena sa mahārathaḥ
c dvāreṇa niryayau tena yatra tau rāmalakṣmaṇau
a tato naṣṭaprabhaḥ sūryo diśaś ca timirāvṛtāḥ
c dvijāś ca nedur ghorāś ca saṃcacāla ca medinī
a vavarṣa rudhiraṃ devaś caskhaluś ca turaṃgamāḥ
c dhvajāgre nyapatad gṛdhro vineduś cāśivaṃ śivāḥ
a nayanaṃ cāsphurad vāmaṃ savyo bāhur akampata
c vivarṇavadanaś cāsīt kiṃ cid abhraśyata svaraḥ
a tato niṣpatato yuddhe daśagrīvasya rakṣasaḥ
c raṇe nidhanaśaṃsīni rūpāṇy etāni jajñire
a antarikṣāt papātolkā nirghātasamanisvanā
c vinedur aśivaṃ gṛdhrā vāyasair anunāditāḥ
a etān acintayan ghorān utpātān samupasthitān
c niryayau rāvaṇo mohād vadhārthī kālacoditaḥ
a teṣāṃ tu rathaghoṣeṇa rākṣasānāṃ mahātmanām
c vānarāṇām api camūr yuddhāyaivābhyavartata
a teṣāṃ sutumulaṃ yuddhaṃ babhūva kapirakṣasām
c anyonyam āhvayānānāṃ kruddhānāṃ jayam icchatām
a tataḥ kruddho daśagrīvaḥ śaraiḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c vānarāṇām anīkeṣu cakāra kadanaṃ mahat
a nikṛttaśirasaḥ ke cid rāvaṇena valīmukhāḥ
c nirucchvāsā hatāḥ ke cit ke cit pārśveṣu dāritāḥ
e ke cid vibhinnaśirasaḥ ke cic cakṣurvivarjitāḥ
a daśānanaḥ krodhavivṛttanetro
yato yato 'bhyeti rathena saṃkhye
c tatas tatas tasya śarapravegaṃ
soḍhuṃ na śekur hariyūthapās te
a tathā taiḥ kṛttagātrais tu daśagrīveṇa mārgaṇaiḥ
c babhūva vasudhā tatra prakīrṇā haribhir vṛtā
a rāvaṇasyāprasahyaṃ taṃ śarasaṃpātam ekataḥ
c na śekuḥ sahituṃ dīptaṃ pataṃgā iva pāvakam
a te 'rditā niśitair bāṇaiḥ krośanto vipradudruvuḥ
c pāvakārciḥsamāviṣṭā dahyamānā yathā gajāḥ
a plavaṃgānām anīkāni mahābhrāṇīva mārutaḥ
c sa yayau samare tasmin vidhaman rāvaṇaḥ śaraiḥ
a kadanaṃ tarasā kṛtvā rākṣasendro vanaukasām
c āsasāda tato yuddhe rāghavaṃ tvaritas tadā
a sugrīvas tān kapīn dṛṣṭvā bhagnān vidravato raṇe
c gulme suṣeṇaṃ nikṣipya cakre yuddhe drutaṃ manaḥ
a ātmanaḥ sadṛśaṃ vīraṃ sa taṃ nikṣipya vānaram
c sugrīvo 'bhimukhaḥ śatruṃ pratasthe pādapāyudhaḥ
a pārśvataḥ pṛṣṭhataś cāsya sarve yūthādhipāḥ svayam
c anujahrur mahāśailān vividhāṃś ca mahādrumān
a sa nadan yudhi sugrīvaḥ svareṇa mahatā mahān
c pātayan vividhāṃś cānyāñ jaghānottamarākṣasān
a mamarda ca mahākāyo rākṣasān vānareśvaraḥ
c yugāntasamaye vāyuḥ pravṛddhān agamān iva
a rākṣasānām anīkeṣu śailavarṣaṃ vavarṣa ha
c aśvavarṣaṃ yathā meghaḥ pakṣisaṃgheṣu kānane
a kapirājavimuktais taiḥ śailavarṣais tu rākṣasāḥ
c vikīrṇaśirasaḥ petur nikṛttā iva parvatāḥ
a atha saṃkṣīyamāṇeṣu rākṣaseṣu samantataḥ
c sugrīveṇa prabhagneṣu patatsu vinadatsu ca
a virūpākṣaḥ svakaṃ nāma dhanvī viśrāvya rākṣasaḥ
c rathād āplutya durdharṣo gajaskandham upāruhat
a sa taṃ dviradam āruhya virūpākṣo mahārathaḥ
c vinadan bhīmanirhrālaṃ vānarān abhyadhāvata
a sugrīve sa śarān ghorān visasarja camūmukhe
c sthāpayām āsā codvignān rākṣasān saṃpraharṣayan
a so 'tividdhaḥ śitair bāṇaiḥ kapīndras tena rakṣasā
c cukrodha ca mahākrodho vadhe cāsya mano dadhe
a tataḥ pādapam uddhṛtya śūraḥ saṃpradhane hariḥ
c abhipatya jaghānāsya pramukhe taṃ mahāgajam
a sa tu prahārābhihataḥ sugrīveṇa mahāgajaḥ
c apāsarpad dhanurmātraṃ niṣasāda nanāda ca
a gajāt tu mathitāt tūrṇam apakramya sa vīryavān
c rākṣaso 'bhimukhaḥ śatruṃ pratyudgamya tataḥ kapim
a ārṣabhaṃ carmakhaḍgaṃ ca pragṛhya laghuvikramaḥ
c bhartsayann iva sugrīvam āsasāda vyavasthitam
a sa hi tasyābhisaṃkruddhaḥ pragṛhya mahatīṃ śilām
c virūpākṣāya cikṣepa sugrīvo jaladopamām
a sa tāṃ śilām āpatantīṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasapuṃgavaḥ
c apakramya suvikrāntaḥ khaḍgena prāharat tadā
a tena khaḍgena saṃkruddhaḥ sugrīvasya camūmukhe
c kavacaṃ pātayām āsa sa khaḍgābhihato 'patat
a sa samutthāya patitaḥ kapis tasya vyasarjayat
c talaprahāram aśaneḥ samānaṃ bhīmanisvanam
a talaprahāraṃ tad rakṣaḥ sugrīveṇa samudyatam
c naipuṇyān mocayitvainaṃ muṣṭinorasy atāḍayat
a tatas tu saṃkruddhataraḥ sugrīvo vānareśvaraḥ
c mokṣitaṃ cātmano dṛṣṭvā prahāraṃ tena rakṣasā
a sa dadarśāntaraṃ tasya virūpākṣasya vānaraḥ
c tato nyapātayat krodhāc chaṅkhadeśe mahātalam
a mahendrāśanikalpena talenābhihataḥ kṣitau
c papāta rudhiraklinnaḥ śoṇitaṃ sa samudvaman
a vivṛttanayanaṃ krodhāt saphena rudhirāplutam
c dadṛśus te virūpākṣaṃ virūpākṣataraṃ kṛtam
a sphurantaṃ parivarjantaṃ pārśvena rudhirokṣitam
c karuṇaṃ ca vinardāntaṃ dadṛśuḥ kapayo ripum
a tathā tu tau saṃyati saṃprayuktau
tarasvinau vānararākṣasānām
c balārṇavau sasvanatuḥ sabhīmaṃ
mahārṇavau dvāv iva bhinnavelau
a vināśitaṃ prekṣya virūpanetraṃ
mahābalaṃ taṃ haripārthivena
c balaṃ samastaṃ kapirākṣasānām
unmattagaṅgāpratimaṃ babhūva
a hanyamāne bale tūrṇam anyonyaṃ te mahāmṛdhe
c sarasīva mahāgharme sūpakṣīṇe babhūvatuḥ
a svabalasya vighātena virūpākṣavadhena ca
c babhūva dviguṇaṃ kruddho rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ
a prakṣīṇaṃ tu balaṃ dṛṣṭvā vadhyamānaṃ valīmukhaiḥ
c babhūvāsya vyathā yuddhe prekṣya daivaviparyayam
a uvāca ca samīpasthaṃ mahodaram ariṃdamam
c asmin kāle mahābāho jayāśā tvayi me sthitā
a jahi śatrucamūṃ vīra darśayādya parākramam
c bhartṛpiṇḍasya kālo 'yaṃ nirveṣṭuṃ sādhu yudhyatām
a evam uktas tathety uktvā rākṣasendraṃ mahodaraḥ
c praviveśārisenāṃ sa pataṃga iva pāvakam
a tataḥ sa kadanaṃ cakre vānarāṇāṃ mahābalaḥ
c bhartṛvākyena tejasvī svena vīryeṇa coditaḥ
a prabhagnāṃ samare dṛṣṭvā vānarāṇāṃ mahācamūm
c abhidudrāva sugrīvo mahodaram anantaram
a pragṛhya vipulāṃ ghorāṃ mahīdhara samāṃ śilām
c cikṣepa ca mahātejās tad vadhāya harīśvaraḥ
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā śilāṃ dṛṣṭvā mahodaraḥ
c asaṃbhrāntas tato bāṇair nirbibheda durāsadām
a rakṣasā tena bāṇaughair nikṛttā sā sahasradhā
c nipapāta śilābhūmau gṛdhracakram ivākulam
a tāṃ tu bhinnāṃ śilāṃ dṛṣṭvā sugrīvaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
c sālam utpāṭya cikṣepa rakṣase raṇamūrdhani
e śaraiś ca vidadārainaṃ śūraḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
a sa dadarśa tataḥ kruddhaḥ parighaṃ patitaṃ bhuvi
c āvidhya tu sa taṃ dīptaṃ parighaṃ tasya darśayan
