e parighāgreṇa vegena jaghānāsya hayottamān
a tasmād dhatahayād vīraḥ so 'vaplutya mahārathāt
c gadāṃ jagrāha saṃkruddho rākṣaso 'tha mahodaraḥ
a gadāparighahastau tau yudhi vīrau samīyatuḥ
c nardantau govṛṣaprakhyau ghanāv iva savidyutau
a ājaghāna gadāṃ tasya parigheṇa harīśvaraḥ
c papāta sa gadodbhinnaḥ parighas tasya bhūtale
a tato jagrāha tejasvī sugrīvo vasudhātalāt
c āyasaṃ musalaṃ ghoraṃ sarvato hemabhūṣitam
a taṃ samudyamya cikṣepa so 'py anyāṃ vyākṣipad gadām
c bhinnāv anyonyam āsādya petatur dharaṇītale
a tato bhagnapraharaṇau muṣṭibhyāṃ tau samīyatuḥ
c tejo balasamāviṣṭau dīptāv iva hutāśanau
a jaghnatus tau tadānyonyaṃ nedatuś ca punaḥ punaḥ
c talaiś cānyonyam āhatya petatur dharaṇītale
a utpetatus tatas tūrṇaṃ jaghnatuś ca parasparam
c bhujaiś cikṣepatur vīrāv anyonyam aparājitau
a ājahāra tadā khagḍam adūraparivartinam
c rākṣasaś carmaṇā sārdhaṃ mahāvego mahodaraḥ
a tathaiva ca mahākhaḍgaṃ carmaṇā patitaṃ saha
c jagrāha vānaraśreṣṭhaḥ sugrīvo vegavattaraḥ
a tau tu roṣaparītāṅgau nardantāv abhyadhāvatām
c udyatāsī raṇe hṛṣṭau yudhi śastraviśāradau
a dakṣiṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ cobhau tau tūrṇaṃ saṃparīyatuḥ
c anyonyam abhisaṃkruddhau jaye praṇihitāv ubhau
a sa tu śūro mahāvego vīryaślāghī mahodaraḥ
c mahācarmaṇi taṃ khaḍgaṃ pātayām āsa durmatiḥ
a lagnam utkarṣataḥ khaḍgaṃ khaḍgena kapikuñjaraḥ
c jahāra saśiras trāṇaṃ kuṇḍalopahitaṃ śiraḥ
a nikṛttaśirasas tasya patitasya mahītale
c tad balaṃ rākṣasendrasya dṛṣṭvā tatra na tiṣṭhati
a hatvā taṃ vānaraiḥ sārdhaṃ nanāda mudito hariḥ
c cukrodha ca daśagrīvo babhau hṛṣṭaś ca rāghavaḥ
a mahodare tu nihate mahāpārśvo mahābalaḥ
c aṅgadasya camūṃ bhīmāṃ kṣobhayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
a sa vānarāṇāṃ mukhyānām uttamāṅgāni sarvaśaḥ
c pātayām āsa kāyebhyaḥ phalaṃ vṛntād ivānilaḥ
a keṣāṃ cid iṣubhir bāhūn skandhāṃś cicheda rākṣasaḥ
c vānarāṇāṃ susaṃkruddhaḥ pārśvaṃ keṣāṃ vyadārayat
a te 'rditā bāṇavarṣeṇa mahāpārśvena vānarāḥ
c viṣādavimukhāḥ sarve babhūvur gatacetasaḥ
a nirīkṣya balam udvignam aṅgado rākṣasārditam
c vegaṃ cakre mahābāhuḥ samudra iva parvaṇi
a āyasaṃ parighaṃ gṛhya sūryaraśmisamaprabham
c samare vānaraśreṣṭho mahāpārśve nyapātayat
a sa tu tena prahāreṇa mahāpārśvo vicetanaḥ
c sasūtaḥ syandanāt tasmād visaṃjñaḥ prāpatad bhuvi
a sarkṣarājas tu tejasvī nīlāñjanacayopamaḥ
c niṣpatya sumahāvīryaḥ svād yūthān meghasaṃnibhāt
a pragṛhya giriśṛṅgābhāṃ kruddhaḥ sa vipulāṃ śilām
c aśvāñ jaghāna tarasā syandanaṃ ca babhañja tam
a muhūrtāl labdhasaṃjñas tu mahāpārśvo mahābalaḥ
c aṅgadaṃ bahubhir bāṇair bhūyas taṃ pratyavidhyata
a jāmbavantaṃ tribhir bāṇair ājaghāna stanāntare
c ṛkṣarājaṃ gavākṣaṃ ca jaghāna bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ
a gavākṣaṃ jāmbavantaṃ ca sa dṛṣṭvā śarapīḍitau
c jagrāha parighaṃ ghoram aṅgadaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
a tasyāṅgadaḥ prakupito rākṣasasya tam āyasaṃ
c dūrasthitasya parighaṃ raviraśmisamaprabham
a dvābhyāṃ bhujābhyāṃ saṃgṛhya bhrāmayitvā ca vegavān
c mahāpārśvāya cikṣepa vadhārthaṃ vālinaḥ sutaḥ
a sa tu kṣipto balavatā parighas tasya rakṣasaḥ
c dhanuś ca saśaraṃ hastāc chirastraṃ cāpy apātayat
a taṃ samāsādya vegena vāliputraḥ pratāpavān
c talenābhyahanat kruddhaḥ karṇamūle sakuṇḍale
a sa tu kruddho mahāvego mahāpārśvo mahādyutiḥ
c kareṇaikena jagrāha sumahāntaṃ paraśvadham
a taṃ tailadhautaṃ vimalaṃ śailasāramayaṃ dṛḍham
c rākṣasaḥ paramakruddho vāliputre nyapātayat
a tena vāmāṃsaphalake bhṛśaṃ pratyavapātitam
c aṅgado mokṣayām āsa saroṣaḥ sa paraśvadham
a sa vīro vajrasaṃkāśam aṅgado muṣṭim ātmanaḥ
c saṃvartayan susaṃkruddhaḥ pitus tulyaparākramaḥ
a rākṣasasya stanābhyāśe marmajño hṛdayaṃ prati
c indrāśanisamasparśaṃ sa muṣṭiṃ vinyapātayat
a tena tasya nipātena rākṣasasya mahāmṛdhe
c paphāla hṛdayaṃ cāśu sa papāta hato bhuvi
a tasmin nipatite bhūmau tat sainyaṃ saṃpracukṣubhe
c abhavac ca mahān krodhaḥ samare rāvaṇasya tu
a mahodaramahāpārśvau hatau dṛṣṭvā tu rākṣasau
c tasmiṃś ca nihate vīre virūpākṣe mahābale
a āviveśa mahān krodho rāvaṇaṃ tu mahāmṛdhe
c sūtaṃ saṃcodayām āsa vākyaṃ cedam uvāca ha
a nihatānām amātyānāṃ ruddhasya nagarasya ca
c duḥkham eṣo 'paneṣyāmi hatvā tau rāmalakṣmaṇau
a rāmavṛkṣaṃ raṇe hanmi sītāpuṣpaphalapradam
c praśākhā yasya sugrīvo jāmbavān kumudo nalaḥ
a sa diśo daśa ghoṣeṇa rathasyātiratho mahān
c nādayan prayayau tūrṇaṃ rāghavaṃ cābhyavartata
a pūritā tena śabdena sanadīgirikānanā
c saṃcacāla mahī sarvā savarāhamṛgadvipā
a tāmasaṃ sumahāghoraṃ cakārāstraṃ sudāruṇam
c nirdadāha kapīn sarvāṃs te prapetuḥ samantataḥ
a tāny anīkāny anekāni rāvaṇasya śarottamaiḥ
c dṛṣṭvā bhagnāni śataśo rāghavaḥ paryavasthitaḥ
a sa dadarśa tato rāmaṃ tiṣṭhantam aparājitam
c lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā viṣṇunā vāsavaṃ yathā
a ālikhantam ivākāśam avaṣṭabhya mahad dhanuḥ
c padmapatraviśālākṣaṃ dīrghabāhum ariṃdamam
a vānarāṃś ca raṇe bhagnān āpatantaṃ ca rāvaṇam
c samīkṣya rāghavo hṛṣṭo madhye jagrāha kārmukam
a visphārayitum ārebhe tataḥ sa dhanur uttamam
c mahāvegaṃ mahānādaṃ nirbhindann iva medinīm
a tayoḥ śarapathaṃ prāpya rāvaṇo rājaputrayoḥ
c sa babhūva yathā rāhuḥ samīpe śaśisūryayoḥ
a rāvaṇasya ca bāṇaughai rāmavispharitena ca
c śabdena rākṣasās tena petuś ca śataśas tadā
a tam icchan prathamaṃ yoddhuṃ lakṣmaṇo niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c mumoca dhanur āyamya śarān agniśikhopamān
a tān muktamātrān ākāśe lakṣmaṇena dhanuṣmatā
c bāṇān bāṇair mahātejā rāvaṇaḥ pratyavārayat
a ekam ekena bāṇena tribhis trīn daśabhir daśa
c lakṣmaṇasya praciccheda darśayan pāṇilāghavam
a abhyatikramya saumitriṃ rāvaṇaḥ samitiṃjayaḥ
c āsasāda tato rāmaṃ sthitaṃ śailam ivācalam
a sa saṃkhye rāmam āsādya krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ
c vyasṛjac charavarṇāni rāvaṇo rāghavopari
a śaradhārās tato rāmo rāvaṇasya dhanuścyutāḥ
c dṛṣṭvaivāpatitāḥ śīghraṃ bhallāñ jagrāha satvaram
a tāñ śaraughāṃs tato bhallais tīkṣṇaiś ciccheda rāghavaḥ
c dīpyamānān mahāvegān kruddhān āśīviṣān iva
a rāghavo rāvaṇaṃ tūrṇaṃ rāvaṇo rāghavaṃ tathā
c anyonyaṃ vividhais tīkṣṇaiḥ śarair abhivavarṣatuḥ
a ceratuś ca ciraṃ citraṃ maṇḍalaṃ savyadakṣiṇam
c bāṇavegān samudīkṣya samareṣv aparājitau
a tayor bhūtāni vitreṣur yugapat saṃprayudhyatoḥ
c raudrayoḥ sāyakamucor yamāntakanikāśayoḥ
a saṃtataṃ vividhair bāṇair babhūva gaganaṃ tadā
c ghanair ivātapāpāye vidyunmālāsamākulaiḥ
a gavākṣitam ivākāśaṃ babhūva śūravṛṣṭibhiḥ
c mahāvegaiḥ sutīkṣṇāgrair gṛdhrapatraiḥ suvājitaiḥ
a śarāndhakāraṃ tau bhīmaṃ cakratuḥ paramaṃ tadā
c gate 'staṃ tapane cāpi mahāmeghāv ivotthitau
a babhūva tumulaṃ yuddham anyonyavadhakāṅkṣiṇoḥ
c anāsādyam acintyaṃ ca vṛtravāsavayor iva
a ubhau hi parameṣvāsāv ubhau śastraviśāradau
c ubhau cāstravidāṃ mukhyāv ubhau yuddhe viceratuḥ
a ubhau hi yena vrajatas tena tena śarormayaḥ
c ūrmayo vāyunā viddhā jagmuḥ sāgarayor iva
a tataḥ saṃsaktahastas tu rāvaṇo lokarāvaṇaḥ
c nārācamālāṃ rāmasya lalāṭe pratyamuñcata
a raudracāpaprayuktāṃ tāṃ nīlotpaladalaprabhām
c śirasā dhārayan rāmo na vyathāṃ pratyapadyata
a atha mantrān api japan raudram astram udīrayan
c śarān bhūyaḥ samādāya rāmaḥ krodhasamanvitaḥ
a mumoca ca mahātejāś cāpam āyamya vīryavān
c tāñ śarān rākṣasendrāya cikṣepācchinnasāyakaḥ
a te mahāmeghasaṃkāśe kavace patitāḥ śarāḥ
c avadhye rākṣasendrasya na vyathāṃ janayaṃs tadā
a punar evātha taṃ rāmo rathasthaṃ rākṣasādhipam
c lalāṭe paramāstreṇa sarvāstrakuśalo 'bhinat
a te bhittvā bāṇarūpāṇi pañcaśīrṣā ivoragāḥ
c śvasanto viviśur bhūmiṃ rāvaṇapratikūlatāḥ
a nihatya rāghavasyāstraṃ rāvaṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
c āsuraṃ sumahāghoram anyad astraṃ samādade
a siṃhavyāghramukhāṃś cānyān kaṅkakāka mukhān api
c gṛdhraśyenamukhāṃś cāpi sṛgālavadanāṃs tathā
a īhāmṛgamuhāṃś cānyān vyāditāsyān bhayāvahān
c pañcāsyāṃl lelihānāṃś ca sasarja niśitāñ śarān
a śarān kharamukhāṃś cānyān varāhamukhasaṃsthitān
c śvānakukkuṭavaktrāṃś ca makarāśīviṣānanān
a etāṃś cānyāṃś ca māyābhiḥ sasarja niśitāñ śarān
c rāmaṃ prati mahātejāḥ kruddhaḥ sarpa iva śvasan
a āsureṇa samāviṣṭaḥ so 'streṇa raghunandanaḥ
c sasarjāstraṃ mahotsāhaḥ pāvakaṃ pāvakopamaḥ
a agnidīptamukhān bāṇāṃs tathā sūryamukhān api
c candrārdhacandravaktrāṃś ca dhūmaketumukhān api
a grahanakṣatravarṇāṃś ca maholkā mukhasaṃsthitān
c vidyujjihvopamāṃś cānyān sasarja niśitāñ śarān
a te rāvaṇaśarā ghorā rāghavāstrasamāhatāḥ
c vilayaṃ jagmur ākāśe jagmuś caiva sahasraśaḥ
a tad astraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇā
c hṛṣṭā nedus tataḥ sarve kapayaḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
a tasmin pratihate 'stre tu rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ
c krodhaṃ ca dviguṇaṃ cakre krodhāc cāstram anantaram
a mayena vihitaṃ raudram anyad astraṃ mahādyutiḥ
c utsraṣṭuṃ rāvaṇo ghoraṃ rāghavāya pracakrame
a tataḥ śūlāni niścerur gadāś ca musalāni ca
c kārmukād dīpyamānāni vajrasārāṇi sarvaśaḥ
a kūṭamudgarapāśāś ca dīptāś cāśanayas tathā
c niṣpetur vividhās tīkṣṇā vātā iva yugakṣaye
a tad astraṃ rāghavaḥ śrīmān uttamāstravidāṃ varaḥ
c jaghāna paramāstreṇa gandharveṇa mahādyutiḥ
a tasmin pratihate 'stre tu rāghaveṇa mahātmanā
c rāvaṇaḥ krodhatāmrākṣaḥ sauram astram udīrayat
a tataś cakrāṇi niṣpetur bhāsvarāṇi mahānti ca
c kārmukād bhīmavegasya daśagrīvasya dhīmataḥ
a tair āsīd gaganaṃ dīptaṃ saṃpatadbhir itas tataḥ
c patadbhiś ca diśo dīptaiś candrasūryagrahair iva
a tāni ciccheda bāṇaughaiś cakrāṇi tu sa rāghavaḥ
c āyudhāni vicitrāṇi rāvaṇasya camūmukhe
a tad astraṃ tu hataṃ dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ
c vivyādha daśabhir bāṇai rāmaṃ sarveṣu marmasu
a sa viddho daśabhir bāṇair mahākārmukaniḥsṛtaiḥ
c rāvaṇena mahātejā na prākampata rāghavaḥ
a tato vivyādha gātreṣu sarveṣu samitiṃjayaḥ
c rāghavas tu susaṃkruddho rāvaṇaṃ bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ
a etasminn antare kruddho rāghavasyānujo balī
c lakṣmaṇaḥ sāyakān sapta jagrāha paravīrahā
a taiḥ sāyakair mahāvegai rāvaṇasya mahādyutiḥ
c dhvajaṃ manuṣyaśīrṣaṃ tu tasya ciccheda naikadhā
a sāratheś cāpi bāṇena śiro jvalitakuṇḍalam
c jahāra lakṣmaṇaḥ śrīmān nairṛtasya mahābalaḥ
a tasya bāṇaiś ca ciccheda dhanur gajakaropamam
c lakṣmaṇo rākṣasendrasya pañcabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a nīlameghanibhāṃś cāsya sadaśvān parvatopamān
c jaghānāplutya gadayā rāvaṇasya vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a hatāśvād vegavān vegād avaplutya mahārathāt
c krodham āhārayat tīvraṃ bhrātaraṃ prati rāvaṇaḥ
a tataḥ śaktiṃ mahāśaktir dīptāṃ dīptāśanīm iva
c vibhīṣaṇāya cikṣepa rākṣasendraḥ pratāpavān
a aprāptām eva tāṃ bāṇais tribhiś ciccheda lakṣmaṇaḥ
c athodatiṣṭhat saṃnādo vānarāṇāṃ tadā raṇe
a sa papāta tridhā chinnā śaktiḥ kāñcanamālinī
c savisphuliṅgā jvalitā maholkeva divaś cyutā
a tataḥ saṃbhāvitatarāṃ kālenāpi durāsadām
c jagrāha vipulāṃ śaktiṃ dīpyamānāṃ svatejasā
a sā veginā balavatā rāvaṇena durātmanā
c jajvāla sumahāghorā śakrāśanisamaprabhā
a etasminn antare vīro lakṣmaṇas taṃ vibhīṣaṇam
c prāṇasaṃśayam āpannaṃ tūrṇam evābhyapadyata
a taṃ vimokṣayituṃ vīraś cāpam āyamya lakṣmaṇaḥ
c rāvaṇaṃ śaktihastaṃ taṃ śaravarṣair avākirat
a kīryamāṇaḥ śaraugheṇa visṛṣṭtena mahātmanā
c na prahartuṃ manaś cakre vimukhīkṛtavikramaḥ
a mokṣitaṃ bhrātaraṃ dṛṣṭvā lakṣmaṇena sa rāvaṇaḥ
c lakṣmaṇābhimukhas tiṣṭhann idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a mokṣitas te balaślāghin yasmād evaṃ vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c vimucya rākṣasaṃ śaktis tvayīyaṃ vinipātyate
a eṣā te hṛdayaṃ bhittvā śaktir lohitalakṣaṇā
c madbāhuparighotsṛṣṭā prāṇān ādāya yāsyati
a ity evam uktvā tāṃ śaktim aṣṭaghaṇṭāṃ mahāsvanām
c mayena māyāvihitām amoghāṃ śatrughātinīm
a lakṣmaṇāya samuddiśya jvalantīm iva tejasā
c rāvaṇaḥ paramakruddhaś cikṣepa ca nanāda ca
a sā kṣiptā bhīmavegena śakrāśanisamasvanā
c śaktir abhyapatad vegāl lakṣmaṇaṃ raṇamūrdhani
a tām anuvyāharac chaktim āpatantīṃ sa rāghavaḥ
c svastyas tu lakṣmaṇāyeti moghā bhava hatodyamā
a nyapatat sā mahāvegā lakṣmaṇasya mahorasi
c jihvevoragarājasya dīpyamānā mahādyutiḥ
a tato rāvaṇavegena sudūram avagāḍhayā
c śaktyā nirbhinnahṛdayaḥ papāta bhuvi lakṣmaṇaḥ
a tadavasthaṃ samīpastho lakṣmaṇaṃ prekṣya rāghavaḥ
c bhrātṛsnehān mahātejā viṣaṇṇahṛdayo 'bhavat
a sa muhūrtam anudhyāya bāṣpavyākulalocanaḥ
c babhūva saṃrabdhataro yugānta iva pāvakaḥ
a na viṣādasya kālo 'yam iti saṃcintya rāghavaḥ
c cakre sutumulaṃ yuddhaṃ rāvaṇasya vadhe dhṛtaḥ
a sa dadarśa tato rāmaḥ śaktyā bhinnaṃ mahāhave
c lakṣmaṇaṃ rudhirādigdhaṃ sapannagam ivācalam
a tām api prahitāṃ śaktiṃ rāvaṇena balīyasā
c yatnatas te hariśreṣṭhā na śekur avamarditum
e arditāś caiva bāṇaughaiḥ kṣiprahastena rakṣasā
a saumitriṃ sā vinirbhidya praviṣṭā dharaṇītalam
c tāṃ karābhyāṃ parāmṛśya rāmaḥ śaktiṃ bhayāvahām
e babhañja samare kruddho balavad vicakarṣa ca
a tasya niṣkarṣataḥ śaktiṃ rāvaṇena balīyasā
c śarāḥ sarveṣu gātreṣu pātitā marmabhedinaḥ
a acintayitvā tān bāṇān samāśliṣyā ca lakṣmaṇam
c abravīc ca hanūmantaṃ sugrīvaṃ caiva rāghavaḥ
e lakṣmaṇaṃ parivāryeha tiṣṭhadhvaṃ vānarottamāḥ
a parākramasya kālo 'yaṃ saṃprāpto me cirepsitaḥ
c pāpātmāyaṃ daśagrīvo vadhyatāṃ pāpaniścayaḥ
e kāṅkṣitaḥ stokakasyeva gharmānte meghadarśanam
a asmin muhūrte nacirāt satyaṃ pratiśṛṇomi vaḥ
c arāvaṇam arāmaṃ vā jagad drakṣyatha vānarāḥ
a rājyanāśaṃ vane vāsaṃ daṇḍake paridhāvanam
c vaidehyāś ca parāmarśaṃ rakṣobhiś ca samāgamam
a prāptaṃ duḥkhaṃ mahad ghoraṃ kleśaṃ ca nirayopamam
c adya sarvam ahaṃ tyakṣye hatvā taṃ rāvaṇaṃ raṇe
a yadarthaṃ vānaraṃ sainyaṃ samānītam idaṃ mayā
c sugrīvaś ca kṛto rājye nihatvā vālinaṃ raṇe
a yadarthaṃ sāgaraḥ krāntaḥ setur baddhaś ca sāgare
c so 'yam adya raṇe pāpaś cakṣurviṣayam āgataḥ
a cakṣurviṣayam āgamya nāyaṃ jīvitum arhati
c dṛṣṭiṃ dṛṣṭiviṣasyeva sarpasya mama rāvaṇaḥ
a svasthāḥ paśyata durdharṣā yuddhaṃ vānarapuṃgavāḥ
c āsīnāḥ parvatāgreṣu mamedaṃ rāvaṇasya ca
a adya rāmasya rāmatvaṃ paśyantu mama saṃyuge
c trayo lokāḥ sagandharvāḥ sadevāḥ sarṣicāraṇāḥ
a adya karma kariṣyāmi yal lokāḥ sacarācarāḥ
c sadevāḥ kathayiṣyanti yāvad bhūmir dhariṣyati
a evam uktvā śitair bāṇais taptakāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c ājaghāna daśagrīvaṃ raṇe rāmaḥ samāhitaḥ
a atha pradīptair nārācair musalaiś cāpi rāvaṇaḥ
c abhyavarṣat tadā rāmaṃ dhārābhir iva toyadaḥ
a rāmarāvaṇamuktānām anyonyam abhinighnatām
c śarāṇāṃ ca śarāṇāṃ ca babhūva tumulaḥ svanaḥ
a te bhinnāś ca vikīrṇāś ca rāmarāvaṇayoḥ śarāḥ
c antarikṣāt pradīptāgrā nipetur dharaṇītale
a tayor jyātalanirghoṣo rāmarāvaṇayor mahān
c trāsanaḥ sarvabūtānāṃ sa babhūvādbhutopamaḥ
a sa kīryamāṇaḥ śarajālavṛṣṭibhir
mahātmanā dīptadhanuṣmatārditaḥ
c bhayāt pradudrāva sametya rāvaṇo
yathānilenābhihato balāhakaḥ
a sa dattvā tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ rāvaṇasya durātmanaḥ
c visṛjan eva bāṇaughān suṣeṇaṃ vākyam abravīt
a eṣa rāvaṇavegena lakṣmaṇaḥ patitaḥ kṣitau
c sarpavad veṣṭate vīro mama śokam udīrayan
a śoṇitārdram imaṃ vīraṃ prāṇair iṣṭataraṃ mama
c paśyato mama kā śaktir yoddhuṃ paryākulātmanaḥ
a ayaṃ sa samaraślāghī bhrātā me śubhalakṣaṇaḥ
c yadi pañcatvam āpannaḥ prāṇair me kiṃ sukhena vā
a lajjatīva hi me vīryaṃ bhraśyatīva karād dhanuḥ
c sāyakā vyavasīdanti dṛṣṭir bāṣpavaśaṃ gatā
e cintā me vardhate tīvrā mumūrṣā copajāyate
a bhrātaraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇena durātmanā
c paraṃ viṣādam āpanno vilalāpākulendriyaḥ
a na hi yuddhena me kāryaṃ naiva prāṇair na sītayā
c bhrātaraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā lakṣmaṇaṃ raṇapāṃsuṣu
a kiṃ me rājyena kiṃ prāṇair yuddhe kāryaṃ na vidyate
c yatrāyaṃ nihataḥ śete raṇamūrdhani lakṣmaṇaḥ
a rāmam āśvāsayan vīraḥ suṣeṇo vākyam abravīt
c na mṛto 'yaṃ mahābāhur lakṣmaṇo lakṣmivardhanaḥ
a na cāsya vikṛtaṃ vaktraṃ nāpi śyāmaṃ na niṣprabham
c suprabhaṃ ca prasannaṃ ca mukham asyābhilakṣyate
a padmaraktatalau hastau suprasanne ca locane
c evaṃ na vidyate rūpaṃ gatāsūnāṃ viśāṃ pate
e māṃ viṣādaṃ kṛtvā vīra saprāṇo 'yam ariṃdama
a ākhyāsyate prasuptasya srastagātrasya bhūtale
c socchvāsaṃ hṛdayaṃ vīra kampamānaṃ muhur muhuḥ
a evam uktvā tu vākyajñaḥ suṣeṇo rāghavaṃ vacaḥ
c samīpastham uvācedaṃ hanūmantam abhitvaran
a saumya śīghram ito gatvā śailam oṣadhiparvatam
c pūrvaṃ hi kathito yo 'sau vīra jāmbavatā śubhaḥ
a dakṣiṇe śikhare tasya jātām oṣadhim ānaya
c viśalyakaraṇī nāma viśalyakaraṇīṃ śubhām
a sauvarṇakaraṇīṃ cāpi tathā saṃjīvanīm api
c saṃdhānakaraṇīṃ cāpi gatvā śīghram ihānaya
e saṃjīvanārthaṃ vīrasya lakṣmaṇasya mahātmanaḥ
a ity evam ukto hanumān gatvā cauṣadhiparvatam
c cintām abhyagamac chrīmān ajānaṃs tā mahauṣadhīḥ
a tasya buddhiḥ samutpannā māruter amitaujasaḥ
c idam eva gamiṣyāmi gṛhītvā śikharaṃ gireḥ
a agṛhya yadi gacchāmi viśalyakaraṇīm aham
c kālātyayena doṣaḥ syād vaiklavyaṃ ca mahad bhavet
a iti saṃcintya hanumān gatvā kṣipraṃ mahābalaḥ
c utpapāta gṛhītvā tu hanūmāñ śikharaṃ gireḥ
a oṣadhīr nāvagachāmi tā ahaṃ haripuṃgava
c tad idaṃ śikharaṃ kṛtsnaṃ gires tasyāhṛtaṃ mayā
a evaṃ kathayamānaṃ taṃ praśasya pavanātmajam
c suṣeṇo vānaraśreṣṭho jagrāhotpāṭya cauṣadhīḥ
a tataḥ saṃkṣodayitvā tām oṣadhiṃ vānarottamaḥ
c lakṣmaṇasya dadau nastaḥ suṣeṇaḥ sumahādyutiḥ
a saśalyaḥ sa samāghrāya lakṣmaṇaḥ paravīrahā
c viśalyo virujaḥ śīghram udatiṣṭhan mahītalāt
a samutthitaṃ te harayo bhūtalāt prekṣya lakṣmaṇam
c sādhu sādhv iti suprītāḥ suṣeṇaṃ pratyapūjayan
a ehy ehīty abravīd rāmo lakṣmaṇaṃ paravīrahā
c sasvaje snehagāḍhaṃ ca bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇaḥ
a abravīc ca pariṣvajya saumitriṃ rāghavas tadā
c diṣṭyā tvāṃ vīra paśyāmi maraṇāt punar āgatam
a na hi me jīvitenārthaḥ sītayā ca jayena vā
c ko hi me jīvitenārthas tvayi pañcatvam āgate
a ity evaṃ vadatas tasya rāghavasya mahātmanaḥ
c khinnaḥ śithilayā vācā lakṣmaṇo vākyam abravīt
a tāṃ pratijñāṃ pratijñāya purā satyaparākrama
c laghuḥ kaś cid ivāsattvo naivaṃ vaktum ihārhasi
a na pratijñāṃ hi kurvanti vitathāṃ sādhavo 'nagha
c lakṣmaṇaṃ hi mahat tv asya pratijñāparipālanam
a nairāśyam upagantuṃ te tad alaṃ matkṛte 'nagha
c vadhena rāvaṇasyādya pratijñām anupālaya
a na jīvan yāsyate śatrus tava bāṇapathaṃ gataḥ
c nardatas tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrasya siṃhasyeva mahāgajaḥ
a ahaṃ tu vadham icchāmi śīghram asya durātmanaḥ
c yāvad astaṃ na yāty eṣa kṛtakarmā divākaraḥ
a lakṣmaṇena tu tad vākyam uktaṃ śrutvā sa rāghavaḥ
c rāvaṇāya śarān ghorān visasarja camūmukhe
a daśagrīvo rathasthas tu rāmaṃ vajropamaiḥ śaraiḥ
c ājaghāna mahāghorair dhārābhir iva toyadaḥ
a dīptapāvakasaṃkāśaiḥ śaraiḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c nirbibheda raṇe rāmo daśagrīvaṃ samāhitaḥ
a bhūmisthitasya rāmasya rathasthasya ca rakṣasaḥ
c na samaṃ yuddham ity āhur devagandharvadānavāḥ
a tataḥ kāñcanacitrāṅgaḥ kiṃkiṇīśatabhūṣitaḥ
c taruṇādityasaṃkāśo vaidūryamayakūbaraḥ
a sadaśvaiḥ kāñcanāpīḍair yuktaḥ śvetaprakīrṇakaiḥ
c haribhiḥ sūryasaṃkāśair hemajālavibhūṣitaiḥ
a rukmaveṇudhvajaḥ śrīmān devarājaratho varaḥ
c abhyavartata kākutstham avatīrya triviṣṭapāt
a abravīc ca tadā rāmaṃ sapratodo rathe sthitaḥ
c prāñjalir mātalir vākyaṃ sahasrākṣasya sārathiḥ
a sahasrākṣeṇa kākutstha ratho 'yaṃ vijayāya te
c dattas tava mahāsattva śrīmāñ śatrunibarhaṇaḥ
a idam aindraṃ mahaccāpaṃ kavacaṃ cāgnisaṃnibham
c śarāś cādityasaṃkāśāḥ śaktiś ca vimalā śitāḥ
a āruhyemaṃ rathaṃ vīra rākṣasaṃ jahi rāvaṇam
c mayā sārathinā rāma mahendra iva dānavān
a ity uktaḥ sa parikramya rathaṃ tam abhivādya ca
c āruroha tadā rāmo lokāṃl lakṣmyā virājayan
a tad babhūvādbhutaṃ yuddhaṃ dvairathaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c rāmasya ca mahābāho rāvaṇasya ca rakṣasaḥ
a sa gāndharveṇa gāndharvaṃ daivaṃ daivena rāghavaḥ
c astraṃ rākṣasarājasya jaghāna paramāstravit
a astraṃ tu paramaṃ ghoraṃ rākṣasaṃ rākasādhipa
c sasarja paramakruddhaḥ punar eva niśācaraḥ
a te rāvaṇadhanurmuktāḥ śarāḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇāḥ
c abhyavartanta kākutsthaṃ sarpā bhūtvā mahāviṣāḥ
a te dīptavadanā dīptaṃ vamanto jvalanaṃ mukhaiḥ
c rāmam evābhyavartanta vyāditāsyā bhayānakāḥ
a tair vāsukisamasparśair dīptabhogair mahāviṣaiḥ
c diśaś ca saṃtatāḥ sarvāḥ pradiśaś ca samāvṛtāḥ
a tān dṛṣṭvā pannagān rāmaḥ samāpatata āhave
c astraṃ gārutmataṃ ghoraṃ prāduścakre bhayāvaham
a te rāghavadhanurmuktā rukmapuṅkhāḥ śikhiprabhāḥ
c suparṇāḥ kāñcanā bhūtvā viceruḥ sarpaśatravaḥ
a te tān sarvāñ śarāñ jaghnuḥ sarparūpān mahājavān
c suparṇarūpā rāmasya viśikhāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
a astre pratihate kruddho rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ
c abhyavarṣat tadā rāmaṃ ghorābhiḥ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
a tataḥ śarasahasreṇa rāmam akliṣṭakāriṇam
c ardayitvā śaraugheṇa mātaliṃ pratyavidhyata
a pātayitvā rathopasthe rathāt ketuṃ ca kāñcanam
c aindrān abhijaghānāśvāñ śarajālena rāvaṇaḥ
a viṣedur devagandharvā dānavāś cāraṇaiḥ saha
c rāmam ārtaṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
a vyathitā vānarendrāś ca babhūvuḥ savibhīṣaṇāḥ
c rāmacandramasaṃ dṛṣṭvā grastaṃ rāvaṇarāhuṇā
a prājāpatyaṃ ca nakṣatraṃ rohiṇīṃ śaśinaḥ priyām
c samākramya budhas tasthau prajānām aśubhāvahaḥ
a sadhūmaparivṛttormiḥ prajvalann iva sāgaraḥ
c utpapāta tadā kruddhaḥ spṛśann iva divākaram
a śastravarṇaḥ suparuṣo mandaraśmir divākaraḥ
c adṛśyata kabandhāṅgaḥ saṃsakto dhūmaketunā
a kosalānāṃ ca nakṣatraṃ vyaktam indrāgnidaivatam
c ākramyāṅgārakas tasthau viśākhām api cāmbare
a daśāsyo viṃśatibhujaḥ pragṛhītaśarāsanaḥ
c adṛśyata daśagrīvo maināka iva parvataḥ
a nirasyamāno rāmas tu daśagrīveṇa rakṣasā
c nāśakad abhisaṃdhātuṃ sāyakān raṇamūrdhani
a sa kṛtvā bhrukuṭīṃ kruddhaḥ kiṃ cit saṃraktalocanaḥ
c jagāma sumahākrodhaṃ nirdahann iva cakṣuṣā
a tasya kruddhasya vadanaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmasya dhīmataḥ
c sarvabhūtāni vitreṣuḥ prākampata ca medinī
a siṃhaśārdūlavāñ śailaḥ saṃcacālācaladrumaḥ
c babhūva cāpi kṣubhitaḥ samudraḥ saritāṃ patiḥ
a khagāś ca kharanirghoṣā gagane paruṣasvanāḥ
c autpātikā vinardantaḥ samantāt paricakramuḥ
a rāmaṃ dṛṣṭvā susaṃkruddham utpātāṃś ca sudāruṇān
c vitreṣuḥ sarvabhūtāni rāvaṇasyāviśad bhayam
a vimānasthās tadā devā gandharvāś ca mahoragāḥ
c ṛṣidānavadaityāś ca garutmantaś ca khecarāḥ
a dadṛśus te tadā yuddhaṃ lokasaṃvartasaṃsthitam
c nānāpraharaṇair bhīmaiḥ śūrayoḥ saṃprayudhyatoḥ
a ūcuḥ surāsurāḥ sarve tadā vigraham āgatāḥ
c prekṣamāṇā mahāyuddhaṃ vākyaṃ bhaktyā prahṛṣṭavat
a daśagrīvaṃ jayety āhur asurāḥ samavasthitāḥ
c devā rāmam athocus te tvaṃ jayeti punaḥ punaḥ
a etasminn antare krodhād rāghavasya sa rāvaṇaḥ
c prahartukāmo duṣṭātmā spṛśan praharaṇaṃ mahat
a vajrasāraṃ mahānādaṃ sarvaśatrunibarhaṇam
c śailaśṛṅganibhaiḥ kūṭaiś citaṃ dṛṣṭibhayāvaham
a sadhūmam iva tīkṣṇāgraṃ yugāntāgnicayopamam
c atiraudram anāsādyaṃ kālenāpi durāsadam
a trāsanaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ dāraṇaṃ bhedanaṃ tathā
c pradīpta iva roṣeṇa śūlaṃ jagrāha rāvaṇaḥ
a tac chūlaṃ paramakruddho madhye jagrāha vīryavān
c anekaiḥ samare śūrai rākṣasaiḥ parivāritaḥ
a samudyamya mahākāyo nanāda yudhi bhairavam
c saṃraktanayano roṣāt svasainyam abhiharṣayan
a pṛthivīṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca diśaś ca pradiśas tathā
c prākampayat tadā śabdo rākṣasendrasya dāruṇaḥ
a atinādasya nādena tena tasya durātmanaḥ
c sarvabhūtāni vitreṣuḥ sāgaraś ca pracukṣubhe
a sa gṛhītvā mahāvīryaḥ śūlaṃ tad rāvaṇo mahat
c vinadya sumahānādaṃ rāmaṃ paruṣam abravīt
a śūlo 'yaṃ vajrasāras te rāma roṣān mayodyataḥ
c tava bhrātṛsahāyasya sadyaḥ prāṇān hariṣyati
a rakṣasām adya śūrāṇāṃ nihatānāṃ camūmukhe
c tvāṃ nihatya raṇaślāghin karomi tarasā samam
a tiṣṭhedānīṃ nihanmi tvām eṣa śūlena rāghava
c evam uktvā sa cikṣepa tac chūlaṃ rākṣasādhipaḥ
a āpatantaṃ śaraugheṇa vārayām āsa rāghavaḥ
c utpatantaṃ yugāntāgniṃ jalaughair iva vāsavaḥ
a nirdadāha sa tān bāṇān rāmakārmukaniḥsṛtān
c rāvaṇasya mahāśūlaḥ pataṃgān iva pāvakaḥ
a tān dṛṣṭvā bhasmasād bhūtāñ śūlasaṃsparśacūrṇitān
c sāyakān antarikṣasthān rāghavaḥ krodham āharat
a sa tāṃ mātalinānītāṃ śaktiṃ vāsavanirmitām
c jagrāha paramakruddho rāghavo raghunandanaḥ
a sā tolitā balavatā śaktir ghaṇṭākṛtasvanā
c nabhaḥ prajvālayām āsa yugāntoklena saprabhā
a sā kṣiptā rākṣasendrasya tasmiñ śūle papāta ha
c bhinnaḥ śaktyā mahāñ śūlo nipapāta gatadyutiḥ
a nirbibheda tato bāṇair hayān asya mahājavān
c rāmas tīkṣṇair mahāvegair vajrakalpaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a nirbibhedorasi tadā rāvaṇaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c rāghavaḥ paramāyatto lalāṭe patribhis tribhiḥ
a sa śarair bhinnasarvāṅgo gātraprasruta śoṇitaḥ
c rākṣasendraḥ samūhasthaḥ phullāśoka ivābabhau
a sa rāmabāṇair atividdhagātro
niśācarendraḥ kṣatajārdragātraḥ
c jagāma khedaṃ ca samājamadhye
krodhaṃ ca cakre subhṛśaṃ tadānīm
a sa tu tena tadā krodhāt kākutsthenārdito raṇe
c rāvaṇaḥ samaraślāghī mahākrodham upāgamat
a sa dīptanayano roṣāc cāpam āyamya vīryavān
c abhyardayat susaṃkruddho rāghavaṃ paramāhave
a bāṇadhārā sahasrais tu sa toyada ivāmbarāt
c rāghavaṃ rāvaṇo bāṇais taṭākam iva pūrayat
a pūritaḥ śarajālena dhanurmuktena saṃyuge
c mahāgirir ivākampyaḥ kākustho na prakampate
a sa śaraiḥ śarajālāni vārayan samare sthitaḥ
c gabhastīn iva sūryasya pratijagrāha vīryavān
a tataḥ śarasahasrāṇi kṣiprahasto niśācaraḥ
c nijaghānorasi kruddho rāghavasya mahātmanaḥ
a sa śoṇita samādigdhaḥ samare lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥ
c dṛṣṭaḥ phulla ivāraṇye sumahān kiṃśukadrumaḥ
a śarābhighātasaṃrabdhaḥ so 'pi jagrāha sāyakān
c kākutsthaḥ sumahātejā yugāntādityavarcasaḥ
a tato 'nyonyaṃ susaṃrabdhāv ubhau tau rāmarāvaṇau
c śarāndhakāre samare nopālakṣayatāṃ tadā
a tataḥ krodhasamāviṣṭo rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ
c uvāca rāvaṇaṃ vīraḥ prahasya paruṣaṃ vacaḥ
a mama bhāryā janasthānād ajñānād rākṣasādhama
c hṛtā te vivaśā yasmāt tasmāt tvaṃ nāsi vīryavān
a mayā virahitāṃ dīnāṃ vartamānāṃ mahāvane
c vaidehīṃ prasabhaṃ hṛtvā śūro 'ham iti manyase
a strīṣu śūra vināthāsu paradārābhimarśake
c kṛtvā kāpuruṣaṃ karma śūro 'ham iti manyase
a bhinnamaryāda nirlajja cāritreṣv anavasthita
c darpān mṛtyum upādāya śūro 'ham iti manyase
a śūreṇa dhanadabhrātrā balaiḥ samuditena ca
c ślāghanīyaṃ yaśasyaṃ ca kṛtaṃ karma mahat tvayā
a utsekenābhipannasya garhitasyāhitasya ca
c karmaṇaḥ prāpnuhīdānīṃ tasyādya sumahat phalam
a śūro 'ham iti cātmānam avagacchasi durmate
c naiva lajjāsti te sītāṃ coravad vyapakarṣataḥ
a yadi matsaṃnidhau sītā dharṣitā syāt tvayā balāt
c bhrātaraṃ tu kharaṃ paśyes tadā matsāyakair hataḥ
a diṣṭyāsi mama duṣṭātmaṃś cakṣurviṣayam āgataḥ
c adya tvāṃ sāyakais tīkṣṇair nayāmi yamasādanam
a adya te maccharaiś chinnaṃ śiro jvalitakuṇḍalam
c kravyādā vyapakarṣantu vikīrṇaṃ raṇapāṃsuṣu
a nipatyorasi gṛdhrās te kṣitau kṣiptasya rāvaṇa
c pibantu rudhiraṃ tarṣād bāṇaśalyāntarothitam
a adya madbāṇābhinnasya gatāsoḥ patitasya te
c karṣantv antrāṇi patagā garutmanta ivoragān
a ity evaṃ sa vadan vīro rāmaḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥ
c rākṣasendraṃ samīpasthaṃ śaravarṣair avākirat
a babhūva dviguṇaṃ vīryaṃ balaṃ harṣaś ca saṃyuge
c rāmasyāstrabalaṃ caiva śatror nidhanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
a prādurbabhūvur astrāṇi sarvāṇi viditātmanaḥ
c praharṣāc ca mahātejāḥ śīghrahastataro 'bhavat
a śubhāny etāni cihnāni vijñāyātmagatāni saḥ
c bhūya evārdayad rāmo rāvaṇaṃ rākṣasāntakṛt
a harīṇāṃ cāśmanikaraiḥ śaravarṣaiś ca rāghavāt
c hanyamāno daśagrīvo vighūrṇahṛdayo 'bhavat
a yadā ca śastraṃ nārebhe na vyakarṣac charāsanam
c nāsya pratyakarod vīryaṃ viklavenāntarātmanā
a kṣiptāś cāpi śarās tena śastrāṇi vividhāni ca
c na raṇārthāya vartante mṛtyukāle 'bhivartataḥ
a sūtas tu rathanetāsya tadavasthaṃ nirīkṣya tam
c śanair yuddhād asaṃbhānto rathaṃ tasyāpavāhayat
a sa tu mohāt susaṃkruddhaḥ kṛtāntabalacoditaḥ
c krodhasaṃraktanayano rāvaṇo sūtam abravīt
a hīnavīryam ivāśaktaṃ pauruṣeṇa vivarjitam
c bhīruṃ laghum ivāsattvaṃ vihīnam iva tejasā
a vimuktam iva māyābhir astrair iva bahiṣkṛtam
c mām avajñāya durbuddhe svayā buddhyā viceṣṭase
a kimarthaṃ mām avajñāya macchandam anavekṣya ca
c tvayā śatrusamakṣaṃ me ratho 'yam apavāhitaḥ
a tvayādya hi mamānārya cirakālasamārjitam
c yaśo vīryaṃ ca tejaś ca pratyayaś ca vināśitha
a śatroḥ prakhyātavīryasya rañjanīyasya vikramaiḥ
c paśyato yuddhalubdho 'haṃ kṛtaḥ kāpuruṣas tvayā
a yas tvaṃ ratham imaṃ mohān na codvahasi durmate
c satyo 'yaṃ pratitarko me pareṇa tvam upaskṛtaḥ
a na hīdaṃ vidyate karma suhṛdo hitakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
c ripūṇāṃ sadṛśaṃ caitan na tvayaitat svanuṣṭhitam
a nivartaya rathaṃ śīghraṃ yāvan nāpaiti me ripuḥ
c yadi vāpy uṣito 'si tvaṃ smaryante yadi vā guṇāḥ
a evaṃ paruṣam uktas tu hitabuddhir abuddhinā
c abravīd rāvaṇaṃ sūto hitaṃ sānunayaṃ vacaḥ
a na bhīto 'smi na mūḍho 'smi nopajapto 'smi śatrubhiḥ
c na pramatto na niḥsneho vismṛtā na ca satkriyā
a mayā tu hitakāmena yaśaś ca parirakṣatā
c snehapraskannamanasā priyam ity apriyaṃ kṛtam
a nāsminn arthe mahārāja tvaṃ māṃ priyahite ratam
c kaś cil laghur ivānāryo doṣato gantum arhasi
a śrūyatām abhidhāsyāmi yannimittaṃ mayā rathaḥ
c nadīvega ivāmbhobhiḥ saṃyuge vinivartitaḥ
a śramaṃ tavāvagacchāmi mahatā raṇakarmaṇā
c na hi te vīra saumukhyaṃ praharṣaṃ vopadhāraye
a rathodvahanakhinnāś ca ta ime rathavājinaḥ
c dīnā gharmapariśrāntā gāvo varṣahatā iva
a nimittāni ca bhūyiṣṭhaṃ yāni prādurbhavanti naḥ
c teṣu teṣv abhipanneṣu lakṣayāmy apradakṣiṇam
a deśakālau ca vijñeyau lakṣmaṇānīṅgitāni ca
c dainyaṃ harṣaś ca khedaś ca rathinaś ca balābalam
a sthalanimnāni bhūmeś ca samāni viṣamāṇi ca
c yuddhakālaś ca vijñeyaḥ parasyāntaradarśanam
a upayānāpayāne ca sthānaṃ pratyapasarpaṇam
c sarvam etad rathasthena jñeyaṃ rathakuṭumbinā
a tava viśrāmahetos tu tathaiṣāṃ rathavājinām
c raudraṃ varjayatā khedaṃ kṣamaṃ kṛtam idaṃ mayā
a na mayā svecchayā vīra ratho 'yam apavāhitaḥ
c bhartṛsnehaparītena mayedaṃ yatkṛtaṃ vibho
a ājñāpaya yathātattvaṃ vakṣyasy ariniṣūdana
c tat kariṣyāmy ahaṃ vīraṃ gatānṛṇyena cetasā
a saṃtuṣṭas tena vākyena rāvaṇas tasya sāratheḥ
c praśasyainaṃ bahuvidhaṃ yuddhalubdho 'bravīd idam
a rathaṃ śīghram imaṃ sūta rāghavābhimukhaṃ kuru
c nāhatvā samare śatrūn nivartiṣyati rāvaṇaḥ
a evam uktvā tatas tuṣṭo rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c dadau tasya śubhaṃ hy ekaṃ hastābharaṇam uttamam
a tato drutaṃ rāvaṇavākyacoditaḥ
pracodayām āsa hayān sa sārathiḥ
c sa rākṣasendrasya tato mahārathaḥ
kṣaṇena rāmasya raṇāgrato 'bhavat
a tam āpatantaṃ sahasā svanavantaṃ mahādhvajam
c rathaṃ rākṣasarājasya nararājo dadarśa ha
a kṛṣṇavājisamāyuktaṃ yuktaṃ raudreṇa varcasā
c taḍitpatākāgahanaṃ darśitendrāyudhāyudham
e śaradhārā vimuñcantaṃ dhārāsāram ivānbudam
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā meghasaṃkāśam āpatantaṃ rathaṃ ripoḥ
c girer vajrābhimṛṣṭasya dīryataḥ sadṛśasvanam
e uvāca mātaliṃ rāmaḥ sahasrākṣasya sārathim
a mātale paśya saṃrabdham āpatantaṃ rathaṃ ripoḥ
c yathāpasavyaṃ patatā vegena mahatā punaḥ
e samare hantum ātmānaṃ tathānena kṛtā matiḥ
a tad apramādam ātiṣṭha pratyudgaccha rathaṃ ripoḥ
c vidhvaṃsayitum icchāmi vāyur megham ivotthitam
a aviklavam asaṃbhrāntam avyagrahṛdayekṣaṇam
c raśmisaṃcāraniyataṃ pracodaya rathaṃ drutam
a kāmaṃ na tvaṃ samādheyaḥ puraṃdararathocitaḥ
c yuyutsur aham ekāgraḥ smāraye tvāṃ na śikṣaye
a parituṣṭaḥ sa rāmasya tena vākyena mātaliḥ
c pracodayām āsa rathaṃ surasārathisattamaḥ
a apasavyaṃ tataḥ kurvan rāvaṇasya mahāratham
c cakrotkṣiptena rajasā rāvaṇaṃ vyavadhūnayat
a tataḥ kruddho daśagrīvas tāmravisphāritekṣaṇaḥ
c rathapratimukhaṃ rāmaṃ sāyakair avadhūnayat
a dharṣaṇāmarṣito rāmo dhairyaṃ roṣeṇa laṅghayan
c jagrāha sumahāvegam aindraṃ yudhi śarāsanam
e śarāṃś ca sumahātejāḥ sūryaraśmisamaprabhān
a tad upoḍhaṃ mahad yuddham anyonyavadhakāṅkṣiṇoḥ
c parasparābhimukhayor dṛptayor iva siṃhayoḥ
a tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
c samīyur dvairathaṃ draṣṭuṃ rāvaṇakṣayakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
a samutpetur athotpātā dāruṇā lomaharṣaṇāḥ
c rāvaṇasya vināśāya rāghavasya jayāya ca
a vavarṣa rudhiraṃ devo rāvaṇasya rathopari
c vātā maṇḍalinas tīvrā apasavyaṃ pracakramuḥ
a mahad gṛdhrakulaṃ cāsya bhramamāṇaṃ nabhastale
c yena yena ratho yāti tena tena pradhāvati
a saṃdhyayā cāvṛtā laṅkā japāpuṣpanikāśayā
c dṛśyate saṃpradīteva divase 'pi vasuṃdharā
a sanirghātā maholkāś ca saṃpracetur mahāsvanāḥ
c viṣādayantyo rakṣāṃsi rāvaṇasya tadāhitāḥ
a rāvaṇaś ca yatas tatra pracacāla vasuṃdharā
c rakṣasāṃ ca praharatāṃ gṛhītā iva bāhavaḥ
a tāmrāḥ pītāḥ sitāḥ śvetāḥ patitāḥ sūryaraśmayaḥ
c dṛśyante rāvaṇasyāṅge parvatasyeva dhātavaḥ
a gṛdhrair anugatāś cāsya vamantyo jvalanaṃ mukhaiḥ
c praṇedur mukham īkṣantyaḥ saṃrabdham aśivaṃ śivāḥ
a pratikūlaṃ vavau vāyū raṇe pāṃsūn samutkiran
c tasya rākṣasarājasya kurvan dṛṣṭivilopanam
a nipetur indrāśanayaḥ sainye cāsya samantataḥ
c durviṣahya svanā ghorā vinā jaladharasvanam
a diśaś ca pradiśaḥ sarvā babhūvus timirāvṛtāḥ
c pāṃsuvarṣeṇa mahatā durdarśaṃ ca nabho 'bhavat
a kurvantyaḥ kalahaṃ ghoraṃ sārikās tadrathaṃ prati
c nipetuḥ śataśas tatra dāruṇā dāruṇasvanāḥ
a jaghanebhyaḥ sphuliṅgāṃś ca netrebhyo 'śrūṇi saṃtatam
c mumucus tasya turagās tulyam agniṃ ca vāri ca
a evaṃ prakārā bahavaḥ samutpātā bhayāvahāḥ
c rāvaṇasya vināśāya dāruṇāḥ saṃprajajñire
a rāmasyāpi nimittāni saumyāni ca śivāni ca
c babhūvur jayaśaṃsīni prādurbhūtāni sarvaśaḥ
a tato nirīkṣyātmagatāni rāghavo
raṇe nimittāni nimittakovidaḥ
c jagāma harṣaṃ ca parāṃ ca nirvṛtiṃ
cakāra yuddhe 'bhyadhikaṃ ca vikramam
a tataḥ pravṛttaṃ sukrūraṃ rāmarāvaṇayos tadā
c sumahad dvairathaṃ yuddhaṃ sarvalokabhayāvaham
a tato rākṣasasainyaṃ ca harīṇāṃ ca mahad balam
c pragṛhītapraharaṇaṃ niśceṣṭaṃ samatiṣṭhata
a saṃprayuddhau tato dṛṣṭvā balavan nararākṣasau
c vyākṣiptahṛdayāḥ sarve paraṃ vismayam āgatāḥ
a nānāpraharaṇair vyagrair bhujair vismitabuddhayaḥ
c tasthuḥ prekṣya ca saṃgrāmaṃ nābhijaghnuḥ parasparam
a rakṣasāṃ rāvaṇaṃ cāpi vānarāṇāṃ ca rāghavam
c paśyatāṃ vismitākṣāṇāṃ sainyaṃ citram ivābabhau
a tau tu tatra nimittāni dṛṣṭvā rāghavarāvaṇau
c kṛtabuddhī sthirāmarṣau yuyudhāte abhītavat
a jetavyam iti kākutstho martavyam iti rāvaṇaḥ
c dhṛtau svavīryasarvasvaṃ yuddhe 'darśayatāṃ tadā
a tataḥ krodhād daśagrīvaḥ śarān saṃdhāya vīryavān
c mumoca dhvajam uddiśya rāghavasya rathe sthitam
a te śarās tam anāsādya puraṃdararathadhvajam
c raktaśaktiṃ parāmṛśya nipetur dharaṇītale
a tato rāmo 'bhisaṃkruddhaś cāpam āyamya vīryavān
c kṛtapratikṛtaṃ kartuṃ manasā saṃpracakrame
a rāvaṇadhvajam uddiśya mumoca niśitaṃ śaram
c mahāsarpam ivāsahyaṃ jvalantaṃ svena tejasā
a jagāma sa mahīṃ bhittvā daśagrīvadhvajaṃ śaraḥ
c sa nikṛtto 'patad bhūmau rāvaṇasya rathadhvajaḥ
a dhvajasyonmathanaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇaḥ sumahābalaḥ
c krodhajenāgninā saṃkhye pradīpta iva cābhavat
a sa roṣavaśam āpannaḥ śaravarṣaṃ mahad vaman
c rāmasya turagān divyāñ śarair vivyādha rāvaṇaḥ
a te viddhā harayas tasya nāskhalan nāpi babhramuḥ
c babhūvuḥ svasthahṛdayāḥ padmanālair ivāhatāḥ
a teṣām asaṃbhramaṃ dṛṣṭvā vājināṃ rāvaṇas tadā
c bhūya eva susaṃkruddhaḥ śaravarṣaṃ mumoca ha
a gadāś ca parighāṃś caiva cakrāṇi musalāni ca
c giriśṛṅgāṇi vṛkṣāṃś ca tathā śūlaparaśvadhān
a māyā vihitam etat tu śastravarṣam apātayat
c sahasraśas tato bāṇān aśrāntahṛdayodyamaḥ
a tumulaṃ trāsajananaṃ bhīmaṃ bhīmapratisvanam
c durdharṣam abhavad yuddhe naikaśastramayaṃ mahat
a vimucya rāghavarathaṃ samantād vānare bale
c sāyakair antarikṣaṃ ca cakārāśu nirantaram
e mumoca ca daśagrīvo niḥsaṅgenāntarātmanā
a vyāyacchamānaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā tatparaṃ rāvaṇaṃ raṇe
c prahasann iva kākutsthaḥ saṃdadhe sāyakāñ śitān
a sa mumoca tato bāṇān raṇe śatasahasraśaḥ
c tān dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇaś cakre svaśaraiḥ khaṃ nirantaram
a tatas tābhyāṃ prayuktena śaravarṣeṇa bhāsvatā
c śarabaddham ivābhāti dvitīyaṃ bhāsvad ambaram
a nānimitto 'bhavad bāṇo nātibhettā na niṣphalaḥ
c tathā visṛjator bāṇān rāmarāvaṇayor mṛdhe
a prāyudhyetām avicchinnam asyantau savyadakṣiṇam
c cakratus tau śaraughais tu nirucchvāsam ivāmbaram
a rāvaṇasya hayān rāmo hayān rāmasya rāvaṇaḥ
c jaghnatus tau tadānyonyaṃ kṛtānukṛtakāriṇau
a tau tathā yudhyamānau tu samare rāmarāvaṇau
c dadṛśuḥ sarvabhūtāni vismitenāntarātmanā
a ardayantau tu samare tayos tau syandanottamau
c parasparavadhe yuktau ghorarūpau babhūvatuḥ
a maṇḍalāni ca vīthīś ca gatapratyāgatāni ca
c darśayantau bahuvidhāṃ sūtau sārathyajāṃ gatim
a ardayan rāvaṇaṃ rāmo rāghavaṃ cāpi rāvaṇaḥ
c gativegaṃ samāpannau pravartana nivartane
a kṣipatoḥ śarajālāni tayos tau syandanottamau
c ceratuḥ saṃyugamahīṃ sāsārau jaladāv iva
a darśayitvā tadā tau tu gatiṃ bahuvidhāṃ raṇe
c parasparasyābhimukhau punar eva ca tasthatuḥ
a dhuraṃ dhureṇa rathayor vaktraṃ vaktreṇa vājinām
c patākāś ca patākābhiḥ sameyuḥ sthitayos tadā
a rāvaṇasya tato rāmo dhanurmuktaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c caturbhiś caturo dīptān hayān pratyapasarpayat
a sa krodhavaśam āpanno hayānām apasarpaṇe
c mumoca niśitān bāṇān rāghavāya niśācaraḥ
a so 'tividdho balavatā daśagrīveṇa rāghavaḥ
c jagāma na vikāraṃ ca na cāpi vyathito 'bhavat
a cikṣepa ca punar bāṇān vajrapātasamasvanān
c sārathiṃ vajrahastasya samuddiśya niśācaraḥ
a mātales tu mahāvegāḥ śarīre patitāḥ śarāḥ
c na sūkṣmam api saṃmohaṃ vyathāṃ vā pradadur yudhi
a tayā dharṣaṇayā kroddho mātaler na tathātmanaḥ
c cakāra śarajālena rāghavo vimukhaṃ ripum
a viṃśatiṃ triṃśataṃ ṣaṣṭiṃ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
c mumoca rāghavo vīraḥ sāyakān syandane ripoḥ
a gadānāṃ musalānāṃ ca parighāṇāṃ ca nisvanaiḥ
c śarāṇāṃ puṅkhavātaiś ca kṣubhitāḥ saptasāgarāḥ
a kṣubdhānāṃ sāgarāṇāṃ ca pātālatalavāsinaḥ
c vyathitāḥ pannagāḥ sarve dānavāś ca sahasraśaḥ
a cakampe medinī kṛtsnā saśailavanakānanā
c bhāskaro niṣprabhaś cābhūn na vavau cāpi mārutaḥ
a tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
c cintām āpedire sarve sakiṃnaramahoragāḥ
a svasti gobrāhmaṇebhyo 'stu lokās tiṣṭhantu śāśvatāḥ
c jayatāṃ rāghavaḥ saṃkhye rāvaṇaṃ rākṣaseśvaram
a tataḥ kruddho mahābāhū raghūṇāṃ kīrtivardhanaḥ
c saṃdhāya dhanuṣā rāmaḥ kṣuram āśīviṣopamam
e rāvaṇasya śiro 'cchindac chrīmaj jvalitakuṇḍalam
a tac chiraḥ patitaṃ bhūmau dṛṣṭaṃ lokais tribhis tadā
c tasyaiva sadṛśaṃ cānyad rāvaṇasyotthitaṃ śiraḥ
a tat kṣipraṃ kṣiprahastena rāmeṇa kṣiprakāriṇā
c dvitīyaṃ rāvaṇaśiraś chinnaṃ saṃyati sāyakaiḥ
a chinnamātraṃ ca tac chīrṣaṃ punar anyat sma dṛśyate
c tad apy aśanisaṃkāśaiś chinnaṃ rāmeṇa sāyakaiḥ
a evam eva śataṃ chinnaṃ śirasāṃ tulyavarcasām
c na caiva rāvaṇasyānto dṛśyate jīvitakṣaye
a tataḥ sarvāstravid vīraḥ kausalyānandivardhanaḥ
c mārgaṇair bahubhir yuktaś cintayām āsa rāghavaḥ
a mārīco nihato yais tu kharo yais tu sudūṣaṇaḥ
c krañcāraṇye virādhas tu kabandho daṇḍakā vane
a ta ime sāyakāḥ sarve yuddhe pratyayikā mama
c kiṃ nu tat kāraṇaṃ yena rāvaṇe mandatejasaḥ
a iti cintāparaś cāsīd apramattaś ca saṃyuge
c vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi rāghavo rāvaṇorasi
a rāvaṇo 'pi tataḥ kruddho rathastho rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c gadāmusalavarṣeṇa rāmaṃ pratyardayad raṇe
a devadānavayakṣāṇāṃ piśācoragarakṣasām
c paśyatāṃ tan mahad yuddhaṃ sarvarātram avartata
a naiva ratriṃ na divasaṃ na muhūrtaṃ na cakṣaṇam
c rāmarāvaṇayor yuddhaṃ virāmam upagacchati
a atha saṃsmārayām āsa rāghavaṃ mātalis tadā
c ajānann iva kiṃ vīra tvam enam anuvartase
a visṛjāsmai vadhāya tvam astraṃ paitāmahaṃ prabho
c vināśakālaḥ kathito yaḥ suraiḥ so 'dya vartate
a tataḥ saṃsmārito rāmas tena vākyena mātaleḥ
c jagrāha sa śaraṃ dīptaṃ niśvasantam ivoragam
a yam asmai prathamaṃ prādād agastyo bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
c brahmadattaṃ mahad bāṇam amoghaṃ yudhi vīryavān
a brahmaṇā nirmitaṃ pūrvam indrārtham amitaujasā
c dattaṃ surapateḥ pūrvaṃ trilokajayakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
a yasya vājeṣu pavanaḥ phale pāvakabhāskarau
c śarīram ākāśamayaṃ gaurave merumandarau
a jājvalyamānaṃ vapuṣā supuṅkhaṃ hemabhūṣitam
c tejasā sarvabhūtānāṃ kṛtaṃ bhāskaravarcasaṃ
a sadhūmam iva kālāgniṃ dīptam āśīviṣaṃ yathā
c rathanāgāśvavṛndānāṃ bhedanaṃ kṣiprakāriṇam
a dvārāṇāṃ parighāṇāṃ ca girīṇām api bhedanam
c nānārudhirasiktāṅgaṃ medodigdhaṃ sudāruṇam
a vajrasāraṃ mahānādaṃ nānāsamitidāruṇam
c sarvavitrāsanaṃ bhīmaṃ śvasantam iva pannagam
a kaṅkagṛdhrabalānāṃ ca gomāyugaṇarakṣasām
c nityaṃ bhakṣapradaṃ yuddhe yamarūpaṃ bhayāvaham
a nandanaṃ vānarendrāṇāṃ rakṣasām avasādanam
c vājitaṃ vividhair vājaiś cārucitrair garutmataḥ
a tam uttameṣuṃ lokānām ikṣvākubhayanāśanam
c dviṣatāṃ kīrtiharaṇaṃ praharṣakaram ātmanaḥ
a abhimantrya tato rāmas taṃ maheṣuṃ mahābalaḥ
c vedaproktena vidhinā saṃdadhe kārmuke balī
a sa rāvaṇāya saṃkruddho bhṛśam āyamya kārmukam
c cikṣepa param āyattas taṃ śaraṃ marmaghātinam
a sa vajra iva durdharṣo vajrabāhuvisarjitaḥ
c kṛtānta iva cāvāryo nyapatad rāvaṇorasi
a sa visṛṣṭo mahāvegaḥ śarīrāntakaraḥ śaraḥ
c bibheda hṛdayaṃ tasya rāvaṇasya durātmanaḥ
a rudhirāktaḥ sa vegena jīvitāntakaraḥ śaraḥ
c rāvaṇasya haran prāṇān viveśa dharaṇītalam
a sa śaro rāvaṇaṃ hatvā rudhirārdrakṛtacchaviḥ
c kṛtakarmā nibhṛtavat svatūṇīṃ punar āviśat
a tasya hastād dhatasyāśu kārmukaṃ tat sasāyakam
c nipapāta saha prāṇair bhraśyamānasya jīvitāt
a gatāsur bhīmavegas tu nairṛtendro mahādyutiḥ
c papāta syandanād bhūmau vṛtro vajrahato yathā
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā patitaṃ bhūmau hataśeṣā niśācarāḥ
c hatanāthā bhayatrastāḥ sarvataḥ saṃpradudruvuḥ
a nardantaś cābhipetus tān vānarā drumayodhinaḥ
c daśagrīvavadhaṃ dṛṣṭvā vijayaṃ rāghavasya ca
a arditā vānarair hṛṣṭair laṅkām abhyapatan bhayāt
c hatāśrayatvāt karuṇair bāṣpaprasravaṇair mukhaiḥ
a tato vineduḥ saṃhṛṣṭā vānarā jitakāśinaḥ
c vadanto rāghavajayaṃ rāvaṇasya ca taṃ vadham
a athāntarikṣe vyanadat saumyas tridaśadundubhiḥ
c divyagandhavahas tatra mārutaḥ susukho vavau
a nipapātāntarikṣāc ca puṣpavṛṣṭis tadā bhuvi
c kirantī rāghavarathaṃ duravāpā manoharāḥ
a rāghavas tava saṃyuktā gagane ca viśuśruve
c sādhu sādhv iti vāg agryā devatānāṃ mahātmanām
a āviveśa mahān harṣo devānāṃ cāraṇaiḥ saha
c rāvaṇe nihate raudre sarvalokabhayaṃkare
a tataḥ sakāmaṃ sugrīvam aṅgadaṃ ca mahābalam
c cakāra rāghavaḥ prīto hatvā rākṣasapuṃgavam
a tataḥ prajagmuḥ praśamaṃ marudgaṇā
diśaḥ prasedur vimalaṃ nabho 'bhavat
c mahī cakampe na ca mārutā vavuḥ
sthiraprabhaś cāpy abhavad divākaraḥ
a tatas tu sugrīvavibhīṣaṇādayaḥ
suhṛdviśeṣāḥ sahalakṣmaṇās tadā
c sametya hṛṣṭā vijayena rāghavaṃ
raṇe 'bhirāmaṃ vidhinābhyapūjayan
a sa tu nihataripuḥ sthirapratijñaḥ
svajanabalābhivṛto raṇe rarāja
c raghukulanṛpanandano mahaujās
tridaśagaṇair abhisaṃvṛto yathendraḥ
a rāvaṇaṃ nihataṃ śrutvā rāghaveṇa mahātmanā
c antaḥpurād viniṣpetū rākṣasyaḥ śokakarśitāḥ
a vāryamāṇāḥ subahuśo vṛṣṭantyaḥ kṣitipāṃsuṣu
c vimuktakeśyo duḥkhārtā gāvo vatsahatā yathā
a uttareṇa viniṣkramya dvāreṇa saha rākṣasaiḥ
c praviśyāyodhanaṃ ghoraṃ vicinvantyo hataṃ patim
a āryaputreti vādinyo hā nātheti ca sarvaśaḥ
c paripetuḥ kabandhāṅkāṃ mahīṃ śoṇitakardamām
a tā bāṣpaparipūrṇākṣyo bhartṛśokaparājitāḥ
c kareṇva iva nardantyo vinedur hatayūthapāḥ
a dadṛśus tā mahākāyaṃ mahāvīryaṃ mahādyutim
c rāvaṇaṃ nihataṃ bhūmau nīlāñjanacayopamam
a tāḥ patiṃ sahasā dṛṣṭvā śayānaṃ raṇapāṃsuṣu
c nipetus tasya gātreṣu chinnā vanalatā iva
a bahumānāt pariṣvajya kā cid enaṃ ruroda ha
c caraṇau kā cid āliṅgya kā cit kaṇṭhe 'valambya ca
a uddhṛtya ca bhujau kā cid bhūmau sma parivartate
c hatasya vadanaṃ dṛṣṭvā kā cin moham upāgamat
a kā cid aṅke śiraḥ kṛtvā ruroda mukham īkṣatī
c snāpayantī mukhaṃ bāṣpais tuṣārair iva paṅkajam
a evam ārtāḥ patiṃ dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇaṃ nihataṃ bhuvi
c cukruśur bahudhā śokād bhūyas tāḥ paryadevayan
a yena vitrāsitaḥ śakro yena vitrāsito yamaḥ
c yena vaiśravaṇo rājā puṣpakeṇa viyojitaḥ
a gandharvāṇām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca surāṇāṃ ca mahātmanām
c bhayaṃ yena mahad dattaṃ so 'yaṃ śete raṇe hataḥ
a asurebhyaḥ surebhyo vā pannagebhyo 'pi vā tathā
c na bhayaṃ yo vijānāti tasyedaṃ mānuṣād bhayam
a avadhyo devatānāṃ yas tathā dānavarakṣasām
c hataḥ so 'yaṃ raṇe śete mānuṣeṇa padātinā
a yo na śakyaḥ surair hantuṃ na yakṣair nāsurais tathā
c so 'yaṃ kaś cid ivāsattvo mṛtyuṃ martyena lambhitaḥ
a evaṃ vadantyo bahudhā rurudus tasya tāḥ striyaḥ
c bhūya eva ca duḥkhārtā vilepuś ca punaḥ punaḥ
a aśṛṇvatā tu suhṛdāṃ satataṃ hitavādinām
c etāḥ samam idānīṃ te vayam ātmā ca pātitāḥ
a bruvāṇo 'pi hitaṃ vākyam iṣṭo bhrātā vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c dhṛṣṭaṃ paruṣito mohāt tvayātmavadhakāṅkṣiṇā
a yadi niryātitā te syāt sītā rāmāya maithilī
c na naḥ syād vyasanaṃ ghoram idaṃ mūlaharaṃ mahat
a vṛttakāmo bhaved bhrātā rāmo mitrakulaṃ bhavet
c vayaṃ cāvidhavāḥ sarvāḥ sakāmā na ca śatravaḥ
a tvayā punar nṛśaṃsena sītāṃ saṃrundhatā balāt
c rākṣasā vayam ātmā ca trayaṃ tulaṃ nipātitam
a na kāmakāraḥ kāmaṃ vā tava rākṣasapuṃgava
c daivaṃ ceṣṭayate sarvaṃ hataṃ daivena hanyate
a vānarāṇāṃ vināśo 'yaṃ rākṣasānāṃ ca te raṇe
c tava caiva mahābāho daivayogād upāgataḥ
a naivārthena na kāmena vikrameṇa na cājñayā
c śakyā daivagatir loke nivartayitum udyatā
a vilepur evaṃ dīnās tā rākṣasādhipayoṣitaḥ
c kurarya iva duḥkhārtā bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇāḥ
a tāsāṃ vilapamānānāṃ tathā rākṣasayoṣitām
c jyeṣṭhā patnī priyā dīnā bhartāraṃ samudaikṣata
a daśagrīvaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmeṇācintyakarmaṇā
c patiṃ mandodarī tatra kṛpaṇā paryadevayat
a nanu nāma mahābāho tava vaiśravaṇānuja
c kruddhasya pramukhe sthātuṃ trasyaty api puraṃdaraḥ
a ṛṣayaś ca mahīdevā gandharvāś ca yaśasvinaḥ
c nanu nāma tavodvegāc cāraṇāś ca diśo gatāḥ
a sa tvaṃ mānuṣamātreṇa rāmeṇa yudhi nirjitaḥ
c na vyapatrapase rājan kim idaṃ rākṣasarṣabha
a kathaṃ trailokyam ākramya śriyā vīryeṇa cānvitam
c aviṣahyaṃ jaghāna tvaṃ mānuṣo vanagocaraḥ
a mānuṣāṇām aviṣaye carataḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
c vināśas tava rāmeṇa saṃyuge nopapadyate
a na caitat karma rāmasya śraddadhāmi camūmukhe
c sarvataḥ samupetasya tava tenābhimarśanam
a indriyāṇi purā jitvā jitaṃ tribhuvaṇaṃ tvayā
c smaradbhir iva tad vairam indriyair eva nirjitaḥ
a atha vā rāmarūpeṇa vāsavaḥ svayam āgataḥ
c māyāṃ tava vināśāya vidhāyāpratitarkitām
a yadaiva hi janasthāne rākṣasair bahubhir vṛtaḥ
c kharas tava hato bhrātā tadaivāsau na mānuṣaḥ
a yadaiva nagarīṃ laṅkāṃ duṣpraveṣāṃ surair api
c praviṣṭo hanumān vīryāt tadaiva vyathitā vayam
a kriyatām avirodhaś ca rāghaveṇeti yan mayā
c ucyamāno na gṛhṇāsi tasyeyaṃ vyuṣṭir āgatā
a akasmāc cābhikāmo 'si sītāṃ rākṣasapuṃgava
c aiśvaryasya vināśāya dehasya svajanasya ca
a arundhatyā viśiṣṭāṃ tāṃ rohiṇyāś cāpi durmate
c sītāṃ dharṣayatā mānyāṃ tvayā hy asadṛśaṃ kṛtam
a na kulena na rūpeṇa na dākṣiṇyena maithilī
c mayādhikā vā tulyā vā tvaṃ tu mohān na budhyase
a sarvathā sarvabhūtānāṃ nāsti mṛtyur alakṣaṇaḥ
c tava tāvad ayaṃ mṛtyur maithilīkṛtalakṣaṇaḥ
a maithilī saha rāmeṇa viśokā vihariṣyati
c alpapuṇyā tv ahaṃ ghore patitā śokasāgare
a kailāse mandare merau tathā caitrarathe vane
c devodyāneṣu sarveṣu vihṛtya sahitā tvayā
a vimānenānurūpeṇa yā yāmy atulayā śriyā
c paśyantī vividhān deśāṃs tāṃs tāṃś citrasragambarā
e bhraṃśitā kāmabhogebhyaḥ sāsmi vīravadhāt tava
a satyavāk sa mahābhāgo devaro me yad abravīt
c ayaṃ rākṣasamukhyānāṃ vināśaḥ paryupasthitaḥ
a kāmakrodhasamutthena vyasanena prasaṅginā
c tvayā kṛtam idaṃ sarvam anāthaṃ rakṣasāṃ kulam
a na hi tvaṃ śocitavyo me prakhyātabalapauruṣaḥ
c strīsvabhāvāt tu me buddhiḥ kāruṇye parivartate
a sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ ca tvaṃ gṛhītvā svāṃ gatiṃ gataḥ
c ātmānam anuśocāmi tvadviyogena duḥkhitām
a nīlajīmūtasaṃkāśaḥ pītāmbaraśubhāṅgadaḥ
c sarvagātrāṇi vikṣipya kiṃ śeṣe rudhirāplutaḥ
e prasupta iva śokārtāṃ kiṃ māṃ na pratibhāṣase
a mahāvīryasya dakṣasya saṃyugeṣv apalāyinaḥ
c yātudhānasya dauhitrīṃ kiṃ tvaṃ māṃ nābhyudīkṣase
a yena sūdayase śatrūn samare sūryavarcasā
c vajro vajradharasyeva so 'yaṃ te satatārcitaḥ
a raṇe śatrupraharaṇo hemajālapariṣkṛtaḥ
c parigho vyavakīrṇas te bāṇaiś chinnaḥ sahasradhā
a dhig astu hṛdayaṃ yasyā mamedaṃ na sahasradhā
c tvayi pañcatvam āpanne phalate śokapīḍitam
a etasminn antare rāmo vibhīṣaṇam uvāca ha
c saṃskāraḥ kriyatāṃ bhrātuḥ striyaś caitā nivartaya
a taṃ praśritas tato rāmaṃ śrutavākyo vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c vimṛśya buddhyā dharmajño dharmārthasahitaṃ vacaḥ
e rāmasyaivānuvṛttyartham uttaraṃ pratyabhāṣata
a tyaktadharmavrataṃ krūraṃ nṛśaṃsam anṛtaṃ tathā
c nāham arho 'smi saṃskartuṃ paradārābhimarśakam
a bhrātṛrūpo hi me śatrur eṣa sarvāhite rataḥ
c rāvaṇo nārhate pūjāṃ pūjyo 'pi gurugauravāt
a nṛśaṃsa iti māṃ rāma vakṣyanti manujā bhuvi
c śrutvā tasya guṇān sarve vakṣyanti sukṛtaṃ punaḥ
a tac chrutvā paramaprīto rāmo dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c vibhīṣaṇam uvācedaṃ vākyajño vākyakovidam
a tavāpi me priyaṃ kāryaṃ tvatprabhavāc ca me jitam
c avaśyaṃ tu kṣamaṃ vācyo mayā tvaṃ rākṣaseśvara
a adharmānṛtasaṃyuktaḥ kāmam eṣa niśācaraḥ
c tejasvī balavāñ śūraḥ saṃgrāmeṣu ca nityaśaḥ
a śatakratumukhair devaiḥ śrūyate na parājitaḥ
c mahātmā balasaṃpanno rāvaṇo lokarāvaṇaḥ
a maraṇāntāni vairāṇi nirvṛttaṃ naḥ prayojanam
c kriyatām asya saṃskāro mamāpy eṣa yathā tava
a tvatsakāśān mahābāho saṃskāraṃ vidhipūrvakam
c kṣipram arhati dharmajña tvaṃ yaśobhāg bhaviṣyasi
a rāghavasya vacaḥ śrutvā tvaramāṇo vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c saṃskāreṇānurūpeṇa yojayām āsa rāvaṇam
a sa dadau pāvakaṃ tasya vidhiyuktaṃ vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c tāḥ striyo 'nunayām āsa sāntvam uktvā punaḥ punaḥ
a praviṣṭāsu ca sarvāsu rākṣasīṣu vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c rāmapārśvam upāgamya tadātiṣṭhad vinītavat
a rāmo 'pi saha sainyena sasugrīvaḥ salakṣmaṇaḥ
c harṣaṃ lebhe ripuṃ hatvā yathā vṛtraṃ śatakratuḥ
a te rāvaṇavadhaṃ dṛṣṭvā devagandharvadānavāḥ
c jagmus tais tair vimānaiḥ svaiḥ kathayantaḥ śubhāḥ kathāḥ
a rāvaṇasya vadhaṃ ghoraṃ rāghavasya parākramam
c suyuddhaṃ vānarāṇāṃ ca sugrīvasay ca mantritam
a anurāgaṃ ca vīryaṃ ca saumitrer lakṣmaṇasya ca
c kathayanto mahābhāgā jagmur hṛṣṭā yathāgatam
a rāghavas tu rathaṃ divyam indradattaṃ śikhiprabham
c anujñāya mahābhāgo mātaliṃ pratyapūjayat
a rāghaveṇābhyanujñāto mātaliḥ śakrasārathiḥ
c divyaṃ taṃ ratham āsthāya divam evāruroha saḥ
a tasmiṃs tu divam ārūḍhe surasārathisattame
c rāghavaḥ paramaprītaḥ sugrīvaṃ pariṣasvaje
a pariṣvajya ca sugrīvaṃ lakṣmaṇenābhivāditaḥ
c pūjyamāno hariśreṣṭhair ājagāma balālayam
a abravīc ca tadā rāmaḥ samīpaparivartinam
c saumitriṃ sattvasaṃpannaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ dīptatejasaṃ
a vibhīṣaṇam imaṃ saumya laṅkāyām abhiṣecaya
c anuraktaṃ ca bhaktaṃ ca mama caivopakāriṇam
a eṣa me paramaḥ kāmo yad imaṃ rāvaṇānujam
c laṅkāyāṃ saumya paśyeyam abhiṣiktaṃ vibhīṣaṇam
a evam uktas tu saumitrī rāghaveṇa mahātmanā
c tathety uktvā tu saṃhṛṣṭaḥ sauvarṇaṃ ghaṭam ādade
a ghaṭena tena saumitrir abhyaṣiñcad vibhīṣaṇam
c laṅkāyāṃ rakṣasāṃ madhye rājānaṃ rāmaśāsanāt
a abhyaṣiñcat sa dharmātmā śuddhātmānaṃ vibhīṣaṇam
c tasyāmātyā jahṛṣire bhaktā ye cāsya rākṣasāḥ
a dṛṣṭvābhiṣiktaṃ laṅkāyāṃ rākṣasendraṃ vibhīṣaṇam
c rāghavaḥ paramāṃ prītiṃ jagāma sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
a sa tad rājyaṃ mahat prāpya rāmadattaṃ vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c prakṛtīḥ sāntvayitvā ca tato rāmam upāgamat
a akṣatān modakāṃl lājān divyāḥ sumanasas tathā
c ājahrur atha saṃhṛṣṭāḥ paurās tasmai niśācarāḥ
a sa tān gṛhītvā durdharṣo rāghavāya nyavedayat
c maṅgalyaṃ maṅgalaṃ sarvaṃ lakṣmaṇāya ca vīryavān
a kṛtakāryaṃ samṛddhārthaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmo vibhīṣaṇam
c pratijagrāha tat sarvaṃ tasyaiva priyakāmyayā
a tataḥ śailopamaṃ vīraṃ prāñjaliṃ pārśvataḥ sthitam
c abravīd rāghavo vākyaṃ hanūmantaṃ plavaṃgamam
a anumānya mahārājam imaṃ saumya vibhīṣaṇam
c praviśya rāvaṇagṛhaṃ vinayenopasṛtya ca
a vaidehyā māṃ kuśalinaṃ sasugrīvaṃ salakṣmaṇam
c ācakṣva jayatāṃ śreṣṭha rāvaṇaṃ ca mayā hatam
a priyam etad udāhṛtya maithilyās tvaṃ harīśvara
c pratigṛhya ca saṃdeśam upāvartitum arhasi
a iti pratisamādiṣṭo hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
c praviveśa purīṃ laṅkāṃ pūjyamāno niśācaraiḥ
a praviśya tu mahātejā rāvaṇasya niveśanam
c dadarśa śaśinā hīnāṃ sātaṅkām iva rohiṇīm
a nibhṛtaḥ praṇataḥ prahvaḥ so 'bhigamyābhivādya ca
c rāmasya vacanaṃ sarvam ākhyātum upacakrame
a vaidehi kuśalī rāmaḥ sasugrīvaḥ salakṣmaṇaḥ
c kuśalaṃ cāha siddhārtho hataśatrur ariṃdamaḥ
a vibhīṣaṇasahāyena rāmeṇa haribhiḥ saha
c nihato rāvaṇo devi lakṣmaṇasya nayena ca
a pṛṣṭvā ca kuśalaṃ rāmo vīras tvāṃ raghunandanaḥ
c abravīt paramaprītaḥ kṛtārthenāntarātmanā
a priyam ākhyāmi te devi tvāṃ tu bhayaḥ sabhājaye
c diṣṭyā jīvasi dharmajñe jayena mama saṃyuge
a labdho no vijayaḥ sīte svasthā bhava gatavyathā
c rāvaṇaḥ sa hataḥ śatrur laṅkā ceyaṃ vaśe sthitā
a mayā hy alabdhanidreṇa dhṛtena tava nirjaye
c pratijñaiṣā vinistīrṇā baddhvā setuṃ mahodadhau
a saṃbhramaś ca na kartavyo vartantyā rāvaṇālaye
c vibhīṣaṇa vidheyaṃ hi laṅkaiśvaryam idaṃ kṛtam
a tad āśvasihi viśvastā svagṛhe parivartase
c ayaṃ cābhyeti saṃhṛṣṭas tvaddarśanasamutsukaḥ
a evam uktā samutpatya sītā śaśinibhānanā
c praharṣeṇāvaruddhā sā vyājahāra na kiṃ cana
a abravīc ca hariśreṣṭhaḥ sītām apratijalpatīm
c kiṃ tvaṃ cintayase devi kiṃ ca māṃ nābhibhāṣase
a evam uktā hanumatā sītā dharme vyavasthitā
c abravīt paramapritā harṣagadgadayā girā
a priyam etad upaśrutya bhartur vijayasaṃśritam
c praharṣavaśam āpannā nirvākyāsmi kṣaṇāntaram
a na hi paśyāmi sadṛśaṃ cintayantī plavaṃgama
c matpriyākhyānakasyeha tava pratyabhinandanam
a na ca paśyāmi tat saumya pṛthivyām api vānara
c sadṛśaṃ matpriyākhyāne tava dātuṃ bhavet samam
a hiraṇyaṃ vā suvarṇaṃ vā ratnāni vividhāni ca
c rājyaṃ vā triṣu lokeṣu naitad arhati bhāṣitum
a evam uktas tu vaidehyā pratyuvāca plavaṃgamaḥ
c pragṛhītāñjalir vākyaṃ sītāyāḥ pramukhe sthitaḥ
a bhartuḥ priyahite yukte bhartur vijayakāṅkṣiṇi
c snigdham evaṃvidhaṃ vākyaṃ tvam evārhasi bhāṣitum
a tavaitad vacanaṃ saumye sāravat snigdham eva ca
c ratnaughād vividhāc cāpi devarājyād viśiṣyate
a arthataś ca mayā prāptā devarājyādayo guṇāḥ
c hataśatruṃ vijayinaṃ rāmaṃ paśyāmi yat sthitam
a imās tu khalu rākṣasyo yadi tvam anumanyase
c hantum icchāmy ahaṃ sarvā yābhis tvaṃ tarjitā purā
a kliśyantīṃ patidevāṃ tvām aśokavanikāṃ gatām
c ghorarūpasamācārāḥ krūrāḥ krūratarekṣaṇāḥ
a rākṣasyo dāruṇakathā varam etaṃ prayaccha me
c icchāmi vividhair ghātair hantum etāḥ sudāruṇāḥ
a muṣṭibhiḥ pāṇibhiś caiva caraṇaiś caiva śobhane
c ghorair jānuprahāraiś ca daśanānāṃ ca pātanaiḥ
a bhakṣaṇaiḥ karṇanāsānāṃ keśānāṃ luñcanais tathā
c bhṛśaṃ śuṣkamukhībhiś ca dāruṇair laṅghanair hataiḥ
a evaṃprakārair bahubhir viprakārair yaśasvini
c hantum icchāmy ahaṃ devi tavemāḥ kṛtakilbiṣāḥ
a evam uktā mahumatā vaidehī janakātmajā
c uvāca dharmasahitaṃ hanūmantaṃ yaśasvinī
a rājasaṃśrayavaśyānāṃ kurvatīnāṃ parājñayā
c vidheyānāṃ ca dāsīnāṃ kaḥ kupyed vānarottama
a bhāgyavaiṣamya yogena purā duścaritena ca
c mayaitet prāpyate sarvaṃ svakṛtaṃ hy upabhujyate
a prāptavyaṃ tu daśā yogān mayaitad iti niścitam
c dāsīnāṃ rāvaṇasyāhaṃ marṣayāmīha durbalā
a ājñaptā rāvaṇenaitā rākṣasyo mām atarjayan
c hate tasmin na kuryur hi tarjanaṃ vānarottama
a ayaṃ vyāghrasamīpe tu purāṇo dharmasaṃhitaḥ
c ṛkṣeṇa gītaḥ śloko me taṃ nibodha plavaṃgama
a na paraḥ pāpam ādatte pareṣāṃ pāpakarmaṇām
c samayo rakṣitavyas tu santaś cāritrabhūṣaṇāḥ
a pāpānāṃ vā śubhānāṃ vā vadhārhāṇāṃ plavaṃgama
c kāryaṃ kāruṇyam āryeṇa na kaś cin nāparādhyati
a lokahiṃsāvihārāṇāṃ rakṣasāṃ kāmarūpiṇam
c kurvatām api pāpāni naiva kāryam aśobhanam
a evam uktas tu hanumān sītayā vākyakovidaḥ
c pratyuvāca tataḥ sītāṃ rāmapatnīṃ yaśasvinīm
a yuktā rāmasya bhavatī dharmapatnī yaśasvinī
c pratisaṃdiśa māṃ devi gamiṣye yatra rāghavaḥ
a evam uktā hanumatā vaidehī janakātmajā
c abravīd draṣṭum icchāmi bhartāraṃ vānarottama
a tasyās tadvacanaṃ śrutvā hanumān pavanātmajaḥ
c harṣayan maithilīṃ vākyam uvācedaṃ mahādyutiḥ
a pūrṇacandrānanaṃ rāmaṃ drakṣyasy ārye salakṣmaṇam
c sthiramitraṃ hatāmitraṃ śacīva tridaśeśvaram
a tām evam uktvā rājantīṃ sītāṃ sākṣād iva śriyam
c ājagāma mahāvego hanūmān yatra rāghavaḥ
a sa uvāca mahāprajñam abhigamya plavaṃgamaḥ
c rāmaṃ vacanam arthajño varaṃ sarvadhanuṣmatām
a yannimitto 'yam ārambhaḥ karmaṇāṃ ca phalodayaḥ
c tāṃ devīṃ śokasaṃtaptāṃ maithilīṃ draṣṭum arhasi
a sā hi śokasamāviṣṭā bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇā
c maithilī vijayaṃ śrutvā tava harṣam upāgamat
a pūrvakāt pratyayāc cāham ukto viśvastayā tayā
c bhartāraṃ draṣṭum icchāmi kṛtārthaṃ sahalakṣmaṇam
a evam ukto hanumatā rāmo dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c agacchat sahasā dhyānam āsīd bāṣpapariplutaḥ
a dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca niśvasya medinīm avalokayan
c uvāca meghasaṃkāśaṃ vibhīṣaṇam upasthitam
a divyāṅgarāgāṃ vaidehīṃ divyābharaṇabhūṣitām
c iha sītāṃ śiraḥsnātām upasthāpaya māciram
a evam uktas tu rāmeṇa tvaramāṇo vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c praviśyāntaḥpuraṃ sītāṃ strībhiḥ svābhir acodayat
a divyāṅgarāgā vaidehī divyābharaṇabhūṣitā
c yānam āroha bhadraṃ te bhartā tvāṃ draṣṭum icchati
a evam uktā tu vaidehī pratyuvāca vibhīṣaṇam
c asnātā draṣṭum icchāmi bhartāraṃ rākṣasādhipa
a tasyās tadvacanaṃ śrutvā pratyuvāca vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c yathāhaṃ rāmo bhartā te tat tathā kartum arhasi
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā maithilī bhrātṛdevatā
c bhartṛbhaktivratā sādhvī tatheti pratyabhāṣata
a tataḥ sītāṃ śiraḥsnātāṃ yuvatībhir alaṃkṛtām
c mahārhābharaṇopetāṃ mahārhāmbaradhāriṇīm
a āropya śibikāṃ dīptāṃ parārdhyāmbarasaṃvṛtām
c rakṣobhir bahubhir guptām ājahāra vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a so 'bhigamya mahātmānaṃ jñātvābhidhyānam āsthitam
c praṇataś ca prahṛṣṭaś ca prāptāṃ sītāṃ nyavedayat
a tām āgatām upaśrutya rakṣogṛhaciroṣitām
c harṣo dainyaṃ ca roṣaś ca trayaṃ rāghavam āviśat
a tataḥ pārśvagataṃ dṛṣṭvā savimarśaṃ vicārayan
c vibhīṣaṇam idaṃ vākyam ahṛṣṭo rāghavo 'bravīt
a rākṣasādhipate saumya nityaṃ madvijaye rata
c vaidehī saṃnikarṣaṃ me śīghraṃ samupagacchatu
a sa tadvacanam ājñāya rāghavasya vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c tūrṇam utsāraṇe yatnaṃ kārayām āsa sarvataḥ
a kañcukoṣṇīṣiṇas tatra vetrajharjharapāṇayaḥ
c utsārayantaḥ puruṣāḥ samantāt paricakramuḥ
a ṛkṣāṇāṃ vānarāṇāṃ ca rākṣasānāṃ ca sarvataḥ
c vṛndāny utsāryamāṇāni dūram utsasṛjus tataḥ
a teṣām utsāryamāṇānāṃ sarveṣāṃ dhvanir utthitaḥ
c vāyunodvartamānasya sāgarasyeva nisvanaḥ
a utsāryamāṇāṃs tān dṛṣṭvā samantāj jātasaṃbhramān
c dākṣiṇyāt tadamarṣāc ca vārayām āsa rāghavaḥ
a saṃrabdhaś cābravīd rāmaś cakṣuṣā pradahann iva
c vibhīṣaṇaṃ mahāprājñaṃ sopālambham idaṃ vacaḥ
a kimarthaṃ mām anādṛtya kṛśyate 'yaṃ tvayā janaḥ
c nivartayainam udyogaṃ jano 'yaṃ svajano mama
a na gṛhāṇi na vastrāṇi na prākārās tiraskriyāḥ
c nedṛśā rājasatkārā vṛttam āvaraṇaṃ striyaḥ
a vyasaneṣu na kṛcchreṣu na yuddhe na svayaṃ vare
c na kratau no vivāhe ca darśanaṃ duṣyate striyaḥ
a saiṣā yuddhagatā caiva kṛcchre mahati ca sthitā
c darśane 'syā na doṣaḥ syān matsamīpe viśeṣataḥ
a tad ānaya samīpaṃ me śīghram enāṃ vibhīṣaṇa
c sītā paśyatu mām eṣā suhṛdgaṇavṛtaṃ sthitam
a evam uktas tu rāmeṇa savimarśo vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c rāmasyopānayat sītāṃ saṃnikarṣaṃ vinītavat
a tato lakṣmaṇasugrīvau hanūmāṃś ca plavaṃgamaḥ
c niśamya vākyaṃ rāmasya babhūvur vyathitā bhṛśam
a kalatranirapekṣaiś ca iṅgitair asya dāruṇaiḥ
c aprītam iva sītāyāṃ tarkayanti sma rāghavam
a lajjayā tv avalīyantī sveṣu gātreṣu maithilī
c vibhīṣaṇenānugatā bhartāraṃ sābhyavartata
a sā vastrasaṃruddhamukhī lajjayā janasaṃsadi
c rurodāsādya bhartāram āryaputreti bhāṣiṇī
a vismayāc ca praharṣāc ca snehāc ca paridevatā
c udaikṣata mukhaṃ bhartuḥ saumyaṃ saumyatarānanā
a atha samapanudan manaḥklamaṃ sā
suciram adṛṣṭam udīkṣya vai priyasya
c vadanam uditapūrṇacandrakāntaṃ
vimalaśaśāṅkanibhānanā tadāsīt
a tāṃ tu pārśve sthitāṃ prahvāṃ rāmaḥ saṃprekṣya maithilīm
c hṛdayāntargatakrodho vyāhartum upacakrame
a eṣāsi nirjitā bhadre śatruṃ jitvā mayā raṇe
c pauruṣād yad anuṣṭheyaṃ tad etad upapāditam
a gato 'smy antam amarṣasya dharṣaṇā saṃpramārjitā
c avamānaś ca śatruś ca mayā yugapad uddhṛtau
a adya me pauruṣaṃ dṛṣṭam adya me saphalaḥ śramaḥ
c adya tīrṇapratijñatvāt prabhavāmīha cātmanaḥ
a yā tvaṃ virahitā nītā calacittena rakṣasā
c daivasaṃpādito doṣo mānuṣeṇa mayā jitaḥ
a saṃprāptam avamānaṃ yas tejasā na pramārjati
c kas tasya puruṣārtho 'sti puruṣasyālpatejasaḥ
a laṅghanaṃ ca samudrasya laṅkāyāś cāvamardanam
c saphalaṃ tasya tac chlāghyam adya karma hanūmataḥ
a yuddhe vikramataś caiva hitaṃ mantrayataś ca me
c sugrīvasya sasainyasya saphalo 'dya pariśramaḥ
a nirguṇaṃ bhrātaraṃ tyaktvā yo māṃ svayam upasthitaḥ
c vibhīṣaṇasya bhaktasya saphalo 'dya pariśramaḥ
a ity evaṃ bruvatas tasya sītā rāmasya tadvacaḥ
c mṛgīvotphullanayanā babhūvāśrupariplutā
a paśyatas tāṃ tu rāmasya bhūyaḥ krodho 'bhyavartata
c prabhūtājyāvasiktasya pāvakasyeva dīpyataḥ
a sa baddhvā bhrukuṭiṃ vaktre tiryakprekṣitalocanaḥ
c abravīt paruṣaṃ sītāṃ madhye vānararakṣasām
a yat kartavyaṃ manuṣyeṇa dharṣaṇāṃ parimārjatā
c tat kṛtaṃ sakalaṃ sīte śatruhastād amarṣaṇāt
a nirjitā jīvalokasya tapasā bhāvitātmanā
c agastyena durādharṣā muninā dakṣiṇeva dik
a viditaś cāstu bhadraṃ te yo 'yaṃ raṇapariśramaḥ
c sa tīrṇaḥ suhṛdāṃ vīryān na tvadarthaṃ mayā kṛtaḥ
a rakṣatā tu mayā vṛttam apavādaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
c prakhyātasyātmavaṃśasya nyaṅgaṃ ca parimārjatā
a prāptacāritrasaṃdehā mama pratimukhe sthitā
c dīpo netrāturasyeva pratikūlāsi me dṛḍham
a tad gaccha hy abhyanujñātā yateṣṭaṃ janakātmaje
c etā daśa diśo bhadre kāryam asti na me tvayā
a kaḥ pumān hi kule jātaḥ striyaṃ paragṛhoṣitām
c tejasvi punar ādadyāt suhṛllekhena cetasā
a rāvaṇāṅkaparibhraṣṭāṃ dṛṣṭāṃ duṣṭena cakṣuṣā
c kathaṃ tvāṃ punarādadyāṃ kulaṃ vyapadiśan mahat
a tadarthaṃ nirjitā me tvaṃ yaśaḥ pratyāhṛtaṃ mayā
c nāsti me tvayy abhiṣvaṅgo yatheṣṭaṃ gamyatām itaḥ
a iti pravyāhṛtaṃ bhadre mayaitat kṛtabuddhinā
c lakṣmaṇe bharate vā tvaṃ kuru buddhiṃ yathāsukham
a sugrīve vānarendre vā rākṣasendre vibhīṣaṇe
c niveśaya manaḥ śīte yathā vā sukham ātmanaḥ
a na hi tvāṃ rāvaṇo dṛṣṭvā divyarūpāṃ manoramām
c marṣayate ciraṃ sīte svagṛhe parivartinīm
a tataḥ priyārhaśvaraṇā tad apriyaṃ
priyād upaśrutya cirasya maithilī
c mumoca bāṣpaṃ subhṛśaṃ pravepitā
gajendrahastābhihateva vallarī
a evam uktā tu vaidehī paruṣaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c rāghaveṇa saroṣeṇa bhṛśaṃ pravyathitābhavat
a sā tad aśrutapūrvaṃ hi jane mahati maithilī
c śrutvā bhartṛvaco rūkṣaṃ lajjayā vrīḍitābhavat
a praviśantīva gātrāṇi svāny eva janakātmajā
c vākśalyais taiḥ saśalyeva bhṛśam aśrūṇy avartayat
a tato bāṣpaparikliṣṭaṃ pramārjantī svam ānanam
c śanair gadgadayā vācā bhartāram idam abravīt
a kiṃ mām asadṛśaṃ vākyam īdṛśaṃ śrotradāruṇam
c rūkṣaṃ śrāvayase vīra prākṛtaḥ prākṛtām iva
a na tathāsmi mahābāho yathā tvam avagacchasi
c pratyayaṃ gaccha me svena cāritreṇaiva te śape
a pṛthak strīṇāṃ pracāreṇa jātiṃ tvaṃ pariśaṅkase
c parityajemāṃ śaṅkāṃ tu yadi te 'haṃ parīkṣitā
a yady ahaṃ gātrasaṃsparśaṃ gatāsmi vivaśā prabho
c kāmakāro na me tatra daivaṃ tatrāparādhyati
a madadhīnaṃ tu yat tan me hṛdayaṃ tvayi vartate
c parādhīneṣu gātreṣu kiṃ kariṣyāmy anīśvarā
a sahasaṃvṛddhabhāvāc ca saṃsargeṇa ca mānada
c yady ahaṃ te na vijñātā hatā tenāsmi śāśvatam
a preṣitas te yadā vīro hanūmān avalokakaḥ
c laṅkāsthāhaṃ tvayā vīra kiṃ tadā na visarjitā
a pratyakṣaṃ vānarendrasya tvadvākyasamanantaram
c tvayā saṃtyaktayā vīra tyaktaṃ syāj jīvitaṃ mayā
a na vṛthā te śramo 'yaṃ syāt saṃśaye nyasya jīvitam
c suhṛjjanaparikleśo na cāyaṃ niṣphalas tava
a tvayā tu naraśārdūla krodham evānuvartatā
c laghuneva manuṣyeṇa strītvam eva puraskṛtam
a apadeśena janakān notpattir vasudhātalāt
c mama vṛttaṃ ca vṛttajña bahu te na puraskṛtam
a na pramāṇīkṛtaḥ pāṇir bālye bālena pīḍitaḥ
c mama bhaktiś ca śīlaṃ ca sarvaṃ te pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtam
a evaṃ bruvāṇā rudatī bāṣpagadgadabhāṣiṇī
c abravīl lakṣmaṇaṃ sītā dīnaṃ dhyānaparaṃ sthitam
a citāṃ me kuru saumitre vyasanasyāsya bheṣajam
c mithyāpavādopahatā nāhaṃ jīvitum utsahe
a aprītasya guṇair bhartus tyaktayā janasaṃsadi
c yā kṣamā me gatir gantuṃ pravekṣye havyavāhanam
a evam uktas tu vaidehyā lakṣmaṇaḥ paravīrahā
c amarṣavaśam āpanno rāghavānanam aikṣata
a sa vijñāya manaśchandaṃ rāmasyākārasūcitam
c citāṃ cakāra saumitrir mate rāmasya vīryavān
a adhomukhaṃ tato rāmaṃ śanaiḥ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam
c upāsarpata vaidehī dīpyamānaṃ hutāśanam
a praṇamya devatābhyaś ca brāhmaṇebhyaś ca maithilī
c baddhāñjalipuṭā cedam uvācāgnisamīpataḥ
a yathā me hṛdayaṃ nityaṃ nāpasarpati rāghavāt
c tathā lokasya sākṣī māṃ sarvataḥ pātu pāvakaḥ
a evam uktvā tu vaidehī parikramya hutāśanam
c viveśa jvalanaṃ dīptaṃ niḥsaṅgenāntarātmanā
a janaḥ sa sumahāṃs tatra bālavṛddhasamākulaḥ
c dadarśa maithilīṃ tatra praviśantīṃ hutāśanam
a tasyām agniṃ viśantyāṃ tu hāheti vipulaḥ svanaḥ
c rakṣasāṃ vānarāṇāṃ ca saṃbabhūvādbhutopamaḥ
a tato vaiśravaṇo rājā yamaś cāmitrakarśanaḥ
c sahasrākṣo mahendraś ca varuṇaś ca paraṃtapaḥ
a ṣaḍardhanayanaḥ śrīmān mahādevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ
c kartā sarvasya lokasya brahmā brahmavidāṃ varaḥ
a ete sarve samāgamya vimānaiḥ sūryasaṃnibhaiḥ
c āgamya nagarīṃ laṅkām abhijagmuś ca rāghavam
a tataḥ sahastābharaṇān pragṛhya vipulān bhujān
c abruvaṃs tridaśaśreṣṭhāḥ prāñjaliṃ rāghavaṃ sthitam
a kartā sarvasya lokasya śreṣṭho jñānavatāṃ varaḥ
c upekṣase kathaṃ sītāṃ patantīṃ havyavāhane
e kathaṃ devagaṇaśreṣṭham ātmānaṃ nāvabudhyase
a ṛtadhāmā vasuḥ pūrvaṃ vasūnāṃ ca prajāpatiḥ
c tvaṃ trayāṇāṃ hi lokānām ādikartā svayaṃprabhuḥ
a rudrāṇām aṣṭamo rudraḥ sādhyānām api pañcamaḥ
c aśvinau cāpi te karṇau candrasūryau ca cakṣuṣī
a ante cādau ca lokānāṃ dṛśyase tvaṃ paraṃtapa
c upekṣase ca vaidehīṃ mānuṣaḥ prākṛto yathā
a ity ukto lokapālais taiḥ svāmī lokasya rāghavaḥ
c abravīt tridaśaśreṣṭhān rāmo dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
a ātmānaṃ mānuṣaṃ manye rāmaṃ daśarathātmajam
c yo 'haṃ yasya yataś cāhaṃ bhagavāṃs tad bravītu me
a iti bruvāṇaṃ kākutsthaṃ brahmā brahmavidāṃ varaḥ
c abravīc chṛṇu me rāma satyaṃ satyaparākrama
a bhavān nārāyaṇo devaḥ śrīmāṃś cakrāyudho vibhuḥ
c ekaśṛṅgo varāhas tvaṃ bhūtabhavyasapatnajit
a akṣaraṃ brahmasatyaṃ ca madhye cānte ca rāghava
c lokānāṃ tvaṃ paro dharmo viṣvaksenaś caturbhujaḥ
a śārṅgadhanvā hṛṣīkeśaḥ puruṣaḥ puruṣottamaḥ
c ajitaḥ khaḍgadhṛg viṣṇuḥ kṛṣṇaś caiva bṛhadbalaḥ
a senānīr grāmaṇīś ca tvaṃ buddhiḥ sattaṃ kṣamā damaḥ
c prabhavaś cāpyayaś ca tvam upendro madhusūdanaḥ
a indrakarmā mahendras tvaṃ padmanābho raṇāntakṛt
c śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ ca tvām āhur divyā maharṣayaḥ
a sahasraśṛṅgo vedātmā śatajihvo maharṣabhaḥ
c tvaṃ yajñas tvaṃ vaṣaṭkāras tvam oṃkāraḥ paraṃtapa
a prabhavaṃ nidhanaṃ vā te na viduḥ ko bhavān iti
c dṛśyase sarvabhūteṣu brāhmaṇeṣu ca goṣu ca
a dikṣu sarvāsu gagane parvateṣu vaneṣu ca
c sahasracaraṇaḥ śrīmāñ śataśīrṣaḥ sahasradhṛk
a tvaṃ dhārayasi bhūtāni vasudhāṃ ca saparvatām
c ante pṛthivyāḥ salile dṛśyase tvaṃ mahoragaḥ
a trīṃl lokān dhārayan rāma devagandharvadānavān
c ahaṃ te hṛdayaṃ rāma jihvā devī sarasvatī
a devā gātreṣu lomāni nirmitā brahmaṇā prabho
c nimeṣas te 'bhavad rātrir unmeṣas te 'bhavad divā
a saṃskārās te 'bhavan vedā na tad asti tvayā vinā
c jagat sarvaṃ śarīraṃ te sthairyamṃ te vasudhātalam
a agniḥ kopaḥ prasādas te somaḥ śrīvatsalakṣaṇa
c tvayā lokās trayaḥ krāntāḥ purāṇe vikramais tribhiḥ
a mahendraś ca kṛto rājā baliṃ baddhvā mahāsuram
c sītā lakṣmīr bhavān viṣṇur devaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ prajāpatiḥ
a vadhārthaṃ rāvaṇasyeha praviṣṭo mānuṣīṃ tanum
c tad idaṃ naḥ kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ tvayā dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
a nihato rāvaṇo rāma prahṛṣṭo divam ākrama
c amoghaṃ balavīryaṃ te amoghas te parākramaḥ
a amoghās te bhaviṣyanti bhaktimantaś ca ye narāḥ
c ye tvāṃ devaṃ dhruvaṃ bhaktāḥ purāṇaṃ puruṣottamam
a ye narāḥ kīrtayiṣyanti nāsti teṣāṃ parābhavaḥ
a etac chrutvā śubhaṃ vākyaṃ pitāmahasamīritam
c aṅkenādāya vaidehīm utpapāta vibhāvasuḥ
a taruṇādityasaṃkāśāṃ taptakāñcanabhūṣaṇām
c raktāmbaradharāṃ bālāṃ nīlakuñcitamūrdhajām
a akliṣṭamālyābharaṇāṃ tathā rūpāṃ manasvinīm
c dadau rāmāya vaidehīm aṅke kṛtvā vibhāvasuḥ
a abravīc ca tadā rāmaṃ sākṣī lokasya pāvakaḥ
c eṣā te rāma vaidehī pāpam asyā na vidyate
a naiva vācā na manasā nānudhyānān na cakṣuṣā
c suvṛttā vṛttaśauṇḍīrā na tvām aticacāra ha
a rāvaṇenāpanītaiṣā vīryotsiktena rakṣasā
c tvayā virahitā dīnā vivaśā nirjanād vanāt
a ruddhā cāntaḥpure guptā tvakcittā tvatparāyaṇā
c rakṣitā rākṣasī saṃghair vikṛtair ghoradarśanaiḥ
a pralobhyamānā vividhaṃ bhartsyamānā ca maithilī
c nācintayata tad rakṣas tvadgatenāntarātmanā
a viśuddhabhāvāṃ niṣpāpāṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva rāghava
c na kiṃ cid abhidhātavyam aham ājñāpayāmi te
a evam ukto mahātejā dhṛtimān dṛḍhavikramaḥ
c abravīt tridaśaśreṣṭhaṃ rāmo dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
a avaśyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu sītā pāvanam arhati
c dīrghakāloṣitā ceyaṃ rāvaṇāntaḥpure śubhā
a bāliśaḥ khalu kāmātmā rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ
c iti vakṣyanti māṃ santo jānakīm aviśodhya hi
a ananyahṛdayāṃ bhaktāṃ maccittaparirakṣaṇīm
c aham apy avagacchāmi maithilīṃ janakātmajām
a pratyayārthaṃ tu lokānāṃ trayāṇāṃ satyasaṃśrayaḥ
c upekṣe cāpi vaidehīṃ praviśantīṃ hutāśanam
a imām api viśālākṣīṃ rakṣitāṃ svena tejasā
c rāvaṇo nātivarteta velām iva mahodadhiḥ
a na hi śaktaḥ sa duṣṭātmā manasāpi hi maithilīm
c pradharṣayitum aprāptāṃ dīptām agniśikhām iva
a neyam arhati caiśvaryaṃ rāvaṇāntaḥpure śubhā
c ananyā hi mayā sītāṃ bhāskareṇa prabhā yathā
a viśuddhā triṣu lokeṣu maithilī janakātmajā
c na hi hātum iyaṃ śakyā kīrtir ātmavatā yathā
a avaśyaṃ ca mayā kāryaṃ sarveṣāṃ vo vaco hitam
c snigdhānāṃ lokamānyānām evaṃ ca bruvatāṃ hitam
a itīdam uktvā vacanaṃ mahābalaiḥ
praśasyamānaḥ svakṛtena karmaṇā
c sametya rāmaḥ priyayā mahābalaḥ
sukhaṃ sukhārho 'nubabhūva rāghavaḥ
a etac chrutvā śubhaṃ vākyaṃ rāghaveṇa subhāṣitam
c idaṃ śubhataraṃ vākyaṃ vyājahāra maheśvaraḥ
a puṣkarākṣa mahābāho mahāvakṣaḥ paraṃtapa
c diṣṭyā kṛtam idaṃ karma tvayā śastrabhṛtāṃ vara
a diṣṭyā sarvasya lokasya pravṛddhaṃ dāruṇaṃ tamaḥ
c apāvṛttaṃ tvayā saṃkhye rāma rāvaṇajaṃ bhayam
a āśvāsya bharataṃ dīnaṃ kausalyāṃ ca yaśasvinīm
c kaikeyīṃ ca sumitrāṃ ca dṛṣṭvā lakṣmaṇamātaram
a prāpya rājyam ayodhyāyāṃ nandayitvā suhṛjjanam
c ikṣvākūṇāṃ kule vaṃśaṃ sthāpayitvā mahābala
a iṣṭvā turagamedhena prāpya cānuttamaṃ yaśaḥ
c brāhmaṇebhyo dhanaṃ dattvā tridivaṃ gantum arhasi
a eṣa rājā vimānasthaḥ pitā daśarathas tava
c kākutstha mānuṣe loke gurus tava mahāyaśāḥ
a indralokaṃ gataḥ śrīmāṃs tvayā putreṇa tāritaḥ
c lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā tvam enam abhivādaya
a mahādevavacaḥ śrutvā kākutsthaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
c vimānaśikharasthasya praṇāmam akarot pituḥ
a dīpyamānaṃ svayāṃ lakṣmyā virajo'mbaradhāriṇam
c lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā dadarśa pitaraṃ prabhuḥ
a harṣeṇa mahatāviṣṭo vimānastho mahīpatiḥ
c prāṇaiḥ priyataraṃ dṛṣṭvā putraṃ daśarathas tadā
a āropyāṅkaṃ mahābāhur varāsanagataḥ prabhuḥ
c bāhubhyāṃ saṃpariṣvajya tato vākyaṃ samādade
a na me svargo bahumataḥ saṃmānaś ca surarṣibhiḥ
c tvayā rāma vihīnasya satyaṃ pratiśṛṇomi te
a kaikeyyā yāni coktāni vākyāni vadatāṃ vara
c tava pravrājanārthāni sthitāni hṛdaye mama
a tvāṃ tu dṛṣṭvā kuśalinaṃ pariṣvajya salakṣmaṇam
c adya duḥkhād vimukto 'smi nīhārād iva bhāskaraḥ
a tārito 'haṃ tvayā putra suputreṇa mahātmanā
c aṣṭāvakreṇa dharmātmā tārito brāhmaṇo yathā
a idānīṃ ca vijānāmi yathā saumya sureśvaraiḥ
c vadhārthaṃ rāvaṇasyeha vihitaṃ puruṣottamam
a siddhārthā khalu kausalyā yā tvāṃ rāma gṛhaṃ gatam
c vanān nivṛttaṃ saṃhṛṣṭā drakṣyate śatrusūdana
a siddhārthāḥ khalu te rāma narā ye tvāṃ purīṃ gatam
c jalārdram abhiṣiktaṃ ca drakṣyanti vasudhādhipam
a anuraktena balinā śucinā dharmacāriṇā
c iccheyaṃ tvām ahaṃ draṣṭuṃ bharatena samāgatam
a caturdaśasamāḥ saumya vane niryāpitās tvayā
c vasatā sītayā sārdhaṃ lakṣmaṇena ca dhīmatā
a nivṛttavanavāso 'si pratijñā saphalā kṛtā
c rāvaṇaṃ ca raṇe hatvā devās te paritoṣitāḥ
a kṛtaṃ karma yaśaḥ ślāghyaṃ prāptaṃ te śatrusūdana
c bhrātṛbhiḥ saha rājyastho dīrgham āyur avāpnuhi
a iti bruvāṇaṃ rājānaṃ rāmaḥ prāñjalir abravīt
c kuru prasādaṃ dharmajña kaikeyyā bharatasya ca
a saputrāṃ tvāṃ tyajāmīti yad uktā kaikayī tvayā
c sa śāpaḥ kaikayīṃ ghoraḥ saputrāṃ na spṛśet prabho
a sa tatheti mahārājo rāmam uktvā kṛtāñjalim
c lakṣmaṇaṃ ca pariṣvajya punar vākyam uvāca ha
a rāmaṃ śuśrūṣatā bhaktyā vaidehyā saha sītayā
c kṛtā mama mahāprītiḥ prāptaṃ dharmaphalaṃ ca te
a dharmaṃ prāpsyasi dharmajña yaśaś ca vipulaṃ bhuvi
c rāme prasanne svargaṃ ca mahimānaṃ tathaiva ca
a rāmaṃ śuśrūṣa bhadraṃ te sumitrānandavardhana
c rāmaḥ sarvasya lokasya śubheṣv abhirataḥ sadā
a ete sendrās trayo lokāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
c abhigamya mahātmānam arcanti puruṣottamam
a etat tad uktam avyaktam akṣaraṃ brahmanirmitam
c devānāṃ hṛdayaṃ saumya guhyaṃ rāmaḥ paraṃtapaḥ
a avāptaṃ dharmacaraṇaṃ yaśaś ca vipulaṃ tvayā
c rāmaṃ śuśrūṣatā bhaktyā vaidehyā saha sītayā
a sa tathoktvā mahābāhur lakṣmaṇaṃ prāñjaliṃ sthitam
c uvāca rājā dharmātmā vaidehīṃ vacanaṃ śubham
a kartavyo na tu vaidehi manyus tyāgam imaṃ prati
c rāmeṇa tvadviśuddhyarthaṃ kṛtam etad dhitaiṣiṇā
a na tvaṃ subhru samādheyā patiśuśrūvaṇaṃ prati
c avaśyaṃ tu mayā vācyam eṣa te daivataṃ param
a iti pratisamādiśya putrau sītāṃ tathā snuṣām
c indralokaṃ vimānena yayau daśaratho jvalan
a pratiprayāte kākutsthe mahendraḥ pākaśāsanaḥ
c abravīt paramaprīto rāghavaṃ prāñjaliṃ sthitam
a amoghaṃ darśanaṃ rāma tavāsmākaṃ paraṃtapa
c prītiyukto 'smi tena tvaṃ brūhi yan manasecchasi
a evam uktas tu kākutsthaḥ pratyuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ
c lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā sītayā cāpi bhāryayā
a yadi prītiḥ samutpannā mayi sarvasureśvara
c vakṣyāmi kuru me satyaṃ vacanaṃ vadatāṃ vara
a mama hetoḥ parākrāntā ye gatā yamasādanam
c te sarve jīvitaṃ prāpya samuttiṣṭhantu vānarāḥ
a matpriyeṣv abhiraktāś ca na mṛtyuṃ gaṇayanti ca
c tvatprasādāt sameyus te varam etad ahaṃ vṛṇe
a nīrujān nirvraṇāṃś caiva saṃpannabalapauruṣān
c golāṅgūlāṃs tathaivarkṣān draṣṭum icchāmi mānada
a akāle cāpi mukhyāni mūlāni ca phalāni ca
c nadyaś ca vimalās tatra tiṣṭheyur yatra vānarāḥ
a śrutvā tu vacanaṃ tasya rāghavasya mahātmanaḥ
c mahendraḥ pratyuvācedaṃ vacanaṃ prītilakṣaṇam
a mahān ayaṃ varas tāta tvayokto raghunandana
c samutthāsyanti harayaḥ suptā nidrākṣaye yathā
a suhṛdbhir bāndhavaiś caiva jñātibhiḥ svajanena ca
c sarva eva sameṣyanti saṃyuktāḥ parayā mudā
a akāle puṣpaśabalāḥ phalavantaś ca pādapāḥ
c bhaviṣyanti maheṣvāsa nadyaś ca salilāyutāḥ
a savraṇaiḥ prathamaṃ gātraiḥ saṃvṛtair nivraṇaiḥ punaḥ
c babhūvur vānarāḥ sarve kim etad iti vismitaḥ
a kākutsthaṃ paripūrṇārthaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve surottamāḥ
c ūcus te prathamaṃ stutvā stavārhaṃ sahalakṣmaṇam
a gacchāyodhyām ito vīra visarjaya ca vānarān
c maithilīṃ sāntvayasvainām anuraktāṃ tapasvinīm
a bhrātaraṃ paśya bharataṃ tvacchokād vratacāriṇam
c abhiṣecaya cātmānaṃ paurān gatvā praharṣaya
a evam uktvā tam āmantrya rāmaṃ saumitriṇā saha
c vimānaiḥ sūryasaṃkāśair hṛṣṭā jagmuḥ surā divam
a abhivādya ca kākutsthaḥ sarvāṃs tāṃs tridaśottamān
c lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā vāsam ājñāpayat tadā
a tatas tu sā lakṣmaṇarāmapālitā
mahācamūr hṛṣṭajanā yaśasvinī
c śriyā jvalantī virarāja sarvato
niśāpraṇīteva hi śītaraśminā
a tāṃ rātrim uṣitaṃ rāmaṃ sukhotthitam ariṃdamam
c abravīt prāñjalir vākyaṃ jayaṃ pṛṣṭvā vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a snānāni cāṅgarāgāṇi vastrāṇy ābharaṇāni ca
c candanāni ca divyāni mālyāni vividhāni ca
a alaṃkāravidaś cemā nāryaḥ padmanibhekṣaṇāḥ
c upasthitās tvāṃ vidhivat snāpayiṣyanti rāghava
a evam uktas tu kākutsthaḥ pratyuvāca vibhīṣaṇam
c harīn sugrīvamukhyāṃs tvaṃ snānenopanimantraya
a sa tu tāmyati dharmātmā mamahetoḥ sukhocitaḥ
c sukumāro mahābāhuḥ kumāraḥ satyasaṃśravaḥ
a taṃ vinā kaikeyīputraṃ bharataṃ dharmacāriṇam
c na me snānaṃ bahumataṃ vastrāṇy ābharaṇāni ca
a ita eva pathā kṣipraṃ pratigacchāma tāṃ purīm
c ayodhyām āyato hy eṣa panthāḥ paramadurgamaḥ
a evam uktas tu kākutsthaṃ pratyuvāca vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c ahnā tvāṃ prāpayiṣyāmi tāṃ purīṃ pārthivātmaja
a puṣpakaṃ nāma bhadraṃ te vimānaṃ sūryasaṃnibham
c mama bhrātuḥ kuberasya rāvaṇenāhṛtaṃ balāt
a tad idaṃ meghasaṃkāśaṃ vimānam iha tiṣṭhati
c tena yāsyasi yānena tvam ayodhyāṃ gajajvaraḥ
a ahaṃ te yady anugrāhyo yadi smarasi me guṇān
c vasa tāvad iha prājña yady asti mayi sauhṛdam
a lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā vaidehyā cāpi bhāryayā
c arcitaḥ sarvakāmais tvaṃ tato rāma gamiṣyasi
a prītiyuktas tu me rāma sasainyaḥ sasuhṛdgaṇaḥ
c satkriyāṃ vihitāṃ tāvad gṛhāṇa tvaṃ mayodyatām
a praṇayād bahumānāc ca sauhṛdena ca rāghava
c prasādayāmi preṣyo 'haṃ na khalv ājñāpayāmi te
a evam uktas tato rāmaḥ pratyuvāca vibhīṣaṇam
c rakṣasāṃ vānarāṇāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ copaśṛṇvatām
a pūjito 'haṃ tvayā vīra sācivyena paraṃtapa
c sarvātmanā ca ceṣṭibhiḥ sauhṛdenottamena ca
a na khalv etan na kuryāṃ te vacanaṃ rākṣaseśvara
c taṃ tu me bhrātaraṃ draṣṭuṃ bharataṃ tvarate manaḥ
a māṃ nivartayituṃ yo 'sau citrakūṭam upāgataḥ
c śirasā yācato yasya vacanaṃ na kṛtaṃ mayā
a kausalyāṃ ca sumitrāṃ ca kaikeyīṃ ca yaśasvinīm
c gurūṃś ca suhṛdaś caiva paurāṃś ca tanayaiḥ saha
a upasthāpaya me kṣipraṃ vimānaṃ rākṣaseśvara
c kṛtakāryasya me vāsaḥ kathaṃ cid iha saṃmataḥ
a anujānīhi māṃ saumya pūjito 'smi vibhīṣaṇa
c manyur na khalu kartavyas tvaritas tvānumānaye
a tataḥ kāñcanacitrāṅgaṃ vaidūryamaṇivedikam
c kūṭāgāraiḥ parikṣiptaṃ sarvato rajataprabham
a pāṇḍurābhiḥ patākābhir dhvajaiś ca samalaṃkṛtam
c śobhitaṃ kāñcanair harmyair hemapadmavibhūṣitam
a prakīrṇaṃ kiṅkiṇījālair muktāmaṇigavākṣitam
c ghaṇṭājālaiḥ parikṣiptaṃ sarvato madhurasvanam
a tan meruśikharākāraṃ nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
c bahubhir bhūṣitaṃ harmyair muktārajatasaṃnibhau
a talaiḥ sphaṭikacitrāṅgair vaidūryaiś ca varāsanaiḥ
c mahārhāstaraṇopetair upapannaṃ mahādhanaiḥ
a upasthitam anādhṛṣyaṃ tad vimānaṃ manojavam
c nivedayitvā rāmāya tasthau tatra vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a upasthitaṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā puṣpakaṃ puṣpabhūṣitam
c avidūre sthitaṃ rāmaṃ pratyuvāca vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a sa tu baddhāñjaliḥ prahvo vinīto rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c abravīt tvarayopetaḥ kiṃ karomīti rāghavam
a tam abravīn mahātejā lakṣmaṇasyopaśṛṇvataḥ
c vimṛśya rāghavo vākyam idaṃ snehapuraskṛtam
a kṛtaprayatnakarmāṇo vibhīṣaṇa vanaukasaḥ
c ratnair arthaiś ca vivibhair bhūṣaṇaiś cābhipūjaya
a sahaibhir arditā laṅkā nirjitā rākṣaseśvara
c hṛṣṭaiḥ prāṇabhayaṃ tyaktvā saṃgrāmeṣv anivartibhiḥ
a evaṃ saṃmānitāś ceme mānārhā mānada tvayā
c bhaviṣyanti kṛtajñena nirvṛtā hariyūthapāḥ
a tyāginaṃ saṃgrahītāraṃ sānukrośaṃ yaśasvinam
c yatas tvām avagacchanti tataḥ saṃbodhayāmi te
a evam uktas tu rāmeṇa vānarāṃs tān vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c ratnārthaiḥ saṃvibhāgena sarvān evānvapūjayat
a tatas tān pūjitān dṛṣṭvā ratnair arthaiś ca yūthapān
c āruroha tato rāmas tad vimānam anuttamam
a aṅkenādāya vaidehīṃ lajjamānāṃ yaśasvinīm
c lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā vikrāntena dhanuṣmatā
a abravīc ca vimānasthaḥ kākutsthaḥ sarvavānarān
c sugrīvaṃ ca mahāvīryaṃ rākṣasaṃ ca vibhīṣaṇam
a mitrakāryaṃ kṛtam idaṃ bhavadbhir vānarottamāḥ
c anujñātā mayā sarve yatheṣṭaṃ pratigacchata
a yat tu kāryaṃ vayasyena suhṛdā vā paraṃtapa
c kṛtaṃ sugrīva tat sarvaṃ bhavatā dharmabhīruṇā
e kiṣkindhāṃ pratiyāhy āśu svasainyenābhisaṃvṛtaḥ
a svarājye vasa laṅkāyāṃ mayā datte vibhīṣaṇa
c na tvāṃ dharṣayituṃ śaktāḥ sendrā api divaukasaḥ
a ayodhyāṃ pratiyāsyāmi rājadhānīṃ pitur mama
c abhyanujñātum icchāmi sarvān āmantrayāmi vaḥ
a evam uktās tu rāmeṇa vānarās te mahābalāḥ
c ūcuḥ prāñjalayo rāmaṃ rākṣasaś ca vibhīṣaṇaḥ
e ayodhyāṃ gantum icchāmaḥ sarvān nayatu no bhavān
a dṛṣṭvā tvām abhiṣekārdraṃ kausalyām abhivādya ca
c acireṇāgamiṣyāmaḥ svān gṛhān nṛpateḥ suta
a evam uktas tu dharmātmā vānaraiḥ savibhīṣaṇaiḥ
c abravīd rāghavaḥ śrīmān sasugrīvavibhīṣaṇān
a priyāt priyataraṃ labdhaṃ yad ahaṃ sasuhṛjjanaḥ
c sarvair bhavadbhiḥ sahitaḥ prītiṃ lapsye purīṃ gataḥ
a kṣipram āroha sugrīva vimānaṃ vānaraiḥ saha
c tvam adhyāroha sāmātyo rākṣasendravibhīṣaṇa
a tatas tat puṣpakaṃ divyaṃ sugrīvaḥ saha senayā
c adhyārohat tvarañ śīghraṃ sāmātyaś ca vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a teṣv ārūḍheṣu sarveṣu kauberaṃ paramāsanam
c rāghaveṇābhyanujñātam utpapāta vihāyasaṃ
a yayau tena vimānena haṃsayuktena bhāsvatā
c prahṛṣṭaś ca pratītaś ca babhau rāmaḥ kuberavat
a anujñātaṃ tu rāmeṇa tad vimānam anuttamam
c utpapāta mahāmeghaḥ śvasanenoddhato yathā
a pātayitvā tataś cakṣuḥ sarvato raghunandanaḥ
c abravīn maithilīṃ sītāṃ rāmaḥ śaśinibhānanām
a kailāsaśikharākāre trikūṭaśikhare sthitām
c laṅkām īkṣasva vaidehi nirmitāṃ viśvakarmaṇā
a etad āyodhanaṃ paśya māṃsaśoṇitakardamam
c harīṇāṃ rākṣasānāṃ ca sīte viśasanaṃ mahat
a tavahetor viśālākṣi rāvaṇo nihato mayā
c kumbhakarṇo 'tra nihataḥ prahastaś ca niśācaraḥ
a lakṣmaṇenendrajic cātra rāvaṇir nihato raṇe
c virūpākṣaś ca duṣprekṣyo mahāpārśvamahodarau
a akampanaś ca nihato balino 'nye ca rākṣasāḥ
c triśirāś cātikāyaś ca devāntakanarāntakau
a atra mandodarī nāma bhāryā taṃ paryadevayat
c sapatnīnāṃ sahasreṇa sāsreṇa parivāritā
a etat tu dṛśyate tīrthaṃ samudrasya varānane
c yatra sāgaram uttīrya tāṃ rātrim uṣitā vayam
a eṣa setur mayā baddhaḥ sāgare salilārṇave
c tavahetor viśālākṣi nalasetuḥ suduṣkaraḥ
a paśya sāgaram akṣobhyaṃ vaidehi varuṇālayam
c apāram abhigarjantaṃ śaṅkhaśuktiniṣevitam
a hiraṇyanābhaṃ śailendraṃ kāñcanaṃ paśya maithili
c viśramārthaṃ hanumato bhittvā sāgaram utthitam
a atra rākṣasarājo 'yam ājagāma vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a eṣā sā dṛśyate sīte kiṣkindhā citrakānanā
c sugrīvasya purī ramyā yatra vālī mayā hataḥ
a dṛśyate 'sau mahān sīte savidyud iva toyadaḥ
c ṛśyamūko giriśreṣṭhaḥ kāñcanair dhātubhir vṛtaḥ
a atrāhaṃ vānarendreṇa sugrīveṇa samāgataḥ
c samayaś ca kṛtaḥ sīte vadhārthaṃ vālino mayā
a eṣā sā dṛśyate pampā nalinī citrakānanā
c tvayā vihīno yatrāhaṃ vilalāpa suduḥkhitaḥ
a asyās tīre mayā dṛṣṭā śabarī dharmacāriṇī
c atra yojanabāhuś ca kabandho nihato mayā
a dṛśyate 'sau janasthāne sīte śrīmān vanaspatiḥ
c yatra yuddhaṃ mahad vṛttaṃ tavahetor vilāsini
e rāvaṇasya nṛśaṃsasya jaṭāyoś ca mahātmanaḥ
a kharaś ca nihataś saṃkhye dūṣaṇaś ca nipātitaḥ
c triśirāś ca mahāvīryo mayā bāṇair ajihmagaiḥ
a parṇaśālā tathā citrā dṛśyate śubhadarśanā
c yatra tvaṃ rākṣasendreṇa rāvaṇena hṛtā balāt
a eṣā godāvarī ramyā prasannasalilā śivā
c agastyasyāśramo hy eṣa dṛśyate paśya maithili
a vaidehi dṛśyate cātra śarabhaṅgāśramo mahān
c upayātaḥ sahasrākṣo yatra śakraḥ puraṃdaraḥ
a ete te tāpasāvāsā dṛśyante tanumadhyame
c atriḥ kulapatir yatra sūryavaiśvānaraprabhaḥ
e atra sīte tvayā dṛṣṭā tāpasī dharmacāriṇī
a asmin deśe mahākāyo virādho nihato mayā
a asau sutanuśailendraś citrakūṭaḥ prakāśate
c yatra māṃ kaikayīputraḥ prasādayitum āgataḥ
a eṣā sā yamunā dūrād dṛśyate citrakānanā
c bharadvājāśramo yatra śrīmān eṣa prakāśate
a eṣā tripathagā gaṅgā dṛśyate varavarṇini
c śṛṅgaverapuraṃ caitad guho yatra samāgataḥ
a eṣā sā dṛśyate 'yodhyā rājadhānī pitur mama
c ayodhyāṃ kuru vaidehi praṇāmaṃ punar āgatā
a tatas te vānarāḥ sarve rākṣasaś ca vibhīṣaṇaḥ
c utpatyotpatya dadṛśus tāṃ purīṃ śubhadarśanām
a tatas tu tāṃ pāṇḍuraharmyamālinīṃ
viśālakakṣyāṃ gajavājisaṃkulām
c purīm ayodhyāṃ dadṛśuḥ plavaṃgamāḥ
purīṃ mahendrasya yathāmarāvatīm
a pūrṇe caturdaśe varṣe pañcabhyāṃ lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥ
c bharadvājāśramaṃ prāpya vavande niyato munim
a so 'pṛcchad abhivādyainaṃ bharadvājaṃ tapodhanam
c śṛṇoṣi ka cid bhagavan subhikṣānāmayaṃ pure
e kaccic ca yukto bharato jīvanty api ca mātaraḥ
a evam uktas tu rāmeṇa bharadvājo mahāmuniḥ
c pratyuvāca raghuśreṣṭhaṃ smitapūrvaṃ prahṛṣṭavat
a paṅkadigdhas tu bharato jaṭilas tvāṃ pratīkṣate
c pāduke te puraskṛtya sarvaṃ ca kuśalaṃ gṛhe
a tvāṃ purā cīravasanaṃ praviśantaṃ mahāvanam
c strītṛtīyaṃ cyutaṃ rājyād dharmakāmaṃ ca kevalam
a padātiṃ tyaktasarvasvaṃ pitur vacanakāriṇam
c svargabhogaiḥ parityaktaṃ svargacyutam ivāmaram
a dṛṣṭvā tu karuṇā pūrvaṃ mamāsīt samitiṃjaya
