c kaikeyīvacane yuktaṃ vanyamūlaphalāśanam
a sāmprataṃ susamṛddhārthaṃ samitragaṇabāndhavam
c samīkṣya vijitāriṃ tvāṃ mama prītir anuttamā
a sarvaṃ ca sukhaduḥkhaṃ te viditaṃ mama rāghava
c yat tvayā vipulaṃ prāptaṃ janasthānavadhādikam
a brāhmaṇārthe niyuktasya rakṣataḥ sarvatāpasān
c mārīcadarśanaṃ caiva sītonmathanam eva ca
a kabandhadarśanaṃ caiva pampābhigamanaṃ tathā
c sugrīveṇa ca te sakhyaṃ yac ca vālī hatas tvayā
a mārgaṇaṃ caiva vaidehyāḥ karma vātātmajasya ca
c viditāyāṃ ca vaidehyāṃ nalasetur yathā kṛtaḥ
e yathā ca dīpitā laṅkā prahṛṣṭair hariyūthapaiḥ
a saputrabāndhavāmātyaḥ sabalaḥ saha vāhanaḥ
c yathā ca nihataḥ saṃkhye rāvaṇo devakaṇṭakaḥ
a samāgamaś ca tridaśair yathādattaś ca te varaḥ
c sarvaṃ mamaitad viditaṃ tapasā dharmavatsala
a aham apy atra te dadmi varaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ vara
c arghyaṃ pratigṛhāṇedam ayodhyāṃ śvo gamiṣyasi
a tasya tac chirasā vākyaṃ pratigṛhya nṛpātmajaḥ
c bāḍham ity eva saṃhṛṣṭaḥ śrīmān varam ayācata
a akālaphalino vṛkṣāḥ sarve cāpi madhusravāḥ
c bhavantu mārge bhagavann ayodhyāṃ prati gacchataḥ
a niṣphalāḥ phalinaś cāsan vipuṣpāḥ puṣpaśālinaḥ
c śuṣkāḥ samagrapatrās te nagāś caiva madhusravāḥ
a ayodhyāṃ tu samālokya cintayām āsa rāghavaḥ
c cintayitvā tato dṛṣṭiṃ vānareṣu nyapātayat
a priyakāmaḥ priyaṃ rāmas tatas tvaritavikramam
c uvāca dhīmāṃs tejasvī hanūmantaṃ plavaṃgamam
a ayodhyāṃ tvarito gaccha kṣipraṃ tvaṃ plavagottama
c jānīhi kaccit kuśalī jano nṛpatimandire
a śṛṅgaverapuraṃ prāpya guhaṃ gahanagocaram
c niṣādādhipatiṃ brūhi kuśalaṃ vacanān mama
a śrutvā tu māṃ kuśalinam arogaṃ vigatajvaram
c bhaviṣyati guhaḥ prītaḥ sa mamātmasamaḥ sakhā
a ayodhyāyāś ca te mārgaṃ pravṛttiṃ bharatasya ca
c nivedayiṣyati prīto niṣādādhipatir guhaḥ
a bharatas tu tvayā vācyaḥ kuśalaṃ vacanān mama
c siddhārthaṃ śaṃsa māṃ tasmai sabhāryaṃ sahalakṣmaṇam
a haraṇaṃ cāpi vaidehyā rāvaṇena balīyasā
c sugrīveṇa ca saṃvādaṃ vālinaś ca vadhaṃ raṇe
a maithilyanveṣaṇaṃ caiva yathā cādhigatā tvayā
c laṅghayitvā mahātoyam āpagāpatim avyayam
a upayānaṃ samudrasya sāgarasya ca darśanam
c yathā ca kāritaḥ setū rāvaṇaś ca yathā hataḥ
a varadānaṃ mahendreṇa brahmaṇā varuṇena ca
c mahādevaprasādāc ca pitrā mama samāgamam
a jitvā śatrugaṇān rāmaḥ prāpya cānuttamaṃ yaśaḥ
c upayāti samṛddhārthaḥ saha mitrair mahābalaḥ
a etac chrutvā yamākāraṃ bhajate bharatas tataḥ
c sa ca te veditavyaḥ syāt sarvaṃ yac cāpi māṃ prati
a jñeyāḥ sarve ca vṛttāntā bharatasyeṅgitāni ca
c tattvena mukhavarṇena dṛṣṭyā vyābhāṣaṇena ca
a sarvakāmasamṛddhaṃ hi hastyaśvarathasaṃkulam
c pitṛpaitāmahaṃ rājyaṃ kasya nāvartayen manaḥ
a saṃgatyā bharataḥ śrīmān rājyenārthī svayaṃ bhavet
c praśāstu vasudhāṃ sarvām akhilāṃ raghunandanaḥ
a tasya buddhiṃ ca vijñāya vyavasāyaṃ ca vānara
c yāvan na dūraṃ yātāḥ smaḥ kṣipram āgantum arhasi
a iti pratisamādiṣṭo hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
c mānuṣaṃ dhārayan rūpam ayodhyāṃ tvarito yayau
a laṅghayitvā pitṛpathaṃ bhujagendrālayaṃ śubham
c gaṅgāyamunayor bhīmaṃ saṃnipātam atītya ca
a śṛṅgaverapuraṃ prāpya guham āsādya vīryavān
c sa vācā śubhayā hṛṣṭo hanūmān idam abravīt
a sakhā tu tava kākutstho rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
c sasītaḥ saha saumitriḥ sa tvāṃ kuśalam abravīt
a pañcamīm adya rajanīm uṣitvā vacanān muneḥ
c bharadvājābhyanujñātaṃ drakṣyasy adyaiva rāghavam
a evam uktvā mahātejāḥ saṃprahṛṣṭatanūruhaḥ
c utpapāta mahāvego vegavān avicārayan
a so 'paśyad rāmatīrthaṃ ca nadīṃ vālukinīṃ tathā
c gomatīṃ tāṃ ca so 'paśyad bhīmaṃ sālavanaṃ tathā
a sa gatvā dūram adhvānaṃ tvaritaḥ kapikuñjaraḥ
c āsasāda drumān phullān nandigrāmasamīpajān
a krośamātre tv ayodhyāyāś cīrakṛṣṇājināmbaram
c dadarśa bharataṃ dīnaṃ kṛśam āśramavāsinam
a jaṭilaṃ maladigdhāṅgaṃ bhrātṛvyasanakarśitam
c phalamūlāśinaṃ dāntaṃ tāpasaṃ dharmacāriṇam
a samunnatajaṭābhāraṃ valkalājinavāsasaṃ
c niyataṃ bhāvitātmānaṃ brahmarṣisamatejasaṃ
a pāduke te puraskṛtya śāsantaṃ vai vasuṃdharām
c caturvarṇyasya lokasya trātāraṃ sarvato bhayāt
a upasthitam amātyaiś ca śucibhiś ca purohitaiḥ
c balamukhyaiś ca yuktaiś ca kāṣāyāmbaradhāribhiḥ
a na hi te rājaputraṃ taṃ cīrakṛṣṇājināmbaram
c parimoktuṃ vyavasyanti paurā vai dharmavatsalāḥ
a taṃ dharmam iva dharmajñaṃ devavantam ivāparam
c uvāca prāñjalir vākayṃ hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
a vasantaṃ daṇḍakāraṇye yaṃ tvaṃ cīrajaṭādharam
c anuśocasi kākutsthaṃ sa tvā kuśalam abravīt
a priyam ākhyāmi te deva śokaṃ tyakṣyasi dāruṇam
c asmin muhūrte bhrātrā tvaṃ rāmeṇa saha saṃgataḥ
a nihatya rāvaṇaṃ rāmaḥ pratilabhya ca maithilīm
c upayāti samṛddhārthaḥ saha mitrair mahābalaiḥ
a lakṣmaṇaś ca mahātejā vaidehī ca yaśasvinī
c sītā samagrā rāmeṇa mahendreṇa śacī yathā
a evam ukto hanumatā bharataḥ kaikayīsutaḥ
c papāta sahasā hṛṣṭo harṣān mohaṃ jagāma ha
a tato muhūrtād utthāya pratyāśvasya ca rāghavaḥ
c hanūmantam uvācedaṃ bharataḥ priyavādinam
a aśokajaiḥ prītimayaiḥ kapim āliṅgya saṃbhramāt
c siṣeca bharataḥ śrīmān vipulair aśrubindubhiḥ
a devo vā mānuṣo vā tvam anukrośād ihāgataḥ
c priyākhyānasya te saumya dadāmi bruvataḥ priyam
a gavāṃ śatasahasraṃ ca grāmāṇāṃ ca śataṃ param
c sakuṇḍalāḥ śubhācārā bhāryāḥ kanyāś ca ṣoḍaśa
a hemavarṇāḥ sunāsorūḥ śaśisaumyānanāḥ striyaḥ
c sarvābharaṇasaṃpannā saṃpannāḥ kulajātibhiḥ
a niśamya rāmāgamanaṃ nṛpātmajaḥ
kapipravīrasya tadādbhutopamam
c praharṣito rāmadidṛkṣayābhavat
punaś ca harṣād idam abravīd vacaḥ
a bahūni nāma varṣāṇi gatasya sumahad vanam
c śṛṇomy ahaṃ prītikaraṃ mama nāthasya kīrtanam
a kalyāṇī bata gātheyaṃ laukikī pratibhāti me
c eti jīvantam ānando naraṃ varṣaśatād api
a rāghavasya harīṇāṃ ca katham āsīt samāgamaḥ
c kasmin deśe kim āśritya tat tvam ākhyāhi pṛcchataḥ
a sa pṛṣṭo rājaputreṇa bṛsyāṃ samupaveśitaḥ
c ācacakṣe tataḥ sarvaṃ rāmasya caritaṃ vane
a yathā pravrajito rāmo mātur datte vare tava
c yathā ca putraśokena rājā daśaratho mṛtaḥ
a yathā dūtais tvam ānītas tūrṇaṃ rājagṛhāt prabho
c tvayāyodhyāṃ praviṣṭena yathā rājyaṃ na cepsitam
a citrakūṭaṃ giriṃ gatvā rājyenāmitrakarśanaḥ
c nimantritas tvayā bhrātā dharmam ācaritā satām
a sthitena rājño vacane yathā rājyaṃ visarjitam
c āryasya pāduke gṛhya yathāsi punar āgataḥ
a sarvam etan mahābāho yathāvad viditaṃ tava
c tvayi pratiprayāte tu yad vṛttaṃ tan nibodha me
a apayāte tvayi tadā samudbhrāntamṛgadvijam
c praviveśātha vijanaṃ sumahad daṇḍakāvanam
a teṣāṃ purastād balavān gacchatāṃ gahane vane
c vinadan sumahānādaṃ virādhaḥ pratyadṛśyata
a tam utkṣipya mahānādam ūrdhvabāhum adhomukham
c nikhāte prakṣipanti sma nadantam iva kuñjaram
a tat kṛtvā duṣkaraṃ karma bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau
c sāyāhne śarabhaṅgasya ramyam āśramam īyatuḥ
a śarabhaṅge divaṃ prāpte rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
c abhivādya munīn sarvāñ janasthānam upāgamat
a caturdaśasahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām
c hatāni vasatā tatra rāghaveṇa mahātmanā
a tataḥ paścāc chūrpaṇakhā rāmapārśvam upāgatā
c tato rāmeṇa saṃdiṣṭo lakṣmaṇaḥ sahasotthitaḥ
a pragṛhya khaḍgaṃ ciccheda karṇanāse mahābalaḥ
c tatas tenārditā bālā rāvaṇaṃ samupāgatā
a rāvaṇānucaro ghoro mārīco nāma rākṣasaḥ
c lobhayām āsa vaidehīṃ bhūtvā ratnamayo mṛgaḥ
a sā rāmam abravīd dṛṣṭvā vaidehī gṛhyatām iti
c aho manoharaḥ kānta āśrame no bhaviṣyati
a tato rāmo dhanuṣpāṇir dhāvantam anudhāvati
c sa taṃ jaghāna dhāvantaṃ śareṇānataparvaṇā
a atha saumyā daśagrīvo mṛgaṃ yāte tu rāghave
c lakṣmaṇe cāpi niṣkrānte praviveśāśramaṃ tadā
e jagrāha tarasā sītāṃ grahaḥ khe rohiṇīm iva
a trātukāmaṃ tato yuddhe hatvā gṛdhraṃ jaṭāyuṣam
c pragṛhya sītāṃ sahasā jagāmāśu sa rāvaṇaḥ
a tatas tv adbhutasaṃkāśāḥ sthitāḥ parvatamūrdhani
c sītāṃ gṛhītvā gacchantaṃ vānarāḥ parvatopamāḥ
e dadṛśur vismitās tatra rāvaṇaṃ rākṣasādhipam
a praviverśa tadā laṅkāṃ rāvaṇo lokarāvaṇaḥ
a tāṃ suvarṇaparikrānte śubhe mahati veśmani
c praveśya maithilīṃ vākyaiḥ sāntvayām āsa rāvaṇaḥ
a nivartamānaḥ kākutstho dṛṣṭvā gṛdhraṃ pravivyathe
a gṛdhraṃ hataṃ tadā dagdhvā rāmaḥ priyasakhaṃ pituḥ
c godāvarīm anucaran vanoddeśāṃś ca puṣpitān
e āsedatur mahāraṇye kabandhaṃ nāma rākṣasaṃ
a tataḥ kabandhavacanād rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
c ṛśyamūkaṃ giriṃ gatvā sugrīveṇa samāgataḥ
a tayoḥ samāgamaḥ pūrvaṃ prītyā hārdo vyajāyata
c itaretara saṃvādāt pragāḍhaḥ praṇayas tayoḥ
a rāmaḥ svabāhuvīryeṇa svarājyaṃ pratyapādayat
c vālinaṃ samare hatvā mahākāyaṃ mahābalam
a sugrīvaḥ sthāpito rājye sahitaḥ sarvavānaraiḥ
c rāmāya pratijānīte rājaputryās tu mārgaṇam
a ādiṣṭā vānarendreṇa sugrīveṇa mahātmanā
c daśakoṭyaḥ plavaṃgānāṃ sarvāḥ prasthāpitā diśaḥ
a teṣāṃ no vipranaṣṭānāṃ vindhye parvatasattame
c bhṛśaṃ śokābhitaptānāṃ mahān kālo 'tyavartata
a bhrātā tu gṛdhrarājasya saṃpātir nāma vīryavān
c samākhyāti sma vasatiṃ sītāyā rāvaṇālaye
a so 'haṃ duḥkhaparītānāṃ duḥkhaṃ tajjñātināṃ nudan
c ātmavīryaṃ samāsthāya yojanānāṃ śataṃ plutaḥ
a tatrāham ekām adrākṣam aśokavanikāṃ gatām
c kauśeyavastrāṃ malināṃ nirānandāṃ dṛḍhavratām
a tayā sametya vidhivat pṛṣṭvā sarvam aninditām
c abhijñānaṃ maṇiṃ labdhvā caritārtho 'ham āgataḥ
a mayā ca punar āgamya rāmasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
c abhijñānaṃ mayā dattam arciṣmān sa mahāmaṇiḥ
a śrutvā tāṃ maithilīṃ hṛṣṭas tv āśaśaṃse sa jīvitam
c jīvitāntam anuprāptaḥ pītvāmṛtam ivāturaḥ
a udyojayiṣyann udyogaṃ dadhre laṅkāvadhe manaḥ
c jighāṃsur iva lokāṃs te sarvāṃl lokān vibhāvasuḥ
a tataḥ samudram āsādya nalaṃ setum akārayat
c atarat kapivīrāṇāṃ vāhinī tena setunā
a prahastam avadhīn nīlaḥ kumbhakarṇaṃ tu rāghavaḥ
c lakṣmaṇo rāvaṇasutaṃ svayaṃ rāmas tu rāvaṇam
a sa śakreṇa samāgamya yamena varuṇena ca
c surarṣibhiś ca kākutstho varāṃl lebhe paraṃtapaḥ
a sa tu dattavaraḥ prītyā vānaraiś ca samāgataḥ
c puṣpakeṇa vimānena kiṣkindhām abhyupāgamat
a taṃ gaṅgāṃ punar āsādya vasantaṃ munisaṃnidhau
c avighnaṃ puṣyayogena śvo rāmaṃ draṣṭum arhasi
a tataḥ sa satyaṃ hanumadvaco mahan
niśamya hṛṣṭo bharataḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
c uvāca vāṇīṃ manasaḥ praharṣiṇī
cirasya pūrṇaḥ khalu me manorathaḥ
a śrutvā tu param ānandaṃ bharataḥ satyavikramaḥ
c hṛṣṭam ājñāpayām āsa śatrughnaṃ paravīrahā
a daivatāni ca sarvāṇi caityāni nagarasya ca
c sugandhamālyair vāditrair arcantu śucayo narāḥ
a rājadārās tathāmātyāḥ sainyāḥ senāgaṇāṅganāḥ
c abhiniryāntu rāmasya draṣṭuṃ śaśinibhaṃ mukham
a bharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā śatrughnaḥ paravīrahā
c viṣṭīr anekasāhasrīś codayām āsa vīryavān
a samīkuruta nimnāni viṣamāṇi samāni ca
c sthānāni ca nirasyantāṃ nandigrāmād itaḥ param
a siñcantu pṛthivīṃ kṛtsnāṃ himaśītena vāriṇā
c tato 'bhyavakiraṃs tv anye lājaiḥ puṣpaiś ca sarvataḥ
a samucchritapatākās tu rathyāḥ puravarottame
c śobhayantu ca veśmāni sūryasyodayanaṃ prati
a sragdāmamuktapuṣpaiś ca sugandhaiḥ pañcavarṇakaiḥ
c rājamārgam asaṃbādhaṃ kirantu śataśo narāḥ
a mattair nāgasahasraiś ca śātakumbhavibhūṣitaḥ
c apare hemakakṣyābhiḥ sagajābhiḥ kareṇubhiḥ
e niryayus tvarayā yuktā rathaiś ca sumahārathāḥ
a tato yānāny upārūḍhāḥ sarvā daśarathastriyaḥ
c kausalyāṃ pramukhe kṛtvā sumitrāṃ cāpi niryayuḥ
a aśvānāṃ khuraśabdena rathanemisvanena ca
c śaṅkhadundubhinādena saṃcacāleva medinī
a kṛtsnaṃ ca nagaraṃ tat tu nandigrāmam upāgamat
c dvijātimukhyair dharmātmā śreṇīmukhyaiḥ sanaigamaiḥ
a mālyamodaka hastaiś ca mantribhir bharato vṛtaḥ
c śaṅkhabherīninādaiś ca bandibhiś cābhivanditaḥ
a āryapādau gṛhītvā tu śirasā dharmakovidaḥ
c pāṇḍuraṃ chatram ādāya śuklamālyopaśobhitam
a śukle ca vālavyajane rājārhe hemabhūṣite
c upavāsakṛśo dīnaś cīrakṛṣṇājināmbaraḥ
a bhrātur āgamanaṃ śrutvā tat pūrvaṃ harṣam āgataḥ
c pratyudyayau tadā rāmaṃ mahātmā sacivaiḥ saha
a samīkṣya bharato vākyam uvāca pavanātmajam
c kaccin na khalu kāpeyī sevyate calacittatā
e na hi paśyāmi kākutsthaṃ rāmam āryaṃ paraṃtapam
a athaivam ukte vacane hanūmān idam abravīt
c arthaṃ vijñāpayann eva bharataṃ satyavikramam
a sadā phalān kusumitān vṛkṣān prāpya madhusravān
c bharadvājaprasādena mattabhramaranāditān
a tasya caiṣa varo datto vāsavena paraṃtapa
c sasainyasya tadātithyaṃ kṛtaṃ sarvaguṇānvitam
a nisvanaḥ śrūyate bhīmaḥ prahṛṣṭānāṃ vanaukasām
c manye vānarasenā sā nadīṃ tarati gomatīm
a rajovarṣaṃ samudbhūtaṃ paśya vālukinīṃ prati
c manye sālavanaṃ ramyaṃ lolayanti plavaṃgamāḥ
a tad etad dṛśyate dūrād vimalaṃ candrasaṃnibham
c vimānaṃ puṣpakaṃ divyaṃ manasā brahmanirmitam
a rāvaṇaṃ bāndhavaiḥ sārdhaṃ hatvā labdhaṃ mahātmanā
c dhanadasya prasādena divyam etan manojavam
a etasmin bhrātarau vīrau vaidehyā saha rāghavau
c sugrīvaś ca mahātejā rākṣasendro vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a tato harṣasamudbhūto nisvano divam aspṛśat
c strībālayuvavṛddhānāṃ rāmo 'yam iti kīrtitaḥ
a rathakuñjaravājibhyas te 'vatīrya mahīṃ gatāḥ
c dadṛśus taṃ vimānasthaṃ narāḥ somam ivāmbare
a prāñjalir bharato bhūtvā prahṛṣṭo rāghavonmukhaḥ
c svāgatena yathārthena tato rāmam apūjayat
a manasā brahmaṇā sṛṣṭe vimāne lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥ
c rarāja pṛthudīrghākṣo vajrapāṇir ivāparaḥ
a tato vimānāgragataṃ bharato bhrātaraṃ tadā
c vavande praṇato rāmaṃ merustham iva bhāskaram
a āropito vimānaṃ tad bharataḥ satyavikramaḥ
c rāmam āsādya muditaḥ punar evābhyavādayat
a taṃ samutthāpya kākutsthaś cirasyākṣipathaṃ gatam
c aṅke bharatam āropya muditaḥ pariṣaṣvaje
a tato lakṣmaṇam āsādya vaidehīṃ ca paraṃtapaḥ
c abhyavādayata prīto bharato nāma cābravīt
a sugrīvaṃ kaikayī putro jāmbavantaṃ tathāṅgadam
c maindaṃ ca dvividaṃ nīlam ṛṣabhaṃ caiva sasvaje
a te kṛtvā mānuṣaṃ rūpaṃ vānarāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
c kuśalaṃ paryapṛṣhanta prahṛṣṭā bharataṃ tadā
a vibhīṣaṇaṃ ca bharataḥ sāntvayan vākyam abravīt
c diṣṭyā tvayā sahāyena kṛtaṃ karma suduṣkaram
a śatrughnaś ca tadā rāmam abhivādya salakṣmaṇam
c sītāyāś caraṇau paścād vavande vinayānvitaḥ
a rāmo mātaram āsādya viṣaṇṇaṃ śokakarśitām
c jagrāha praṇataḥ pādau mano mātuḥ prasādayan
a abhivādya sumitrāṃ ca kaikeyīṃ ca yaśasvinīm
c sa mātṝś ca tadā sarvāḥ purohitam upāgamat
a svāgataṃ te mahābāho kausalyānandavardhana
c iti prāñjalayaḥ sarve nāgarā rāmam abruvan
a tany añjalisahasrāṇi pragṛhītāni nāgaraiḥ
c ākośānīva padmāni dadarśa bharatāgrajaḥ
a pāduke te tu rāmasya gṛhītvā bharataḥ svayam
c caraṇābhyāṃ narendrasya yojayām āsa dharmavit
a abravīc ca tadā rāmaṃ bharataḥ sa kṛtāñjaliḥ
c etat te rakṣitaṃ rājan rājyaṃ niryātitaṃ mayā
a adya janma kṛtārthaṃ me saṃvṛttaś ca manorathaḥ
c yas tvāṃ paśyāmi rājānam ayodhyāṃ punar āgatam
a avekṣatāṃ bhavān kośaṃ koṣṭhāgāraṃ puraṃ balam
c bhavatas tejasā sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ daśaguṇaṃ mayā
a tathā bruvāṇaṃ bharataṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ bhrātṛvatsalam
c mumucur vānarā bāṣpaṃ rākṣasaś ca vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a tataḥ praharṣād bharatam aṅkam āropya rāghavaḥ
c yayau tena vimānena sasainyo bharatāśramam
a bharatāśramam āsādya sasainyo rāghavas tadā
c avatīrya vimānāgrād avatasthe mahītale
a abravīc ca tadā rāmas tadvimānam anuttamam
c vaha vaiśravaṇaṃ devam anujānāmi gamyatām
a tato rāmābhyanujñātaṃ tadvimānam anuttamam
c uttarāṃ diśam uddiśya jagāma dhanadālayam
a purohitasyātmasamasya rāghavo
bṛhaspateḥ śakra ivāmarādhīaph
c nipīḍya pādau pṛthag āsane śubhe
sahaiva tenopaviveśa vīryavān
a śirasy añjalim ādāya kaikeyīnandivardhanaḥ
c babhāṣe bharato jyeṣṭhaṃ rāmaṃ satyaparākramam
a pūjitā māmikā mātā dattaṃ rājyam idaṃ mama
c tad dadāmi punas tubhyaṃ yathā tvam adadā mama
a dhuram ekākinā nyastām ṛṣabheṇa balīyasā
c kiśoravad guruṃ bhāraṃ na voḍhum aham utsahe
a vārivegena mahatā bhinnaḥ setur iva kṣaran
c durbandhanam idaṃ manye rājyacchidram asaṃvṛtam
a gatiṃ khara ivāśvasya haṃsasyeva ca vāyasaḥ
c nānvetum utsahe deva tava mārgam ariṃdama
a yathā ca ropito vṛkṣo jātaś cāntarniveśane
c mahāṃś ca sudurāroho mahāskandhaḥ praśākhavān
a śīryeta puṣpito bhūtvā na phalāni pradarśayet
c tasya nānubhaved arthaṃ yasya hetoḥ sa ropyate
a eṣopamā mahābāho tvam arthaṃ vettum arhasi
c yady asmān manujendra tvaṃ bhaktān bhṛtyān na śādhi hi
a jagad adyābhiṣiktaṃ tvām anupaśyatu sarvataḥ
c pratapantam ivādityaṃ madhyāhne dīptatejasaṃ
a tūryasaṃghātanirghoṣaiḥ kāñcīnūpuranisvanaiḥ
c madhurair gītaśabdaiś ca pratibudhyasva śeṣva ca
a yāvad āvartate cakraṃ yāvatī ca vasuṃdharā
c tāvat tvam iha sarvasya svāmitvam abhivartaya
a bharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā rāmaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
c tatheti pratijagrāha niṣasādāsane śubhe
a tataḥ śatrughnavacanān nipuṇāḥ śmaśruvardhakāḥ
c sukhahastāḥ suśīghrāś ca rāghavaṃ paryupāsata
a pūrvaṃ tu bharate snāte lakṣmaṇe ca mahābale
c sugrīve vānarendre ca rākṣasendre vibhīṣaṇe
a viśodhitajaṭaḥ snātaś citramālyānulepanaḥ
c mahārhavasanopetas tasthau tatra śriyā jvalan
a pratikarma ca rāmasya kārayām āsa vīryavān
c lakṣmaṇasya ca lakṣmīvān ikṣvākukulavardhanaḥ
a pratikarma ca sītāyāḥ sarvā daśarathastriyaḥ
c ātmanaiva tadā cakrur manasvinyo manoharam
a tato rāghavapatnīnāṃ sarvāsām eva śobhanam
c cakāra yatnāt kausalyā prahṛṣṭā putravatsalā
a tataḥ śatrughnavacanāt sumantro nāma sārathiḥ
c yojayitvābhicakrāma rathaṃ sarvāṅgaśobhanam
a arkamaṇḍalasaṃkāśaṃ divyaṃ dṛṣṭvā rathaṃ sthitam
c āruroha mahābāhū rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
a ayodhyāyāṃ tu sacivā rājño daśarathasya ye
c purohitaṃ puraskṛtya mantrayām āsur arthavat
a mantrayan rāmavṛddhyarthaṃ vṛttyarthaṃ nagarasya ca
c sarvam evābhiṣekārthaṃ jayārhasya mahātmanaḥ
e kartum arhatha rāmasya yad yan maṅgalapūrvakam
a iti te mantriṇaḥ sarve saṃdiśya tu purohitam
c nagarān niryayus tūrṇaṃ rāmadarśanabuddhayaḥ
a hariyuktaṃ sahasrākṣo ratham indra ivānaghaḥ
c prayayau ratham āsthāya rāmo nagaram uttamam
a jagrāha bharato raśmīñ śatrughnaś chatram ādade
c lakṣmaṇo vyajanaṃ tasya mūrdhni saṃparyavījayat
a śvetaṃ ca vālavyajanaṃ sugrīvo vānareśvaraḥ
c aparaṃ candrasaṃkāśaṃ rākṣasendro vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a ṛṣisaṃghair tadākāśe devaiś ca samarudgaṇaiḥ
c stūyamānasya rāmasya śuśruve madhuradhvaniḥ
a tataḥ śatruṃjayaṃ nāma kuñjaraṃ parvatopamam
c āruroha mahātejāḥ sugrīvo vānareśvaraḥ
a navanāgasahasrāṇi yayur āsthāya vānarāḥ
c mānuṣaṃ vigrahaṃ kṛtvā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ
a śaṅkhaśabdapraṇādaiś ca dundubhīnāṃ ca nisvanaiḥ
c prayayū puruṣavyāghras tāṃ purīṃ harmyamālinīm
a dadṛśus te samāyāntaṃ rāghavaṃ sapuraḥsaram
c virājamānaṃ vapuṣā rathenātirathaṃ tadā
a te vardhayitvā kākutsthaṃ rāmeṇa pratinanditāḥ
c anujagmur mahātmānaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritam
a amātyair brāhmaṇaiś caiva tathā prakṛtibhir vṛtaḥ
c śriyā viruruce rāmo nakṣatrair iva candramāḥ
a sa purogāmibhis tūryais tālasvastikapāṇibhiḥ
c pravyāharadbhir muditair maṅgalāni yayau vṛtaḥ
a akṣataṃ jātarūpaṃ ca gāvaḥ kanyās tathā dvijāḥ
c narā modakahastāś ca rāmasya purato yayuḥ
a sakhyaṃ ca rāmaḥ sugrīve prabhāvaṃ cānilātmaje
c vānarāṇāṃ ca tat karma vyācacakṣe 'tha mantriṇām
e śrutvā ca vismayaṃ jagmur ayodhyāpuravāsinaḥ
a dyutimān etad ākhyāya rāmo vānarasaṃvṛtaḥ
c hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākīrṇām ayodhyāṃ praviveśa ha
a tato hy abhyucchrayan paurāḥ patākās te gṛhe gṛhe
c aikṣvākādhyuṣitaṃ ramyam āsasāda pitur gṛham
a pitur bhavanam āsādya praviśya ca mahātmanaḥ
c kausalyāṃ ca sumitrāṃ ca kaikeyīṃ cābhyavādayat
a athābravīd rājaputro bharataṃ dharmiṇāṃ varam
c athopahitayā vācā madhuraṃ raghunandanaḥ
a yac ca madbhavanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sāśokavanikaṃ mahat
c muktāvaidūryasaṃkīrṇaṃ sugrīvasya nivedaya
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bharataḥ satyavikramaḥ
c pāṇau gṛhītvā sugrīvaṃ praviveśa tam ālayam
a tatas tailapradīpāṃś ca paryaṅkāstaraṇāni ca
c gṛhītvā viviśuḥ kṣipraṃ śatrughnena pracoditāḥ
a uvāca ca mahātejāḥ sugrīvaṃ rāghavānujaḥ
c abhiṣekāya rāmasya dūtān ājñāpaya prabho
a sauvarṇān vānarendrāṇāṃ caturṇāṃ caturo ghaṭān
c dadau kṣipraṃ sa sugrīvaḥ sarvaratnavibhūṣitān
a yathā pratyūṣasamaye caturṇāṃ sāgarāmbhasām
c pūrṇair ghaṭaiḥ pratīkṣadhvaṃ tathā kuruta vānarāḥ
a evam uktā mahātmāno vānarā vāraṇopamāḥ
c utpetur gaganaṃ śīghraṃ garuḍā iva śīghragāḥ
a jāmbavāṃś ca hanūmāṃś ca vegadarśī ca vānaraḥ
c ṛṣabhaś caiva kalaśāñ jalapūrṇān athānayan
e nadīśatānāṃ pañcānāṃ jale kumbhair upāharan
a pūrvāt samudrāt kalaśaṃ jalapūrṇam athānayat
c suṣeṇaḥ sattvasaṃpannaḥ sarvaratnavibhūṣitam
a ṛṣabho dakṣiṇāt tūrṇaṃ samudrāj jalam āharat
a raktacandanakarpūraiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ kāñcanaṃ ghaṭam
c gavayaḥ paścimāt toyam ājahāra mahārṇavāt
a ratnakumbhena mahatā śītaṃ mārutavikramaḥ
c uttarāc ca jalaṃ śīghraṃ garuḍānilavikramaḥ
a abhiṣekāya rāmasya śatrughnaḥ sacivaiḥ saha
c purohitāya śreṣṭhāya suhṛdbhyaś ca nyavedayat
a tataḥ sa prayato vṛddho vasiṣṭho brāhmaṇaiḥ saha
c rāmaṃ ratnamayo pīṭhe sahasītaṃ nyaveśayat
a vasiṣṭho vāmadevaś ca jābālir atha kāśyapaḥ
c kātyāyanaḥ suyajñaś ca gautamo vijayas tathā
a abhyaṣiñcan naravyāghraṃ prasannena sugandhinā
c salilena sahasrākṣaṃ vasavo vāsavaṃ yathā
a ṛtvigbhir brāhmaṇaiḥ pūrvaṃ kanyābhir mantribhis tathā
c yodhaiś caivābhyaṣiñcaṃs te saṃprahṛṣṭāḥ sanaigamaiḥ
a sarvauṣadhirasaiś cāpi daivatair nabhasi sthitaiḥ
c caturhir lokapālaiś ca sarvair devaiś ca saṃgataiḥ
a chatraṃ tasya ca jagrāha śatrughnaḥ pāṇḍuraṃ śubham
c śvetaṃ ca vālavyajanaṃ sugrīvo vānareśvaraḥ
e aparaṃ candrasaṃkāśaṃ rākṣasendro vibhīṣaṇaḥ
a mālāṃ jvalantīṃ vapuṣā kāñcanīṃ śatapuṣkarām
c rāghavāya dadau vāyur vāsavena pracoditaḥ
a sarvaratnasamāyuktaṃ maṇiratnavibhūṣitam
c muktāhāraṃ narendrāya dadau śakrapracoditaḥ
a prajagur devagandharvā nanṛtuś cāpsaro gaṇāḥ
c abhiṣeke tad arhasya tadā rāmasya dhīmataḥ
a bhūmiḥ sasyavatī caiva phalavantaś ca pādapāḥ
c gandhavanti ca puṣpāṇi babhūvū rāghavotsave
a sahasraśatam aśvānāṃ dhenūnāṃ ca gavāṃ tathā
c dadau śataṃ vṛṣān pūrvaṃ dvijebhyo manujarṣabhaḥ
a triṃśatkoṭīr hiraṇyasya brāhmaṇebhyo dadau punaḥ
c nānābharaṇavastrāṇi mahārhāṇi ca rāghavaḥ
a arkaraśmipratīkāśāṃ kāñcanīṃ maṇivigrahām
c sugrīvāya srajaṃ divyāṃ prāyacchan manujarṣabhaḥ
a vaidūryamaṇicitre ca vajraratnavibhūṣite
c vāliputrāya dhṛtimān aṅgadāyāṅgade dadau
a maṇipravarajuṣṭaṃ ca muktāhāram anuttamam
c sītāyai pradadau rāmaś candraraśmisamaprabham
a araje vāsasī divye śubhāny ābharaṇāni ca
c avekṣamāṇā vaidehī pradadau vāyusūnave
a avamucyātmanaḥ kaṇṭhād dhāraṃ janakanandinī
c avaikṣata harīn sarvān bhartāraṃ ca muhur muhuḥ
a tām iṅgitajñaḥ saṃprekṣya babhāṣe janakātmajām
c pradehi subhage hāraṃ yasya tuṣṭāsi bhāmini
a pauruṣaṃ vikramo buddhir yasminn etāni nityadā
c dadau sā vāyuputrāya taṃ hāram asitekṣaṇā
a hanūmāṃs tena hāreṇa śuśubhe vānararṣabhaḥ
c candrāṃśucayagaureṇa śvetābhreṇa yathācalaḥ
a tato dvivida maindābhyāṃ nīlāya ca paraṃtapaḥ
c sarvān kāmaguṇān vīkṣya pradadau vasudhādhipaḥ
a sarvavānaravṛddhāś ca ye cānye vānareśvarāḥ
c vāsobhir bhūṣaṇaiś caiva yathārhaṃ pratipūjitāḥ
a yathārhaṃ pūjitāḥ sarve kāmai ratnaiś ca puṣkalair
c prahṛṣṭamanasaḥ sarve jagmur eva yathāgatam
a rāghavaḥ paramodāraḥ śaśāsa parayā mudā
c uvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ rāmo dharmajñaṃ dharmavatsalaḥ
a ātiṣṭha dharmajña mayā sahemāṃ
gāṃ pūrvarājādhyuṣitāṃ balena
c tulyaṃ mayā tvaṃ pitṛbhir dhṛtā yā
tāṃ yauvarājye dhuram udvahasva
a sarvātmanā paryanunīyamāno
yadā na saumitrir upaiti yogam
c niyujyamāno bhuvi yauvarājye
tato 'bhyaṣiñcad bharataṃ mahātmā
a rāghavaś cāpi dharmātmā prāpya rājyam anuttamam
c īje bahuvidhair yajñaiḥ sasuhṛdbhrātṛbāndhavaḥ
a pauṇḍarīkāśvamedhābhyāṃ vājapeyena cāsakṛt
c anyaiś ca vividhair yajñair ayajat pārthivarṣabhaḥ
a rājyaṃ daśasahasrāṇi prāpya varṣāṇi rāghavaḥ
c śatāśvamedhān ājahre sadaśvān bhūridakṣiṇān
a ājānulambibāhuś ca mahāskandhaḥ pratāpavān
c lakṣmaṇānucaro rāmaḥ pṛthivīm anvapālayat
a na paryadevan vidhavā na ca vyālakṛtaṃ bhayam
c na vyādhijaṃ bhayaṃ vāpi rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati
a nirdasyur abhaval loko nānarthaḥ kaṃ cid aspṛśat
c na ca sma vṛddhā bālānāṃ pretakāryāṇi kurvate
a sarvaṃ muditam evāsīt sarvo dharmaparo 'bhavat
c rāmam evānupaśyanto nābhyahiṃsan parasparam
a āsan varṣasahasrāṇi tathā putrasahasriṇaḥ
c nirāmayā viśokāś ca rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati
a nityapuṣpā nityaphalās taravaḥ skandhavistṛtāḥ
c kālavarṣī ca parjanyaḥ sukhasparśaś ca mārutaḥ
a svakarmasu pravartante tuṣṭhāḥ svair eva karmabhiḥ
c āsan prajā dharmaparā rāme śāsati nānṛtāḥ
a sarve lakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ sarve dharmaparāyaṇāḥ
c daśavarṣasahasrāṇi rāmo rājyam akārayat
